# EFFECTS_INDEX

Purpose: cut token usage when implementing cards by quickly mapping "card text intent" to existing reusable effects and their constructor signatures.

## How to use this index

1. Parse card text into primitive actions (damage, draw, bounce, etc.).
2. Find each primitive below in the categorized sections and reuse existing effects.
3. Only add new effect records when no existing effect can express the behavior.
4. If you add a new effect record, create a `<EffectName>EffectHandler` `@Component` implementing `NormalEffectHandlerBean` in `service/effect/normalfx/`. `GameEngineConfig` auto-registers `@Component` handlers for production, card tests (`GameTestEngineContext`), and headless simulation (`HeadlessSimulationContext`). See provider map at bottom.
5. If your new effect targets something, override `targetSpec()` on the effect record to return a non-NONE `TargetSpec` (category + harmful flag + optional predicate — see targeting section below). The engine's declarative interpreter offers and type-checks the target from the spec; you do NOT add a validator for ordinary structural targeting.
6. If the new effect's `targetSpec()` includes permanents and it goes in the SPELL or ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD slot, the AI must know which board to aim it at: add a rule or map entry to `TargetPolarityClassifier` (`magical-vibes-ai`). `TargetPolarityGuardTest` scans the whole card pool and fails the build if the shape is unclassified — its failure message explains the polarity choices.
7. Only if legal targeting depends on a NON-structural rule the spec cannot express (opponent-relation, controller/owner compare, chosen-source, null-target tolerance) add a `@ValidatesTarget`-annotated method in the appropriate validator class under `service/validate/` — AND still declare the structural `targetSpec()` (see target validator map at bottom).

## Marker interfaces

| Interface | Extends | Purpose |
|-----------|---------|---------|
| `CostEffect` | `CardEffect` | Marks effects that represent additional costs (sacrifice, discard, exile, counter removal, tap creature). Cost effects are filtered out during effect snapshotting and excluded from mana ability detection. Implement this instead of `CardEffect` for new cost effects. Also carries DESCRIPTIVE AI cost-valuation facets (all default to neutral): `consumedPermanentFilter()` (`PermanentPredicate` for a payer-chosen sacrifice/return target), `consumesSourcePermanent()`, `sacrificesChosenCreature()`, `lifePaid(int)`, `sourceCountersRemoved()`, `consumedGraveyardCardCount()`, `consumedGraveyardCardType()`. Let `GameSimulator` (payment-planning) and `HardAiDecisionEngine` (cost scoring) read what a cost consumes without `instanceof`-ing each concrete record. Overridden by `SacrificeCreatureCost`, `SacrificeArtifactCost`, `SacrificePermanentCost`, `SacrificeSelfCost`, `PayLifeCost`, `RemoveChargeCountersFromSourceCost`, `ExileNCardsFromGraveyardCost`; other cost records inherit defaults. Payment execution stays concrete in `AbilityActivationService`. |
| `ManaProducingEffect` | `CardEffect` | Marks effects that produce mana. Used to identify mana abilities (CR 605.1a) without listing individual effect types. Implement this instead of `CardEffect` for new mana-producing effects. |
| `DamageDealingEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for effects that deal a single evaluated `DynamicAmount` to one target category: `damageAmount()`, `canDamageCreatures()`, `canDamagePlayers()`. Lets AI evaluators score burn without `instanceof`-ing each concrete type. Implemented by `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect`, `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect`, `DealDamageToPlayersEffect`. Not for split/mass damage (`DealDividedDamageEffect`, `MassDamageEffect`) or amount-less X burn. |
| `GlobalDamageMultiplyingEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for a static permanent that multiplies ALL damage dealt in the game, regardless of source/target/controller (Furnace of Rath): `damageMultiplierFactor()` (2 for a plain doubler; multiple stack multiplicatively). Read by `GameQueryService.getDamageMultiplier` and the Myr Battlesphere damage path in `MultiPermanentChoiceHandlerService`. Implemented by `DoubleDamageEffect`. Deliberately narrow — the selective doublers (`DoubleControllerDamageEffect`, `DoubleDamageToEnchantedPlayerEffect`, `DoubleEquippedCreatureCombatDamageEffect`) each pick out a different permanent subset in their own dedicated query methods and remain concrete. |
| `RemovalEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for single-target removal: `removalKind()` returns `RemovalKind` (`DESTROY`/`EXILE`/`BOUNCE`) or `null` when the config isn't single-target removal (e.g. mass bounce). Implemented by `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect`, `ExileTargetPermanentEffect`, `ReturnTargetPermanentToHandWithManaValueConditionalEffect`, `ReturnToHandEffect` (only for `BounceScope.TARGET`). |
| `BoardWipeEffect` | `CardEffect` | Recognition-only capability for board sweeps: `sweepsBoard()` (true when the current config is a mass sweep). Lets the AI's phase / defensive-pressure multipliers detect a wipe without naming the concrete type; the per-type wipe SCORING stays concrete (each sweep is valued differently). Implemented by `MassDamageEffect` (always), `DestroyAllPermanentsEffect` (always), `ReturnToHandEffect` (only for `BounceScope.ALL_MATCHING`). |
| `CardDrawingEffect` | `CardEffect` | `drawnCardAmount()` (`DynamicAmount`). Impl `DrawCardEffect`. |
| `LifeGainEffect` | `CardEffect` | `lifeGainAmount()` (`DynamicAmount`). Impl `GainLifeEffect`. |
| `TokenCreatingEffect` | `CardEffect` | Token profile: `tokenAmount()`, `tokenType()`, `tokenPower()`, `tokenToughness()`. Impl `CreateTokenEffect`. |
| `CreatureBoostEffect` | `CardEffect` | Targeted P/T pump: `powerBoost()`, `toughnessBoost()` (`DynamicAmount`). Impl `BoostTargetCreatureEffect`, `BoostTargetCreatureWhileSourceTappedEffect`. |
| `StaticCreatureBoostEffect` | `CardEffect` | Continuous anthem/aura boost: `powerBoost()`, `toughnessBoost()` (int), `grantedKeywords()`, `scope()`, `filter()`. Impl `StaticBoostEffect`. Optional `scalingCounter` (via `StaticBoostEffect(int, int, GrantScope, CounterType)`) multiplies the flat boost by the count of that counter type on the source — "All creatures get +1/+0 for each time counter on this" (Infinite Hourglass, `ALL_CREATURES` + `CounterType.TIME`). |
| `KeywordGrantingEffect` | `CardEffect` | `keywords()`, `scope()`, `filter()` (`PermanentPredicate` narrowing which permanents in scope receive the keyword(s), or `null`). Impl `GrantKeywordEffect`. |
| `ControlStealingEffect` | `CardEffect` | `controlDuration()`. Impl `GainControlOfTargetEffect`, `StealDyingOpponentPermanentUnlessPaysLifeEffect`. |
| `CounterSpellingEffect` | `CardEffect` | Marker: "counter target spell". Impl `CounterSpellEffect`, `CounterUnlessPaysEffect`, `CounterEachTargetSpellEffect`. |
| `CounterUnlessEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for the "counter target spell/ability unless its controller pays a ransom" family: `ransomKind()` returns `RansomKind` (`PAY_MANA`/`DISCARD_CARD`); `ransomMagnitude()` gives the generic mana amount (or 1 for a discard). Lets `TriggerCollectionService`, `MayAbilityHandlerService` and `MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService` recognise the family and route on the kind of ransom without `instanceof`-ing each concrete variant — the pay/discard choice-flow orchestration itself stays in those services. Implemented by `CounterUnlessPaysEffect` (also `CounterSpellingEffect`) and `CounterUnlessDiscardsEffect`. |
| `ClashOutcomeConditionalEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for a clash-trigger effect whose wrapped effect applies only on one clash outcome (CR 701.29c): `wrapped()` + `appliesOnWin()` (`true` = won, `false` = lost/tied). Read by `TriggerCollectionService.fireClashTriggers` to resolve the won/lost clause at trigger time without branching on the two wrapper types. Targeting still delegates to the wrapped effect on the concrete records. Implemented by `IfWonClashEffect`, `IfLostClashEffect`. |
| `RegenerationEffect` | `CardEffect` | Marker: regeneration. Impl `RegenerateEffect`. |
| `ProtectionGrantingEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for static "protection from …", read by the engine query layer (`GameQueryService`) not the AI: `protectionFromColors()` + `protectionScope()` (`GrantScope` null=self / `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`), `protectionFromCardTypes()`, `protectionFromSubtypes()`, `protectionFromManaValueAtLeast()` (`OptionalInt`); a record fills only its facet, inheriting empty/self defaults. Implemented by `ProtectionFromColorsEffect`, `ProtectionFromCardTypesEffect`, `ProtectionFromSubtypesEffect`, `ProtectionFromManaValueEffect`. Not for runtime-only protection (chosen-color `ProtectionFromChosenColorEffect`, or "protection from non-[subtype] creatures" tracked on the `Permanent`). |
| `BlockabilityRestrictionEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for attacker-side evasion (who may block this creature), read by the engine query layer (`GameQueryService`) not the AI: `cantBeBlocked()`, `unblockableIfDefenderControls()` (`PermanentPredicate`), `unblockableIfControllerCastHistoricSpellThisTurn()`, `unblockableWhileAttackingAlone()`, `blockableOnlyBy()` + `blockableOnlyByDescription()`, `cantBeBlockedByCreaturesMatching()`; a record fills only its facet, inheriting empty/`false` defaults. The engine evaluates the returned predicates and supplies engine-computed facts (attacking-alone, historic-spell-cast) itself. Implemented by `CantBeBlockedEffect`, `CanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterEffect`, `CantBeBlockedByCreaturesMatchingPredicateEffect`, `CantBeBlockedIfDefenderControlsMatchingPermanentEffect`, `CantBeBlockedIfControllerCastHistoricSpellThisTurnEffect`, `CantBeBlockedIfAttackingAloneEffect`. |
| `BlockingRestrictionEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for blocker-side restrictions (what a creature may block), read by `GameQueryService`: `cantBlock()`, `canBlockOnlyAttackersMatching()` + `canBlockOnlyAttackersDescription()`, and the board-wide `globalCantBlockBlockerMatcher()` / `globalCantBlockAttackerMatcher()` / `globalCantBlockDescription()` (e.g. Boldwyr Intimidator "Cowards can't block Warriors"); a record fills only its facet. Implemented by `CantBlockEffect`, `CanBlockOnlyIfAttackerMatchesPredicateEffect`, `MatchingCreaturesCantBlockMatchingCreaturesEffect`. |
| `BlockCostEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for a static per-block mana tax, read by `CombatBlockService.declareBlockers`: `blockCost(int attackerPower)` returns the generic mana that must be paid to declare this creature as a blocker of an attacker with the given effective power (0 = free). Block-side counterpart of the attack tax; the block is legal, only the cost gates it. Implemented by `CantBlockHighPowerCreaturesUnlessPaysEffect` (Hipparion). |
| `AttackOrBlockRestrictionEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for combined "can't attack or block" restrictions — attack side enforced in `CombatAttackService`, block side in `GameQueryService`: `globallyCantAttackOrBlock()` (`PermanentPredicate`, board-wide, e.g. Kulrath Knight / Light of Day), `cantAttackOrBlockUnless()` (`Condition`, per-creature, e.g. Blind-Spot Giant), `restrictionDescription()`. Implemented by `MatchingCreaturesCantAttackOrBlockEffect`, `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessEffect`. |
| `NoDefenderAttackPermissionEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability for "can attack as though it didn't have defender", read by `GameQueryService.canAttackDespiteDefender`: `grantsCarrierAttackAsThoughNoDefender()` (self grant — also matched when `ConditionalEffect`-wrapped, e.g. metalcraft, and as a floating until-end-of-turn grant) and `noDefenderAttackMatcher()` (`PermanentPredicate`, board-wide grant, e.g. Rolling Stones for Walls). Implemented by `CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect`, `MatchingCreaturesCanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect`. |
| `CombatDamageTriggerContextEffect` | `CardEffect` | Descriptive capability telling `CombatDamageService` how to build a fired `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` trigger's stack entry: `combatDamageTriggerContext()` returns a `TriggerContext` — `DAMAGED_PLAYER_WITH_DAMAGE_AMOUNT` (xValue = combat damage dealt, targetId = damaged player, no source; Balefire Dragon), `SOURCE_SELF` (source = the dealing creature, no target; explore / self-counter triggers), `DAMAGED_PLAYER` (targetId = damaged player, source = the dealing creature; "that player discards a card") — or `null` for the plain no-context entry (also the default for non-implementing effects). Recipient-dependent records report `DAMAGED_PLAYER` only when their recipient is the target player and `null` otherwise. Implemented by `ReturnPermanentsOnCombatDamageToPlayerEffect`, `DealDamageToEachCreatureDamagedPlayerControlsEffect`, `LookAtTopXCardsPermanentsToBattlefieldRestToGraveyardEffect`, `PutCountersOnSourceEffect`, `RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect`, `ExploreEffect`, `ExileTopCardsRepeatOnDuplicateEffect`, `TargetPlayerRandomDiscardOrControllerDrawsEffect`, `RevealRandomCardFromTargetPlayerHandEffect`, `SphinxAmbassadorEffect`, `TargetPlayerExilesFromHandEffect`, `ChooseCardsFromTargetHandEffect`, `SkipNextCombatPhaseEffect`, `TargetPlayerCantGainLifeRestOfGameEffect`, and `DiscardEffect` / `MillEffect` / `DealDamageToPlayersEffect` (only when recipient is the target player). Not for the bespoke `MayEffect`-wrapped or destroy/sacrifice "damaged player controls" flows, which remain concrete in `CombatDamageService`. |

The descriptive interfaces above let the AI (and engine query layer) read a FACT about an effect
instead of `instanceof`-ing the concrete type; implement the matching one when adding an effect to
that family (see `EFFECTS_QUICK_REFERENCE.md`). `CostEffect` is both a marker (cost snapshotting /
mana-ability exclusion) and a descriptive capability (its AI cost-valuation facets). `EffectDispatchRatchetTest` enforces that no new
concrete-effect `instanceof` is added outside `service/effect/**` / `service/validate/**`.

### Target predicate — the `TargetSpec.predicate()` field

Effects that target permanents can optionally restrict valid targets by putting a `PermanentPredicate` in their `targetSpec()`'s `predicate` field (`benign(CREATURE, predicate)` / `harmful(PERMANENT, predicate)`). The declarative interpreter enforces it at cast, and saga-chapter / end-step targeting pipelines read it through `EffectResolution.targetPredicateOf(effect)`. Absent = `null` (no restriction).

Dual note: `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect.withTargetRestriction(CounterType, int count, PermanentPredicate)` keeps the predicate on a dedicated record COMPONENT (its `targetSpec()` carries a `null` predicate, so there is no cast-time gate); it is honoured only by the saga/end-step pipelines via `EffectResolution.targetPredicateOf`. `GrantKeywordEffect` carries its `filter` in the spec's predicate when `scope == TARGET`.

### Self-targeting — the `TargetSpec.selfTargeting()` field

Effects that implicitly target their source permanent (boost-self, animate-self, regenerate-self, etc.) set `selfTargeting = true` in their `targetSpec()` — written `new TargetSpec(TargetCategory.NONE, false, null, true, 1)`. `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService` reads `targetSpec().selfTargeting()` to auto-assign the source as the target when no explicit target is provided.

Effects doing so: `BoostSelfEffect`, `DoubleSelfPowerToughnessEffect`, `TapPermanentsEffect`/`UntapPermanentsEffect` (only when `scope == TapUntapScope.SELF`), `AnimatePermanentsEffect` (only when `scope == GrantScope.SELF`), `PutCountersOnSelfEffect`, `PutSlimeCounterAndCreateOozeTokenEffect`, `RegenerateEffect` (when `!targetsPermanent()`), `GrantKeywordEffect` (when `scope == SELF`).

### `isPowerToughnessDefining()` default method on `CardEffect`

Effects that are characteristic-defining abilities (CDAs) for power/toughness (`*/*` effects) override `isPowerToughnessDefining()` to return `true`. Per CR 707.9d, when a copy effect provides specific P/T values (e.g. "except it's 7/7"), CDAs that define P/T are not copied. Used by `CopyPermanentOnEnterEffect` with `powerOverride`/`toughnessOverride`.

Effects returning `true`: `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect` (the single CDA record that replaced the entire `PowerToughnessEqualTo*` family and the ooze-token `BoostSelfBySlimeCountersOnLinkedPermanentEffect`).

---

## Effect targeting declarations

An effect declares what it targets by overriding the single `targetSpec()` method on `CardEffect` to
return a `TargetSpec` (a `TargetCategory` + a `harmful` flag + an optional `PermanentPredicate` + the
`selfTargeting` / `playerTargetCount` fields). The eleven legacy `canTarget*` / `isSelfTargeting` /
`isDamageOrDestruction` / `targetPredicate` / `requiredPlayerTargetCount` booleans were DELETED
(TargetSpec migration, July 2026) — `targetSpec()` is now the ONE source of truth, and everything
(`EffectResolution.needsTarget(card)` / `needsSpellTarget(card)`, the AI, the trigger collectors, the
`TargetValidationService` interpreter) derives from it. Never call
`setNeedsTarget`/`setNeedsSpellTarget`. For kicker/modal spells use
`EffectResolution.resolveEffects(effects, kicked, modeIndex)` first to get the resolved effect list.

**Modal triggered abilities** (e.g. a "choose one" upkeep trigger, Etherwrought Page): spells/ETB
pick their `ChooseOneEffect` mode at cast time and never reach the stack as a raw ChooseOneEffect; a
triggered ability has no cast, so put the `ChooseOneEffect` directly in the trigger slot and the mode
is picked as the ability resolves. `ChooseOneEffectHandler` (normalfx, handles `ChooseOneEffect.class`)
opens a `ChoiceContext.ChooseModeChoice` list pick; `ChoiceHandlerService.handleChooseModeChoice`
splices the chosen mode's effects into the paused resolution so they resolve in card-text order
(gain/lose life resolve immediately; a surveil mode still queues its "may" prompt). Non-targeting modes
only — a targeted mode would need per-mode trigger-time target selection (cf. RelicBindModeChoice).

**Factories** (all on `TargetSpec`): `harmful(cat)` / `benign(cat)` and the predicate-carrying
`harmful(cat, predicate)` / `benign(cat, predicate)`; plus `TargetSpec.NONE` (targets nothing). Use
the full canonical constructor for self-targeting or a two-player count:
`new TargetSpec(TargetCategory.NONE, false, null, /*selfTargeting*/ true, 1)`,
`new TargetSpec(TargetCategory.PLAYER, false, null, false, /*playerTargetCount*/ 2)`.

**`harmful`** = true exactly when the effect damages / fights / destroys / exiles / sacrifices its
target (i.e. the target must survive a `checkProtection` test — protection means "can't be
targeted"). Counters, bounces, control-changes, boosts, taps, text changes are `benign`.

`TargetCategory` values and what each offers/type-checks:

| Category | Legal target |
|----------|--------------|
| `NONE` | nothing (default) |
| `PLAYER` | a player |
| `PLAYER_OR_PERMANENT` | a player or any permanent |
| `PERMANENT` | any permanent |
| `CREATURE` | a creature (layer-aware) |
| `LAND` | a land |
| `CREATURE_OR_PLANESWALKER` | a creature or planeswalker |
| `PLAYER_OR_PLANESWALKER` | a player or planeswalker |
| `ANY_TARGET` | any target (player / creature / planeswalker) |
| `SPELL_ON_STACK` | a spell on the stack (validated on the stack path) |
| `GRAVEYARD_CARD` | a card in a graveyard (opponent's, the default) |
| `ANY_GRAVEYARD_CARD` | a card in any graveyard |
| `CONTROLLERS_GRAVEYARD_CARD` | a card in the controller's own graveyard |
| `EXILE_CARD` | a card in exile |

Fine-grained narrowing (artifact-only, nonland, a subtype) is the spec's `PermanentPredicate` field,
NOT a new category. Conditional effects (a `scope` / `recipient` that sometimes targets nothing)
compute a per-instance spec, e.g. `recipient == TARGET_PLAYER ? benign(PLAYER) : NONE`.

### Worked example — a new "deal N damage to target creature" effect

```java
public record ZapTargetCreatureEffect(int damage) implements CardEffect {
    @Override
    public TargetSpec targetSpec() {
        return TargetSpec.harmful(TargetCategory.CREATURE); // damage → harmful; creature-only category
    }
}
```

That is the WHOLE targeting declaration: the interpreter in `TargetValidationService` offers only
creatures, rejects a creature with protection from the source (because `harmful`), and needs no
`@ValidatesTarget` validator (the category is purely structural). To restrict further — say "target
artifact creature" — pass a predicate: `TargetSpec.harmful(TargetCategory.CREATURE, new
PermanentIsArtifactPredicate())`.

Add a `@ValidatesTarget` validator ONLY when legality depends on a rule the category + predicate
cannot express (opponent-relation, controller/owner compare, chosen-source, null-target tolerance) —
and such an effect STILL declares its structural `targetSpec()` (the `TargetSpecRatchetTest` guard
enforces this). See the target validator map at the bottom.

### Multi-target group binding (spells with several distinct targets)

A spell like "Target creature gets +1/+1 … Another target creature gets -1/-1" declares one
`target(filter)` group per distinct target and binds an ordinary, position-agnostic effect to
each group:

```java
target(creatureFilter).addEffect(EffectSlot.SPELL, new BoostTargetCreatureEffect(1, 1));
target(creatureFilter).addEffect(EffectSlot.SPELL, new BoostTargetCreatureEffect(-1, -1));
```

At resolution, an effect bound to a group applies to **all targets chosen for that group**
(`StackEntry.targetsForEffect` slices the flat target list by the card's declarations;
`EffectResolutionService` also remaps `entry.targetId` to the group's first target for
single-target handlers). An unbound effect (plain `addEffect`) keeps the legacy semantics —
the whole flat target list. **Never create position-named effect classes**
(`XxxFirstTargetEffect`/`XxxSecondTargetEffect`); reuse the generic effect and bind it to the
right group. Wrapper effects (`ConditionalEffect`, `MayEffect`, …) propagate the binding to
their inner effect automatically.

Rules of thumb:
- Per CR 608.2b the spell resolves partially: a group whose targets are all gone simply does
  nothing; the spell fizzles only when ALL chosen targets are illegal.
- A variable-count group ("up to N": `target(filter, 0, N)`) must be the **last** declared
  group — the flat wire format fills groups in declaration order, so an earlier variable group
  would be ambiguous.
- The only effects that inherently read two targets carry their group indices as record DATA:
  `FightTargetsEffect(firstGroup, secondGroup)` and
  `TargetDealsPowerDamageToTargetEffect(sourceGroup, victimGroup)` (both default to `(0, 1)`).
  For activated abilities (which declare targets via `multiTargetFilters`, not `target()`),
  these indices address flat target positions instead.

### Per-blocker trigger mode

Effects in the `ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED` slot can be registered with `TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER` via `addEffect(slot, effect, TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER)`, causing CombatService to create one stack entry per blocking creature (e.g. "whenever this creature becomes blocked **by a creature**"). Cards using this: `SylvanBasilisk`, `EngulfingSlagwurm` (ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED only), `InfiltrationLens`.

`ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED` fires only for *this* creature. For "whenever **a creature you control** becomes blocked" (any of your creatures), use `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_BECOMES_BLOCKED` — fires once per blocked attacker on every permanent with the slot on the blocked creature's controller's battlefield; the blocked creature is the non-targeting `sourcePermanentId` so `BoostSelfEffect` applies to "it". Used by `UnstoppableAsh`.

### Becomes-target-of-spell trigger

Effects in the `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_SPELL` slot fire when the permanent (or the creature an equipment is attached to) becomes the target of a spell (spells only — not abilities). Two kinds of effect are supported, split by `targetSpec()`:
- **Targeting effects** (non-`NONE` category, e.g. `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect`) route through the shared "choose any target" interaction — "deal 2 damage to any target" when the equipped creature becomes targeted (`LivewireLash`).
- **Non-targeting effects** (`TargetSpec.NONE`, e.g. `SacrificeSelfEffect`) go straight onto the stack as a `TRIGGERED_ABILITY` with `sourcePermanentId` set to the source — "When this creature becomes the target of a spell, sacrifice it" (`LabyrinthGuardian`; `JaceCunningCastaway`'s Illusion tokens). The any-target interaction never records a source, so a self-referential effect must take this path or it would no-op.

### Becomes-target-of-spell-or-ability trigger

Effects in the `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_SPELL_OR_ABILITY` slot fire when the permanent (or a permanent it is attached to) becomes the target of any spell or activated ability. The triggered ability goes directly on the stack with `sourcePermanentId` set to the source permanent. Cards using this: `IceCage`.

Special case — "counter that spell or ability for the first time each turn" (`GlyphKeeper`): put a `CounterSpellEffect` (any `CounterSpellingEffect`) in this slot. `TriggerCollectionService` recognizes the counterspelling effect, fires the trigger **at most once per turn per permanent** (gated by `Permanent.becomeTargetCounterUsedThisTurn`, reset at turn start), and sets the trigger's `targetId`/`targetZone` to the triggering spell/ability's card in the STACK zone so the counter finds the object that targeted it. No controller restriction — it counters the controller's own spells too.

### Ally creature becomes target of opponent spell or ability trigger

Effects in the `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_OPPONENT_SPELL_OR_ABILITY` slot fire on ALL permanents with this slot on the creature's controller's battlefield whenever a creature that player controls becomes the target of a spell or ability controlled by an opponent. Unlike the `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_*` slots (which fire on the targeted permanent itself), this slot fires on a separate permanent that monitors the event globally. Cards using this: `ShapersSanctuary`.

### Any creature becomes target of spell or ability trigger

Effects in the `ON_ANY_CREATURE_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_SPELL_OR_ABILITY` slot fire on ALL permanents with this slot across every battlefield whenever ANY creature (any controller) becomes the target of ANY spell or ability. Broader than `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_OPPONENT_SPELL_OR_ABILITY` (no controller/opponent restriction). The targeted creature is set as the non-targeting `targetId` so the resolved effect can act on it — pair with `ReturnToHandEffect.target()` for "return that creature to its owner's hand". Cards using this: `Cowardice`.

## Wrapper / modifier effects

### Conditional effects (the `Condition` model)

Game-state conditions are **data**, not classes: the sealed interface
`model/condition/Condition` has one small record per condition (`Metalcraft`, `Morbid`,
`Kicked`, `Raid`, `Equipped`, `ControlsPermanent(filter)`,
`ControlsPermanentCount(minCount, filter)` (at least), `ControlsPermanentCountAtMost(maxCount, filter)` (at most),
`AnyPlayerControlsPermanent(filter)`, `AnyPlayerControlsPermanentCount(minCount, filter)` (N+ across all battlefields),
`AnyPlayerControlsPermanentCountAtMost(maxCount, filter)` (at most N across all battlefields — use `0` for "no matching permanents on the battlefield"; Pestilence's end-step self-sacrifice when no creatures exist),
`OpponentControlsPermanent(filter)`, `DefendingPlayerControlsPermanent(filter)`, `DefendingPlayerPoisoned`,
`OpponentPoisoned`, `OpponentDealtDamageThisTurn(minimumAmount)` (an opponent was dealt N+ damage this turn — use `1` for "any damage"; Bloodcrazed Goblin, Spinerock Knoll), `OpponentLostLifeThisTurn(minimumAmount)` (an opponent lost N+ life this turn from any source, damage included — reads `lifeLostThisTurn`; Sygg, River Cutthroat),
`ControllerLifeAtLeast(n)`,
`ControllerLifeAtMost(n)`, `GraveyardCardThreshold(n, filter)`, `CardsInLibraryAtLeast(n)` (controller has N+ cards in library; Battle of Wits), `AnyLibraryAtMost(n)` (some player's library has N or fewer cards; Shelldock Isle), `CardsInHandAtLeast(n)` (controller has N+ cards in hand; Imaginary Pet), `CardsInHandAtMost(n)` (controller has N or fewer cards in hand; Thresher Lizard STATIC +1/+2 with threshold 1), `ActivePlayerHandEmpty` (the player whose upkeep/step it is has no cards in hand — gates upkeep triggers that read "if you/that player have no cards in hand"; Hollowborn Barghest), `CastFromZone(zone)`,
`AttacksAlone`, `FirstCombatPhase` (met when the current combat phase is the turn's first — reads `GameData.combatPhasesThisTurn == 1`; gates additional-combat effects from looping across the extra combats they create, Finest Hour's intervening "if it's the first combat phase of the turn"), `MinimumAttackers(n)`, `AttackedWithCreaturesThisTurn(minimum)` (controller declared N+ attacking creatures this turn, cumulative across combats; Windbrisk Heights), `HasAttacker(predicate)`, `NoSpellsCastLastTurn`,
`TwoOrMoreSpellsCastLastTurn`, `SourceCounterThreshold(n, type)`, `SourceUntapped` (the source permanent is untapped — Sphinx Sovereign's end-step branch), `TopCardOfLibraryColor(color)`,
`SelfHasKeyword(keyword)`, `ControllerTurn`, `NotControllerTurn`, `SourceHasSubtype(subtype)`,
`TargetPermanentMatches(filter)`, `WonClash` (the controller won their most recent clash — written by
`ClashEffect` during resolution, read by a later effect on the same stack entry; e.g. Whirlpool Whelm's
"if you win, you may put that creature on top of its owner's library instead"), and more — see the
package for the full list). Two generic wrappers combine a condition with effects:

- `ConditionalEffect(Condition condition, CardEffect wrapped)` — resolves/applies `wrapped`
  only while the condition is met (intervening-if / "as long as" patterns). Targeting
  delegates to the wrapped effect.
- `ConditionalReplacementEffect(Condition condition, CardEffect baseEffect, CardEffect upgradedEffect)`
  — resolves `upgradedEffect` when the condition is met, otherwise `baseEffect`
  ("instead" upgrade patterns, e.g. kicker). Targeting delegates to both. A 2-arg convenience
  form `ConditionalReplacementEffect(condition, upgradedEffect)` sets `baseEffect` to `null`
  ("apply this effect iff the condition is met, otherwise nothing"); it is meaningful only for
  entry-time replacement effects (the conditional enters-tapped land cycles), never for stack
  resolution.

All conditions are evaluated in one place, the engine's `ConditionEvaluationService`
(exhaustive switch over the sealed hierarchy — adding a condition without an evaluation is a
compile error). New conditions: add the record to `model/condition/`, add it to the `permits`
list on `Condition`, and add its case to `ConditionEvaluationService.isMet`. Never add a new
per-condition wrapper effect class.

### Dynamic amounts (the `DynamicAmount` model)

Dynamically computed quantities are **data** too — the numeric sibling of `Condition`. The
sealed interface `model/amount/DynamicAmount` has one small record per derivation:

- `Fixed(int value)` — a constant (`new BoostSelfEffect(2, 2)` is sugar for two `Fixed`s)
- `XValue()` — the stack entry's snapshotted `xValue` (mana spent to cast the triggering
  spell, X paid, …); **cast-time** data
- `EventValue()` — the stack entry's snapshotted `eventValue`: the **trigger-event or
  prior-resolution** integer behind the entry (life gained, damage dealt, excess damage).
  Snapshotted by the trigger collector that enqueues the entry (Sanguine Bond: life gained →
  `LoseLifeEffect(new EventValue(), TARGET_PLAYER)`) or by an earlier effect on the same entry
  (Archaic's Agony: `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect` stores the excess, then
  `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect(EventValue())` reads it). Distinct from `XValue`
  (cast-time) — see the snapshotting note below
- `Scaled(DynamicAmount amount, int factor)` — base amount × constant ("+2/+0 per Equipment"
  = `Scaled(count, 2)`)
- `Divided(DynamicAmount amount, int divisor)` — base amount ÷ constant, rounded down ("half
  the number of Zombies you control, rounded down" = `Divided(count, 2)`, Endless Ranks of
  the Dead)
- `HalvedRoundedUp(DynamicAmount amount)` — base amount halved and rounded *up* (the round-up
  sibling of `Divided(amount, 2)`, which floors). "That player loses half their life, rounded up"
  (Quietus Spike) = `LoseLifeEffect(new HalvedRoundedUp(new TargetPlayerLifeTotal()), LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)`
- `Sum(List<DynamicAmount> amounts)` (varargs ctor) — components summed independently, so a
  permanent matching two summed `PermanentCount`s counts twice (War Report: creature count +
  artifact count, artifact creatures add 2)
- `Min(List<DynamicAmount> amounts)` (varargs ctor) — the smallest of the components (the
  clamp/cap sibling of `Sum`); empty → `0`. Models "up to N" reductions: Blood Lust's toughness
  change of `-min(4, toughness - 1)` = `Scaled(Min(Fixed(4), Sum(TargetToughness, Fixed(-1))), -1)`
- `Max(List<DynamicAmount> amounts)` (varargs ctor) — the largest of the components (the floor
  sibling of `Min`); empty → `0`. Floors a "minus N" amount at 0 so it never goes negative: Ivory
  Tower's "gain X life, where X is the number of cards in your hand minus 4" (never loses life) =
  `Max(Fixed(0), Sum(CardsInHand(CONTROLLER), Fixed(-4)))`
- `DuringControllerTurn(DynamicAmount amount)` — the wrapped amount during the source
  controller's turn (`activePlayerId == controllerId`), else `0`. Models "during your turn, …"
  CDA wordings: Angry Mob's "2 plus the number of Swamps your opponents control" on your turn
  and a flat 2 otherwise = `Sum(Fixed(2), DuringControllerTurn(PermanentCount(SWAMP, OPPONENTS)))`
- `IfSourceAttacking(DynamicAmount whileAttacking, DynamicAmount otherwise)` — `whileAttacking`
  when the source permanent is attacking, else `otherwise` (and `otherwise` when there is no
  source). Models CDAs that switch on the source's combat state: Gaea's Liege = `IfSourceAttacking(PermanentCount(FOREST, DEFENDING_PLAYER), PermanentCount(FOREST, CONTROLLER))`
- `PermanentCount(PermanentPredicate filter, CountScope scope[, boolean excludeSource])` —
  matching battlefield permanents; `CountScope` is `CONTROLLER` / `OPPONENTS` / `ANY_PLAYER` /
  `TARGET_PLAYER` / `DEFENDING_PLAYER` (the player the source is attacking — its attack target
  if a player, else the attacked planeswalker's controller; nothing when not attacking);
  `excludeSource=true` models "each *other* …" wordings
- `CardsInGraveyard(CardPredicate filter, CountScope scope)` — matching non-token cards in
  the graveyard(s) in scope (`null` filter = every card)
- `CardsInHand(CountScope scope)` — cards in the hand(s) of the players in scope
- `MatchingCardsInHand(CountScope scope, CardPredicate predicate)` — cards matching `predicate`
  in the hand(s) in scope (filtered sibling of `CardsInHand`). Sacellum Godspeaker = "Add {G} for
  each creature card with power 5+ revealed" (`CONTROLLER`, `CardAllOf(CREATURE, CardPowerAtLeast(5))`)
- `CardsInLibrary(CountScope scope)` — cards in the library/libraries of the players in scope
  (`gameData.playerDecks`; Invincible Hymn = `CONTROLLER`)
- `UntappedLandsAtTurnStart()` — the number of untapped lands the *targeted* player controlled at
  the beginning of the current turn, read from the `gameData.untappedLandsAtTurnStart` snapshot
  (taken as each player's upkeep begins, post-untap, in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers`).
  Locked at turn start, so tapping lands in response to the upkeep trigger doesn't lower it (Power
  Surge, CR ruling). Target player id comes from the stack entry's target channel
- `ControllerLifeTotal()` — the controller's current life total (Serra Avatar / Ajani
  Goldmane's Avatar token, whose P/T are each equal to their controller's life total)
- `TargetPlayerLifeTotal()` — the *targeted* player's current life total, read from the stack
  entry's target channel (0 without a legal target player). Player-facing sibling of
  `ControllerLifeTotal`; for combat-damage triggers the damaged player is baked in as the target.
  Wrap in `HalvedRoundedUp` for "loses half their life, rounded up" (Quietus Spike)
- `HalfControllerLifeRoundedUp()` — half the controller's current life total, rounded up
  (`(life + 1) / 2`); "its owner loses half their life, rounded up" (Personal Incarnation)
- `CountersOnSource(CounterType counterType)` — counters of that type on the source
  permanent; reads the stack entry's live source, falling back to the last-known
  `sourcePermanentSnapshot` when the source left the battlefield as a cost (Golden Urn)
- `CountersOnLinkedPermanent(CounterType counterType, UUID linkedPermanentId)` — counters
  of that type on a specific permanent identified by ID (0 if it has left the battlefield);
  for token CDAs referencing another permanent, e.g. Gutter Grime's Ooze tokens
- `GreatestPowerAmongControlled()` — greatest effective power among creatures the
  controller controls (0 if none)
- `AttachmentsOnSource(boolean countAuras, boolean countEquipment)` — Auras/Equipment
  attached to the source
- `CreaturesBlockingSource()` — creatures currently blocking the source
- `OtherAttackersSharingCreatureTypeWithTarget()` — attacking creatures (other than the stack
  entry's target) that share a creature type with the target, counted once each (Changeling-aware
  via `GameQueryService.shareCreatureType`). Reads the target from the stack entry's target channel;
  pair with `BoostTargetCreatureEffect` on an `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS` trigger whose target is the
  triggering attacker (recorded non-targeting by `CombatAttackService`). Shared Animosity =
  `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(new OtherAttackersSharingCreatureTypeWithTarget(), new Fixed(0))`
- `OpponentPoisonCounters()` — total poison counters on opponents
- `ColorManaSymbolsAmongControlledPermanents(ManaColor color)` — chroma-across-permanents: total
  `color` mana symbols in the mana costs of all permanents the controller controls (hybrid/Phyrexian
  of that color count once each; generic/{X} never; via `ManaCost.countColorSymbols`). Springjack
  Shepherd = `CreateTokenEffect(new ColorManaSymbolsAmongControlledPermanents(ManaColor.WHITE), "Goat", 0, 1, …)`
- `ColorManaSymbolsInGraveyard(ManaColor color, CountScope scope)` — chroma-across-graveyard: total
  `color` mana symbols in the mana costs of the non-token cards in the graveyard(s) in scope
  (hybrid/Phyrexian of that color count once each; generic/{X} never; via `ManaCost.countColorSymbols`).
  Umbra Stalker = `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(a, a)` with
  `a = new ColorManaSymbolsInGraveyard(ManaColor.BLACK, CountScope.CONTROLLER)`
- `ColorManaSymbolsInHand(ManaColor color)` — chroma-across-hand: total `color` mana symbols in the
  mana costs of the cards in the controller's hand (hybrid/Phyrexian of that color count once each;
  generic/{X} never; via `ManaCost.countColorSymbols`). Models "reveal any number of cards in your
  hand" as the whole hand (revealing more only raises the count). Phosphorescent Feast =
  `GainLifeEffect(new Scaled(new ColorManaSymbolsInHand(ManaColor.GREEN), 2))`
- `CreatureDeathsThisTurn(CountScope scope)` — creatures put into a graveyard from the
  battlefield this turn, summed over the players in scope (per-controller
  `GameData.creatureDeathCountThisTurn`; Fresh Meat = `CONTROLLER`)
- `DamageDealtToTargetPlayerThisTurn()` — total damage dealt to the *targeted* player this turn
  from any source (combat/spell/ability, including damage dealt as poison), read from
  `GameData.damageDealtToPlayersThisTurn` (populated via `GameData.recordDamageToPlayer`). Reads the
  target from the stack entry's target channel, so pair with a player-targeting effect; Final
  Punishment = `LoseLifeEffect(new DamageDealtToTargetPlayerThisTurn(), LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)`
- `CardsDiscardedByTargetPlayerThisTurn()` — number of cards the *targeted* player discarded this
  turn (any discard, any source), read from `GameData.cardsDiscardedThisTurn` (incremented in
  `TriggerCollectionService.checkDiscardTriggers`, the central discard hook). Reads the target from
  the stack entry's target channel, so pair with a player-targeting effect. `DrawCardEffect` advertises
  a player target when its amount is this record; Dream Salvage = `DrawCardEffect(new
  CardsDiscardedByTargetPlayerThisTurn())` + `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))`
- `CardsPutIntoGraveyardByTargetPlayerThisTurn()` — number of non-token cards put into the *targeted*
  player's graveyard from anywhere this turn, read from `GameData.cardsPutIntoGraveyardFromAnywhereThisTurn`
  (populated at the single zone→graveyard choke point in `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard`; tokens
  excluded, and cards that later left the graveyard still count — the set is cleared only at turn start).
  Reads the target from the stack entry's target channel, so pair with a player-targeting/curse effect;
  Fraying Sanity = `MillEffect(new CardsPutIntoGraveyardByTargetPlayerThisTurn(), MillRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)`
  in the `ENCHANTED_PLAYER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` slot (enchanted player baked as `targetId`)
- `DamageDealtToOpponentsThisTurn()` — total damage dealt to the controller's opponents this turn,
  summed over every opponent, from `GameData.damageDealtToPlayersThisTurn`. Controller-relative (no
  target needed); Notorious Throng = `CreateTokenEffect(new DamageDealtToOpponentsThisTurn(), …)`
- `DamageDealtToControllerThisTurn()` — total damage dealt to the effect's controller this turn from
  any source (combat/spell/ability, including damage dealt as poison), from
  `GameData.damageDealtToPlayersThisTurn`. Controller-relative counterpart of
  `DamageDealtToTargetPlayerThisTurn` (no target needed); Simulacrum = `GainLifeEffect(new
  DamageDealtToControllerThisTurn())` + `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(new DamageDealtToControllerThisTurn())`
- `LifeLostThisTurn(CountScope scope)` — total life lost this turn (direct loss and damage, since
  damage causes loss of life; net life change is irrelevant — life gained does not reduce it), summed
  over the players in scope, from `GameData.lifeLostThisTurn` (cleared each turn). Tainted Sigil =
  `GainLifeEffect(new LifeLostThisTurn(CountScope.ANY_PLAYER))` ("gain life equal to the total life lost by all players this turn")
- `ImprintedCreaturePower()` / `ImprintedCreatureToughness()` — the imprinted creature
  card's P/T (0 if nothing imprinted)
- `LandsMatchingImprintedName()` — lands on any battlefield whose name matches the source's
  imprinted card (0 if nothing imprinted); Strata Scythe
- `BasicLandTypesAmongControlledLands()` — Domain (CR 702.42): the number of distinct basic land
  types (Plains/Island/Swamp/Mountain/Forest) among lands the controller controls. Respects CR
  305.7 land-type overrides (via `GameQueryService.effectiveBasicLandTypes`) except in static
  evaluation, where only intrinsic printed types are read to avoid `computeStaticBonus` recursion.
  Wrap in `Scaled(amount, 2)` for "{2} for each basic land type" (Draco cost reduction + upkeep tax)
- `SourcePower()` / `SourceToughness()` — the source permanent's effective power/toughness
  at evaluation time, never negative; uses the live source or the last-known snapshot when
  it left the battlefield (CR 608.2h — Spikeshot Elder, Steadfast Armasaur)
- `TargetToughness()` — the resolved target permanent's effective toughness at resolution,
  never negative; 0 when there is no legal target (matching the fizzle behaviour of the
  handlers it replaces). The target is read from the stack entry's `targetId` (Condemn)
- `TargetPower()` — the resolved target permanent's effective power at resolution, never
  negative; 0 when there is no legal target. The power analogue of `TargetToughness`; target
  read from the stack entry's `targetId` (Chastise: gain life = target's power, then destroy it)
- `TargetManaValue()` — the resolved target permanent's mana value at resolution; 0 when there
  is no legal target. Target read from the stack entry's `targetId`. Used for "becomes a creature
  with power and toughness each equal to its mana value" animations (Xenic Poltergeist)
- `ManaSpentToCast()` — total mana spent to cast the spell, snapshotted into the entry's
  xValue at cast time (`SpellCastingService` keys the snapshot on this amount inside a
  spell-slot damage effect — distinct from `XValue` so converge/X payments aren't
  overwritten; Molten Note)
- `FixedIfControlMoreCreaturesThanEachOtherPlayer(int amount, int otherwise)` — `amount` when
  the controller controls strictly more creatures than every other player, else `otherwise`.
  Feeds the `chooseCount` of a `LookAtTopCardsEffect` for "put two … if you control more
  creatures than each other player, otherwise put one" (Advice from the Fae, `(2, 1)`)

All amounts are evaluated in one place, the engine's `AmountEvaluationService` (exhaustive
switch, parallel to `ConditionEvaluationService`; contexts built via
`AmountContext.forStackEntry` / `forStaticEffect`). `AmountContext` carries the values that
differ per evaluation site: `controllerId`, `sourcePermanent` (source-relative amounts),
`targetPermanentId` (target-relative amounts such as `TargetToughness`, read from the entry's
`targetId` the same way `ConditionContext.targetId` is), plus two snapshotted integer channels
— `xValue` (**cast-time** data, read by `XValue`/`ManaSpentToCast`) and `eventValue`
(**trigger-event / prior-resolution** data, read by `EventValue`). `forStackEntry` pulls all of
these off the `StackEntry`; the source-less/static/estimation factories leave them null/0.

**Who snapshots `eventValue`, and when:** the entry's `eventValue` is populated either by the
**trigger collector** that enqueues the entry (parallel to how `SpellCastTriggerCollectorService`
snapshots spell-mana-spent into `xValue`) or by an **earlier effect on the same entry** that
produced the number (the excess-damage case). Both guard the write with
`AmountEvaluationService.referencesEventValue(amount)` (the event-value analogue of
`referencesXValue`) so an entry only carries a value when some effect actually reads it —
e.g. `MiscTriggerCollectorService` snapshots life-gained only when the enqueued
`LoseLifeEffect`'s amount references it, and `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffectHandler`
stores the excess damage only when a following `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect` reads it.
Prefer `EventValue` for numbers known only at trigger/resolution time; `XValue` stays cast-time.

Effects that only differ in HOW A NUMBER
IS COMPUTED must be a single record parameterized with `DynamicAmount` — see
`BoostSelfEffect(DynamicAmount, DynamicAmount)` (replaced the entire `BoostSelfPer*` family),
`SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(DynamicAmount power, DynamicAmount toughness)` (the CDA sibling —
sets P/T on a 0/0 base via the selfOnly `SetPowerToughnessToAmountSelfEffectHandler`; replaced the
entire `PowerToughnessEqualTo*` family and the ooze-token `BoostSelfBySlimeCountersOnLinkedPermanentEffect`),
`AttachedBoostEffect(DynamicAmount, DynamicAmount, GrantScope)` (the attached-scope sibling —
replaced `BoostCreaturePerCardsInAllGraveyardsEffect`, `BoostCreaturePerCardsInControllerGraveyardEffect`,
`BoostCreaturePerControlledCardTypeEffect`, `BoostCreaturePerControlledSubtypeEffect`, and
`BoostCreaturePerMatchingLandNameEffect`; amounts evaluate against the Aura/Equipment's
controller, so `CountScope.CONTROLLER` = "you"/"you control" per CR 109.5),
`BoostTargetCreatureEffect(DynamicAmount, DynamicAmount)` (replaced the
`BoostTargetCreaturePerControlledPermanentEffect`, `BoostTargetCreaturePerCardsInControllerGraveyardEffect`,
and `BoostTargetCreatureXEffect` variants — counting contexts resolve against the effect's
controller, not the pumped target), `GainLifeEffect(DynamicAmount, GainLifeRecipient)` (replaced the
`GainLife*` family and `GainLifeEqualToTargetToughnessEffect`; `recipient=TARGET_CONTROLLER` routes the
life to the target permanent's controller — Condemn's `GainLifeEffect(TargetToughness(), TARGET_CONTROLLER)`),
`LoseLifeEffect(DynamicAmount, LoseLifeRecipient, boolean controllerGainsLifeLost)` (replaced the whole
life-loss family — `TargetPlayerLosesLifeEffect` [+ `TargetPlayerLosesLifeEqualToLifeGainedEffect` →
Sanguine Bond `EventValue()`, `TargetPlayerLosesLifePerControlledPermanentEffect` → Bishop of the
Bloodstained `PermanentCount(filter, CONTROLLER)`, the wording counts *your* Vampires not the target's],
`EachPlayerLosesLifeEffect`, `EachOpponentLosesLifeEffect`, `EachOpponentLosesLifeAndControllerGainsLifeLostEffect`,
and `EachOpponentLosesXLifeAndControllerGainsLifeLostEffect` — the last two via the `controllerGainsLifeLost`
drain flag; `recipient=TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` routes the loss to the controller of the *targeted
permanent* — Soul Reap's "its controller loses 3 life", list it before the accompanying
`DestroyTargetPermanentEffect` so the creature is still present, fires "loses life" triggers via
`applyLifeLoss`; `recipient=DEFENDING_PLAYER` routes the loss to the player being attacked (or the
attacked planeswalker's controller), read from the combat trigger's `attackedTargetId` — chooses no
target, fires "loses life" triggers, used by Vedalken Ghoul's `ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED`),
`ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect(DynamicAmount count)`
(absorbed `ExileTopCardsEqualToStackEntryExcessDamageMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect` → Archaic's Agony
`EventValue()`),
`DrawCardEffect(DynamicAmount)` / `DrawCardForTargetPlayerEffect(DynamicAmount, …)`
(replaced `DrawXCardsEffect`, `DrawXCardsForTargetPlayerEffect`,
`DrawCardsEqualToChargeCountersOnSourceEffect`, `DrawCardsEqualToControlledCreatureCountEffect`,
`DrawCardsPerCreatureCardInGraveyardEffect`), and `CreateTokenEffect(…, DynamicAmount amount, …)`
(replaced `CreateXCreatureTokenEffect`, `CreateTokenPerAttachmentOnSourceEffect`,
`CreateTokenPerEquipmentOnSourceEffect`, `CreateTokenPerOpponentPoisonCounterEffect`,
`CreateTokensEqualToChargeCountersOnSourceEffect`, `CreateTokensEqualToControlledCreatureCountEffect`,
`CreateTokensPerCreatureCardInGraveyardEffect`, `CreateTokensPerOwnCreatureDeathsThisTurnEffect`,
`CreateTokensPerControlledCreatureSubtypeEffect`, `CreateTokensPerControlledLandSubtypeEffect`),
and the damage bases `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect` / `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect` /
`DealDamageToPlayersEffect` (TARGET_PLAYER / EACH_OPPONENT) /
`DealDamageToEachTargetEffect` (replaced `DealXDamageToAnyTargetEffect`,
`DealXDamageToTargetCreatureEffect`, `DealXDamageToEachTargetEffect`,
`DealDamageEqualToSourcePowerToAnyTargetEffect`,
`DealDamageEqualToSourceToughnessToTargetCreatureEffect`,
`DealDamageToAnyTargetEqualToChargeCountersOnSourceEffect`,
`DealDamageToTargetCreatureEqualToControlledSubtypeCountEffect`,
`DealDamageToTargetCreatureEqualToManaSpentToCastEffect`,
`DealDamageToTargetPlayerEqualToCardTypeCountInGraveyardEffect`,
`DealDamageToEachOpponentEqualToPlusOnePlusOneCountersOnSourceEffect`),
and the mill base `MillEffect(DynamicAmount, MillRecipient)` (one record for the whole family —
replaced `MillControllerEffect`, `MillTargetPlayerEffect`, `EachOpponentMillsEffect`,
`MillByHandSizeEffect`; `recipient` ∈ {CONTROLLER, TARGET_PLAYER, EACH_OPPONENT, TARGET_SPELL_CONTROLLER}
routes who mills — `TARGET_SPELL_CONTROLLER` mills the controller of the spell at `entry.getTargetId()`,
for "counter target spell ... that spell's controller mills N" cards like Broken Ambitions (wrap the
mill in `ClashEffect` and list it *before* the counter so the targeted spell is still on the stack),
`CardsInHand(TARGET_PLAYER)` covers Dreamborn Muse's hand-size count), the discard base
`DiscardEffect(DynamicAmount, DiscardRecipient, boolean random)` (one record for the whole family —
replaced `DiscardCardEffect`, `TargetPlayerDiscardsEffect`, `EachPlayerDiscardsEffect`,
`EachOpponentDiscardsEffect`, `TargetPlayerRandomDiscardEffect`, `EachPlayerRandomDiscardEffect`;
`recipient` routes who discards, `random` picks chosen vs random), and the mana base
`AwardManaEffect(ManaColor, DynamicAmount)` (replaced `AddManaPerControlledPermanentEffect`
[→ `PermanentCount(filter, CONTROLLER)`], `AddColorlessManaPerChargeCounterOnSourceEffect`
[→ `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)`], and `AwardManaEqualToSourcePowerEffect` [→ `SourcePower()`]).
Mana abilities resolve outside the stack, so their amount is evaluated from the source
permanent via `AmountContext.forManaAbility(Permanent, UUID controllerId)` (no `xValue`);
stack-resolved mana (Koth's `-2`, Molten-Core Maestro's Opus) uses `forStackEntry`.
`AddManaPerAttackingCreatureEffect` is intentionally NOT collapsed — its attacker count is
locked at trigger time (Grand Warlord Radha ruling), which a resolution-time `PermanentCount`
would get wrong.
New amounts: add the record to `model/amount/`, add it to the `permits` list on
`DynamicAmount`, and add its case to `AmountEvaluationService.evaluate`. Never add a new
per-derivation effect record.


| Effect | Constructor | Description |
|--------|-------------|-------------|
| `SequenceEffect` | `(List<CardEffect> steps)` or `SequenceEffect.of(step1, step2, …)` (>=2 steps) | Resolves its steps strictly in order, as if they were consecutive flat effects on the same stack entry — engine-inline: `EffectResolutionService` splices the steps into the entry's live effect list when reached (never reaches handler dispatch; async pause/resume and nested wrappers work unchanged). NO data flow between steps (no "if you do" contingency); a step that no-ops does not stop later steps. `targetSpec()` = the first step's non-NONE spec; the entry's single target is shared by every targeting step (multi-target groups inside a sequence are unsupported). **Use ONLY** when a single-effect wrapper must gate several steps as one unit (`MayEffect(SequenceEffect.of(a, b))`, `ConditionalEffect(cond, SequenceEffect.of(a, b))`, `FlipCoinWinEffect(SequenceEffect.of(a, b))`) or when several steps must stay one atomic triggered ability on a trigger slot (collectors push one entry per slot effect). **Do NOT** wrap a plain spell/ability effect list — prefer flat `addEffect(...)` calls (the Act of Treason / Drain Life pattern) |
| `MayEffect` | `(CardEffect wrapped, String prompt)` | Wraps any effect with "you may" choice. For "becomes blocked by a creature" triggers that fire once per blocker, register with `TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER` via `addEffect()` (e.g. Infiltration Lens) |
| `MayPayManaEffect` | `(String manaCost, CardEffect wrapped, String prompt)` or `(…, boolean payerIsEnchantedController)` | Wraps any effect with "you may pay {X}. If you do, [effect]" choice. The mana cost is charged before resolving. Used for Spellbomb cycle and similar cards. Set `payerIsEnchantedController=true` in an `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` slot to prompt the enchanted permanent's controller (the stack entry's `targetId`) instead of the Aura's controller — "that player may pay {X}" (Paralyze, wrapping `UntapEquippedCreatureEffect` which untaps the Aura's host via its `attachedTo`) |
| `MayPayTapPermanentsEffect` | `(TapMultiplePermanentsCost tapCost, CardEffect wrapped, String prompt)` | Wraps any effect with "you may tap N untapped permanents matching filter. If you do, [effect]" choice. Tap cost is paid before resolving the wrapped effect. Used by Aziza, Mage Tower Captain via `CopyControllerCastSpellOnSpellCastEffect` |
| `MayRevealSubtypeFromHandEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype, CardEffect thenEffect, String prompt)` | "You may reveal a [subtype] card from your hand. If you do, [thenEffect]." At trigger time, checks if controller's hand contains a card with the subtype; if so, queues a MayEffect wrapping thenEffect; otherwise silently skips. Used by Priest of the Wakening Sun (DINOSAUR, GainLifeEffect(2)) |
| `RevealSubtypeOrEntersTappedEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | As-enters replacement (STATIC slot): "As this enters, you may reveal a [subtype] card from your hand. If you don't, this enters tapped." Handled in `BattlefieldEntryService.applyRevealSubtypeOrEntersTapped` after the permanent is on the battlefield — if the controller has no matching card in hand it enters tapped automatically; otherwise a "you may reveal" prompt is raised via the pending-may-ability pipeline (declining taps the permanent, handled in `MayAbilityHandlerService`). Used by the Lorwyn dual lands, e.g. Ancient Amphitheater (GIANT) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new Metalcraft(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with metalcraft condition (3+ artifacts). For ETB triggers: checked at trigger time and resolution time, delegates targeting to wrapped effect. For static effects: wraps GrantKeywordEffect or StaticBoostEffect, applied only while metalcraft is met (selfOnly handler). Also wraps `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(N))` for "this spell costs {N} less if you control three or more artifacts" (Stoic Rebuttal) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new Morbid(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with morbid condition (a creature died this turn). For ETB triggers: checked at trigger time (intervening-if) and resolution time, delegates targeting to wrapped effect. For END_STEP_TRIGGERED: checked at trigger time (intervening-if) and resolution time; if wrapped effect targets, queued via `EndStepTriggerTarget` for target selection. Used by Festerhide Boar with PutCountersOnSourceEffect, Reaper from the Abyss with DestroyTargetPermanentEffect |
| `ConditionalEffect(new Raid(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with raid condition (controller attacked with a creature this turn). For ETB triggers: checked at trigger time (intervening-if) and resolution time, delegates targeting to wrapped effect. For CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED: checked as intervening-if; if wrapped is MayEffect, queued via queueMayAbility; otherwise pushed onto stack. Uses `gameData.playersDeclaredAttackersThisTurn`. Used by Deadeye Tormentor (ETB), Marauding Looter (end step with MayEffect(SequenceEffect.of(DrawCardEffect(1), DiscardEffect(1, CONTROLLER)))) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerCastAnotherSpellThisTurn(filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any spell effect with "if you've cast another spell matching filter this turn" condition. Excludes the resolving spell. Checked at resolution time via `GameQueryService.hasControllerCastAnotherSpellThisTurn`. Used by Burrog Barrage with instant/sorcery filter |
| `ConditionalEffect(new PermanentEnteredThisTurn(predicate, minCount), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "if at least N permanents matching predicate entered the battlefield under that player's control this turn" condition. Checked at trigger time via `permanentsEnteredBattlefieldThisTurn`. Used by Tunnel Ignus with `CardTypePredicate(LAND), 2` |
| `EnteringCreatureMinPowerConditionalEffect` | `(int minPower, CardEffect wrapped)` | Wraps any ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD effect with "entering creature has power >= minPower" condition. Checked at trigger time. Inner effect can be MayEffect or mandatory. Used by Garruk's Packleader (minPower=3, MayEffect(DrawCardEffect)) |
| `EnteringCreatureMaxPowerConditionalEffect` | `(int maxPower, CardEffect wrapped)` | Wraps any ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD effect with "entering creature has power <= maxPower" condition. Checked at trigger time. Inner effect can be MayPayManaEffect, MayEffect, or mandatory. Used by Mentor of the Meek (maxPower=2, MayPayManaEffect("{1}", DrawCardEffect)) |
| `EnteringCreatureExactStatsConditionalEffect` | `(int power, int toughness, CardEffect wrapped)` | Wraps any ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD effect with "entering creature's printed power AND toughness both equal the given values" condition ("if that creature is 1/1"). Checked at trigger time. Used by Sigil Captain (`(1, 1, PutCountersOnEnteringCreatureEffect(2, false))`) |
| `PutCountersOnEnteringCreatureEffect` | `(int count[, boolean optional])` | ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD trigger-materialising marker: put `count` +1/+1 counters on the creature that just entered. `optional` defaults to `true` ("you may": the ally-enter collector queues `MayEffect(PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, count))` with `targetId` baked to that creature); `optional=false` bakes the mandatory `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect` directly onto the stack (no prompt). Wrap in `EnteringCreatureMinPowerConditionalEffect` ("with power N+" gate — Mighty Emergence `(2)`, minPower=5, may) or `EnteringCreatureExactStatsConditionalEffect` ("is X/Y" gate — Sigil Captain `(2, false)`, is 1/1, mandatory) |
| `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate, CardEffect wrapped)` | Wraps trigger effects whose event has a triggering card. The wrapped effect fires only if the triggering card matches the predicate. Supports composed predicates such as `CardSubtypePredicate(HUMAN)` and `CardNotPredicate(CardSubtypePredicate(SPIRIT))`. Works with ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD (checked in BattlefieldEntryService), ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES, ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DIES, ON_EQUIPPED_CREATURE_DIES (checked in TriggerCollectionService), and ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS (checked in CombatAttackService). Used by Champion of the Parish, Village Cannibals, Avacyn's Collar, Sanctum Seeker, Slimefoot, and Requiem Angel |
| `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, CardEffect wrapped)` | Wraps trigger effects whose event subject is a permanent. The wrapped effect fires only if that triggering permanent matches the predicate. Currently supports ON_ALLY_PERMANENT_SACRIFICED in MiscTriggerCollectorService, evaluating last-known sacrificed-card data as a permanent. Used by Captain Lannery Storm with `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(TREASURE)` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ImprintedCardNameMatchesEnteringPermanent(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any ON_OPPONENT_LAND_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD effect with "entering permanent name matches source's imprinted card name" condition. Checked at trigger time. Used by Invader Parasite |
| `ConditionalEffect(new DefendingPlayerPoisoned(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "if defending player is poisoned" condition. Used for ON_ATTACK triggers that only fire when opponent has 1+ poison counters. Used by Septic Rats |
| `ConditionalEffect(new OpponentPoisoned(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as an opponent is poisoned" condition. Used for STATIC effects (e.g. conditional keyword grants) that apply when any opponent has 1+ poison counters. Used by Viridian Betrayers |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsAnotherPermanent(filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Intervening-if wrapper: "if you control another [matching permanent]". Checked at trigger time and resolution time per CR 603.4. The source permanent is excluded. Compose predicates for subtype/token restrictions, e.g. `PermanentAllOfPredicate(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(PIRATE), PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentIsTokenPredicate()))` for "another nontoken Pirate", or `PermanentHasAnySubtypePredicate(Set.of(MERFOLK, ISLAND))` for "another Merfolk or an Island". Used by Ghitu Journeymage, Fathom Fleet Captain, Kumena's Speaker, Shaper Apprentice, Headstrong Brute, and Thrash of Raptors |
| `ConditionalEffect(new NoOtherPermanent(filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Intervening-if wrapper: "if you control no other [matching permanent]". Checked at trigger time and resolution time per CR 603.4. The source permanent is excluded. Use `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(...)` for subtype cases. Trigger-time check wired for `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` and `END_STEP_TRIGGERED`. Used by Thopter Assembly with THOPTER subtype (upkeep) and Stenchskipper with GOBLIN subtype (end step: "if you control no Goblins, sacrifice this creature") |
| `ConditionalEffect(new GraveyardCardThreshold(threshold, filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as there are N or more [filtered] cards in your graveyard" condition. For static effects: wraps StaticBoostEffect or GrantKeywordEffect, applied only while controller's graveyard contains >= threshold non-token cards matching filter (selfOnly handler). Used by Ghitu Lavarunner with threshold=2, instant/sorcery filter, wrapping StaticBoostEffect(+1/+0, HASTE) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new SourceCounterThreshold(threshold, counterType), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as there are N or more [counter type] counters on this permanent" condition. For static effects: wraps StaticBoostEffect or GrantKeywordEffect, applied only while the source permanent has >= threshold counters of the given type. Used by Comforting Counsel with threshold=5, GROWTH, wrapping StaticBoostEffect(+3/+3, OWN_CREATURES) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerTurn(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "during your turn" condition. The wrapped effect only applies when the source permanent's controller is the active player. Supports GrantKeywordEffect and StaticBoostEffect as wrapped effects. Used by Jousting Lance for conditional first strike |
| `ConditionalEffect(new NotControllerTurn(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "during turns other than yours" condition. The wrapped effect only applies when the source permanent's controller is not the active player. Supports GrantKeywordEffect, StaticBoostEffect, ProtectionFromColorsEffect, and `AnimatePermanentsEffect` (scope=SELF) as wrapped effects. Used by Warden of the Wall for opponent-turn self-animation |
| `ConditionalEffect(new NotCondition(inner), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Logical negation wrapper: met exactly when `inner` is not met, evaluated with the same `ConditionContext` (recurses into `ConditionEvaluationService.isMet`). Use for "unless …" phrasings over any existing condition. Used by Hotheaded Giant for "enters with two -1/-1 counters unless you've cast another red spell this turn" (`NotCondition(new ControllerCastAnotherSpellThisTurn(new CardColorPredicate(RED)))`) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerLifeAtLeast(threshold), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as you have N or more life" condition. Works in both static effects (wraps StaticBoostEffect or GrantKeywordEffect, applied only while controller's life total >= threshold) and effect resolution (intervening-if in activated abilities, checked at resolution time in EffectResolutionService). Used by Serra Ascendant with threshold 30 (static), Chalice of Life with threshold 30 wrapping TransformSelfEffect (activated ability) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerLifeAtMost(threshold), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "if you have N or less life" (fateful hour) condition. Works in three places: trigger time (StepTriggerService), resolution time / intervening-if (EffectResolutionService), and **static effects** (wraps StaticBoostEffect or GrantKeywordEffect, applied only while controller's life total <= threshold). Static handlers honor the wrapped effect's GrantScope (SELF/ALL_OWN_CREATURES via the self handler, OWN_CREATURES/ALL_CREATURES/etc. via the others handler). Used by Arguel's Blood Fast with threshold 5 wrapping MayEffect(TransformSelfEffect()) (intervening-if), and Gavony Ironwright with threshold 5 wrapping StaticBoostEffect(1, 4, OWN_CREATURES) (static "fateful hour — other creatures you control get +1/+4") |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanent(filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "if/as long as you control a [permanent matching predicate]" condition. For static effects, wraps StaticBoostEffect, GrantKeywordEffect, ProtectionFromColorsEffect, or GrantEffectEffect (selfOnly handler). For ON_ATTACK triggers, checked at trigger time in CombatAttackService and re-checked at resolution time per CR 603.4. Also checked at resolution time for spells/abilities. Use `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(...)` for subtype cases. Used by Temporal Machinations, Angelic Overseer, Karplusan Hound, Teferi's Sentinel, and Jace's Sentinel. Also wraps `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(N))` for "this spell costs {N} less if you control a matching permanent" (Academy Journeymage/Wizard's Retort/Wizard's Lightning with WIZARD, Lookout's Dispersal with PIRATE) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanentCount(minCount, filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "if you control N or more [permanents matching predicate]" intervening-if condition. `ControlsPermanentCount` is an **ETB trigger gate** (`isEtbTriggerGate()`), so it also works on `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`: checked as the trigger goes on the stack (CR 603.4) and re-checked at resolution; a gated targeted ETB defers its target to trigger time (CR 603.3d) — with no card-level `target(...)`, the ETB permanent-target defaults to creatures. Also checked at trigger time for CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED (StepTriggerService) and resolution time (EffectResolutionService). Used by Gwyllion Hedge-Mage (two ETBs: `(2, PLAINS)` wrapping `MayEffect(CreateTokenEffect)`, `(2, SWAMP)` wrapping `MayEffect(PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE))`) and Growing Rites of Itlimoc with minCount=4, PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, wrapping TransformSelfEffect() |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new ControlsPermanent(filter), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | Replacement wrapper: picks between baseEffect and upgradedEffect based on whether the controller controls a permanent matching the predicate. Used for planeswalker-signature spells like "If you control a [subtype] planeswalker, do X instead." Condition checked at resolution time. Use `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(...)` for subtype cases. Used by Huatli's Spurring with HUATLI |
| `ConditionalEffect(new OpponentControlsPermanent(filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as an opponent controls a permanent matching [filter]" condition. For static effects, wraps StaticBoostEffect, GrantKeywordEffect, ProtectionFromColorsEffect, or GrantEffectEffect (selfOnly handler). Also supports resolution-time conditional checks. Use `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(...)` for subtype cases. Used by Night Revelers with HUMAN |
| `ConditionalEffect(new OpponentControlsMoreCreatures(minimumCreatureDifference), wrapped)` | see construction shape | "if an opponent controls at least N more creatures than you". Evaluated in `ConditionEvaluationService` (counts creatures via `GameQueryService.isCreature`). Used at **cast-cost** time wrapping `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(N))` — Avatar of Might with `minimumCreatureDifference=4` wrapping `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(6))` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new CardsLeftGraveyardThisTurn(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | "if one or more cards left your graveyard this turn". Reads `GameData.playersWhoseCardsLeftGraveyardThisTurn` (populated in `GraveyardService.notifyCardsLeftGraveyard`, cleared at turn cleanup). Used at **cast-cost** time wrapping `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(N))` — Wilt in the Heat with `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(2))` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new SelfHasKeyword(keyword), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as this creature has [keyword]" condition. For static effects: wraps GrantKeywordEffect or StaticBoostEffect, applied only while the source permanent has the specified keyword (selfOnly handler). Accounts for temporary keyword removal from activated abilities. Used by Manor Gargoyle with DEFENDER wrapping INDESTRUCTIBLE |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ActivationCount(threshold, abilityIndex), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "if ability has been activated N or more times this turn" condition. Checked at resolution time via `activatedAbilityUsesThisTurn`. Used by Dragon Whelp with threshold=4, abilityIndex=0, wrapping SacrificeSelfEffect |
| `ConditionalEffect(new NthAbilityResolutionThisTurn(n), wrapped)` | see construction shape | "if this is the Nth time this ability has resolved this turn" — met only on the exact n-th resolution, never a later one. Counts *resolutions*, not activations (copies of the ability count; activations countered on the stack do not): `StackResolutionService` increments `GameData.permanentAbilityResolutionsThisTurn` (per source permanent, reset each turn) whenever an activated ability carrying this condition resolves. Used by Ashling the Pilgrim with n=3 |
| `ConditionalEffect(new DidntAttack(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Intervening-if wrapper: "if this creature didn't attack this turn". Checked at trigger time (StepTriggerService) and resolution time (EffectResolutionService). Used by Homicidal Brute's CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED wrapping `SequenceEffect.of(TapPermanentsEffect(SELF), TransformSelfEffect)` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new CameUnderControlThisTurn(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Source-state wrapper: true while the source is still summoning sick, i.e. it came under its controller's control this turn (summoning sickness only clears at that player's untap step). Almost always used inside `NotCondition` (Erg Raiders: "unless it came under your control this turn"). Evaluated via `Permanent.isSummoningSick()` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new AllOf(List.of(a, b, ...)), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Logical conjunction of several conditions — met only when every inner condition is met; evaluation recurses with the same ConditionContext. Lets a card compose a compound intervening-"if" from existing leaf conditions instead of a bespoke one. StepTriggerService's controller-end-step loop gates on it generically. Used by Erg Raiders: `AllOf(List.of(new DidntAttack(), new NotCondition(new CameUnderControlThisTurn())))` wrapping DealDamageToPlayersEffect(2, CONTROLLER) in CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED |
| `ConditionalEffect(new AnyOf(List.of(a, b, ...)), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Logical disjunction of several conditions (the OR analogue of `AllOf`) — met when at least one inner condition is met; evaluation recurses with the same ConditionContext. Compose a compound intervening-"if" from existing leaf conditions instead of a bespoke one. Used by Desert's Hold: `AnyOf(List.of(new ControlsPermanent(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(DESERT)), new GraveyardCardThreshold(1, new CardSubtypePredicate(DESERT))))` ("if you control a Desert or there is a Desert card in your graveyard") wrapping GainLifeEffect(3) in ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD |
| `ConditionalEffect(new AttacksAlone(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Trigger-condition wrapper: "whenever this creature attacks alone". Filtered at trigger collection time in CombatAttackService (only fires if creature is the sole attacker, per CR 506.5) and re-checked at resolution time. Place in ON_ATTACK slot. Used by Grunn, the Lonely King wrapping DoubleSelfPowerToughnessEffect |
| `ConditionalEffect(new MinimumAttackers(minimumAttackers), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Trigger-condition wrapper: "whenever you attack with N or more creatures". Filtered at trigger collection time in CombatAttackService (only fires if attacker count >= minimumAttackers) and re-checked at resolution time using xValue. Place in GRAVEYARD_ON_ALLY_CREATURES_ATTACK slot. Used by Warcry Phoenix with minimumAttackers=3 wrapping MayPayManaEffect |
| `ConditionalEffect(new HasAttacker(predicate), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Trigger-condition wrapper: "whenever one or more matching permanents you control attack". Filtered at trigger collection time in CombatAttackService (only fires if at least one attacking permanent matches the predicate) and re-checked at resolution time. Place in ON_ALLY_CREATURES_ATTACK slot. Compose predicates such as `PermanentAllOfPredicate(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(VAMPIRE), PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentIsTokenPredicate))` for "one or more nontoken Vampires". Used by Mavren Fein, Dusk Apostle |
| `ConditionalEffect(new BlockedByMinCreatures(minBlockers), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as N or more creatures are blocking this" condition. For static effects: wraps StaticBoostEffect or GrantKeywordEffect, applied only while source is blocked by >= minBlockers creatures (selfOnly handler). Used by Rampaging Cyclops with minBlockers=2, StaticBoostEffect(-2, 0, SELF) |
| `NthSpellCastTriggerEffect` | `(int spellNumber, List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects)` | trigger-condition wrapper: "whenever you cast your Nth spell in a turn". Checked at trigger time in `SpellCastTriggerCollectorService` against `getSpellsCastThisTurnCount`. When count matches, resolved effects are placed on the stack. Typically wrapped in `MayEffect` for "you may" variants. Place in ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL slot. Used by Vance's Blasting Cannons (spellNumber=3, TransformSelfEffect) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new NoSpellsCastLastTurn(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Intervening-if wrapper: "if no spells were cast last turn". Checked at trigger time (StepTriggerService) and resolution time (EffectResolutionService). Used by Innistrad werewolf front faces with EACH_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED wrapping TransformSelfEffect (e.g. Daybreak Ranger) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new TwoOrMoreSpellsCastLastTurn(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Intervening-if wrapper: "if a player cast two or more spells last turn". Checked at trigger time (StepTriggerService) and resolution time (EffectResolutionService). Used by Innistrad werewolf back faces with EACH_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED wrapping TransformSelfEffect (e.g. Nightfall Predator) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new TopCardOfLibraryColor(color), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as the top card of your library is [color]" condition. For static effects: wraps StaticBoostEffect or GrantKeywordEffect, applied only while top card of controller's library has the specified color (self + others handlers). Used by Vampire Nocturnus with BLACK |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new Metalcraft(), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | Picks between base and upgraded effect at resolution based on metalcraft. Resolves `metalcraftEffect` if 3+ artifacts, otherwise `baseEffect`. Targeting delegates to both inner effects (union). No new handler needed — unwrapped in `EffectResolutionService` |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new Morbid(), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | Picks between base and upgraded effect at resolution based on morbid. Resolves `morbidEffect` if a creature died this turn, otherwise `baseEffect`. Targeting delegates to both inner effects (union). No new handler needed — unwrapped in `EffectResolutionService`. Used by Brimstone Volley |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new Raid(), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | Picks between base and upgraded effect at resolution based on raid. Resolves `raidEffect` if the controller attacked with a creature this turn, otherwise `baseEffect`. Targeting delegates to both inner effects (union). No new handler needed — unwrapped in `EffectResolutionService`. Used by Firecannon Blast |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new TargetPermanentMatches(filter), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | Picks between base and upgraded effect at resolution based on whether the target permanent matches the predicate. If the target is missing or does not match, uses the base effect. Targeting delegates to both inner effects (union). No new handler needed — unwrapped in `EffectResolutionService`.
