Use `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(...)` for subtype cases. Used by Elder Cathar (HUMAN) |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new SourceHasSubtype(subtype), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | Picks between base and upgraded effect at resolution based on whether the source permanent (the creature activating the ability) has the specified subtype. Falls back to the card on the stack (last-known info) if the source left the battlefield. Targeting delegates to both inner effects (union). No new handler needed — unwrapped in `EffectResolutionService`. Used by Sorcerer's Wand (WIZARD) |
| `FlipCoinWinEffect` | `(CardEffect wrapped)` or `(CardEffect wrapped, CardEffect lost)` | "Flip a coin. If you win the flip, [wrapped]. If you lose the flip, [lost]." Flips a coin at resolution time; on a win dispatches `wrapped`, on a loss dispatches `lost` (or nothing when `lost` is null / the 1-arg form is used). Used by Sorcerer's Strongbox (win-only) and Bottle of Suleiman (win: 5/5 Djinn token; loss: 5 damage to controller) |
| `FlipTwoCoinsEffect` | `(CardEffect bothHeads, CardEffect bothTails)` | Wraps two effects with "Flip two coins." If both heads, dispatches `bothHeads`. If both tails, dispatches `bothTails`. On a split result, nothing happens. Used by Two-Headed Giant |
| `ManaClashEffect` | `()` | You and the targeted opponent (stack entry `targetId`) each flip a coin; each player whose coin is tails takes 1 damage; repeats until both coins come up heads on the same flip. Self-contained loop in `ManaClashEffectHandler` — damage runs through `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` (prevention + damage multipliers apply). the spec targets a player; restrict to opponents with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)` on the card. Used by Mana Clash |
| `ManaClashEffect` | `()` | You and the targeted opponent (stack entry `targetId`) each flip a coin; each player whose coin is tails takes 1 damage; repeats until both coins come up heads on the same flip. Self-contained loop in `ManaClashEffectHandler` — damage runs through `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` (prevention + damage multipliers apply). `canTargetPlayer()` returns true; restrict to opponents with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)` on the card. Used by Mana Clash |
| `GameOfChaosEffect` | `()` | Targets an opponent (`targetSpec` PLAYER; restrict to opponents with `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)` on the card). Flips a coin from the controller's perspective at an escalating life stake (starts at 1, doubles each flip): on a win the controller gains and the opponent loses that much life; on a loss the reverse. After each flip the winner is offered a repeating "flip again?" yes/no via a `PendingMayAbility` carrying `GameOfChaosFlipAgainEffect`. `GameOfChaosSupport` holds the shared flip/life-swap logic; `GameOfChaosEffectHandler` (normalfx) runs the first flip, `GameOfChaosFlipAgainHandler` (mayfx) runs the rest. Used by Game of Chaos |
| `GameOfChaosFlipAgainEffect` | `(UUID spellControllerId, UUID opponentId, int stake)` | Non-targeted continuation marker carried in the "flip again?" `PendingMayAbility`; routes the yes/no answer to `GameOfChaosFlipAgainHandler`. Never placed on the stack. Used by Game of Chaos |
| `ChooseOneEffect` | `(List<ChooseOneOption> options)` or `(List<ChooseOneOption> options, boolean optional)` or `(List<ChooseOneOption> options, int choicesRequired)` | Modal spell: defines the available modes for "Choose one" / "Choose two" spells. Pass `optional=true` for "choose up to one" (mode index `-1` at cast time skips all modes). Pass `choicesRequired=2` for "choose two" (cast with negative bitmask from `encodeModeSelection`). Each `ChooseOneOption(String label, CardEffect effect)` or `ChooseOneOption(String label, CardEffect effect, TargetFilter targetFilter)` pairs a display label with its effect and optional per-mode target filter. **Mode is chosen at cast time** (per CR 700.2a): `SpellCastingService` unwraps the `ChooseOneEffect` using the `xValue` parameter as the mode index (0-based) for choose-one, or as a negative bitmask for choose-multiple, and places only the chosen inner effect(s) on the stack in card-text order. For ETB creatures, the per-mode `targetFilter` (if present) is set on the triggered ability's StackEntry for resolution-time validation. Used by Slagstorm, Deceiver Exarch, Biblioplex Tomekeeper, Austere Command |
| `RelicBindTapEffect` | `()` | Relic Bind's modal enchanted-artifact-tap triggered ability. Placed in `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED`; the trigger goes on the stack non-targeting. At resolution `RelicBindTapEffectHandler` prompts the aura controller for the "choose one" mode (a `ChoiceContext.RelicBindModeChoice` list pick), then hands the chosen mode's targeted effect — `DealDamageToTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerEffect(1)` or `TargetPlayerGainsLifeEffect(1)` — to the shared `PermanentChoiceContext.MayAbilityTriggerTarget` target-selection flow. The engine has no cast-time modal machinery for triggered abilities, so mode + target are chosen as the ability resolves (equivalent here — both modes' targets are free) |

---

## Damage

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect` | `(DynamicAmount damage, boolean cantRegenerate, boolean exileInsteadOfDie)`; convenience `(int)`, `(int, boolean cantRegenerate)`, `(DynamicAmount)`, `(DynamicAmount, Condition unpreventableWhen)` | deal damage to any target. The amount is any `DynamicAmount` — `Fixed` (Shock), `XValue` (Blaze, Fling — X paid or a cost-snapshotted value), `SourcePower` (Spikeshot Elder, Flayer of the Hatebound), `CountersOnSource` (Shrine of Burning Rage). `cantRegenerate=true` for Incinerate-style; `exileInsteadOfDie=true` for Red Sun's Zenith-style CR 614.6 replacement. `unpreventableWhen` (a `Condition` — Banefire's `new SpellXAtLeast(5)`) makes the damage unpreventable for that one event while the gate holds (handler suppresses `isDamagePreventable`); `null` = normal prevention. `forTargetGroup(int damage, int targetGroup)` aims the damage at that target group's chosen target instead of the entry's single target (flat additional-target positions for cards without `target()` declarations — Goblin Barrage's kicked "4 damage to target player or planeswalker" = `ConditionalEffect(new Kicked(), DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect.forTargetGroup(4, 0))`) |
| `DealDamageToSourceEffect` | `(DynamicAmount damage)`; convenience `(int)` | the source permanent deals `damage` to itself (not targeting). Reuses the any-target damage path against the source's id, so prevention/lethal/multipliers apply. Pair with `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect` for "deals X to any target and X to itself" — Sunflare Shaman (`amount = new CardsInGraveyard(new CardSubtypePredicate(ELEMENTAL), CONTROLLER)`) |
| `DealDamageToAttackedTargetEffect` | `(int damage)` | deal N damage to the player or planeswalker attacked by the creature that caused this attack trigger. Uses `StackEntry.attackedTargetId`, populated by `CombatAttackService` for `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ATTACKS` triggers; this is not targeting. Used by Hellrider |
| `EquippedCreatureDealsPowerToAttackedTargetEffect` | `()` | on an Equipment's `ON_ATTACK` slot: the equipped creature deals damage equal to its power to the player or planeswalker it's attacking. Non-targeting; the handler resolves the equipped creature via the Equipment's `attachedTo` and the recipient via the creature's live `attackTarget`, then deals power-based damage with the equipped creature as the damage source (so its power, colour, and keywords like infect apply). Fires even if the creature is blocked. Used by Mage Slayer |
| `DealDamageToTriggeringAttackerEffect` | `(int damage, PermanentPredicate attackerCondition)` | deal N damage to the attacking creature that caused this `ON_CREATURE_ATTACKS_YOU` trigger (`StackEntry.targetId`, non-targeting). The `attackerCondition` restricts which attackers fire the trigger — `CombatAttackService.declareAttackers` evaluates it against the attacker at declaration time, so the damage is dealt unconditionally on resolution. Used by Raking Canopy (`PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(FLYING)`, 4 damage) |
| `SourceFightsTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | source permanent and target creature deal damage to each other equal to their respective powers (fight mechanic). Both use effective power at resolution |
| `PackHuntEffect` | `(CardSubtype creatureSubtype)` | pack hunt: tap all untapped creatures of given subtype controller controls, each deals damage equal to its power to target creature, target creature deals its power divided evenly among those creatures. Uses effective power at resolution |
| `DealDamageToTargetAndTheirCreaturesEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` / `(int damage)` | deal N damage to target player or planeswalker AND each creature that player or that planeswalker's controller controls. Amount is any `DynamicAmount`: `Fixed` (Chandra Nalaar ultimate, Flame Wave) or `XValue` (Lavalanche, `{X}` spell) |
| `DealDamageToEachCreatureDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` | `()` | deal damage equal to combat damage dealt (from xValue) to each creature the damaged player controls (from targetId). Used with ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER slot. CombatDamageService passes damageDealt and defenderId automatically. Used by Balefire Dragon |
| `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect` | `(DynamicAmount damage, boolean unpreventable)`; convenience `(int)`, `(int, boolean)`, `(DynamicAmount)` | deal damage to target creature. The amount is any `DynamicAmount` — `Fixed`, `XValue` (Ballista Squad, Chandra Nalaar −X, Corpse Lunge/Harvest Pyre cost-snapshotted values, Archaic's Agony converge), `SourceToughness` (Steadfast Armasaur), `PermanentCount` (Seismic Strike, Spitting Earth, Firefist Adept; Tendrils of Corruption pairs it with `GainLifeEffect` on the same amount), `ManaSpentToCast` (Molten Note). When `unpreventable=true`, bypasses all damage prevention. Supports multi-target via `targetIds`. When paired with an `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect(EventValue())`, records the excess damage on the stack entry's `eventValue` |
| `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEqualToChosenTypeCountEffect` | `()` | "Choose a creature type. Deals damage to target creature equal to the number of permanents you control of the chosen type" (Coordinated Barrage). At resolution prompts a creature-type choice via `PlayerInputService.beginSpellCreatureTypeChoice` (answer stored on `GameData.chosenSpellSubtype`), re-runs, then deals damage = count of the controller's permanents matching a `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate` (Changeling-aware) via `DamageSupport.resolveCreatureTargetDamage`. Two-phase self-continuing flow using `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction` |
| `DealDamageToAnyTargetEqualToChosenTypeCountEffect` | `()` | "Choose a creature type. Deals damage to any target equal to the number of permanents you control of the chosen type" (Roar of the Crowd). Any-target sibling of `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEqualToChosenTypeCountEffect`: same two-phase creature-type choice, but self-declares any-target (spec `ANY_TARGET`) and deals via `DamageSupport.resolveAnyTargetDamage` (applies the damage multiplier). Two-phase self-continuing flow using `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction` |
| `DealDamageToTargetCreatureOrPlaneswalkerEffect` | `(int damage)`; `(int damage, PermanentPredicate targetRestriction)` | deal N damage to target creature or planeswalker (not player). Optional `targetRestriction` narrows the legal target via the spec predicate (`null` = any); e.g. Chandra's Defeat uses `PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(RED))` for "target red creature or red planeswalker". Used by Chandra, Bold Pyromancer's -3 |

| `BoostTargetCreaturePerChosenTypeCountEffect` | `(int powerPer, int toughnessPer)` | "Choose a creature type. | `SacrificeArtifactThenDealDividedDamageEffect` | `(int totalDamage)` | Sacrifice an artifact, then deal N total damage divided among any number of targets (creatures/players). | `SacrificePermanentThenEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, CardEffect thenEffect, String permanentDescription)` | "Sacrifice a [permanent matching filter]. If you do, [thenEffect]." Controller must sacrifice a permanent matching the predicate; if successful, the wrapped effect executes. If no matching permanent exists, nothing happens. `thenEffect` may be `null` for a bare "sacrifice a permanent" (e.g. `new PermanentTruePredicate()` + `null` for Tragedy Feaster's Infusion). Uses `PermanentChoiceContext.SacrificePermanentThen` for interactive choice |
| `SacrificeAnotherCreatureDealPowerDamageToAnyTargetEffect` | `()` | "You may sacrifice another creature. When you do, this creature deals damage equal to that creature's power to any target." Placed inside a `MayEffect` on `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` (Heart-Piercer Manticore). `targetSpec()` = `ANY_TARGET` harmful, so the resolution-time may pipeline offers creatures/players; on accept the controller picks the target, then another creature to sacrifice. Effective power (clamped ≥ 0) is captured before the creature leaves and dealt via `DamageSupport.dealDividedDamageToAnyTargets` (single assignment, source = the entering creature). Uses `PermanentChoiceContext.SacrificeAnotherCreatureDealPowerDamage`. No other creature ⇒ nothing |
| `SacrificeOtherCreatureOrDamageEffect` | `(int damage)` | sacrifice another creature or take N damage (upkeep trigger) |
| `SacrificeOtherCreatureOpponentsLoseLifeOrTapAndLoseLifeEffect` | `(int lifeLoss)` | sacrifice another creature, then each opponent loses life equal to sacrificed creature's power; if can't sacrifice, tap self and controller loses N life (upkeep trigger) |
| `SpellCastTriggerEffect` | `(CardPredicate spellFilter, List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects)` or `(CardPredicate spellFilter, List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects, String manaCost)` or `(CardPredicate spellFilter, List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects, String manaCost, TargetFilter targetFilter)` | generic trigger descriptor: when a spell matching the predicate is cast, put the resolved effects on the stack. Works in both `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL` and `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` slots. Wrap in `MayEffect` for optional triggers. Set `manaCost` (e.g. `"{1}"`) for "may pay" triggers. Use `spellFilter = null` for "whenever you cast a spell" (any spell). Set `targetFilter` for triggers that target (e.g. "tap target creature an opponent controls") — uses `SpellTargetTriggerAnyTarget` queue for target selection; skips trigger if no valid targets exist. See D'Avenant Trapper for targeted usage. |
| `DealDamageEqualToSpellManaValueToAnyTargetEffect` | `(CardPredicate spellFilter)` | spell-cast trigger: when controller casts a spell matching the filter, deal damage equal to that spell's mana value to any target. Uses `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Target selection via `SpellTargetTriggerAnyTarget` queue. See Rage Extractor |
| `BoostSelfByCastSpellManaValueEffect` | `(CardPredicate spellFilter)` | spell-cast trigger: when controller casts a spell matching the filter (`null` = any spell), this permanent gets +X/+X until end of turn where X is that spell's mana value (`spellCard().getManaValue()`, the mana-value sibling of the mana-spent `XValue` path). Uses `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` slot; enqueues a self-targeting `BoostSelfEffect(mv, mv)`. See Manaplasm |
| `CastFromGraveyardTriggerEffect` | `(List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects)` | trigger descriptor: whenever controller casts a spell from the graveyard (flashback, etc.), put the resolved effects on the stack. Uses `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` slot. If resolved effects need any-target selection, uses `SpellTargetTriggerAnyTarget` queue. See Burning Vengeance |
| `KickedSpellCastTriggerEffect` | `(List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects)` | trigger descriptor: whenever controller casts a spell, if that spell was kicked, put the resolved effects on the stack. Uses `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Checks the stack for the spell's kicked status. See Bloodstone Goblin |
| `CasterLosesLifeOnSpellCastEffect` | `(CardPredicate spellFilter, int amount)` | trigger descriptor: "whenever a player casts a [filter] spell, that player loses N life". Uses `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Collector filters the cast card by `spellFilter` (null = any) and queues a `LoseLifeEffect(amount, TARGET_PLAYER)` whose `targetId` is preset to the casting player — mandatory, no target choice. See Soot Imp (nonblack filter). Differs from `SpellCastTriggerEffect` + `LoseLifeEffect(TARGET_PLAYER)`, which prompts the controller to choose a target player (Quillslinger Boggart) |
| `ChosenSubtypeSpellCastTriggerEffect` | `(List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects[, boolean creatureSpellOnly])` | trigger descriptor: whenever controller casts a spell of the source permanent's chosen subtype, put the resolved effects on the stack. Uses `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` slot. The chosen subtype is read from `Permanent.getChosenSubtype()` at trigger-check time. `creatureSpellOnly` (default `true`) restricts to creature spells (Vanquisher's Banner); pass `false` for "a spell of the chosen type" including non-creature Tribal spells (Door of Destinies). Pair with `ChooseSubtypeOnEnterEffect` |
| `BecomePreparedEffect` | `()` | "Prepared" (Secrets of Strixhaven): the source permanent becomes prepared. `targetSpec().selfTargeting()=true` so the trigger framework stamps the source permanent id. On resolution, exiles a copy of the source's prepare spell (its `backFaceCard`) with a non-expiring `exilePlayPermissions` entry and links it via `Permanent.preparedSpellCardId`; no-op if already prepared or no back face. Casting the exiled copy unprepares the permanent (in `SpellCastingService.playCardFromExile`), and `PermanentRemovalService` removes the copy if the prepared permanent leaves the battlefield. Pair with a `SpellCastTriggerEffect` in `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` and a back-face prepare spell. See Abigale, Poet Laureate // Heroic Stanza |
| `MakeTargetCreaturePreparedEffect` | `()` | target creature becomes prepared; exiles a castable copy of its prepare spell (`backFaceCard`) for its controller. No-op if already prepared or no prepare spell. Used by Biblioplex Tomekeeper, Skycoach Waypoint |
| `MakeTargetCreatureUnpreparedEffect` | `()` | target creature becomes unprepared; removes its exiled prepare-spell copy. No-op if not prepared. Used by Biblioplex Tomekeeper |
| `PlaneswalkerDealDamageAndReceivePowerDamageEffect` | `(int damage)` | source planeswalker deals N damage to target creature, then that creature deals damage equal to its power back to the source planeswalker (removing loyalty counters). permanent-targeting spec. Used by Garruk Relentless |

## Destruction / sacrifice

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect` | `(boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` or `(boolean cannotBeRegenerated, CreateTokenEffect tokenForController)` | destroy target permanent. When `tokenForController` is non-null, creates that token for the target's controller regardless of whether destruction succeeds (e.g. Beast Within, Pongify) |
| `DestroyTargetPermanentAtEndStepEffect` | `()` | schedule target permanent for destruction at the beginning of the next end step. The target is registered in `GameData.delayedActions` (a `DelayedPermanentAction(DESTROY_AT_END_STEP)`) and destroyed when end step is processed (direct, not via stack). Used by Stone Giant |
| `SacrificeTargetPermanentAtEndStepEffect` | `()` | schedule the targeted permanent to be *sacrificed* at the beginning of the next end step. Registers a `DelayedPermanentAction(SACRIFICE_AT_END_STEP)` in `GameData.delayedActions`, drained by `StepTriggerService`. Sacrifice, not destruction (ignores indestructible/regeneration). Used by Lowland Oaf |
| `DestroyTargetCreatureAndCreateSpiritCopyToSacrificeEffect` | `()` | capture the target's effective power/toughness, destroy it (can't be regenerated), then create a black Spirit creature token for the controller with that power/toughness and register a `DelayedPermanentAction(SACRIFICE_AT_END_STEP)` for the new token. Token is created regardless of whether destruction succeeds (indestructible targets). `RemovalEffect` (DESTROY). Card supplies the target filter. Used by Broken Visage (nonartifact attacking creature) |
| `ReturnTargetPermanentToHandAtEndStepEffect` | `()` | schedule the targeted permanent to be returned to its owner's hand at the beginning of the next end step. Registers a `DelayedPermanentAction(RETURN_TO_HAND_AT_END_STEP)` in `GameData.delayedActions`, drained by `StepTriggerService` via `removePermanentToHand`. Used by Dragon Mask (pairs with a `BoostTargetCreatureEffect` on the shared target) |
| `ExileSelfAtEndStepEffect` | `()` | schedule the *source* permanent (no target) to be exiled at the beginning of the next end step. Registers an `DelayedPermanentAction(EXILE_AT_END_STEP)` in `GameData.delayedActions`, drained by `StepTriggerService` via `removePermanentToExile`. Used by Dark Maze (pairs with `CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect` on its own `{0}` attack ability) |
| `SacrificeSelfAtEndStepEffect` | `()` | schedule the *source* permanent (no target) to be *sacrificed* at the beginning of the next end step. Registers a `DelayedPermanentAction(SACRIFICE_AT_END_STEP)` in `GameData.delayedActions`, drained by `StepTriggerService`. Sacrifice, not destruction (ignores indestructible/regeneration). Put on `ON_ATTACK`/`ON_BLOCK` for "when this creature attacks or blocks, sacrifice it at the beginning of the next end step". Used by Brackwater Elemental |
| `DestroyAllPermanentsEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` / `(filter, boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` / `(filter, CardEffect thenEffect)` / `(filter, EachPermanentScope scope, CardEffect thenEffect)` | destroy all permanents matching the predicate filter — on every battlefield (`ALL_PLAYERS`, default) or only the targeted player's (`TARGET_PLAYER`; the card must `target(...)` a player). Optional `thenEffect` rider resolves afterwards with the count of permanents *actually destroyed* (skips indestructible/regenerated) on `eventValue`, so "for each permanent destroyed this way" riders are built from existing effects: Fracturing Gust / Righteous Fury = `GainLifeEffect(Scaled(EventValue(), 2))`, Paraselene = `GainLifeEffect(EventValue())`, Rain of Daggers = `TARGET_PLAYER` + `LoseLifeEffect(Scaled(EventValue(), 2), CONTROLLER)`, Overwhelming Forces = `TARGET_PLAYER` + `DrawCardEffect(EventValue())`, Phyrexian Rebirth = `CreateTokenEffect` with `EventValue()` power/toughness. Use `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` for creatures, compose with `PermanentAllOfPredicate`/`PermanentAnyOfPredicate` for multiple conditions |
| `DestroyPermanentsTargetPlayerControlsEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | destroy every permanent matching `filter` the targeted player controls (skips indestructible/regenerated). Targets a player (`harmful`, `TargetSpec` PLAYER); `BoardWipeEffect`. Ajani Vengeant −7 uses `PermanentIsLandPredicate` for "destroy all lands target player controls" |
| `EachPlayerChoosesCreatureDestroyRestEffect` | `()` | each player chooses a creature they control; destroy the rest. APNAP ordering, respects indestructible and regeneration. Players with 0-1 creatures auto-resolve. Uses the forced sacrifice queue in destroy-rest mode. Used by Divine Reckoning |
| `EachPlayerSacrificesGreatestManaValueCreatureUnlessPaysEffect` | `()` | non-targeting SPELL. In APNAP order, each player sacrifices the creature they control with the greatest mana value **unless they pay that creature's mana cost**; ties let that player choose which tied creature is at risk. If the player can pay, a may-ability prompt asks whether to pay (decline ⇒ sacrifice); if they can't afford it, the creature is sacrificed with no prompt. Sequenced one player at a time by `TariffSupport` via `gameData.tariffRemainingPlayers`; the tie-break is a `PermanentChoiceContext.TariffTieBreak` permanent choice. Used by Tariff |
| `DestroyTargetAndEachPlayerSearchesBasicLandToBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | destroy target permanent, then each player searches their library for a basic land card, puts it onto the battlefield, then shuffles. Searches in APNAP order (active player first). Search is mandatory but players can fail to find. Uses `LibrarySearchFollowUp.eachPlayerBasicLand` carried on the search interaction. Used by Field of Ruin |
| `EachOpponentMaySearchLibraryForBasicLandToBattlefieldTappedEffect` | `()` | each opponent may search their library for a basic land card, put it onto the battlefield tapped, then shuffle. Opponents search in APNAP order. Uses `LibrarySearchFollowUp.eachPlayerBasicLand` (tapped variant) carried on the search interaction. Used by Old-Growth Dryads |
| `EachOpponentMaySearchLibraryForCreatureToBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | each opponent may search their library for a creature card, put it onto the battlefield (untapped), then shuffle. Opponents search in APNAP order (active player first among opponents). Uses `LibrarySearchFollowUp.eachPlayerCreatureToBattlefield` carried on the search interaction. Used by Boldwyr Heavyweights |
| `EachPlayerMaySearchLibraryForCreaturesToHandEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count)`; convenience `()` = `new XValue()` | each player, in APNAP order (active player first), may search their library for up to `count` creature cards, reveal them, put them into their hand, then shuffle. Each per-player search is a "may" (a player may take fewer than `count`, or none); empty-library / no-creature / Leonin Arbiter players are skipped. `count <= 0` does nothing. Uses `LibrarySearchFollowUp.eachPlayerCreaturesToHand` (queue + shared count) carried on the search interaction. Used by Weird Harvest (`()`, count = the spell's X) |
| `DestroyTargetPermanentAndDamageControllerIfDestroyedEffect` | `(int damage)` | destroy target permanent and deal N damage to its controller only if the permanent is actually put into a graveyard (e.g. no damage if indestructible). Used by Werewolf Ransacker |
| `DestroyUpToTargetsThenReturnFromGraveyardEffect` | `()` | destroy each targeted permanent (up to ability max targets) and return each card actually put into a graveyard this way to the battlefield under the controller's control. Targeting/filter handled by the activating ability. Used by Sorin, Lord of Innistrad |
| `DestroyEachTargetPermanentEffect` | `(boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` / `()` | destroy every permanent in `entry.getTargetIds()`. Bind to a single multi-target group (use `targetX(filter, cap)` for X-scaled target counts). Snapshots the number actually put into a graveyard this way (indestructible/regenerated targets excluded) onto the entry's event value, so a later same-entry effect can read "that many" via `EventValue`. Used by Dregs of Sorrow ("Destroy X target nonblack creatures. Draw X cards." = `targetX(...).addEffect(SPELL, new DestroyEachTargetPermanentEffect())` + `DrawCardEffect(new XValue())`) and Volcanic Eruption (`+ MassDamageEffect(new EventValue(), true)`) |
| `DestroyBlockedCreatureAndSelfEffect` | `()` | destroy creature this blocks and itself (Deathtrap-style) |
| `DestroySourcePermanentEffect` | `()` / `(boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` | destroy the source permanent (identified by sourcePermanentId on the stack entry). Pass `true` to ignore regeneration shields ("It can't be regenerated" — Aether Storm's Pay-4-life ability). Used by Ice Cage's becomes-target trigger |
| `DestroySourceAndDamageControllerIfDestroyedEffect` | `(int damage)` | destroy the source permanent (sourcePermanentId on the stack entry, regeneration/indestructible respected) and, only if it is actually put into a graveyard, deal `damage` noncombat damage to its controller. Self analog of `DestroyTargetPermanentAndDamageControllerIfDestroyedEffect`. Fallback-only: interpreted by `DestructionSupport.resolveForcedCostElseEffects`, not dispatched through the effect registry. Used as a `ForcedCostOrElseEffect` else-effect by Cosmic Horror ("destroy this unless you pay {3}{B}{B}{B}; if destroyed this way, it deals 7 damage to you") |
| `DestroyEnchantedPermanentEffect` | `()` | destroy the permanent the source Aura is attached to (re-derived at resolution via the Aura's `attachedTo`; regeneration/indestructible apply). Placed on `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` (Spreading Algae, "When enchanted land becomes tapped, destroy it") or `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` (Yoke of the Damned, "When a creature dies, destroy enchanted creature"). Both collectors bake the Aura's source-permanent id onto the stack entry; fizzles if the Aura is no longer attached |
| `DestroyEnchantedPermanentUnlessPaysManaOrLifeEffect` | `(String manaCost, int lifeCost)` | `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` punisher: the enchanted permanent's controller (baked onto the trigger's `targetId`) may pay `manaCost` **or** `lifeCost` life to save the permanent, otherwise it's destroyed. A player who can pay neither loses it automatically (no prompt); otherwise the choice is offered via the may-ability system — accepting spends floating mana if the pool can pay it, else pays the life. Handler: `DestroyEnchantedPermanentUnlessPaysManaOrLifeEffectHandler` + `mayfx/DestroyEnchantedPermanentUnlessPaysManaOrLifeHandler` (`MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService.handleDestroyEnchantedPermanentUnlessPaysChoice`). Used by Erosion (`"{1}", 1`) |
| `DestroyCreatureBlockingThisEffect` | `()` | destroy creature that blocks this (combat trigger) |
| `DestroyTargetPermanentThenEffect` | `(EventStat stat, CardEffect thenEffect, ThenEffectRecipient recipient, PermanentPredicate thenCondition)` (+ `(thenEffect, recipient)` and `(stat, thenEffect, recipient)` sugar) | **collapsed destroy-plus-value family.** Destroy the target permanent, then resolve an existing `thenEffect` via its own handler. `recipient` = `CONTROLLER` (you gain life / this permanent gets +X/+0), `TARGET_CONTROLLER` (the destroyed permanent's controller — snapshotted before destruction — loses life / gets poison / searches their library), `TARGET_OWNER` (the destroyed permanent's owner — its original controller absent any control-changing effect; "its owner gains N life", Path of Peace), or `TARGET_CONTROLLER_AS_TARGET` (rider stays under the caster but the derived entry's `targetId` becomes the destroyed permanent's controller — for `TARGET_PLAYER`-recipient riders like "~ deals 3 damage to that land's controller", keeping damage shields keyed on the caster). `stat` (`NONE`/`MANA_VALUE`/`TOUGHNESS`) snapshots that last-known value onto the entry's `eventValue` so a then-effect built on `EventValue()` reads it. The then-effect always happens regardless of destruction (indestructible); `thenCondition` gates it on the destroyed permanent's last-known state (Death's Caress `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(HUMAN)`). Examples: DivineOffering `(MANA_VALUE, GainLifeEffect(EventValue()), CONTROLLER)`, HoardSmelterDragon `(MANA_VALUE, BoostSelfEffect(EventValue(), Fixed(0)), CONTROLLER)`, EngulfingSlagwurm/DeathsCaress `(TOUGHNESS, GainLifeEffect(EventValue()), CONTROLLER[, HUMAN])`, GlissasScorn `(LoseLifeEffect(1), TARGET_CONTROLLER)`, PistusStrike `(GivePoisonCountersEffect(1, CONTROLLER), TARGET_CONTROLLER)`, FleshAllergy `(LoseLifeEffect(CreatureDeathsThisTurn(ANY_PLAYER), CONTROLLER), TARGET_CONTROLLER)`, PathOfPeace `(GainLifeEffect(4), TARGET_OWNER)`, Cryoclasm/MeltTerrain `(DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, TARGET_PLAYER), TARGET_CONTROLLER_AS_TARGET)` ("destroy target land, ~ deals N damage to its controller"), GhostQuarter/Erode `(SearchLibraryEffect(basicLand, BATTLEFIELD[_TAPPED]), TARGET_CONTROLLER)` ("its controller may search … a basic land" — a restricted search can always fail to find, so "may" needs no flag) |
| `ExileTargetPermanentThenEffect` | `(CardEffect thenEffect, ThenEffectRecipient recipient)` or `(CardEffect thenEffect, ThenEffectRecipient recipient, PermanentPredicate thenCondition)` | **exile sibling of `DestroyTargetPermanentThenEffect`.** Exile the target permanent, then resolve an existing `thenEffect` via its own handler. `recipient` routes the then-effect: `CONTROLLER` (the caster), `TARGET_CONTROLLER` (the exiled permanent's controller — snapshotted before exile — so a `SearchLibraryEffect` searches their library), `TARGET_OWNER`, or `TARGET_CONTROLLER_AS_TARGET`. Exile always removes the permanent (no regeneration / indestructible), so with the 2-arg form the then-effect always happens. The 3-arg form gates it on `thenCondition`, a `PermanentPredicate` evaluated against the target as last known **before** exile — the then-effect runs only if it matches (`null` = always). Path to Exile = `(SearchLibraryEffect(basicLand, BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED), TARGET_CONTROLLER)` ("its controller may search … a basic land, put it onto the battlefield tapped" — a restricted search can always fail to find, so "may" needs no flag). Gideon's Defeat = `(GainLifeEffect(5), CONTROLLER, PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(GIDEON))` ("exile target white creature that's attacking or blocking; if it was a Gideon planeswalker, you gain 5 life") |
| `DestroySubtypeCombatOpponentEffect` | `(CardSubtype requiredSubtype, boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` | equipment combat trigger: when equipped creature blocks or becomes blocked by a creature with the required subtype, destroy that creature. At trigger creation time, the combat opponent's subtype is checked; if it matches, a `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect(cannotBeRegenerated)` is auto-targeted on the opponent and placed on the stack as non-targeting. Use ON_BLOCK (non-per-blocker) + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (PER_BLOCKER). See Wooden Stake |
| `DestroyOneOfTargetsAtRandomEffect` | `()` | destroy one permanent at random from `targetIds` on the stack entry. Filters out targets that left the battlefield before resolution. Used by Capricious Efreet's upkeep trigger (multi-target random destruction) |
| `DestroyAttachmentsOnTargetCreatureEffect` | `(boolean auras, boolean equipment)` | destroy the Auras and/or Equipment attached to the target creature (`(true, true)` = both, Strip Bare; `(false, true)` = Equipment only, Turn to Slag). Declares its own creature target (protection honoured). Effect order doesn't matter; lethal damage destruction is deferred until all effects on the stack entry resolve. Resolved by `DestructionResolutionService` |
| `DestroyEquipmentOnEquippedCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `()` | creature combat trigger: when this creature blocks or becomes blocked by an equipped creature, destroy all Equipment attached to that creature at end of combat. At trigger creation time in CombatBlockService, the combat opponent is checked for attached Equipment; if equipped, a trigger is placed on the stack with the equipped creature as target. On resolution, the target creature ID is recorded in `GameData.delayedActions` (a `DestroyEquipmentAtEndOfCombat`). At end of combat, all Equipment currently attached to those creatures is destroyed. Use ON_BLOCK (non-per-blocker) + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (PER_BLOCKER). See Corrosive Ooze |
| `DestroyCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` | Basilisk-style creature combat trigger: when this creature blocks or becomes blocked by a creature matching `filter`, destroy that creature **at end of combat** (so it still deals combat damage). The referenced opponent is carried as the stack entry's non-targeting target (ON_BLOCK auto-targets the blocked attacker via CombatBlockService's `needsAttackerTarget` list; ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED targets each blocker). On resolution the opponent is re-checked against `filter` (e.g. nonblack = `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentColorInPredicate({BLACK}))`) and, if it matches, a `DelayedPermanentAction(DESTROY_AT_END_OF_COMBAT)(id, cannotBeRegenerated)` delayed action is queued; drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatDestructions()`. Use ON_BLOCK (non-per-blocker) + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (PER_BLOCKER). See Deathgazer |
| `SacrificePermanentsEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count, PermanentPredicate filter, SacrificeRecipient recipient)` (int-count sugar ctor) | collapsed forced-sacrifice family. `SacrificeRecipient` routes who sacrifices: CONTROLLER, TARGET_PLAYER (player-targeting spec), EACH_PLAYER, EACH_OPPONENT (each-player recipients use the APNAP simultaneous `PendingForcedSacrifice` queue per CR 101.4), DEFENDING_PLAYER (non-targeting `ON_ATTACK` edict — reads the trigger's `attackedTargetId`, i.e. the attacked player or the attacked planeswalker's controller; "Whenever this creature attacks, defending player sacrifices a creature of their choice" — Thraximundar). **Two mechanics, selected by filter:** a bare `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` routes through the single-select "sacrifice a creature" primitive (`PermanentChoiceContext.SacrificeCreature`; auto-sac when the player has exactly one creature) — used by Cruel Edict / Geth's Verdict / Sheoldred / Liliana of the Veil −2 (TARGET_PLAYER), Stitcher's Apprentice (CONTROLLER), Grave Pact (EACH_OPPONENT). Any other filter uses the multi-permanent `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ForcedSacrifice` choice (auto-sac all when matches ≤ count) — used by Storm Fleet Arsonist (TARGET_PLAYER, PermanentTruePredicate), Yawning Fissure / Lorehold Charm / The Eldest Reborn (EACH_OPPONENT), Destructive Force (EACH_PLAYER, 5 lands). Both mechanics are behaviourally tested and rules-correct |
| `PlayerDestroysPermanentsEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count, PermanentPredicate filter, DestroyRecipient recipient)` (int-count sugar ctor) | the **destroy** analog of `SacrificePermanentsEffect`: a player chooses and destroys `count` of their own permanents matching `filter` (regeneration/indestructible apply). `DestroyRecipient` = CONTROLLER / TARGET_PLAYER (TARGET_PLAYER player-targeting spec). `PlayerDestroysPermanentsEffectHandler` → `DestructionSupport.destroyPlayerMatchingPermanents`: ≤count matching ⇒ all destroyed with no choice; >count ⇒ `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ForcedDestroy` multi-select, chosen permanents destroyed simultaneously then effect resolution resumes. Used by Burning of Xinye (`(4, PermanentIsLandPredicate, CONTROLLER)` + `(4, PermanentIsLandPredicate, TARGET_PLAYER)` + `MassDamageEffect(4)`) |
| `SacrificePermanentOrLoseLifeEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, int lifeLoss)` | the player on the stack entry's `targetId` (the enchanted player, for a Curse upkeep trigger baked by `StepTriggerService`) sacrifices one permanent matching `filter` of their choice; if they control none, they lose `lifeLoss` life instead (edict-with-punisher). `SacrificePermanentOrLoseLifeEffectHandler`: 0 matching ⇒ `LifeSupport.applyLifeLoss` + win check; 1 ⇒ auto-sacrifice; 2+ ⇒ single-select via the reused `PermanentChoiceContext.SacrificeCreature` context. Non-targeting (`targetSpec()` NONE). Cruel Reality (`PermanentAnyOfPredicate(creature, planeswalker)`, 5) |
| `LoseLifeUnlessSacrificeNonlandOrDiscardEffect` | `(int lifeLoss)` / `(int lifeLoss, LoseLifeRecipient recipient)` | a player loses `lifeLoss` life unless they sacrifice a nonland permanent of their choice or discard a card; the affected player picks. `recipient` (only `TARGET_PLAYER` / `TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` supported) selects that player: `TARGET_PLAYER` (compact ctor default) = the player on the stack entry's `targetId` (the enchanted player, for a Curse upkeep trigger baked by `StepTriggerService` — Torment of Scarabs); `TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` = the controller of the targeted permanent (`targetId` is a permanent), which itself is excluded from the sacrifice options ("sacrifice **another** nonland permanent") — adds no target, so pair it with a sibling targeting effect that owns the permanent target (`PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect`), listed first so the creature is still present at resolution (Torment of Venom). `LoseLifeUnlessSacrificeNonlandOrDiscardEffectHandler` is the single-player, single-pass slice of `TormentOfHailfireEffectHandler`: it reuses `ChoiceContext.TormentPenaltyChoice` (three-way list-pick, pruned to available options — life always offered) and `PermanentChoiceContext.TormentSacrifice`, driving them off the shared `GameData.torment` state (`chosenMode` written back by `handleTormentPenaltyChoice`), re-running per sacrifice/discard sub-choice via `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction`. No-nonland/no-hand ⇒ auto life-loss (no prompt). Non-targeting (`targetSpec()` NONE). Torment of Scarabs (3), Torment of Venom (3, TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER) |
| `TargetPlayerChoosesCreatureDestroyEffect` | `()` | target opponent chooses a creature they control, then it is **destroyed** (player-targeting spec). The destroy analog of the "sacrifice a creature" edict: routes through `destructionSupport.tryDestroyAndLog`, so regeneration and indestructible apply. 0 creatures ⇒ nothing; 1 ⇒ auto-destroy; 2+ ⇒ target picks via `PermanentChoiceContext.DestroyChosenCreature` choice context. E.g. Imperial Edict |
| `TargetPlayerChoosesCreatureExileEffect` | `()` | target opponent chooses a creature they control, then it is **exiled** (player-targeting spec). The exile analog of `TargetPlayerChoosesCreatureDestroyEffect`: ignores regeneration/indestructible and fires no "dies" triggers. 0 creatures ⇒ nothing; 1 ⇒ auto-exile; 2+ ⇒ target picks via `PermanentChoiceContext.DestroyChosenCreature` (with `exile=true`). E.g. Doomfall mode 1 |
| `OpponentChoosesCreatureToDestroyEffect` | `()` | an opponent of the controller chooses **any** creature on the battlefield and it is destroyed (non-targeting resolution choice). 0 creatures ⇒ nothing; 1 ⇒ auto-destroy; 2+ ⇒ opponent picks via `PermanentChoiceContext.DestroyChosenCreature`. Regeneration/indestructible apply. Second half of Diaochan, Artful Beauty ("destroy target creature of an opponent's choice"), paired after a `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect` for the controller's own choice |
| `SacrificeCreatureAndControllerGainsLifeEqualToToughnessEffect` | `(boolean sacrificerIsController)` | sacrificing player sacrifices a creature; effect's controller gains life equal to the sacrificed creature's toughness. `false` = the sacrificer is a chosen target (edict; player-targeting spec) — Tribute to Hunger. `true` = the controller both sacrifices and gains life, non-targeting — Doomgape's upkeep trigger. Uses `SacrificeCreatureControllerGainsLifeEqualToToughness` choice context when multiple creatures |
| `SacrificeCreatureToCreateTokensEqualToToughnessEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate, PermanentPredicate filter)` | controller chooses a creature they control matching `filter` to sacrifice (non-targeting). Captures the creature's effective toughness, sacrifices it, then creates that many copies of `tokenTemplate` for the controller (`tokenTemplate.amount()` ignored). Uses `SacrificeCreatureCreateTokensEqualToToughness` choice context. Wrap in `MayEffect` for the "you may sacrifice" optional case. E.g. Feed the Pack (`PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentIsTokenPredicate)` for nontoken; 2/2 green Wolf template) |
| `SacrificeTargetCreatureThenCreateTokensEqualToPowerEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | targets a creature (permanent-targeting spec). At resolution its controller sacrifices it and — using the creature's effective power captured before removal — that same player creates that many copies of `tokenTemplate` (`tokenTemplate.amount()` ignored). Fizzles if the target is no longer a legal creature. The power-based, targeted, controller-creates analog of `SacrificeCreatureToCreateTokensEqualToToughnessEffect`. Used by Mercy Killing (1/1 green-and-white Elf Warrior template) |
| `SacrificeCreatureCreateSizedTokenEqualToPowerEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate, PermanentPredicate filter)` | controller chooses a creature they control matching `filter` to sacrifice (non-targeting). Captures the creature's effective power (floored at 0), sacrifices it, then creates ONE `tokenTemplate` token whose power and toughness are each set to that value (`tokenTemplate.power()`/`toughness()`/`amount()` ignored). Uses `SacrificeCreatureCreateSizedTokenEqualToPower` choice context. The single-token, power-sized analog of `SacrificeCreatureToCreateTokensEqualToToughnessEffect` (which creates X copies). Used by Ooze Garden (`PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(OOZE))` for "non-Ooze"; green Ooze template) |
| `ExileTargetCreatureCardCreateTokensEqualToToughnessEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | SPELL targeting one graveyard card (`benign(ANY_GRAVEYARD_CARD)`; the creature-card restriction is enforced by a `GraveyardTargetValidators` `@ValidatesTarget` validator). At resolution captures the target card's printed toughness (null/negative → 0), exiles it from its graveyard, then creates that many copies of `tokenTemplate` for the controller (`tokenTemplate.amount()` ignored). Single target ⇒ the whole spell fizzles before this effect (no tokens) if the card has left the graveyard. Resolved by `ExileTargetCreatureCardCreateTokensEqualToToughnessEffectHandler` via `PermanentControlSupport.applyCreateToken`. The graveyard-exile analog of `SacrificeCreatureToCreateTokensEqualToToughnessEffect`. Used by Morbid Bloom (1/1 green Saproling template) |
| `SacrificeAttackingCreaturesEffect` | `(int baseCount, int metalcraftCount)` | target player sacrifices attacking creatures; metalcraft upgrades count |
| `EachPlayerReturnsCardsFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect` | `(int maxCount, CardPredicate filter)` or `(int maxCount, CardPredicate filter, CounterType enterWithCounter)` | each player returns up to maxCount cards matching filter from their graveyard to the battlefield. Players with fewer matching cards return all automatically. Players with more are prompted to choose in APNAP order. Optional `enterWithCounter` puts one counter of that type on each card as it enters (auto-return path only). Used by Fall of the Thran; Pyrrhic Revival returns ALL creatures (`Integer.MAX_VALUE`, `MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE`) |
| `ReturnCardsFromControllerGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, int maxCount)` | the controller returns up to maxCount cards matching filter from their OWN graveyard to the battlefield. Fewer matching cards → all return automatically; more → sequential "up to N" prompts via `pendingGraveyardReturnQueue` (choice made at resolution, not cast/trigger time). Non-targeting, so it drops straight onto the stack from any trigger slot. Used by Reveillark's `ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` ("return up to two target creature cards with power 2 or less from your graveyard to the battlefield") |
| `DamageSourceControllerGetsPoisonCounterEffect` | `(UUID damageSourceControllerId)` | damage source's controller gets a poison counter (e.g. Reaper of Sheoldred). Register as marker (null) on ON_DEALT_DAMAGE; actual UUID filled at trigger time |
| `DamageSourceControllerSacrificesPermanentsEffect` | `(int count, UUID sacrificingPlayerId)` | damage source's controller sacrifices that many permanents of their choice (e.g. Phyrexian Obliterator). Register as marker (0, null) on ON_DEALT_DAMAGE; actual values filled at trigger time |
| `SacrificeSelfEffect` | `()` | sacrifice this permanent (source of the stack entry). Implements `CombatDamageTriggerContextEffect` → `SOURCE_SELF`, so it works on an `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` slot ("…and sacrifice this creature", e.g. Kathari Bomber). Bundle with a `CreateTokenEffect` etc. via `SequenceEffect.of(...)` — `SequenceEffect` propagates the richest combat-damage trigger context of its steps |
| `SacrificeSelfThenDealDamageToTargetPlayerEffect` | `(int damage)` | sacrifice the source permanent; only if it was sacrificed ("if you do") deal N damage to the stack entry's `targetId` player. Used by Booby Trap's draw trigger (damage=10, targetId = the chosen player who drew the named card) |
| `SacrificeSelfIfEvokedEffect` | `()` | evoke sacrifice (CR 702.75e): place in `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`. `EtbEffectResolver` resolves it to a `SacrificeSelfEffect` when the permanent was cast for its evoke (alternate) cost, else drops the trigger. Pair with `AlternateHandCast(ManaCastingCost)` + `GameService.playCardWithEvoke` (Dawnfluke) |
| `SacrificeUnlessDiscardCardTypeEffect` | `(CardType requiredType)` / `(CardType requiredType, boolean random)` | sacrifice unless you discard a card of type (null = any). `random=true` (Pillaging Horde) discards the card at random instead of letting the player choose which; `random` only makes sense with `requiredType == null`. The convenience `(CardType)` ctor is non-random (Hidden Horror) |
| `SacrificeUnlessReturnOwnPermanentTypeToHandEffect` | `(CardType permanentType)` | sacrifice this permanent unless you return a permanent of the specified type you control to its owner's hand (ETB bounce-or-sacrifice, e.g. Glint Hawk) |
| `ChampionCreatureEffect` | `(CardSubtype... championedSubtypes)` — no-arg ctor = any creature; multiple subtypes match inclusively ("Goblin or Shaman", Lightning Crafter) | champion a creature (or creature of one of the subtypes): on ETB sacrifice unless you exile another matching creature you control; when this leaves the battlefield the exiled card returns. Uses `PermanentChoiceContext.ChampionCreature` + `exileReturnOnPermanentLeave`. Used by Changeling Hero. For a "when a creature is championed with this" follow-up trigger, add the triggered effect to the `ON_CHAMPIONED` slot — it fires from `PermanentChoiceBattlefieldHandlerService.handleChampionCreature` right after the exile (player-targeting effects route through `PermanentChoiceContext.ChampionedTriggerTarget`; Mistbind Clique) |
| `DestroyNonlandPermanentsWithManaValueEqualToChargeCountersEffect` | `()` | destroy each nonland permanent with mana value equal to the number of charge counters on source (reads snapshotted count from xValue). Used by Ratchet Bomb |
| `DestroyNonlandPermanentsWithManaValueXDealtCombatDamageEffect` | `()` | destroy each nonland permanent with mana value equal to X whose controller was dealt combat damage by the source permanent this turn. Reads X from xValue, checks combatDamageToPlayersThisTurn. Used by Steel Hellkite |
| `SacrificeSelfAndDrawCardsEffect` | `(int amount)` | "sacrifice this, then draw N cards." Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may" behavior. Used on ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER triggers. StackEntry context: sourcePermanentId = source creature. Resolved by `PlayerInteractionResolutionService` |
| `SacrificeSelfAndTargetDiscardsPerPoisonCounterEffect` | `()` | "sacrifice this, then that player discards a card for each poison counter they have." Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may" behavior. Used on ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER triggers where "that player" is the damaged player. StackEntry context: targetId = damaged player, sourcePermanentId = source creature. Resolved by `PlayerInteractionResolutionService` |
| `SacrificeSelfAndTargetPlayerDiscardsEffect` | `(int amount)` | "sacrifice this, then that player discards N cards." Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may" behavior. Used on ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED triggers where "that player" is the defending player. StackEntry context: targetId = affected player, sourcePermanentId = source creature. Interactive discard (fewer if hand smaller). Mindstab Thrull (3) |
| `SacrificeSelfToDestroyCreatureDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` | `(boolean cannotBeRegenerated)` (no-arg = `false`) | "sacrifice this, then destroy target creature that player controls." Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may" behavior. Used on ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER (Blind Zealot) and ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED (Necrite, `cannotBeRegenerated=true`) triggers where "that player" is the damaged / defending player. StackEntry context: targetId = affected player, sourcePermanentId = source creature. Presents multi-permanent choice (max 1); `cannotBeRegenerated=true` ignores regeneration shields. Resolved by `DestructionResolutionService` |
| `TransformSelfAndAttachToCreatureDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` | `()` | "transform this, then attach it to target creature that player controls." Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may transform" behavior. Used on ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER triggers where "that player" is the damaged player (e.g. Soul Seizer). StackEntry context: targetId = damaged player, sourcePermanentId = source permanent. Presents multi-permanent choice (max 1), then transforms and attaches via `AnimationResolutionService.completeTransformAndAttach`. Applies `ControlEnchantedCreatureEffect` steal when present on the back face |
| `SacrificeAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `()` or `(int damageToController)` | sacrifice the source at end of combat. With `damageToController > 0` ("sacrifice it and it deals N damage to you", Time Elemental = 5) the source also deals that much damage to its controller at end of combat via `CombatService.processEndOfCombatSacrifices`; the damage is a delayed trigger dealt with last-known information, so it fires even if the creature already left the battlefield. Put on ON_ATTACK / ON_BLOCK |
| `DestroySelfAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `()` | schedule the source permanent for **destruction** at end of combat (regeneration/indestructible apply, unlike sacrifice). "When this creature blocks/attacks, destroy it at end of combat." Put on ON_BLOCK / ON_ATTACK; queues a `DelayedPermanentAction(DESTROY_AT_END_OF_COMBAT)` delayed action drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatDestructions()`. See Cinder Wall |
| `PutCounterOnCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int amount)` | schedule the **combat opponent** (the creature this permanent blocks, or that becomes blocked by it) to get `amount` counters of `counterType` at end of combat. "At end of combat, put a [counter] on each creature blocking or blocked by this creature." Put on ON_BLOCK (`needsAttackerTarget` in `CombatBlockService` binds the blocked attacker) + ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED (`TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER`, binds each blocker); queues a `PutCounterOnPermanentAtEndOfCombat` delayed action drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatOpponentCounters()` (respects `cantHaveCounters`). Greater Werewolf = `(CounterType.MINUS_ZERO_MINUS_TWO, 1)`; the `MINUS_ZERO_MINUS_TWO` counter subtracts 2 toughness each (`Permanent.getEffectiveToughness`/`getToughnessModifiers`, `CharacteristicState`) |
| `PutMinusOneCounterOnSourceAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `()` | schedule the source permanent to get a **-1/-1 counter at end of combat** (delayed, so it stays full size for the combat damage step — unlike the immediate `PutCountersOnSourceEffect(-1,-1,1)`). "Whenever this creature attacks or blocks, put a -1/-1 counter on it at end of combat." Put on ON_ATTACK and/or ON_BLOCK; queues a `PutMinusOneCounterAtEndOfCombat` delayed action drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatSourceCounters()` (respects `cantHaveCounters`/`cantHaveMinusOneMinusOneCounters`, fires -1/-1 put-on-creature triggers). See Wicker Warcrawler |
| `SacrificeTargetThenRevealUntilTypeToBattlefieldEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | sacrifice the targeted permanent, then its controller reveals cards from the top of their library until a card matching one of the specified types is found; that card is put onto the battlefield under that player's control, and all other revealed cards are shuffled into their library. Polymorph-style effect (used by Shape Anew for artifact→artifact) |
| `DestroyTargetThenRevealUntilTypeToBattlefieldEffect` | `(boolean cannotBeRegenerated, Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | destroy the targeted permanent (optionally preventing regeneration), then its controller reveals cards from the top of their library until a card matching one of the specified types is found; that card is put onto the battlefield under that player's control, and all other revealed cards are shuffled into their library. Reveal happens regardless of whether destruction succeeds (indestructible). Used by Polymorph (creature→creature with cannotBeRegenerated=true) |
| `ExileAllCreaturesYouControlThenRevealCreaturesToBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | exile all creatures you control, then reveal cards from the top of your library until you reveal that many creature cards; put all revealed creature cards onto the battlefield, then shuffle the rest into your library. Mass Polymorph-style effect |
| `SeparatePermanentsIntoPilesAndSacrificeEffect` | `()` | separate all permanents target player controls into two piles; target player sacrifices all permanents in the chosen pile (Liliana of the Veil ultimate). Two-step async flow: controller assigns piles via multi-permanent choice, then target player picks pile to sacrifice via may-ability choice |

### Sacrifice costs (for activated abilities)

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `ExileSelfCost` | `()` | exile this permanent as cost (e.g. Brittle Effigy). Handled in `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService` via `removePermanentToExile` |
| `SacrificeSelfCost` | `()` | sacrifice this permanent as cost |
| `RemoveAllCountersAsCostEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` | additional cost: remove all counters of the given type from the source. The number removed is snapshotted into the ability's xValue (in `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService`, via `Permanent.getCounterCount`/`setCounterCount`) before the counters are cleared, so a companion effect (e.g. `LookAtTopCardsEffect` with an `XValue()` look count) scales with the count removed. Used by Jar of Eyeballs (`CounterType.EYEBALL`) |
| `RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` | resolution effect (not a cost): remove all counters of the given type from the source permanent and snapshot the removed count as the entry's *event value*, so a later effect on the same entry reads "that much" via `EventValue` — e.g. Ashling the Pilgrim's `ConditionalEffect(NthAbilityResolutionThisTurn(3), RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE))` + `ConditionalEffect(..., MassDamageEffect(new EventValue(), true))`. Contrast `RemoveAllCountersAsCostEffect`, which is paid at activation and snapshots into xValue |
| `RemoveCountersToCreateTetraviteTokensEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | Tetravus upkeep trigger 1 ("you may remove any number of +1/+1 counters from this creature. If you do, create that many … tokens"). Its handler prompts a 0..N number choice (`ChoiceContext.TetravusCounterRemoval`; 0 = decline, so no `MayEffect` wrapper); the completion in `ChoiceHandlerService` removes that many +1/+1 counters and creates that many tokens from `tokenTemplate`, adding each created id to `GameData.tetravusCreatedTokens` (source permanent id → token id set) as "created with" the source. Does nothing if the source has no +1/+1 counters |
| `ExileTetraviteTokensToPutCountersOnSelfEffect` | `()` | Tetravus upkeep trigger 2 ("you may exile any number of tokens created with this creature. If you do, put that many +1/+1 counters on this creature"). Its handler gathers the source's still-alive tracked tokens from `GameData.tetravusCreatedTokens` (any controller) and opens a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ExileTetraviteTokensPutCountersOnSource` multi-permanent choice; the completion in `MultiPermanentChoiceHandlerService` exiles the chosen tokens and puts that many +1/+1 counters on the source. Does nothing if the source has no surviving tokens |
| `SacrificeCreatureCost` | `()` or `(boolean trackSacrificedManaValue)` or `(boolean trackSacrificedManaValue, boolean trackSacrificedPower)` or `(boolean trackSacrificedManaValue, boolean trackSacrificedPower, boolean trackSacrificedToughness)` or `(boolean trackSacrificedManaValue, boolean trackSacrificedPower, boolean trackSacrificedToughness, boolean excludeSelf)` | sacrifice a creature as cost. When `trackSacrificedManaValue=true`, the sacrificed creature's mana value is stored in the StackEntry's xValue (e.g. Birthing Pod). When `trackSacrificedPower=true`, the sacrificed creature's effective power (including static bonuses) is stored in xValue (e.g. Ichor Explosion). When `trackSacrificedToughness=true`, the sacrificed creature's effective toughness is stored in xValue (e.g. Disciple of Griselbrand). When `excludeSelf=true`, the source permanent cannot be chosen as the sacrifice target — use for "Sacrifice another creature" costs (e.g. Grimgrin, Corpse-Born) |
| `SacrificeArtifactCost` | `()` | sacrifice an artifact as cost (works for both activated abilities and spell costs) |
| `SacrificePermanentCost` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, String description)` or `(PermanentPredicate filter, String description, boolean excludeSource)` | sacrifice a permanent matching filter as cost. Works for spell costs, activated abilities (via `MultiplePermanentSacrificeCostHandler`), and predicate-backed forced costs. Uses `PredicateEvaluationService.matchesPermanentPredicate()` for validation. Use `PermanentAllOfPredicate(List.of(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(subtype)))` with `excludeSource=false` for "Sacrifice a [subtype]" creature costs that can sacrifice the source |
| `SacrificeMultiplePermanentsCost` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter)` | sacrifice N permanents matching filter as cost (e.g. "Sacrifice three artifacts: ..." with `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate`). Multi-step UI: if exactly N match, auto-sacrifices all; otherwise prompts one-at-a-time. Validated and paid in `AbilityActivationService` |
| `SacrificeAllCreaturesYouControlCost` | `()` | sacrifice all creatures you control as cost |
| `ReturnMultiplePermanentsToHandCost` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter)` | return N permanents matching filter from battlefield to owner's hand as cost (e.g. "Return two lands you control to their owner's hand" with `PermanentIsLandPredicate`). Multi-step UI: if exactly N match, auto-returns all; otherwise prompts one-at-a-time. Validated and paid in `AbilityActivationService`. Works with both battlefield and graveyard activated abilities |
| `ReturnCreatureToHandCost` | `()` | additional cost to cast a **spell**: return a creature you control to its owner's hand (Familiar's Ruse). SPELL slot. The creature is supplied via `PlayCardRequest.sacrificePermanentId` (reuses the sacrifice-cost id field) and paid in `SpellCastingService`; spell is unplayable if you control no creature (`CastingCostService.canPayAdditionalSpellCosts`). This is the spell-cast analogue of `ReturnMultiplePermanentsToHandCost` (which is activated-ability only) |
| `PutCounterOnControlledCreatureCost` | `(CounterType counterType, int count)` | put `count` counter(s) of the given type on a creature you control. **Spell cost** (SPELL slot, Scarscale Ritual: `MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1`): creature supplied via `PlayCardRequest.sacrificePermanentId` and paid in `SpellCastingService`; spell is unplayable if you control no creature (`CastingCostService.canPayAdditionalSpellCosts`). Also usable as an **activated-ability cost** (Hatchet Bully): dispatched to `PutCounterOnCreatureCostHandler` via the `PermanentChoiceCostHandler` pattern — auto-selects when only one creature qualifies, prompts when multiple. Counter placed directly; creature dies later via state-based actions if toughness reaches 0 |
| `DiscardCardTypeCost` | `(CardPredicate predicate, String label)` or `(CardPredicate predicate, String label, boolean manaValueEqualsX)` | discard a card matching a predicate as cost (null predicate = any card). The `label` is used in UI messages. E.g. `new DiscardCardTypeCost(new CardTypePredicate(CardType.LAND), "land")`, `new DiscardCardTypeCost(new CardIsHistoricPredicate(), "historic")`, `new DiscardCardTypeCost(null, null)` for any card. Set `manaValueEqualsX=true` for "discard a card with mana value X" — the discardable cards are additionally restricted to those whose mana value equals the ability's chosen X (Knollspine Invocation, paired with an `{X}` mana cost). Also usable as a **spell cost** (SPELL slot, Seize the Spoils): the discard is supplied via `PlayCardRequest.discardHandCardIndex`, validated before any cost is paid (`AdditionalSpellCostService`), and the spell is unplayable without another matching card in hand (`CastingCostService.canPayAdditionalSpellCosts` / `validDiscardCostIndices` — the spell can never be its own discard) |
| — additional cast costs (all of the above SPELL-slot cost types) | | **`AdditionalSpellCostService`** (`service/effect/cost/`) is the single home for non-mana additional cast costs: extraction, satisfiability and mutate-nothing validation, run BEFORE the mana payment on every cast path (CR 601.2h — a rejected cast must leak nothing). Payment stays in `SpellCastingService`. A NEW `CostEffect` type must be added to `AdditionalSpellCostService.HANDLED_SPELL_COST_TYPES` (spell-castable) or `CostEffectClassificationTest`'s ability-only list, or the build fails |
| `DiscardRandomCardCost` | `()` | discard one uniformly-random card from the controller's hand as an activation cost (no player choice, paid immediately). Requires a non-empty hand to activate. Sets `discardCausedByOpponent=false` and fires the discarded card's discard triggers. Contrast `DiscardCardTypeCost` (player chooses) and `DiscardHandCost` (whole hand). Coral Helm (`{3}, Discard a card at random: Target creature gets +2/+2`) |
| `RemoveCounterFromSourceCost` | `(int count, CounterType counterType)` | remove N counters of the specified type from this permanent as cost. `CounterType.CHARGE` for charge counters, `MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE` for "-1/-1 counters", `PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE` for "+1/+1 counters", `STUDY` for study counters, `WISH` for wish counters, `ANY` to prefer -1/-1 then +1/+1. Compact: `()` defaults to `(1, ANY)`, `(int count)` defaults to `(count, ANY)` |
| `RemoveCounterFromSourceEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int amount)` | resolved effect (NOT a cost): removes up to `amount` counters of the type from the source permanent, clamped at zero (no-op if none). Self-targeting (`targetSpec().selfTargeting()`), so the spell-cast / trigger collectors carry the source permanent id onto the stack entry. Handled by `RemoveCounterFromSourceEffectHandler`. Pair with `SpellCastTriggerEffect(new CardColorPredicate(...), List.of(...))` for "whenever you cast a [color] spell, remove a -1/-1 counter from this" (Shrewd Hatchling). Distinct from the immediate `RemoveCounterFromSourceCost` |
| `PutCounterOnSourceCost` | `(int powerModifier, int toughnessModifier, int count)` | put N counters on this permanent as an activation cost (paid immediately). Positive powerModifier = +1/+1 counters, otherwise -1/-1. Respects `cantHaveCounters`/`cantHaveMinusOneMinusOneCounters`. Compact `()` defaults to `(-1, -1, 1)`. Barrenton Medic ("Put a -1/-1 counter on this creature: Untap this creature.") |
| `RemoveCounterFromControlledCreatureCost` | `(int count, CounterType counterType)` | remove N counters of the specified type from a creature you control as cost. Unlike `RemoveCounterFromSourceCost`, this allows choosing ANY creature the player controls (not just the source). Uses `PermanentChoiceCostHandler` pattern — auto-selects when only one creature qualifies, prompts when multiple. Used by Shapers of Nature |
| `RemoveChargeCountersFromSourceCost` | `(int count)` | remove N charge counters from source as cost (e.g. "Remove three charge counters: ..."). Validated and paid in `AbilityActivationService` |
| `CrewCost` | `(int requiredPower)` | Crew keyword cost: tap any number of untapped creatures you control with total power >= requiredPower. Uses power-based completion (not fixed count). Auto-pays when all creatures must be tapped to meet threshold; prompts interactively when player has choices. E.g. `new CrewCost(3)` for "Crew 3". Pair with `AnimatePermanentsEffect.crew()` in the ability's effects list |
| `TapCreatureCost` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate)` or `(PermanentPredicate predicate, boolean excludeSelf, boolean trackTappedCreaturePower)` | tap an untapped creature matching predicate you control as cost. Auto-selects if only one valid target; presents permanent choice if multiple. The creature can be summoning sick (no tap symbol in cost). E.g. `new TapCreatureCost(new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLUE)))` for "tap an untapped blue creature". `excludeSelf=true` forbids tapping the source ("other than this creature"); `trackTappedCreaturePower=true` remembers the tapped creature so a companion `BoostSelfEffect(new ChosenPermanentPower(), …)` reads its power at resolution (Impelled Giant) |
| `TapMultiplePermanentsCost` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter, boolean excludeSource)` | tap N untapped permanents matching filter as cost. Auto-selects if exactly N valid; presents permanent choice one at a time if more. Use `excludeSource=true` when the ability also has `requiresTap=true` ({T} in cost) to prevent the source from being counted twice. E.g. `new TapMultiplePermanentsCost(5, new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.MYR))` for "tap five untapped Myr you control"; `new TapMultiplePermanentsCost(2, new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), true)` for "{T}, tap two untapped creatures you control" |
| `UntapMultiplePermanentsCost` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter, boolean excludeSource)` | the `{Q}` untap-symbol mirror of `TapMultiplePermanentsCost`: untap N *tapped* permanents matching filter as cost. Auto-selects if exactly N valid; presents permanent choice one at a time if more. Use `excludeSource=true` when the ability also has `{Q}` (`requiresUntap`) so the source isn't counted twice. Pair with `.withRequiresUntap()` on the ability. E.g. `new UntapMultiplePermanentsCost(2, new PermanentAllOfPredicate(List.of(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), new PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(CardColor.BLUE)))), true)` for Crackleburr's "Untap two tapped blue creatures you control" |
| `TapXPermanentsCost` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(PermanentPredicate filter, boolean excludeSource)` | tap X untapped permanents matching filter as cost, where X is the xValue chosen by the player at activation time. Like `TapMultiplePermanentsCost` but with dynamic count from xValue. Use `excludeSource=true` when the ability also has `requiresTap=true`. E.g. `new TapXPermanentsCost(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.KNIGHT), true)` for "{T}, tap X untapped Knights you control" (Aryel, Knight of Windgrace) |
| `PayLifeCost` | `(int amount)` / `halfLifeRoundedUp()` | pay N life as cost. `PayLifeCost.halfLife()` instead pays half your life rounded up (computed from current life at activation, e.g. Murderous Betrayal). Validated (checks sufficient life) and paid in `AbilityActivationService`. Used by Adanto Vanguard |
| `ExileCardFromGraveyardCost` | `(CardType requiredType)`, `(CardSubtype requiredSubtype)`, `(CardType requiredType, boolean payExiledCardManaCost, boolean imprintOnSource)`, or `(CardType requiredType, boolean payExiledCardManaCost, boolean imprintOnSource, boolean trackExiledPower)` | exile a card of specific type (or subtype) from your graveyard as cost (null = any). Use the `(CardSubtype)` ctor for "Exile an Elf card" (Scarred Vinebreeder); when both type and subtype are set, both must match. For activated abilities: two-phase async flow prompts graveyard choice, then resumes activation (handled by `AbilityActivationService`). For spell costs: add to SPELL slot and pass `exileGraveyardCardIndex` (handled by `SpellCastingService`). When `payExiledCardManaCost=true`, the exiled card's mana cost is dynamically charged. When `imprintOnSource=true`, the exiled card is stored as imprinted card. When `trackExiledPower=true`, the exiled card's power becomes the X value (e.g. Corpse Lunge). 1-arg and 3-arg constructors default `trackExiledPower` to false |
| `ExileXCardsFromGraveyardCost` | `()` | exile X cards (any type) from your graveyard as an additional cost to cast a spell. The number of exiled cards becomes the X value. Player chooses which and how many cards to exile (0 or more). Add to SPELL slot and pass `exileGraveyardCardIndices` (List<Integer>) via `PlayCardRequest`. Handled by `SpellCastingService`. E.g. Harvest Pyre |
| `ExileNCardsFromGraveyardCost` | `(int count, CardType requiredType)` | exile exactly N cards of the specified type from your graveyard as an additional cost to cast a spell (null requiredType = any). Unlike `ExileXCardsFromGraveyardCost`, requires an exact count and does not set the X value. Add to SPELL slot and pass `exileGraveyardCardIndices` (List<Integer>) via `PlayCardRequest`. `GameBroadcastService` checks graveyard has enough matching cards for castability. Handled by `SpellCastingService`. E.g. Skaab Ruinator (3, CREATURE). Also usable as an **activated-ability** cost (Immortal Coil "Exile two cards from your graveyard"): `AbilityActivationService` gates on graveyard size ≥ count and auto-exiles the front N (`GraveyardService.exileCardsFromGraveyard`) — no per-card choice interaction |
| `ExileSelfFromGraveyardCost` | `()` | **Embalm / Eternalize** cost: exile the graveyard-activated ability's own source card from the controller's graveyard ("Exile this card from your graveyard"). Paid at activation time in `AbilityActivationService.activateGraveyardAbilityImpl` (like `ExileNCardsFromGraveyardCost`) — the source leaves the graveyard before the ability goes on the stack, so it can't be activated twice off the same card. Pair with `CreateTokenCopyOfSourceEffect(..., colorOverride, addedSubtype, removeManaCost)`. E.g. Angel of Sanctions |

## Counter spells

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `CounterSpellEffect` | `()` / `(CounteredSpellDestination destination)` | counter target spell (or ability); `destination` (default `GRAVEYARD`) sends the countered card to `EXILE` (Dissipate, Faerie Trickery) or `LIBRARY_TOP` (Memory Lapse) instead. Copies and countered abilities cease to exist regardless. |
| `CounterEachTargetSpellEffect` | `()` | counter every spell chosen for this effect's target group — an "up to N target spells" counter (Double Negative). Bind to a single `target(filter, 0, N)` spell-on-stack group; the handler counters each spell in `targetsForEffect` (mirrors `DealDamageToEachTargetEffect`), so a target that left the stack or is uncounterable is skipped while the rest are countered. Enables the non-modal multi-spell-target cast path: `SpellCastingService.multipleSpellTargets` = `!wasModal && !unwrappedNeedsTarget && getMaxTargets() > 1`, validated by `TargetLegalityService.validateMultiSpellTargetsOnStack` (now accepts `getMinTargets()..maxTargets` distinct spells). |
| `CounterSpellAndCreateTreasureTokensEffect` | `()` | counter target spell and create Treasure tokens equal to that spell's mana value. Treasures are created even if the spell can't be countered (uncounterable). Used by Spell Swindle |
| `CounterSpellAndExileAllWithSameNameEffect` | `()` | counter target spell, then search its controller's graveyard, hand, and library for all cards with the same name and exile them; that player shuffles. Per rulings, an uncounterable/protected spell stays on the stack but the search still happens. The countered spell (now in the graveyard) is caught by the search and exiled too. Used by Counterbore |
| `CounterSpellAndGainControlIfArtifactOrCreatureEffect` | `()` | counter target spell; if it is an artifact or creature spell, put that card onto the battlefield under the caster's control (ownership tracked) instead of into its owner's graveyard. Used by Desertion |
| `CounterSpellIfControllerPoisonedEffect` | `()` | counter target spell if its controller is poisoned (has at least one poison counter) |
| `TargetSpellControllerLosesLifeEffect` | `(int amount)` | target spell's controller loses N life. Companion effect for counter spells (e.g. Psychic Barrier). Place before CounterSpellEffect so target is still on stack |
| `TargetSpellControllerDiscardsEffect` | `(int amount)` | target spell's controller discards N cards. Companion effect for counter spells (e.g. Frightful Delusion). Place before counter effect so target is still on stack |
| `TargetSpellControllerDrawsCardEffect` | `()` | target spell's controller draws a card. Companion effect for counter spells (Dream Fracture: "Counter target spell. Its controller draws a card. Draw a card."). Place before the counter effect so the target is still on the stack; draws regardless of whether the spell was actually countered (handles uncounterable spells). Not a chosen player target |
| `TargetPermanentControllerDrawsCardEffect` | `()` | the controller of the permanent targeted by this stack entry draws a card (permanent analogue of `TargetSpellControllerDrawsCardEffect`). Piggyback effect — reads `entry.getTargetId()` and never contributes a chosen target, so pair it with a sibling effect that owns the permanent target (e.g. `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect`, or the ability's own `TargetFilter`). Gwafa Hazid, Profiteer ("Put a bribery counter on target creature you don't control. Its controller draws a card.") |
| `CounterlashEffect` | `()` | counter target spell, then controller may cast a spell from hand that shares a card type with the countered spell without paying its mana cost. Per rulings: still offers cast if spell is uncounterable; fizzles (no cast) if target is illegal. Queues one PendingMayAbility per eligible hand card using MayCastFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect. Accepting one removes the rest. Used by Counterlash |
| `MayCastFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect` | `()` | internal marker effect used in PendingMayAbility to route "may cast from hand without paying mana cost" choices. Not placed on cards directly — queued by CounterlashEffect resolution in CounterResolutionService, handled by MayCastHandlerService.handleMayCastFromHandWithoutPaying() |
| `MayCastFromHandSharingNameWithSpellCastThisTurnEffect` | `()` | activated-ability effect for Twinning Glass (`{1}, {T}`). On resolution offers each nonland hand card whose name matches a spell **any** player cast this turn (via GameData.getSpellsCastThisTurn across orderedPlayerIds) as a MayCastFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect PendingMayAbility; casting one clears the rest. Handled by MayCastFromHandSharingNameWithSpellCastThisTurnEffectHandler |
| `MayCastAnySpellFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect` | `()` | "you may cast a spell from your hand without paying its mana cost" with **no** filter (Maelstrom Archangel, ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER). On resolution offers each nonland hand card as a MayCastFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffect PendingMayAbility; casting one clears the rest. Handled by MayCastAnySpellFromHandWithoutPayingManaCostEffectHandler |
| `ReplaceControlledCounterWithExileAndPlayEffect` | `()` | STATIC replacement (Guile): "If a spell or ability you control would counter a spell, instead exile that spell and you may play that card without paying its mana cost." Checked in `CounterSupport` — applies to every counter effect (counterSpell/counterSpellAndExile) controlled by this permanent's controller. Only replaces the countering of spells (not abilities/copies); uncounterable spells are unaffected (no counter event). Queues a `MayPlayExiledCounteredCardEffect` PendingMayAbility |
| `MayPlayExiledCounteredCardEffect` | `()` | internal marker effect used in PendingMayAbility to route the "may play the exiled countered spell without paying its mana cost" choice queued by `ReplaceControlledCounterWithExileAndPlayEffect`. Handled in MayAbilityHandlerService via `ExileFreeCastSupport.castFromExileWithoutPaying`; declining leaves the card exiled |
| `CounterUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int amount)` or `(int amount, boolean useXValue, boolean exileIfCountered)` or `(int amount, boolean useXValue, boolean exileIfCountered, List<CardEffect> onNotPaidEffects)` | counter unless controller pays N generic mana.
