Use `(int)` for fixed amount (e.g. Mana Leak). Use 3-arg form with `useXValue=true` to read amount from stack entry's X value, and `exileIfCountered=true` to exile instead of graveyard (e.g. Syncopate: `new CounterUnlessPaysEffect(0, true, true)`). Use the 4-arg `onNotPaidEffects` form for a "if that player doesn't pay, …" rider (Power Sink): those effects resolve against the countered spell's controller (their id becomes the rider entry's target) on both the couldn't-afford and declined branches |
| `CounterUnlessDiscardsEffect` | `()` | counter target spell/ability unless its controller discards a card. Models "Ward—Discard a card" (e.g. Forum Necroscribe) via `ON_BECOMES_TARGET_OF_OPPONENT_SPELL`. If the controller has no card, it is countered immediately; otherwise they are prompted to discard or be countered |
| `CounterSpellsNamedLikeCardsExiledWithSourceEffect` | `()` | non-targeting: counter every spell on the stack whose name matches a card exiled with the source permanent (looked up via the resolving entry's `sourcePermanentId`, which survives the sacrifice cost). Respects uncounterable/protection via `CounterSupport.findCounterTarget`. Used by Grimoire Thief's `{U}, Sacrifice` ability (pair with `SacrificeSelfCost`) |
| `RegisterDelayedCounterTriggerEffect` | `(int genericManaAmount)` | registers a delayed trigger (opening hand reveal) that counters each opponent's first spell unless they pay N generic mana. Handled by MayAbilityHandlerService, not GameService |
| `RegisterDelayedManaTriggerEffect` | `(ManaColor color, int amount)` | registers a delayed trigger (opening hand reveal) that adds N mana of the given color at the beginning of the revealing player's first precombat main phase. Handled by MayAbilityHandlerService, not GameService |
| `LeylineStartOnBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | marker effect for leyline cards: if in opening hand, player may begin the game with the card on the battlefield (CR 103.6a). Used as wrapped effect inside MayEffect, queued in MulliganService.startGame(), handled by MayMiscHandlerService.handleLeylineChoice(). Used by Leyline of Anticipation, Leyline of the Void |
| `ExileOpponentCardsInsteadOfGraveyardEffect` | `()` | static replacement effect: if a card would be put into an opponent's graveyard from anywhere, exile it instead (CR 614.1). Checked in GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard(). Used by Leyline of the Void |
| `RevealAndPutOnBottomOfLibraryInsteadOfGraveyardEffect` | `()` | static replacement effect on a player aura: if a card would be put into the enchanted player's graveyard from anywhere, instead it is revealed and put on the bottom of that player's library (CR 614.1). Checked in GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard() by scanning for a permanent carrying this effect attached to the graveyard's owner; tokens (not cards) are unaffected. Pair with `setEnchantPlayer(true)` since it's a non-Curse "Enchant player" aura. Used by Wheel of Sun and Moon |
| `ExileOwnCardsInsteadOfGraveyardEffect` | `()` | static replacement effect: if a card would be put into the controller's own graveyard from anywhere, exile it instead (CR 614.1). Controller-side counterpart of `ExileOpponentCardsInsteadOfGraveyardEffect`. Checked in GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard(). Used by Forbidden Crypt |
| `ExileWithEggCountersInsteadOfDyingEffect` | `(int count)` | static replacement effect: "If [this] would die, instead exile it with N egg counters on it." (CR 614). Only applies when sourceZone is BATTLEFIELD (i.e. "die"). Checked in GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard(). Pair with upkeep trigger in StepTriggerService that scans exiledCardEggCounters. Used by Darigaaz Reincarnated (3) |
| `PutOnTopOfLibraryInsteadOfDyingEffect` | `()` | static replacement effect: "If [this creature] would die, put it on top of its owner's library instead." (CR 614). Only applies when sourceZone is BATTLEFIELD (i.e. "die"). Checked in GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard(). Used by Gravebane Zombie |
| `DiscardToTopOfLibraryInsteadEffect` | `()` | static replacement (Library of Leng): "If an effect causes you to discard a card, you may put it on top of your library instead of into your graveyard." Applies to the discarding player's own discards only. Checked in `GraveyardService.discardCard()` (the choke point all discard sites route through). Modeled as always keeping the card; the card is still discarded so discard triggers still fire. Pair with `NoMaximumHandSizeEffect` |
| `RemoveEggCounterFromExileAndReturnEffect` | `(UUID cardId)` | triggered ability effect: "remove an egg counter from [exiled card]. Then if it has no egg counters, return it to the battlefield." Pushed onto stack by StepTriggerService during owner's upkeep. Resolved by ExileEggCounterResolutionService. Used by Darigaaz Reincarnated |
| `CantBeCounteredEffect` | `()`; `(Condition condition)` | this spell can't be countered (static). Replaces `setCantBeCountered(true)`. A non-null `condition` makes it conditional, evaluated against the spell's stack entry by `GameQueryService.isUncounterable` — Banefire's "If X is 5 or more" uses `new SpellXAtLeast(5)` |
| `MakeTargetSpellUncounterableEffect` | `()` | "Target spell can't be countered." Spec `SPELL_ON_STACK`, so an activated ability with it (no target filter needed) targets any spell on the stack. On resolution marks the target spell's card id in `GameData.spellsMadeUncounterable`, which `GameQueryService.isUncounterable` reads. Used by Vexing Shusher's `{R/G}` ability |
| `CreatureSpellsCantBeCounteredEffect` | `()` | creature spells can't be countered (static) |
| `ControllerCreatureSpellsCantBeCounteredEffect` | `(int minimumPower)` | "Creature spells you control with power N or greater can't be countered" (static, Spellbreaker Behemoth). Read by `GameQueryService.isUncounterable`: protects a creature spell only if its stack-entry controller controls a permanent with this effect and the spell's power ≥ `minimumPower`. Unlike `CreatureSpellsCantBeCounteredEffect`, restricted to the controller and by power |
| `CreatureEnteringDontCauseTriggersEffect` | `()` | creatures entering don't cause abilities to trigger (static, e.g. Torpor Orb) |
| `ETBDoubleTriggerEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate)` | if a creature matching the predicate you control entering causes a triggered ability of a permanent you control to trigger, that ability triggers an additional time (static, e.g. Naban with `CardSubtypePredicate(WIZARD)`). Each copy adds one extra trigger. |
| `CreaturesEnterAsCopyOfSourceEffect` | `()` | creatures you control enter as a copy of this creature (static replacement effect, e.g. Essence of the Wild). Handled in BattlefieldEntryService.putPermanentOntoBattlefield() |

## Bounce / return to hand

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `ReturnToHandEffect` | **static factories only** (private ctor) | bounce permanents to owners' hands over `BounceScope{TARGET, SELF, ALL_MATCHING, TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS, TARGET_PLAYERS_OWNED}`. Factories: `target()` (bounce the chosen target); `targetAndControllerLosesLife(int)` (Vapor Snag — controller, snapshotted before the bounce, loses N); `targetAndControllerDraws(int)` (Call to Heel — controller, snapshotted before the bounce, draws N); `self()` (bounce the source); `allPermanentsMatching(PermanentPredicate filter)` (every permanent matching `filter` across all battlefields, null = every permanent — Evacuation uses `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate`); `permanentsTargetPlayerControls(filter)` (River's Rebuke — the target player's matching permanents; makes the spec player-targeting); `permanentsTargetPlayerOwns(filter)` (Hurkyl's Recall — the target player's owned matching permanents, any controller; makes the spec player-targeting) |
| `ReturnTargetPermanentToHandWithManaValueConditionalEffect` | `(int maxManaValue, CardEffect conditionalEffect)` | return target permanent to owner's hand; if its mana value was ≤ `maxManaValue`, resolve the bonus effect (e.g. `new ScryEffect(2)` for Perilous Voyage) |
| `ReturnTargetPermanentToHandOrLibraryTopByPredicateEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate libraryTopCondition)` | return target permanent to owner's hand, but if it matches `libraryTopCondition`, put it on top of its owner's library **instead** (destination replacement, not additive). Consign to Dream uses `PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(RED, GREEN))` |
| `ReturnLandControlledByPlayerToHandEffect` | `()` | a player returns a land they control to its owner's hand. The acting player is the entry's `targetId` if set, else the resolving controller. Spell-cast trigger collector (`ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL`) stamps the casting player onto `targetId` (Mana Breach); wrap in `MayEffect` on a controller ability for "you may return a land you control" (Kefnet the Mindful). Resolver collects that player's lands and prompts via the shared `BounceCreature` choice context (no lands ⇒ nothing) |
| `ReturnSelfToHandOnCoinFlipLossEffect` | `()` | return self to hand if coin flip is lost |
| `ReturnPermanentsOnCombatDamageToPlayerEffect` | `()` or `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | return permanents when combat damage dealt to player (Ninja-style). Optional filter restricts which permanents can be chosen (e.g. `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` for creatures only) |
| `BouncePermanentOnUpkeepEffect` | `(Scope scope, Set<TargetFilter> filters, String prompt)` | at upkeep, the choosing player returns a permanent they control matching `filters` to hand. Permanent type comes entirely from `filters` (supply a type predicate — empty matches everything): `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` (Sunken Hope), creature+green (Stampeding Wildebeests), `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate` (Esperzoa). Scope: `SOURCE_CONTROLLER`, `TRIGGER_TARGET_PLAYER` |
| `SacrificeEnchantedCreatureAndCreateTokenEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenEffect)` | sacrifice the enchanted creature, then create a token for the aura's controller (compound upkeep effect, e.g. Parasitic Implant) |
| `SacrificeEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | sacrifice the enchanted creature without additional effects. Use with `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` for "at the beginning of your upkeep, sacrifice this creature" (e.g. Necrotic Plague) |
| `ExileEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | exile the creature the source Aura is attached to (exile variant of `SacrificeEnchantedCreatureEffect`; resolves via the stack entry's `sourcePermanentId`). Use in an Aura's activated ability, e.g. Weight of Conscience "...: Exile enchanted creature." |
| `SacrificeEnchantedCreatureOnLeaveEffect` | `()` | "When this Aura leaves the battlefield, that creature's controller sacrifices it." Use in `ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` on a reanimation Aura (Animate Dead). The enchanted creature's permanent id is baked in at trigger time (captured before the Aura is gone), so it works even though `sourcePermanentId` no longer resolves. Pairs with the reanimation-Aura resolution described in ORACLE_TEXT_EFFECT_MAP.md |
| `EnchantedControllerSacrificesCreatureOnLeaveEffect` | `()` | "When enchanted creature leaves the battlefield, its controller sacrifices a creature of their choice." Use in `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` on an Aura (Funeral March). The leaving creature's controller — **not** the Aura controller (they differ when enchanting an opponent's creature) — is baked in at trigger time and routes through the single-select sacrifice-a-creature primitive at resolution |
| `ReturnSourceAuraToOpponentCreatureOnDeathEffect` | `()` / `(UUID enchantedCreatureControllerId)` | when enchanted creature dies, return this aura from owner's graveyard to battlefield attached to a creature controlled by an opponent of the dying creature's controller. UUID is baked in at trigger time. Use with `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD` (e.g. Necrotic Plague) |
| `EnchantedPermanentLeavesConditionalEffect` | `(CardPredicate permanentFilter, List<CardEffect> resolvedEffects)` | when enchanted permanent leaves the battlefield (any zone: graveyard, exile, hand, library), if the leaving permanent matches the filter (null = always), put resolvedEffects on the stack. Use with `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` slot. Broader than `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD` — fires on bounce, exile, tuck too (e.g. Curator's Ward with CardIsHistoricPredicate) |
| `ReturnEnchantedCreatureToOwnerHandOnDeathEffect` | `()` / `(UUID dyingCreatureCardId)` | when enchanted creature dies, return that creature card from graveyard to its owner's hand. UUID is baked in at trigger time. Use with `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD` (e.g. Demonic Vigor) |
| `ReturnEnchantedCreatureToBattlefieldUnderOwnersControlOnDeathEffect` | `()` / `(UUID dyingCreatureCardId)` | when enchanted creature dies, return that creature card from graveyard to the **battlefield** under its owner's control (contrast the hand variant above). UUID is baked in at trigger time. Use with `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD` (e.g. Abduction) |
| `ReturnSourceAuraToSharedTypeCreatureOnDeathEffect` | `()` / `(UUID dyingCreatureCardId)` | when enchanted creature dies, you may return this aura from owner's graveyard to battlefield attached to a creature that shares a creature type with the dying creature (Changeling-aware, reads the dying creature's types from the graveyard as last-known info). Dying creature ID is baked in at trigger time; the collector auto-wraps it in a `MayEffect` for the optional "you may". Use with `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD` (e.g. Reins of the Vinesteed) |
| `ReturnDamageSourcePermanentToHandEffect` | `()` | whenever a permanent deals damage to controller, return it to owner's hand (Dissipation Field-style). Use with `ON_ANY_PERMANENT_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_YOU` slot |
| `DamageSourceControllerGainsControlOfThisPermanentEffect` | `(boolean combatOnly, boolean creatureOnly)` | whenever a permanent deals damage to controller, the damage source's controller gains control of this permanent (Contested War Zone-style). Use with `ON_ANY_PERMANENT_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_YOU` slot. `combatOnly=true` restricts to combat damage only; `creatureOnly=true` restricts to creature damage sources only |
| `DestroyDamageSourcePermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | whenever a permanent deals damage to controller, destroy the damage source if it matches the filter (Mikaeus, the Unhallowed-style). Use with `ON_ANY_PERMANENT_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_YOU` slot |
| `ReflectAllyDamageToDamagedCreatureControllerEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate sourceFilter)` | marker for `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_CREATURE`: whenever a creature you control matching `sourceFilter` deals damage (combat or non-combat) to a creature, that creature deals that much damage to the damaged creature's controller. The collector translates each match into a `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(damage, TARGET_PLAYER)` dealt by the damage-source creature (works even if it died), so the marker itself is never resolved (Greatbow Doyen) |
| `DamageDamagedCreatureControllerAndSelfEffect` | `(int amountToDamagedCreatureController, int amountToSelf)` | marker for `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_CREATURE`, self-scoped: whenever *this* creature deals damage (combat or non-combat) to a creature, it deals N damage to that creature's controller and M damage to you. Fires only when the watcher is itself the damage source. The collector expands each match into `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(N, TARGET_PLAYER)` + `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(M, CONTROLLER)` on one stack entry, so the marker itself is never resolved (Bellowing Fiend) |
| `ReflectSourceDamageToItsControllerEffect` | `(CardColor color)` | global marker for `ON_ANY_SOURCE_DEALS_DAMAGE`: whenever any source (creature or spell) of `color` deals damage to anything, this permanent deals that much damage to that source's controller (Justice, `CardColor.RED`). All damage a single source deals simultaneously is summed into one reflection (CR ruling) — combat batches per source via `state.combatDamageDealt`; non-combat accumulates in `GameData.pendingSourceDamageForReflection` during a resolution and flushes in `EffectResolutionService`. The collector translates each match into a `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(total, TARGET_PLAYER)` dealt by the watcher, so the marker itself is never resolved |
| `PutTargetOnBottomOfLibraryEffect` | `()` | put target permanent on bottom of owner's library |
| `PutTargetOnTopOfLibraryEffect` | `()` | put target permanent on top of owner's library |
| `PutControlledCreatureOnTopOfLibraryEffect` | `()` | "put a creature you control on top of its owner's library" (Nulltread Gargantuan ETB). **Non-targeted** — resolved as a mandatory choice at resolution time (no card `target(...)` filter, `targetSpec()` stays `NONE`). The source is a legal choice, and forced when it's the only creature you control. Resolves automatically when there is one candidate; otherwise prompts `PermanentChoiceContext.PutControlledCreatureOnTopOfLibrary` (completed in `PermanentChoiceBattlefieldHandlerService`). Contrast `PutTargetOnTopOfLibraryEffect` (a real cast-time target) |
| `PutTargetPermanentIntoLibraryNFromTopEffect` | `(int position)` | put target permanent into its owner's library at position N from the top (0-indexed: 0=top, 1=second, 2=third). Used by Teferi, Hero of Dominaria -3 (position=2 for "third from top") |
| `PutSourceCardFromGraveyardIntoLibraryNFromTopEffect` | `(int position)` | death trigger: put the dying source card from its owner's graveyard into its owner's library at position N from the top (0-indexed: 0=top, 1=second, 2=third; clamped to bottom if the library is shorter). Graveyard-source analogue of `PutTargetPermanentIntoLibraryNFromTopEffect`. Used by Undying Beast (`position=0`) and Enigma Sphinx (`position=2`, "third from the top") |
| `ExileSourceCardFromGraveyardEffect` | `()` | death trigger: exile the dying source card from its owner's graveyard ("When this creature dies, exile it."). Exile analogue of `PutSourceCardFromGraveyardIntoLibraryNFromTopEffect` / `ReturnSourceCardFromGraveyardToOwnerHandEffect`. Used by Cyclopean Mummy (`ON_DEATH`) |

## Graveyard return

### Unified effect: `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect`

All graveyard-to-hand and graveyard-to-battlefield return effects are handled by a single unified record.

**Builder pattern:**
```
ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder()
    .destination(GraveyardChoiceDestination)   // HAND, BATTLEFIELD, or TOP_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY (required)
    .filter(CardPredicate)                     // which cards qualify (default: null = any)
    .source(GraveyardSearchScope)              // default: CONTROLLERS_GRAVEYARD — omit unless ALL_GRAVEYARDS or OPPONENT_GRAVEYARD
    .targetGraveyard(boolean)                  // true = player chooses whose graveyard to search at cast time (default: false)
    .returnAll(boolean)                        // true = return all matching cards, false = choose one (default: false)
    .thisTurnOnly(boolean)                     // true = only CREATURE cards put there from battlefield this turn (default: false)
    .fromBattlefieldThisTurn(boolean)          // true = ALL cards (any type) put there from battlefield this turn (default: false; Twilight Shepherd)
    .fromAnywhereThisTurn(boolean)             // true = only cards put there from any zone this turn (default: false)
    .discardedOrCycledThisTurn(boolean)        // true = only cards the controller cycled or discarded this turn (default: false; Shadow of the Grave)
    .attachmentTarget(PermanentPredicate)      // non-null = aura attaches to matching permanent on ETB (default: null)
    .gainLifeEqualToManaValue(boolean)         // true = controller gains life equal to returned card's mana value (default: false)
    .attachToSource(boolean)                   // true = auto-attach returned equipment to the source permanent (default: false)
    .grantHaste(boolean)                       // true = grant haste to the returned permanent (default: false)
    .exileAtEndStep(boolean)                   // true = exile at next end step (default: false)
    .requiresManaValueEqualsX(boolean)         // true = restrict to cards with MV = X (default: false)
    .maxManaValueEqualsLifeGainedThisTurn(boolean) // true = restrict to cards with MV <= life gained this turn (default: false); e.g. Moseo
    .grantColor(CardColor)                     // non-null = permanently grant this color "in addition to" (default: null)
    .grantSubtype(CardSubtype)                 // non-null = permanently grant this subtype "in addition to" (default: null)
    .enterTapped(boolean)                      // true = enters the battlefield tapped (default: false)
    .underOwnersControl(boolean)               // true = put each card onto battlefield under its owner's control (default: false)
    .returnAtRandom(boolean)                   // true = return a random matching card instead of player choice (default: false)
    .choosePermanentType(boolean)              // true = prompt controller to choose a permanent type at resolution, then return all matching (default: false); implies returnAll
    .exileSourceFromGraveyard(boolean)         // true = exile the source card from graveyard before selecting random cards (default: false); e.g. Moldgraf Monstrosity
    .grantSourceHasteIfSubtype(CardSubtype)    // non-null = source permanent gains haste until end of turn if the returned card has this subtype (default: null); HAND search-and-choose only; e.g. Warren Pilferers (Goblin)
    .greatestPower(boolean)                    // true = restrict the (mandatory) controller's-graveyard search-and-choose to the matching card(s) with greatest power; single card auto-forced, ties chosen and cannot be declined (default: false); e.g. Desecrator Hag
    .build()
```

Only `destination` is required. All booleans default to `false`, all object references default to `null`, and `source` defaults to `CONTROLLERS_GRAVEYARD`. Only set fields that differ from defaults.

**CardPredicate filter system** (in `model/filter/`):

| Predicate | Constructor | Matches |
|-----------|-------------|---------|
| `CardTypePredicate` | `(CardType cardType)` | cards of a given type (CREATURE, ARTIFACT, etc.) |
| `CardSubtypePredicate` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | cards of a given subtype (ZOMBIE, GOBLIN, etc.) |
| `CardKeywordPredicate` | `(Keyword keyword)` | cards with a given keyword (INFECT, FLYING, etc.) |
| `CardIsSelfPredicate` | `()` | only the source card itself (Squee-style self-return) |
| `CardIsAuraPredicate` | `()` | aura cards |
| `CardIsPermanentPredicate` | `()` | permanent cards (creature, artifact, enchantment, planeswalker, land, kindred — not instant/sorcery) |
| `CardMaxManaValuePredicate` | `(int maxManaValue)` | cards with mana value ≤ maxManaValue |
| `CardMinManaValuePredicate` | `(int minManaValue)` | cards with mana value ≥ minManaValue |
| `CardSupertypePredicate` | `(CardSupertype supertype)` | cards with a given supertype (BASIC, LEGENDARY) |
| `CardColorPredicate` | `(CardColor color)` | cards that ARE the colour — the colour is present among `getColors()` (multicolour-aware per CR 105.2c; a Black-Green card matches both `CardColorPredicate(BLACK)` and `CardColorPredicate(GREEN)`, order-independent). Used by "whenever a {colour} spell is cast" triggers and colour-filtered searches (Green Sun's Zenith) |
| `CardNotPredicate` | `(CardPredicate predicate)` | NOT — inverts a predicate |
| `CardAllOfPredicate` | `(List<CardPredicate> predicates)` | AND — all predicates must match |
| `CardAnyOfPredicate` | `(List<CardPredicate> predicates)` | OR — any predicate matches |

Pass `null` as filter to allow any card.

**GraveyardSearchScope enum** (in `model/`):

| Value | Meaning |
|-------|---------|
| `CONTROLLERS_GRAVEYARD` | search only the controller's graveyard (default) |
| `ALL_GRAVEYARDS` | search any player's graveyard |
| `OPPONENT_GRAVEYARD` | search only opponent's graveyard |

**GraveyardChoiceDestination enum** (in `model/`):

| Value | Meaning |
|-------|---------|
| `HAND` | return chosen card(s) to hand |
| `BATTLEFIELD` | put chosen card(s) onto battlefield |
| `TOP_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY` | put card on top of its owner's library (e.g. Noxious Revival) |
| `BOTTOM_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY` | put card on the bottom of its owner's library (e.g. Mistveil Plains) |

**Migration from old effects:**

| Old effect | New equivalent |
|------------|----------------|
| `ReturnCardFromGraveyardToHandEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).targetGraveyard(true).build()` |
| `ReturnCardFromGraveyardToHandEffect(CardType.CREATURE)` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).build()` |
| `ReturnCardOfSubtypeFromGraveyardToHandEffect(subtype)` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype)).build()` |
| `ReturnCardWithKeywordFromGraveyardToHandEffect(type, kw)` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardAllOfPredicate(List.of(new CardTypePredicate(type), new CardKeywordPredicate(kw)))).build()` |
| `ReturnSelfFromGraveyardToHandEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardIsSelfPredicate()).returnAll(true).build()` |
| `ReturnCreatureFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).build()` |
| `ReturnArtifactOrCreatureFromAnyGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardAnyOfPredicate(List.of(new CardTypePredicate(ARTIFACT), new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)))).source(ALL_GRAVEYARDS).build()` |
| `ReturnAuraFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardIsAuraPredicate()).attachmentTarget(attachmentTarget).build()` |
| `ReturnCreatureCardsPutIntoYourGraveyardFromBattlefieldThisTurnToHandEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).returnAll(true).thisTurnOnly(true).build()` |
| `ReturnCreatureCardsPutIntoYourGraveyardFromAnywhereThisTurnToHandEffect()` | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).returnAll(true).fromAnywhereThisTurn(true).build()` |

**Common usage examples:**

| Card | Usage |
|------|-------|
| Recollect | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).targetGraveyard(true).build()` — any card, targets graveyard |
| Gravedigger | `MayEffect(ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).build())` — creature to hand |
| Corpse Cur | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardAllOfPredicate(List.of(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), new CardKeywordPredicate(INFECT)))).build()` — creature with infect |
| Lord of the Undead | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardSubtypePredicate(ZOMBIE)).build()` — Zombie subtype |
| Doomed Necromancer | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).build()` — creature to battlefield |
| Beacon of Unrest | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardAnyOfPredicate(...)).source(ALL_GRAVEYARDS).build()` — artifact or creature from any graveyard |
| Nomad Mythmaker | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardIsAuraPredicate()).attachmentTarget(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate()).build()` — aura to battlefield attached to creature |
| Auriok Survivors | `MayEffect(ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardSubtypePredicate(EQUIPMENT)).attachToSource(true).build())` — equipment to battlefield attached to source |
| Squee, Goblin Nabob | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardIsSelfPredicate()).returnAll(true).build()` — self-return |
| No Rest for the Wicked | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).returnAll(true).thisTurnOnly(true).build()` — all creatures that died this turn |
| Twilight Shepherd | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).returnAll(true).fromBattlefieldThisTurn(true).build()` — ETB: all cards (any type) put into your graveyard from the battlefield this turn |
| Garna, the Bloodflame | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).returnAll(true).fromAnywhereThisTurn(true).build()` — all creature cards put into graveyard from anywhere this turn |
| Shadow of the Grave | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).returnAll(true).discardedOrCycledThisTurn(true).build()` — return all cards in your graveyard that you cycled or discarded this turn (cycling is a discard; tracked in the central discard hook `TriggerCollectionService.checkDiscardTriggers` via `GameData.cardsDiscardedOrCycledThisTurn`) |
| Razor Hippogriff | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(ARTIFACT)).gainLifeEqualToManaValue(true).build()` — artifact to hand + gain life equal to mana value |
| Noxious Revival | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(TOP_OF_OWNERS_LIBRARY).source(ALL_GRAVEYARDS).targetGraveyard(true).build()` — any card from any graveyard on top of owner's library |
| Postmortem Lunge | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).targetGraveyard(true).grantHaste(true).exileAtEndStep(true).requiresManaValueEqualsX(true).build()` — X-cost creature with MV=X from your graveyard to battlefield with haste; exile at next end step |
| Moseo, Vein's New Dean | `new ConditionalEffect(new GainedLifeThisTurn(), ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).targetGraveyard(true).maxManaValueEqualsLifeGainedThisTurn(true).build())` in `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` — end-step "if you gained life this turn, return up to one target creature card with MV X or less, X = life gained this turn". End-step graveyard targeting reuses the `SpellGraveyardTargetTrigger` flow |
| Rise from the Grave | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).source(ALL_GRAVEYARDS).grantColor(CardColor.BLACK).grantSubtype(CardSubtype.ZOMBIE).build()` — creature from any graveyard to battlefield as a black Zombie in addition to other colors/types |
| Reassembling Skeleton | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardIsSelfPredicate()).returnAll(true).enterTapped(true).build()` — self-return to battlefield tapped (graveyard activated ability) |
| Warcry Phoenix | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardIsSelfPredicate()).returnAll(true).enterTapped(true).enterAttacking(true).build()` — self-return to battlefield tapped and attacking (graveyard attack trigger) |
| Fatestitcher (Unearth) | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardIsSelfPredicate()).returnAll(true).grantHaste(true).exileAtEndStep(true).build()` — Unearth self-return with haste, exiled at next end step (graveyard activated ability with `SORCERY_SPEED` timing). `grantHaste`/`exileAtEndStep` are honored on the `returnAll` self-return path as well as the targeted path |
| Open the Vaults | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardAnyOfPredicate(List.of(new CardTypePredicate(ARTIFACT), new CardTypePredicate(ENCHANTMENT)))).source(ALL_GRAVEYARDS).returnAll(true).underOwnersControl(true).build()` — return all artifacts and enchantments from all graveyards under their owners' control |
| Charmbreaker Devils | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardAnyOfPredicate(List.of(new CardTypePredicate(INSTANT), new CardTypePredicate(SORCERY)))).returnAtRandom(true).build()` — return a random instant or sorcery from your graveyard to hand |
| Make a Wish | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).returnAtRandom(true).randomCount(2).build()` — return two cards at random from your graveyard to hand |
| Creeping Renaissance | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).returnAll(true).choosePermanentType(true).build()` — choose a permanent type, return all cards of that type from your graveyard to hand |
| Moldgraf Monstrosity | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(BATTLEFIELD).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).returnAtRandom(true).randomCount(2).exileSourceFromGraveyard(true).build()` — on death, exile self from graveyard then return two random creature cards to battlefield |
| Warren Pilferers | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).filter(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)).grantSourceHasteIfSubtype(CardSubtype.GOBLIN).build()` in `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` — return a creature card from your graveyard; if it's a Goblin card, this creature gains haste until end of turn |
| Vengeful Rebirth | `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect.builder().destination(HAND).targetGraveyard(true).build()` + `RecordReturnedGraveyardCardManaValueEffect()` + `target(AnyTargetPredicateTargetFilter(...)).addEffect(new DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(new EventValue(), false, false, 0))` + `ExileSpellEffect()` — return target graveyard card to hand, then deal its mana value as damage to any target if it was a returned nonland, then exile the spell. See `RecordReturnedGraveyardCardManaValueEffect` below |

### `RecordReturnedGraveyardCardManaValueEffect`

Vengeful Rebirth glue effect (`TargetSpec.NONE`). Sets the entry's event value to the mana value of the card on `entry.targetId` (a graveyard target, Yawgmoth's-Vile-Offering two-target shape: graveyard card on `targetId`/targetZone GRAVEYARD, any target on a `target(...)` group) **only when that nonland card was actually returned to the controller's hand** — the handler confirms the card is now in hand rather than reading its type in place, so a graveyard target that became illegal (exiled/removed in response, CR 608.2b) records 0 and deals no damage. A returned land also records 0.

Add it **UNBOUND**, right after the `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect`. `EffectResolutionService` remaps `entry.targetId` to a bound effect's target group for the duration of that effect (so `DestroyTargetPermanentEffect`-style bound effects read the group via `targetId`); leaving this effect unbound keeps `targetId` pointing at the graveyard card while it runs. Pair with a **bound** `DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect(new EventValue(), false, false, 0)` on the any-target group — binding is what makes the position accept player targets (`Card.doesPositionAllowPlayerTargets`) and lets the AI classify it as harmful damage. `0` event value = no damage (`dealDamageToPlayer` no-ops on `<= 0`).

### Other graveyard effects

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `ReturnOneOfEachSubtypeFromGraveyardToHandEffect` | `(List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` | return one card of each listed subtype from controller's graveyard to hand, processed sequentially. Single matches auto-return; multiple matches prompt choice. A multi-typed card can only satisfy one subtype. Used by Grim Captain's Call |
| `PutTargetCardsFromGraveyardOnTopOfLibraryEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | put any number of target cards matching filter from controller's graveyard on top of library. Multi-target selection at cast time via SpellCastingService "any number" graveyard targeting. Used by Frantic Salvage |
| `ReturnTargetCardsFromGraveyardToHandEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, int maxTargets)` | return up to maxTargets target cards matching filter from controller's graveyard to hand. Multi-target selection at cast time via SpellCastingService "up to N" graveyard targeting. Used by Morbid Plunder |
| `ShuffleTargetCardsFromGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, int maxTargets)` | target player shuffles up to maxTargets target cards matching filter from their graveyard into their library. player-targeting spec. Target player chosen at cast time, then graveyard card selection prompted via "up to N target player's graveyard" targeting. Used by Memory's Journey |
| `ShuffleCardFromControllerGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | "you may shuffle up to one card (matching `filter`, or any card when `null`) from your graveyard into your library". Non-targeted at cast time — it pauses at **resolution** and prompts the controller with a single-card `GraveyardChoice` over their own graveyard (destination `SHUFFLE_INTO_OWNERS_LIBRARY`), which they may decline. Does nothing if the controller has no matching cards. Because it declares no targeting flags it composes with an effect that targets a spell on the stack (like Discombobulate pairs a counter with a non-targeted extra). Used by Put Away (`CounterSpellEffect` + this) |
| `ReturnDyingCreatureToBattlefieldAndAttachSourceEffect` | `(UUID dyingCardId)` or `()` | return a dying nontoken creature to the battlefield and attach the source equipment to it. No-arg constructor (dyingCardId is null) used in card definition; dyingCardId populated at trigger time in GameHelper. Wrap in MayPayManaEffect for "you may pay {X}" triggers. Used by Nim Deathmantle |
| `ReturnDyingOpponentCreatureUnderYourControlEffect` | `(UUID dyingCardId)` or `()` | ON_OPPONENT_CREATURE_DIES only (Necroskitter): steal the dying creature card from its owner's graveyard onto your battlefield, tracked as a stolen creature (permanent control). No-arg in the card definition; the collector `DeathTriggerCollectorService#handleOpponentCreatureReturnUnderControl` bakes the concrete dying card id and wraps it in the "you may" — add the bare effect to the slot (typically inside `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(PermanentHasCountersPredicate(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE), …)`), not a MayEffect. Fizzles if the card left the graveyard |
| `PutCardFromOpponentGraveyardOntoBattlefieldEffect` | `(boolean tapped, CardPredicate filter, boolean requireManaValueEqualsX)` | put target card matching `filter` from an opponent's graveyard onto battlefield under your control (tapped if `tapped=true`); registered in `stolenCreatures` so it goes to its owner on leaving. When `requireManaValueEqualsX=true`, targeting is restricted to MV==X and that player mills X cards afterward. `(boolean tapped)`/`()` default to `filter`=artifact-or-creature and `requireManaValueEqualsX`=true (Geth). Ashen Powder: `(false, CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), false)` — creature only, any MV, no mill |
| `PutCreatureFromOpponentGraveyardOntoBattlefieldWithExileEffect` | `()` | put target creature card from opponent's graveyard onto battlefield under your control with haste; exile at beginning of next end step; if it would leave the battlefield, exile it instead. Works as `SPELL` (Gruesome Encore, target at cast time) or `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` (Puppeteer Clique — target chosen at trigger time via a multi-graveyard choice over opponents' creature cards; skips silently with no valid target) |
| `PutImprintedCreatureOntoBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | when this creature dies, reveal imprinted card; if creature, put onto battlefield (Clone Shell dies trigger) |
| `UndyingReturnEffect` | `()` | Undying (CR 702.93) resolution half: return the dying card from its owner's graveyard to the battlefield with a +1/+1 counter, flagged as entering from the graveyard. Pushed automatically by `PermanentRemovalService.collectUndyingTrigger` when a creature with `Keyword.UNDYING` dies with no +1/+1 counters — never add it to a card. The `UNDYING` keyword is loaded from Scryfall. Used by Flayer of the Hatebound |
| `PersistReturnEffect` | `()` | Persist (CR 702.79) resolution half: return the dying card from its owner's graveyard to the battlefield with a -1/-1 counter, flagged as entering from the graveyard. Pushed automatically by `PermanentRemovalService.collectPersistTrigger` when a creature with `Keyword.PERSIST` dies with no -1/-1 counters — never add it to a card. The `PERSIST` keyword is loaded from Scryfall. Used by Twilight Shepherd |
| `PutImprintedCardIntoOwnersHandEffect` | `()` | when this permanent dies, put the imprinted (exiled) card into its owner's hand (Hoarding Dragon dies trigger) |
| `PlayImprintedCardWithoutPayingManaCostEffect` | `()` | Hideaway "you may play the exiled card" activated ability (Howltooth Hollow). Turns the source permanent's imprinted (face-down exiled) card face up and offers a may-play via a PendingMayAbility; a land is put onto the battlefield and counts as the land play for the turn (per the hideaway ruling), any other card is cast from exile without paying. Routed by `MayCastHandlerService.handlePlayImprintedCardChoice`. Wrap in `ConditionalEffect(<play condition>, ...)` for the card's gate (e.g. `NoPlayerHasCardsInHand`). Pair with `ImprintFromTopCardsEffect(N)` on ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD |

## Draw / discard / hand manipulation

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `DrawCardEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | controller draws that many cards, one at a time (draw-replacement effects and "whenever you draw" triggers see each draw). Convenience ctors: `(int amount)`, `()` = 1. Covers "draw X cards" (`XValue`), "draw a card for each creature you control" (`PermanentCount`), "for each creature card in your graveyard" (`CardsInGraveyard`), "for each charge counter on [source]" (`CountersOnSource` — evaluates the live source, falling back to `sourcePermanentSnapshot` when sacrificed as a cost, e.g. Culling Dais) |
| `EachPlayerDrawsCardEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` / `(int amount)` | each player (turn order) draws that many cards; the amount is re-evaluated with each drawing player as the controller context, so player-relative amounts (`CardsInGraveyard(..., CONTROLLER)` = each player's own graveyard, Nature's Resurgence) count that player's objects. `XValue()` for "each player draws X" (Prosperity) |
| `EachPlayerMayDrawUpToNGainLifePerCardBelowEffect` | `(int maxDraw, int lifePerCardBelow)` | each player, in APNAP order (active player first), may draw up to `maxDraw` cards; each draws their chosen amount then gains `lifePerCardBelow` life per card fewer than `maxDraw` drawn. Sequential per-player `XValueChoice` interactions; APNAP remainder rides `GameData.pendingEachPlayerDrawUpToQueue`. Used by Temporary Truce (2, 2) |
| `DrawCardForTargetPlayerEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount, boolean requireSourceUntapped, boolean targetsPlayer)` | the player in the entry's targetId draws that many cards ("target player draws X" = `XValue`, e.g. Blue Sun's Zenith); optionally requires source untapped (intervening-if); when `targetsPlayer=true`, auto-derives player targeting for activated abilities. Convenience ctors: `(int amount)` = `(Fixed, false, false)`, `(int amount, boolean requireSourceUntapped)` |
| `DrawAndLoseLifePerSubtypeEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | draw cards and lose life for each permanent of subtype you control |
| `DefendingPlayerMayDrawCardEffect` | `()` | ON_ATTACK marker (Sibilant Spirit): whenever this creature attacks, the defending player may draw a card. `CombatAttackService` derives the defending player from the attacker's attack target (the attacked player, or the controller of the attacked planeswalker) and queues a `MayEffect(DrawCardEffect())` for that player instead of the attacking creature's controller. Consumed at trigger time; never reaches `resolveStackEntry` |
| `DyingCreatureControllerMayDrawCardEffect` | `()` | ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES marker (Fecundity): whenever any creature dies, the dying creature's controller may draw a card. Its collector routes the optional draw (`MayEffect(DrawCardEffect())`) to `dyingCreatureControllerId` — who may be an opponent of the source's controller — instead of the source's controller like the generic `MayEffect` handler. Consumed at trigger time; never reaches `resolveStackEntry` |
| `DyingCreatureControllerDiscardsCardEffect` | `()` | ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES marker (Bereavement): whenever a qualifying creature dies, its controller discards a card. Its collector stacks a mandatory `DiscardEffect(1, CONTROLLER)` under `dyingCreatureControllerId` (may be an opponent of the source's controller). Wrap in `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(<CardPredicate>, …)` to restrict which creatures qualify (Bereavement uses `CardColorPredicate(GREEN)`). Consumed at trigger time; never reaches `resolveStackEntry` |
| _compose, no dedicated effect_ | `DrawCardEffect(N)` + `DiscardEffect(M, DiscardRecipient.CONTROLLER)` | Loot ("draw N, then discard M"). Flat pair on a spell/ability effect list (they share one stack entry, so the draw resolves strictly before the discard). On a single-effect wrapper or a trigger slot, bundle as `SequenceEffect.of(new DrawCardEffect(N), new DiscardEffect(M, DiscardRecipient.CONTROLLER))` — e.g. `MayEffect(SequenceEffect.of(...), prompt)` for "you may draw a card. If you do, discard a card." (Stadium Tidalmage, Daring Saboteur, Murder of Crows, Marauding/Shipwreck Looter, Faithless Looting, Catalog, Jalum Tome, Jace Cunning Castaway's +1). NOT the same as rummage (`DiscardAndDrawCardEffect`), whose draw is contingent on an actual discard |
| `DrawAndRandomDiscardWithSharedTypeCountersEffect` | `(int drawAmount, int discardAmount, int counterAmount)` | draw N cards, then discard M at random. If the discarded cards share at least one card type, put counterAmount +1/+1 counters on the source permanent. Used by Rowdy Crew (draw 3, discard 2, 2 counters) |
| `DiscardAndDrawCardEffect` | `(int discardAmount, int drawAmount)` | discard N cards then draw N cards (rummage). Convenience ctor: `()` defaults to `(1, 1)`. Commonly wrapped in MayEffect for "you may discard a card. If you do, draw a card." Uses `DiscardFollowUp.rummage` carried on the discard choice to draw after the interactive discard completes. |
| `DrawCardRevealDiscardUnlessLandEffect` | `()` | controller draws a card and reveals it (public log); if the drawn card isn't a `LAND`, it is discarded (`discardCausedByOpponent = false`; fires discard triggers via `checkDiscardTriggers`). Card-filtering — only land cards are kept. The freshly drawn card is the last card appended to hand, so nothing is discarded if the draw produced no card (empty library / draw-replacement interaction). `CardDrawingEffect` (drawnCardAmount = 1). Resolved by `DrawCardRevealDiscardUnlessLandEffectHandler` → `PlayerInteractionSupport.applyDrawRevealDiscardUnlessLand`. Used by Sindbad (`{T}:`) |
| `DiscardCardAndUntapSelfEffect` | `()` | discard a card, then untap the source permanent. Commonly wrapped in MayEffect for "you may discard a card. If you do, untap [source]." Uses `DiscardFollowUp.untap` carried on the discard choice to untap after the interactive discard completes. Used by Elaborate Firecannon |
| `DiscardCardUnlessAttackedThisTurnEffect` | `()` | discard a card unless the controller declared at least one attacker this turn (raid-style check via `playersDeclaredAttackersThisTurn`). If the controller attacked, the discard is skipped entirely. Used by Chart a Course. |
| `DiscardUnlessExileCardFromGraveyardEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate)` | discard a card unless you exile a card matching predicate from your graveyard. If no matching cards exist, discard is mandatory. Uses may-ability prompt to let controller choose. |
| `DiscardUnlessReturnLandToHandEffect` | `()` | discard a card unless you return a land you control to its owner's hand. If you control no lands, the discard is mandatory. May-ability prompt: accept returns a chosen land (shared `BounceCreature` context), decline discards. Return-a-land counterpart of `DiscardUnlessExileCardFromGraveyardEffect`. Pair with a leading `DrawCardEffect` (Tragic Lesson). |
| `DrawCardsEqualToLifeGainedEffect` | `()` | triggered: draw cards equal to life gained. Slot: `ON_CONTROLLER_GAINS_LIFE`. Amount from trigger context |
| `PayXLifeDrawXCardsEffect` | `()` | SPELL: resolution-time X choice — controller picks X (capped at current life, since you can't pay more life than you have), pays X life, then draws X cards. Prompts via `PendingInteraction.XValueChoice` and re-runs reading `gameData.chosenXValue` (like `PayXManaGainXLifeEffect`). Necrologia's "as an additional cost to cast, pay X life / draw X cards"; pair with `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(YOUR_END_STEP)` |
| `DiscardEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount, DiscardRecipient recipient, boolean random)` | the whole discard family. `recipient` routes who discards — `CONTROLLER` (self / rummaging, `discardCausedByOpponent=false`), `TARGET_PLAYER` (targets a player via `entry.getTargetId()`, `discardCausedByOpponent=true`), `TARGET_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER` (the controller of the targeted *permanent* discards — `entry.getTargetId()` is a permanent, no own target added, `discardCausedByOpponent=true`; run before any accompanying destroy so the permanent is still on the battlefield — Gloomlance), `EACH_PLAYER` (all players, APNAP), `EACH_OPPONENT` (opponents only, APNAP). `random=true` discards at random, `false` lets the discarding player choose. Convenience ctors: `(int, recipient, random)`, `(DynamicAmount, recipient)` and `(int, recipient)` (both non-random). Single-player recipients evaluate the amount and log "discards 0 cards" when it is ≤0; chosen each-player discards ride a `DiscardFollowUp` queue (sequential picks) while random each-player discards run inline. Use `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)` for "a card for each charge counter" (Shrine of Limitless Power), `XValue()` for Mind Shatter |
| `DiscardHandEffect` | `(DiscardRecipient)` / `()` | discard entire hand(s) — no count or player choice, every card goes straight to graveyard, firing discard triggers per card. `recipient` routes who discards; no-arg = `CONTROLLER`. Each-player recipients iterate in APNAP order. Used by The Flame of Keld (Chapter I, `CONTROLLER`) and Mindslicer (`EACH_PLAYER`) |
| `DiscardOwnHandThenDrawThatManyEffect` | `()` | discard controller's entire hand, then draw that many cards. All discards are automatic (no player choice). Fires discard triggers for each card. Used by Shattered Perception |
| `DiscardOwnHandThenEachOpponentSacrificesCreaturePerCardEffect` | `()` | discard controller's entire hand, then each opponent sacrifices a creature of their choice for each card discarded this way (sacrifice count = cards discarded, snapshotted before the discard). Delegates to `DiscardHandEffectHandler` + `SacrificePermanentsEffectHandler` (EACH_OPPONENT, creature filter wrapped in `PermanentAllOfPredicate` so the multi-permanent choice honours the count instead of forcing exactly one). Empty hand ⇒ no discard, no sacrifice. Used by Malfegor (ETB) |
| `TargetPlayerDiscardsThenDrawsThatManyEffect` | `(int amount)` | target player discards `amount` cards (mandatory, player-chosen), then draws as many as they discarded this way. Draw count is snapshotted as `min(amount, hand size)` before the discard and drawn to the target via a rummage `DiscardFollowUp`, so a target holding fewer than `amount` cards discards their whole hand and draws only that many. player-targeting spec; empty hand ⇒ discards and draws 0. Used by Forget |
| `DiscardOwnHandThenDrawEqualToTargetPlayerHandSizeEffect` | `()` | discard controller's entire hand, then draw cards equal to target player's hand size (counted at draw time). Targets player. Used by Borrowed Knowledge (modal mode 0) |
| `DiscardOwnHandThenDrawEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | discard controller's entire hand, then draw cards equal to `amount` (evaluated at draw time, independent of how many were discarded). All discards automatic; fires discard triggers per card. the spec targets a player only for target-relative amounts (currently `DamageDealtToTargetPlayerThisTurn`). Used by Knollspine Dragon (`MayEffect`-wrapped ETB, draws = damage dealt to target opponent this turn) |
| `EachPlayerDiscardsHandThenDrawsThatManyEffect` | `()` | in APNAP order, each player discards their entire hand then draws that many cards (own discard count). All discards automatic; fires discard triggers. Used by Incendiary Command (modal mode) |
| `EachPlayerDiscardsAnyNumberThenDrawsThatManyEffect` | `()` | in APNAP order, each player chooses how many cards to discard (X-value choice, 0..hand size), discards exactly that many (own selection), then draws that many, before the next player. Driven one player at a time via `GameData.eachPlayerRummage`; re-runs on each X-value choice and (via `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction`) on each discard completion. Used by Flux (pair with a trailing `DrawCardEffect(1)` for "Draw a card") |
| `EachPlayerMayDiscardUpToThenTakeDamageEffect` | `(int amount)` | in APNAP order, each player may discard up to `amount` cards (X-value choice, 0..min(amount, hand size)), discards exactly that many (own selection), then is dealt `amount - discarded` damage, before the next player. Empty/zero-discard players take the full `amount`. Reuses `GameData.eachPlayerRummage`; re-runs on each X-value choice and (via `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction`) on each discard completion. Used by Mind Bomb (`amount` = 3) |
| `EachPlayerCreatesTokenEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect token)` | each player (turn order) creates the wrapped `token` under their own control. The token's `amount` (a `DynamicAmount`) is re-evaluated relative to each creating player, so a `CountScope.CONTROLLER` count reads that player's own board. Used by Waiting in the Weeds (a 1/1 green Cat per untapped Forest they control) |
| `EachPlayerPaysAnyLifeForTokensEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect token)` | starting with the controller, each player may pay any amount of life (X-value choice, 0..their current life); repeats round-robin in turn order until a full round passes with no payment (per ruling, it doesn't end the first single decline); then each player creates one `token` (single-token template) per 1 life they paid. Life is paid immediately (via `LifeSupport.applyLifeLoss`). Driven one player at a time via `GameData.eachPlayerPayLife`; re-runs on each X-value choice. Used by Plague of Vermin |
| `DiscardUpToThenDrawThatManyEffect` | `(int maxDiscard)` / `(int maxDiscard, int extraDraw)` / `(ANY_NUMBER, int extraDraw)` | discard up to N (or any number with `ANY_NUMBER` sentinel), then draw that many cards plus `extraDraw`. Uses X value choice for count selection, then sequential discard interaction, then draws. Used by Jaya Ballard and Colossus of the Blood Age |
| `TargetPlayerDiscardsByConvergeEffect` | `()` | target player discards X cards where X = number of colors of mana spent to cast this spell (Converge; snapshotted into xValue at cast time) |
| `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count)` / `(int count)` | exile top `count` cards of controller's library; grants play permission (any type) until end of controller's next turn via `exileSupport.grantPlayUntilOwnersNextTurn`. `(int)` for a fixed impulse (Elemental Mascot); use `EventValue()` for "equal to the excess damage dealt this way" — pair after `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(new XValue())` on Converge spells (Archaic's Agony), where the damage handler stores the excess on the entry's `eventValue` |
| `TargetPlayerDiscardsReturnSelfIfCardTypeEffect` | `(int amount, CardType returnIfType)` | target player discards N cards; if a discarded card matches the type, return the source spell from graveyard to owner's hand (e.g. Psychic Miasma) |
| `DiscardThenReturnFromGraveyardToHandEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | controller discards `amount` cards (chosen), then returns a card from their own graveyard to hand for each card discarded this way — `min(amount, hand size)` sequential single-card graveyard picks queued once the interactive discard completes (via a `DiscardFollowUp.graveyardReturn` on the discard choice; resumed by `CardChoiceHandlerService.handleDiscardCardChosen`). Recall = `XValue()`; put a trailing `ExileSpellEffect()` on the same slot to exile the spell |
| `TargetPlayerRandomDiscardOrControllerDrawsEffect` | `()` | target player discards a card at random. If they can't (empty hand), the controller draws a card instead. Used by Urgoros, the Empty One. |
| `RevealHandAndRandomDiscardCardTypeEffect` | `(CardType cardType)` | target player reveals their whole hand, then discards one card of `cardType` at random (uniform among matching cards; nothing discarded if none match). player-targeting spec; pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter`. Sets `discardCausedByOpponent`, fires discard triggers. Used by Rag Man (CREATURE) |
| `ChooseCardsFromTargetHandEffect` | `(int count, List<CardType> excludedTypes, HandChoiceDestination destination)` / `(int count, List<CardType> excludedTypes, CardPredicate filter, HandChoiceDestination destination)` / `(…, List<CardType> includedTypes, HandChoiceDestination destination)` / `(…, includedTypes, destination, boolean returnOnSourceLeave)` / `(DynamicAmount count, List<CardType> excludedTypes, HandChoiceDestination destination)` | reveal target's hand, caster chooses N card(s), each goes to `destination` (`DISCARD` / `EXILE` / `TOP_OF_LIBRARY`). `count` is a `DynamicAmount`, so it takes a fixed int (convenience ctors) or an `XValue` (Mind Warp — "choose X cards"); the choice is capped to the hand and an evaluated count ≤ 0 does nothing. `includedTypes` (non-empty) restricts choices to those types, else `excludedTypes` can't be chosen. The optional `CardPredicate filter` (non-null) narrows choosable cards further — e.g. "nonlegendary" via `CardNotPredicate(CardSupertypePredicate(LEGENDARY))` (Lay Bare the Heart, layered on `excludedTypes=[LAND]`); applies to `DISCARD`/`EXILE` only. `DISCARD` fires discard triggers + sets `discardCausedByOpponent` (Duress, Distress, Divest, Despise, Entomber Exarch, Gruesome Discovery, Thrull Surgeon, Mind Warp). `EXILE` with `returnOnSourceLeave=true` returns exiled cards to hand when the source permanent leaves (Kitesail Freebooter; Night Terrors exiles permanently). `TOP_OF_LIBRARY` ignores the type filters, first chosen ends up on top (Agonizing Memories). |
| `RevealCardsChooseOneToDiscardEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate countFilter)` | target player reveals X cards **they choose** from their hand (X = number of the caster's permanents matching `countFilter`), then the caster picks one revealed card for the target to discard (opponent-caused; fires discard triggers). Two-phase interaction: `RevealCardsFromHandChoice` (target's reveal picks, skipped when hand ≤ X) → `ChooseRevealedCardToDiscardChoice` (caster's discard pick; only the revealed subset is shown, keeping the rest hidden). Thieving Sprite with `PermanentHasAnySubtypePredicate(FAERIE)`. Contrast `ChooseCardsFromTargetHandEffect`, which reveals the whole hand. |
| `LookAtHandEffect` | `()` | look at target player's hand |
| `LookAtHandChooseNonlandToBottomAndDrawEffect` | `()` | look at target player's hand; the caster **may** choose a nonland card (optional — the caster can decline even when a legal choice exists); if chosen, the target reveals it, puts it on the bottom of their library, then draws a card. player-targeting spec; pair with `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(ANY)`. Reuses the `RevealedHandChoice` interaction with its `bottomThenDrawMode`+`optional` flags (decline = `cardIndex == -1`). Used by Vendilion Clique (`ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`) |
| `RevealOpponentHandsEffect` | `()` | reveal all opponents' hands (to the controller only, e.g. Telepathy) |
| `PlayWithHandsRevealedEffect` | `()` | static marker: "Players play with their hands revealed." While any player controls one, every hand is visible to everyone (unlike `RevealOpponentHandsEffect`, which only reveals opponents' hands to the controller). Consumed by `GameBroadcastService.getRevealedOpponentHand`. Used by Zur's Weirding |
| `RevealTargetHandDrawPerMatchingCardEffect` | `(List<CardSubtype> subtypes, List<CardColor> colors)` | target opponent reveals their hand; caster draws one card for each card in it whose subtypes or colors intersect the filters (each card counted once). player-targeting spec; pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)`. Used by Baleful Stare (MOUNTAIN / RED) |
| `RevealHandChooseCreatureGainLifeDiscardEffect` | `(List<CardColor> colors)` | target opponent reveals their hand; caster chooses one creature card whose colors intersect `colors` (empty = any color), gains life equal to its toughness, then the target discards it (opponent-caused). player-targeting spec; pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)`. Reuses the `RevealedHandChoice` discard interaction with the `gainLifeToChooserEqualToChosenToughness` flag (applied in `CardChoiceHandlerService`). Used by Talara's Bane (GREEN / WHITE) |
| `DiscardAllCardsOfChosenColorEffect` | `()` | target player reveals their hand and discards every card of a color the caster chooses. player-targeting spec; pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(ANY)`. Pauses on resolution for the caster's color choice (`ChoiceContext.DiscardChosenColorChoice`), handled in `ChoiceHandlerService`; a card is "of that color" if its colors contain the chosen color (colorless/land cards never discarded). Fires per-card discard triggers. Used by Persecute |
| `RevealRandomCardFromTargetPlayerHandEffect` | `()` | target player reveals a card at random from their hand (e.g. Merfolk Spy combat damage trigger) |
| `RevealRandomCardFromTargetPlayerHandLoseLifeEqualToManaValueEffect` | `()` | target player reveals a card at random from their hand, then loses life equal to that card's mana value (`benign(PLAYER)`; empty hand = nothing revealed, no life lost). Life loss goes through `LifeSupport.applyLifeLoss` (fires loses-life triggers). Used by Singe-Mind Ogre (ETB) |
| `LookAtRandomCardInTargetPlayerHandEffect` | `()` | the controller privately looks at a card chosen at random from target player's hand (`benign(PLAYER)`; card shown only to controller, unlike the public `RevealRandomCardFromTargetPlayerHandEffect`). Used by Urza's Bauble |
| `ExileTargetPlayerHandEffect` | `()` | exile every card in target player's hand (whole hand, no choice, no play permission). Not a discard — no discard triggers fire; cards go straight from hand to that player's exile zone. `harmful(PLAYER)`; empty hand ⇒ nothing exiled. Resolved by `ExileTargetPlayerHandEffectHandler`. Identity Crisis pairs it with `ExileGraveyardCardsEffect(TARGET_PLAYER_ENTIRE)` on the same SPELL slot — both PLAYER specs collapse to one target |
| `TempestEfreetAnteExchangeEffect` | `(int lifeCost)` | ante punisher (`benign(PLAYER)`, "target opponent"): the targeted opponent may pay `lifeCost` life; if they don't (or can't), they reveal a card at random from their hand, that card goes to the ability controller's hand, and the source (Tempest Efreet, in the controller's graveyard after being sacrificed as a cost) goes to the opponent's graveyard. Payable opponents are prompted via the may-ability system (normalfx handler enqueues; accept/decline lives in `mayfx/TempestEfreetAnteExchangeHandler`); an unpayable opponent exchanges immediately. The oracle "exchange ownership … permanent" is an ante concept resolved as single-game zone movements only — no runtime `ownerId` change (frozen at setup). Used by Tempest Efreet |
| `BronzeTabletAnteExchangeEffect` | `(int lifeCost)` | ante trade (`harmful(PERMANENT)`, pair with a "nontoken permanent an opponent owns" `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter`): exiles both the source (Bronze Tablet) and the targeted permanent unconditionally, then the permanent's **owner** may pay `lifeCost` life; if they do, the source moves from exile to its owner's graveyard (the targeted permanent stays exiled); if they don't (or can't), the ante swap resolves and both cards remain exiled. Payable owners are prompted via the may-ability system (normalfx handler enqueues; accept/decline lives in `mayfx/BronzeTabletAnteExchangeHandler`); an unpayable owner swaps immediately. The oracle "that player owns this card and you own the other exiled card" is an ante concept resolved as single-game zone movements only — no runtime `ownerId` change (frozen at setup). Used by Bronze Tablet |
| `HeadGamesEffect` | `()` | exchange target player's hand with cards from your library (Head Games) |
| `RedirectDrawsEffect` | `()` | redirect opponent's draws to controller (static, e.g. Plagiarize-style) |
| `ShuffleHandIntoLibraryAndDrawEffect` | `()` | each player shuffles cards from their hand into their library, then draws that many cards (wheel effect) |
| `PutHandOnBottomOfLibraryAndDrawEffect` | `()` | the effect's target player puts the cards in their hand on the bottom of their library (order hidden, no prompt), then draws that many cards. Used by Teferi's Puzzle Box in the `EACH_DRAW_TRIGGERED` slot (targetId = the player whose draw step it is) |
| `SylvanLibraryDrawEffect` | `()` | the controller draws two additional cards, then must resolve `min(2, cards drawn this turn still in hand)` of those cards: for each, put it on top of the library or pay 4 life. Wrap in a `MayEffect` in `DRAW_TRIGGERED` (the "may draw two additional cards" gate). Reads per-card draw tracking `GameData.cardsDrawnThisTurnIds`; the resolve step is a single multi-select `PendingInteraction.SylvanLibraryChoice` (selected cards go on top, the rest of the resolved count cost 4 life each; a player who can't pay is forced to top a card instead). Sylvan Library |
| `DrawThenPutCardsFromHandOnTopOrBottomOfLibraryEffect` | `(int drawCount, int putCount[, boolean topOnly])` | controller draws `drawCount`, then multi-selects `putCount` cards from hand and puts them back on their library (first chosen ends nearest the top when placed on top). With `topOnly=false` (2-arg default) a single shared top/bottom pick applies to all chosen cards — Dream Cache `(3, 2)`; chains `PutCardsFromHandOnLibraryCardChoice` (reuses `ChooseMultipleCardsMessage`) → `PutCardsFromHandOnLibraryDestinationChoice` (reuses `ChooseFromListMessage` Top/Bottom). With `topOnly=true` the chosen cards go straight on top in the chosen order with no destination prompt — Brainstorm `(3, 2, true)` |
| `EachPlayerShufflesHandAndGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect` | `()` | each player shuffles their hand and graveyard into their library. Used by Timetwister-family cards (Time Reversal, Timetwister). Combine with EachPlayerDrawsCardEffect for the draw portion |
| `EachPlayerKeepsCardsShufflesRestIntoLibraryEffect` | `(int keepCount)` | each player (APNAP order, active player first) chooses up to `keepCount` cards in their hand to keep, then shuffles the rest into their library. Interactive: prompts one player at a time via `PendingInteraction.KeepCardsInHandChoice` (reuses `ChooseMultipleCardsMessage`); once every player has chosen, the spell's remaining effects resume. Players with an empty hand are skipped. Worldpurge (`keepCount=7`) |
| `EachPlayerLosesUnspentManaEffect` | `()` | each player's mana pool is emptied ("loses all unspent mana"). Worldpurge |

## Library manipulation

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `SacrificeCreatureSearchLibraryForCreatureToHandEffect` | `()` | sacrifice a creature (as effect, not cost); if you do, search library for a creature card, reveal it, put it into your hand, then shuffle. With 0 creatures nothing happens; with 1 auto-sacrifices; with 2+ prompts choice via `SacrificeCreatureThenSearchLibrary` context. Used by Garruk, the Veil-Cursed |
| `TargetPlayerSacrificesCreatureThenCreateTokensIfSubtypeEffect` | `(CardSubtype requiredSubtype, CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | targets a player (player-targeting spec); that player sacrifices a creature of their choice and, if it had `requiredSubtype` (last-known info, evaluated before removal so type-adding effects/changeling count), the same player creates the `tokenTemplate` tokens under their own control. With 0 target-player creatures nothing happens; with 1 auto-sacrifices; with 2+ prompts choice via `SacrificeCreatureCreateTokensIfSubtype` context. Encode "gains haste until end of turn" via the template's `grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn`. Used by Warren Weirding |
| `SearchLibraryEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count, CardPredicate filter, LibrarySearchDestination destination, ManaValueBound manaValueBound, int castFromGraveyardCount)`; convenience `()`, `(filter)`, `(filter, destination)`, `(count, filter, destination)`, `(filter, int count, int castFromGraveyardCount)`, `(filter, destination, manaValueBound)` | unified library search (collapsed the whole `SearchLibraryFor*` family). Find `count` cards matching `filter` (+ optional `ManaValueBound` mana-value constraint) and move them to `destination` (`HAND`/`BATTLEFIELD`/`BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED`/`TOP_OF_LIBRARY`), then shuffle. `filter == null` ⇒ unrestricted (any card; not revealed, can't fail to find — Diabolic Tutor); non-null filter or a bound ⇒ restricted (reveals for `HAND`/`TOP_OF_LIBRARY`, may fail to find; prompt/no-match text via `CardPredicateUtils.describeFilter()`). Flashback casts (`StackEntry.isCastWithFlashback()`) search `castFromGraveyardCount`. By-name search = `CardNamedPredicate` (Squadron Hawk). To-top = `TOP_OF_LIBRARY` (Liliana Vess, Brutalizer Exarch). Creature-to-battlefield with MV/colour/subtype via filter + `ManaValueBound` (Citanul Flute `(false,0)`, Birthing Pod `(true,1)`, Green Sun's Zenith `CardColorPredicate(GREEN)`, Myr Turbine subtype). `ManaValueBound(amount, exact, offset)` bounds MV ≤/= `amount + offset`; the `(exact, offset)` ctor uses X (`XValue`), other `DynamicAmount`s give board-derived bounds — Beseech the Queen bounds by `PermanentCount` of lands controlled (null filter, any card). Used by Diabolic Tutor `()`, Increasing Ambition `(null,1,2)`, land fetchers `(basicLand())`, Fabricate/Trinket Mage `(predicate)`, Rampant Growth/Primeval Titan `(count, filter, BATTLEFIELD_TAPPED)` |
| `SearchLibraryForCardToHandAndCardToGraveyardEffect` | `()` | search library for two cards (unrestricted): first to hand, second to graveyard, then shuffle. Uses pending flag for second pick. Used by Final Parting |
| `SearchLibraryAndOrGraveyardForNamedCardToHandEffect` | `(String cardName)` | search library and/or graveyard for a card with specified name, reveal it, put into hand. Checks graveyard first; if not found, searches library (with shuffle). Used by Chandra's Outburst |
| `SearchZonesForCardNamedToBattlefieldEffect` | `(String cardName)` | search the controller's graveyard, hand, and/or library for a card with the given name and put it onto the battlefield. Graveyard then hand matches are taken automatically; only the library search presents an interactive pick and shuffles ("If you search your library this way, shuffle"). Battlefield-destination sibling of `SearchLibraryAndOrGraveyardForNamedCardToHandEffect` that also checks the hand. Used by Gate to the Afterlife (God-Pharaoh's Gift) |
| `SearchLibraryForBasicLandsToBattlefieldTappedAndHandEffect` | `()` | search library for up to two basic lands: one to battlefield tapped, one to hand. Single search action (one Leonin Arbiter check). Used by Cultivate, Kodama's Reach |
| `SearchLibraryForOneCardOfEachColorToHandEffect` | `()` | search library for one white, one blue, one black, one red, and one green card (five different cards, WUBRG order). Each colour is a separate revealed pick to HAND (may fail to find); a colour with no matching card left in the library is skipped without prompting. Runs through the shared `LibrarySearchFollowUp.colorToHandPicks` colour queue (`LibrarySearchSupport.startNextColorToHandPick`), shuffling the library once after the last colour. Used by Conflux |
| `SearchLibraryForCardTypeToExileAndImprintEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | search library for card of specific types, exile it, and imprint on source permanent |
| `SearchLibraryForSubtypeToBattlefieldAttachedToTargetPlayerEffect` | `(CardSubtype requiredSubtype)` | search library for card with specified subtype and put it onto the battlefield attached to target player. player-targeting spec. Used for Curse search (e.g. Bitterheart Witch) |
| `SearchLibraryForCurseToBattlefieldAttachedToEnchantedPlayerEffect` | `()` | search library for a Curse card whose name differs from every Curse already attached to the source aura's enchanted player, put it onto the battlefield attached to that player, then shuffle. Enchanted player is read from the source permanent's `attachedTo` at resolution time (no target chosen). Pair with `MayEffect` in `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED`. Used by Curse of Misfortunes |
| `SearchLibraryForEquipmentToBattlefieldAndAttachEffect` | `()` | search library for an Equipment card, put it onto the battlefield (`LibrarySearchDestination.BATTLEFIELD_ATTACHED_TO_CREATURE`), shuffle, then prompt the controller to choose one creature they control and attach the Equipment to it via `PermanentChoiceContext.AttachEquipmentToCreature` (skipped if they control no creatures). Non-targeted. Used by Stonehewer Giant |
| `SearchLibraryForAuraToBattlefieldAttachedToTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | search library for an Aura card that could enchant the lone attacker recorded on the trigger — the entry's `sourcePermanentId` (the MayEffect resolution-time path), falling back to `targetId` — put it onto the battlefield attached to that creature (`LibrarySearchDestination.BATTLEFIELD_ATTACHED_TO_PERMANENT` with `attachToPermanentId`), then shuffle. "Could enchant" = the card is an Aura enchanting a permanent (not a player) whose declared target filter accepts that creature (hexproof/shroud ignored — not targeted). Wrap in `MayEffect`. Used by Sovereigns of Lost Alara |
| `SearchLibraryForSubtypeCardsToTopEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | search library for **any number** of cards of `subtype`, reveal them, then shuffle and put those cards on top in any order. Unlike `SearchLibraryEffect`+`TOP_OF_LIBRARY` (single card), this holds the matching cards out and begins a `PendingInteraction.SearchLibraryToTopChoice` (`ChooseMultipleCardsMessage`, maxCount = matches): the controller picks any subset, the rest are returned and the whole library is shuffled, then the chosen cards go on top (ordered via `PendingInteraction.LibraryReorder` when >1). Changeling-aware via `CardSubtypePredicate`. Used by Goblin Recruiter (GOBLIN) |
| `CastTopOfLibraryWithoutPayingManaCostEffect` | `(Set<CardType> castableTypes)` | look at top card of controller's library; if it matches one of the castable types, may cast it without paying its mana cost |
| `ExileTopCardOfOpponentLibraryControllerMayPlayThisTurnEffect` | `()` | target opponent exiles the top card of their library; the source's **controller** may play that card (lands and spells, at normal costs/timing) until **end of turn**. The card is owned by the opponent; grants `exilePlayPermissions`→controller + `exilePlayPermissionsExpireEndOfTurn`. Two-player: the single opponent is derived. Used by Knacksaw Clique (`{1}{U}, {Q}` activated ability) |
| `ExileTopCardMayPlayThisTurnEffect` | `(boolean withoutPayingManaCost)` | exile the top card of the **controller's** library; until **end of turn** the controller may play it (any type, lands included). `false` = normal costs/timing; `true` = cast without paying its mana cost. Grants `exilePlayPermissions` + `exilePlayPermissionsExpireEndOfTurn`, plus `exilePlayWithoutPayingManaCost` for the free variant (read in `SpellCastingService.playCardFromExile` to skip payment, cleared during cleanup). Oracle's Vault (`{2},{T}` normal + brick counter; `{T}` free, gated on 3 brick counters). Unlike `ExileTopCardMayCastNonlandThisTurnEffect` (nonland only) lands get permission too |
| `RevealTopCardMayPlayFreeOrExileEffect` | `(boolean exileIfNotPlayed)` | reveal top card of controller's library; may play it (any type, including lands) without paying its mana cost. `exileIfNotPlayed=true`: a card not (or that can't be) played is exiled (Djinn of Wishes). `exileIfNotPlayed=false`: such a card stays on top of the library (Leaf-Crowned Elder's Kinship reveal effect) |
| `CastTargetInstantOrSorceryFromGraveyardEffect` | `(GraveyardSearchScope scope, boolean withoutPayingManaCost)` | Target instant or sorcery from a graveyard matching scope, you may cast it (without paying mana cost if flag is true). Has a graveyard-targeting spec (`GRAVEYARD_CARD`). Works as an ETB effect (Chancellor of the Spires — graveyard targeting via GameHelper ETB flow) or as a `SPELL` slot effect (Memory Plunder — single graveyard target chosen at cast time; validated by `GraveyardTargetValidators`). Handler reads the target from `targetCardIds` (ETB) or the single `targetId` (spell) |
| `DistantMemoriesEffect` | `()` | search library for any card, exile it, shuffle; opponent may let you have it, otherwise draw 3 |
| `LibraryOfLatNamEffect` | `()` | SPELL: an opponent chooses one of two modes for the controller via the may-ability (accept/decline) prompt (`getOpponentId` + `pendingMayAbilities.addFirst` in `LibraryOfLatNamEffectHandler`). Accept schedules a `DrawCardsAtNextUpkeep(controllerId, 3, source)` delayed action (drained in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers` → the controller draws 3 at the next turn's upkeep); decline pushes an unrestricted `SearchLibraryEffect()` (to hand, then shuffle) onto the stack for the controller. Choice dispatched in `MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService.handleLibraryOfLatNamChoice`. Library of Lat-Nam |
| `CovenantOfMindsEffect` | `()` | SPELL, targets a player (`targetSpec` benign PLAYER): reveals the top 3 cards of the controller's library, then the targeted opponent chooses via the may-ability (accept/decline) prompt (`CovenantOfMindsEffectHandler` reveals + `pendingMayAbilities.addFirst`; the revealed cards stay on top of the library while the opponent decides). Accept puts the revealed cards into the controller's hand; decline puts them into the controller's graveyard and the controller draws five. Choice dispatched in `MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService.handleCovenantOfMindsChoice` (re-reads the top 3 — resolution is paused so they are unchanged). Covenant of Minds |
| `SearchTargetLibraryForCardsToGraveyardEffect` | `(int maxCount, Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | search target opponent's library for up to N cards of specified types and put them into that player's graveyard, then shuffle. Targets player. Multi-pick via remainingCount |
| `SearchTargetLibraryForCardToExileWithPlayPermissionEffect` | `()` / `(boolean expiresAtNextUpkeep)` | search target opponent's library for any card, exile it face down, shuffle. Grants caster permission to play the exiled card. Default (`false`, Praetor's Grasp): permission lasts for as long as it remains exiled. `true` (Grinning Totem): permission lasts only until the caster's next upkeep — an unplayed card is then put into its owner's graveyard (via the `EXILE_PLAYABLE_UNTIL_NEXT_UPKEEP` library-search destination + `ExileToOwnerGraveyardAtNextUpkeep` delayed action drained in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers`). Targets player |
| `SearchTargetPlayerLibraryAndCastEffect` | `(Set<CardType> castableTypes)` | search target opponent's library for a card of one of the given types, caster may cast it without paying its mana cost, then that player shuffles. Targets player. Uses the `CAST_WITHOUT_PAYING` library-search destination (routed through `LibraryChoiceHandlerService.castCardWithoutPaying`). Knowledge Exploitation (INSTANT/SORCERY) |
