| `SearchTargetLibraryForCardToBattlefieldUnderControlEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | search target opponent's library for a card matching `filter`, put it onto the battlefield under the SEARCHER's control (owner unchanged), then that player shuffles. Targets player, may fail to find. Uses the `BATTLEFIELD_UNDER_SEARCHER` library-search destination (blocked by Grafdigger's Cage etc.). Bribery (`new CardTypePredicate(CardType.CREATURE)`) |
| `SearchTargetLibraryForCardsToExileEffect` | `(int count)` / `(DynamicAmount count, boolean upTo)` | search target player's library for up to `count` cards, exile them (owned by that player), then that player shuffles. `count` may be board-derived (`PermanentCount`); `upTo=true` models "up to X" (searcher may exile fewer — drives `canFailToFind`). Targets player; no play permission. Jester's Cap (`3`), Nightmare Incursion (`PermanentCount(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(SWAMP), CONTROLLER), true`). Drives the multi-card `EXILE` loop in `LibraryChoiceHandlerService` |
| `PayManaAndSearchLibraryForCardNamedToBattlefieldEffect` | `(String manaCost, String cardName)` | pay mana, search for named card to battlefield |
| `LookAtTopCardMayRevealTypeTransformEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | look at top card, the controller may reveal it (regardless of type). If revealed card matches one of the card types, transform the source permanent. Card stays on top of library. Used by Delver of Secrets with `Set.of(INSTANT, SORCERY)` and `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` |
| `KinshipEffect` | `(List<CardEffect> revealEffects)` | Kinship (Morningtide) — look at the top card of your library; if it shares a creature type with the source creature (Changeling counts as every type), the controller may reveal it, and on reveal the `revealEffects` resolve against the source permanent. Card stays on top of the library. `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` slot. The reveal prompt (`PendingMayAbility`) is completed in `MayAbilityHandlerService`. Used by Kithkin Zephyrnaut with `BoostSelfEffect(2,2) + GrantKeywordEffect(FLYING, SELF) + GrantKeywordEffect(VIGILANCE, SELF)` |
| `LookAtTopCardsCreatureSharingTypeWithEnchantedToBattlefieldEffect` | `(int count)` | look at top N cards, may put a creature card that shares a creature type with the enchanted creature onto the battlefield, rest on bottom in any order. For auras — uses source permanent's attachedTo to find enchanted creature at resolution time. Handles Changeling. Used by Call to the Kindred. NOT folded into `LookAtTopCardsEffect` (attachment-relative predicate + does-nothing-when-unattached early exit) |
| `ImprintFromTopCardsEffect` | `(int count)` | look at top N cards, exile one face down (imprint on source), rest on bottom in any order |
| `LookAtTopCardsOfTargetLibraryEffect` | `(int count, TargetLibraryAction action)` | look at the top N cards of **target player's** library, then apply `action` — the collapsed target-library look family (one switch handler). `LOOK_ONLY`: private peek, cards stay on top in their original order; `count==1` uses a blocking `LibrarySearch` acknowledge (Dewdrop Spy, Moonring Island), `count>1` leaves the library untouched and sends a non-blocking `RevealLibraryTopMessage` (Orcish Spy `{T}`, count 3 — no reordering permitted). `MAY_EXILE_ONE`: may exile one, rest on top in any order (Psychic Surgery `(2)`); with **no target** it falls back to the controller's own library — use `(1, MAY_EXILE_ONE)` with no `target(...)` for Puresight Merrow. `MAY_SHUFFLE`: pure look (same order, no reorder), names shown in a may-ability prompt wrapping `ShuffleLibraryEffect(true)` (Visions `(5)`); this action carries a benign `PLAYER` targetSpec. `PUT_ONE_INTO_GRAVEYARD`: mandatorily put one into that player's graveyard, rest on top in any order (Cruel Fate `(5)`, Wu Spy `(2)`); targets via `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter)`. Contrast with the public `RevealTopCardOfLibraryEffect` and the costed `LookAtTargetPlayerTopCardMayGraveyardEffect` |
| `LookAtTopCardsEffect` | build via static factories — mandatory to-hand: `chooseOneToHandRestOnBottom(DynamicAmount lookCount)`, `chooseOneToHandRestToExile(DynamicAmount lookCount)`, `chooseNToHandRestToGraveyard(int look, int choose[, CardPredicate choosePredicate, boolean reveal])`; optional may-reveal to hand: `mayRevealOneToHandRestOnBottom(int look, CardPredicate)`, `mayRevealAnyNumberToHandRestOnBottom(int look, CardPredicate)`, `mayRevealUpToToHandRestOnBottom(int look, CardPredicate, int maxReveal)`; other chosen destinations: `mayPutMatchingOntoBattlefield(int look, CardPredicate)`, `putOneOnTopRestOnBottom(int look)` — canonical `(DynamicAmount lookCount, DynamicAmount chooseCount, CardPredicate choosePredicate, LookDestination restDestination, boolean reveal, LibrarySearchDestination chosenDestination, boolean optional)` (5-arg ctor = `HAND`, mandatory) | look at (or reveal) the top `lookCount` cards, choose up to `chooseCount` (optionally `choosePredicate`-restricted) for `chosenDestination` (`HAND`, `BATTLEFIELD`, or `TOP_OF_LIBRARY`), put the rest to `restDestination` (`BOTTOM_OF_LIBRARY`, `GRAVEYARD`, or `EXILE`). `reveal`=public look (whole look is logged); the may-reveal flows instead reveal only the chosen cards. `optional`=a "may" — the player can decline/pick fewer and no auto-move-to-hand shortcut applies. With `chooseCount == lookCount` on the graveyard flow this is the choice-free "reveal N, all matching to hand, rest to graveyard" shape (Mulch `chooseNToHandRestToGraveyard(4,4,CardTypePredicate(LAND),true)`). Collapses the ChooseOne / ChooseN / PerChargeCounter / MayRevealByPredicate / PutMatchingOnBattlefield / PutOneOnTop records. Used by Stress Dream `chooseOneToHandRestOnBottom(Fixed(2))`, Shrine of Piercing Vision `chooseOneToHandRestOnBottom(CountersOnSource(CHARGE))`, Jar of Eyeballs `chooseOneToHandRestOnBottom(XValue())` (X from its remove-all-counters cost), Browse `chooseOneToHandRestToExile(Fixed(5))`, Forbidden Alchemy `(4,1)`, Dark Bargain `(3,2)`, Tower Geist `(2,1)`, Tracker's Instincts `(4,1,CardTypePredicate(CREATURE),true)`, Commune with Nature `mayRevealOneToHandRestOnBottom(5, CardTypePredicate(CREATURE))`, Lead the Stampede `mayRevealAnyNumberToHandRestOnBottom(5, CardTypePredicate(CREATURE))`, Follow the Lumarets `mayRevealUpToToHandRestOnBottom(4, creatureOrLand, 2)`, Weatherlight `mayRevealOneToHandRestOnBottom(5, CardIsHistoricPredicate())`, Mayael the Anima `mayPutMatchingOntoBattlefield(5, AllOf(CREATURE, powerAtLeast 5))`, Mitotic Manipulation `mayPutMatchingOntoBattlefield(7, CardSharesNameWithAPermanentPredicate())`, Cream of the Crop (materialised `putOneOnTopRestOnBottom(power)`) |
| `LookAtTopCardsRevealTwoTypesToHandThenRestEffect` | `(int count, CardType firstType, CardType secondType, LookDestination restDestination, boolean reveal)` — factories `creatureAndLandToHandRestOnBottom(count)` (Gift of the Gargantuan, `count=4`, private look, rest on bottom) / `creatureAndEnchantmentToHandRestToGraveyard(count)` (Benefaction of Rhonas, `count=5`, public reveal, rest to graveyard) | look at (or reveal) top N cards, may put up to one `firstType` card **and/or** one `secondType` card into hand, rest to `restDestination` (`BOTTOM_OF_LIBRARY` or `GRAVEYARD`). At-most-one-per-type bound is enforced by two sequential single-pick `LibrarySearch` interactions (first type, then second) rather than a multi-select — the first pick carries `LibrarySearchFollowUp.forSecondBoundedPick(secondType, restToGraveyard)`, whose completion (in `LibraryChoiceHandlerService`) begins the second pick; the second pick disposes the remaining looked-at cards (bottom via `LibraryReorder`, or graveyard via the `restToGraveyard` param). Prefer `LookAtTopCardsEffect.mayRevealOneToHandRestOnBottom`/`mayRevealUpToToHandRestOnBottom` when a single combined predicate with an unbounded/`maxReveal` count is correct |

Cards matching alwaysEligiblePredicate are eligible regardless of MV; cards matching mvCappedEligiblePredicate are eligible only if MV ≤ X. Routes through `PermanentRemovalService.removePermanentToLibraryShuffled` (fires leave-the-battlefield triggers, then shuffles) |
| `ShuffleGraveyardIntoLibraryEffect` | `(boolean targetPlayer)` | shuffle graveyard into library. When `targetPlayer=true`: targets a player (player-targeting spec), shuffles target player's graveyard (e.g. Reminisce). When `targetPlayer=false`: no targeting, shuffles controller's graveyard (e.g. Archangel's Light). As ON_SELF_MILLED: triggers when this card is milled from library, shuffles owner's graveyard into their library (e.g. Gaea's Blessing). As SAGA_CHAPTER / TRIGGERED_ABILITY (no target): falls back to controller's graveyard (e.g. The Mending of Dominaria chapter III) |

Distinct from `ShuffleIntoLibraryReplacementEffect`: the card enters the graveyard first (firing dies/graveyard triggers), then this trigger shuffles it in. Used by Purity |
| `ShuffleSelfIntoOwnerLibraryRevealUntilNameToBattlefieldEffect` | `(String cardName)` | shuffle source permanent into owner's library, then reveal cards until finding one with the given name — found card goes to battlefield under owner's control, all other revealed cards go to owner's graveyard |
| `ShuffleSelfIntoOwnerLibraryEffect` | `()` | non-targeted self effect: the source permanent's owner shuffles it into their library. Acts on the stack entry's source permanent via `PermanentRemovalService.removePermanentToLibraryShuffled` (fires leave-the-battlefield triggers, then shuffles). Used by Blitz Hellion (`END_STEP_TRIGGERED`). Distinct from `ShuffleTargetPermanentIntoLibraryEffect` (targeted) and `ShuffleIntoLibraryEffect` (a spell card on the stack, not a battlefield permanent) |
| `ShuffleLibraryEffect` | `(boolean targetPlayer)` | shuffle a library (no cards moved). `false` = controller's library — used with MayEffect for "you may shuffle" (Ponder). `true` = target player shuffles their library (Boggart Forager) |

## Mill

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `MillEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count, MillRecipient recipient)` | the recipient mills cards. `recipient` ∈ {`CONTROLLER`, `TARGET_PLAYER`, `EACH_OPPONENT`}; `(int, recipient)` convenience ctor for a fixed count. the spec targets a player iff `recipient == TARGET_PLAYER`. Use `XValue()` for "mills X", `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)` for Grindclock, `CardsInHand(TARGET_PLAYER)` for "mills cards equal to their hand size" (Dreamborn Muse). "Each player mills N" = `MillEffect(N, CONTROLLER)` + `MillEffect(N, EACH_OPPONENT)` (Ghoulcaller's Bell, Chill of Foreboding). For flashback "twice X" (Increasing Confusion), wrap two mills in `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new CastFromZone(Zone.GRAVEYARD), Mill(XValue(), TARGET_PLAYER), Mill(Scaled(XValue(),2), TARGET_PLAYER))` |
| `MillControllerAndMayPlayFromGraveyardThisTurnEffect` | `()` | mills 1 card from controller's library, grants permission to play that card from graveyard this turn (lands or spells, normal costs). Permission expires at end of turn. Used by Ark of Hunger |
| `PlayAdditionalLandsEffect` | `(int count)` | grants the controller `count` extra land plays this turn on top of the normal one-per-turn allowance (`GameData.additionalLandsThisTurn` / `getMaxLandsThisTurn`). Resets at end of turn. Used by Summer Bloom (3) |
| `EachPlayerPlaysAdditionalLandEffect` | `()` | **Static** marker in `EffectSlot.STATIC`: while on the battlefield, raises **every** player's per-turn land-play allowance by one (counted in `GameData.getMaxLandsThisTurn`, which scans all battlefields for this effect — symmetric, unlike the controller-only one-shot `PlayAdditionalLandsEffect`). Used by Storm Cauldron |
| `MillControllerAndDealDamageByHighestManaValueEffect` | `(int count)` | mills N cards from controller's library, deals damage to any target equal to greatest mana value among milled cards. Used by Heretic's Punishment |
| `MillControllerCost` | `(int count)` | **Cost**: controller mills N cards as activation cost. Blocks activation if library too small. Used by Deranged Assistant |
| `MillTargetPlayerAndBoostSelfByManaValueEffect` | `()` | target player mills one card, source creature gets +X/+X until end of turn where X is milled card's mana value. Used by Mindshrieker |
| `MillHalfLibraryEffect` | `(boolean roundUp)` | target player mills half their library. `roundUp=false` rounds down (Traumatize), `roundUp=true` rounds up (Fleet Swallower). NOT folded into `MillEffect` — a fraction-of-library amount does not yet exist (follow-up) |
| `MillDefendingPlayerEffect` | `(int count)` | `ON_ATTACK`, non-targeting: the defending player (the attacked player, or the controller of the attacked planeswalker) mills `count` cards. `CombatAttackService` stamps the attacked player/planeswalker onto the trigger's `attackedTargetId`; the handler resolves the player and reuses `GraveyardService.resolveMillPlayer`. Nemesis of Reason (10). Use instead of `MillEffect(TARGET_PLAYER)` on an attack trigger — the latter would prompt the controller to *choose* a player target |
| `MillOpponentOnLifeLossEffect` | `()` | triggered effect: whenever an opponent loses life, that player mills that many cards. Amount determined at trigger time. Used by Mindcrank |
| `MillBottomOfTargetLibraryConditionalTokenEffect` | `(CardType conditionType, String tokenName, int tokenPower, int tokenToughness, CardColor tokenColor, List<CardSubtype> tokenSubtypes)` | target player puts bottom card of library into graveyard; if it matches conditionType, controller creates a creature token. Used by Cellar Door |
| `RevealUntilNonlandCardsToHandRestToBottomEffect` | `(int count)` | caster reveals cards from the top of their library until they reveal `count` nonland cards (or the library empties); the nonland cards go into hand, then the rest (lands) are put on the bottom of the library in any order (async `LibraryReorder` when more than one). Used by Fathom Trawl |
| `RevealUntilLandToBattlefieldRestToBottomEffect` | `()` | caster reveals cards from the top of their library until a land is revealed; that land is put onto the battlefield under the caster's control, and the rest of the revealed cards are put on the bottom of the library in any order (async `LibraryReorder` when more than one). If the library is exhausted with no land, all revealed cards go to the bottom. Used by Recross the Paths (nested as a `ClashEffect` pre-clash body) |
| `RevealTargetPlayerLibraryUntilCreatureStealRestToGraveyardEffect` | `()` | target player reveals cards from the top of their library until a creature card is revealed; that player puts all revealed noncreature cards into their graveyard, then the caster puts the creature card onto the battlefield under their control (the card keeps its original owner, like Bribery). If the library is exhausted with no creature, every revealed card is milled and nothing is stolen. Targets a player; harmful. Used by Telemin Performance |
| `RevealUntilTypeMillAndBoostAttackerEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes, int powerBoostPerCard, int toughnessBoostPerCard)` | defending player reveals cards from top of library until a card matching one of the specified types is found; equipped creature gets +powerBoostPerCard/+toughnessBoostPerCard per card revealed; all revealed cards go to graveyard. Used on equipment ON_ATTACK triggers. Defending player derived as opponent. Used by Trepanation Blade |
| `RevealUntilLandsMillTargetPlayerEffect` | `(int landCount)` | target player reveals cards from the top of their library until `landCount` land cards are revealed (or the library empties); all revealed cards go to that player's graveyard. Targets a player; harmful. Used by Mind Funeral (`landCount = 4`); pair with `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))` for "target opponent" |
| `ReplaceCombatDamageWithMillEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate attackerPredicate)` | static replacement: if a creature matching the predicate you control would deal combat damage to a player, instead that player mills that many cards. Checked in CombatDamageService.accumulatePlayerDamage(). Used by Undead Alchemist (Zombie predicate) |
| `ExileMilledCreatureAndCreateTokenEffect` | `(String tokenName, int tokenPower, int tokenToughness, CardColor tokenColor, List<CardSubtype> tokenSubtypes)` | triggered: whenever a creature card is put into an opponent's graveyard from their library, exile that card and create a creature token. Uses ON_OPPONENT_CREATURE_CARD_MILLED slot. Handled by MiscTriggerCollectorService. Used by Undead Alchemist |
| `RevealTopCardsMillTargetByColorSymbolsEffect` | `(int count, ManaColor color)` | chroma mill: reveal the top `count` cards of the controller's library, target player mills one card per `color` mana symbol among the revealed cards' mana costs (hybrid/Phyrexian of that color count once, via `ManaCost.countColorSymbols`), then the revealed cards go on the bottom of the controller's library in any order (async `LibraryReorder` when more than one). Targets a player (player-targeting spec); pair with `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT))` for "target opponent". Used by Sanity Grinding `(10, ManaColor.BLUE)` |

## Exile

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `ExileGraveyardCardsEffect` | `(int count, GraveyardExileScope scope[, CardPredicate filter[, UUID affectedPlayerId]])` or `(GraveyardExileScope scope)` | unified graveyard-exile effect; `scope` selects which graveyard(s) and derives the `targetSpec()` category. Scopes: `OWN` (a player exiles `count` cards from their own graveyard, their choice; `affectedPlayerId` baked at trigger time — Curse of Oblivion), `TARGET_CARDS_ANY_GRAVEYARD` (spec `ANY_GRAVEYARD_CARD`; exile one target card from any graveyard, optional `CardTypePredicate` filter — Cemetery Reaper/Thraben Heretic/Conversion Chamber/Ascendant Dustspeaker/Glorious Decay/Purify the Grave; fizzles if target removed; validated by `GraveyardTargetValidators`), `TARGET_CARDS_OPPONENT_GRAVEYARD` (spec `GRAVEYARD_CARD`, opponent-only; exile exactly `count` target cards via `targetCardIds`, validated by `TargetLegalityService.validateMultiTargetGraveyardAbility()` — Deadeye Tracker count=2), `TARGET_PLAYER_ENTIRE` (player-targeting spec; exile a target player's whole graveyard — Nihil Spellbomb), `ALL_PLAYERS` (exile every player's graveyard — Sentinel Totem), `ALL_OPPONENTS` (exile every opponent's graveyard — Phyrexian Scriptures chapter III). Resolved by `ExileGraveyardCardsEffectHandler` |
| `ExileAllPermanentsEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | exile all permanents matching the predicate filter across all battlefields. Use with `PermanentAllOfPredicate` for compound conditions (e.g. nonland + nonlegendary). Used by Urza's Ruinous Blast |
| `ExileAllPermanentsUntilSourceLeavesEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, boolean returnTapped)` | O-ring style mass exile: exile every permanent matching `filter` across all battlefields until the source permanent leaves, then return each exiled card under its owner's control (tapped iff `returnTapped`). Registers one `PendingExileReturn` per card in `GameData.exileReturnOnPermanentLeave` (now a `Map<UUID, List<PendingExileReturn>>`). Combines the mass-exile scan with the `ExileTargetPermanentUntilSourceLeavesEffect` return linkage; the "leaves the battlefield" trigger is implicit (handled by `PermanentRemovalService`). Used by Realm Razer (`new PermanentIsLandPredicate(), true`) |
| `PutAllPermanentsOnBottomOfLibraryEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | put all permanents matching the predicate on the bottom of their owners' libraries across all battlefields (not a destroy — ignores indestructible/regeneration). Used by Hallowed Burial (`PermanentIsCreaturePredicate`) |
| `ExileTargetCreatureAndAllWithSameNameEffect` | `()` | exile target creature and all other creatures on the battlefield with the same name. Fizzles if target leaves. Used by Sever the Bloodline |
| `DestroyTargetNonlandPermanentAndAllWithSameNameEffect` | `()` | destroy target nonland permanent and all other permanents on the battlefield (any controller, incl. the caster's) with the same name as that permanent. Destruction respects regeneration / indestructible (routes through `DestructionSupport.destroyBatch`). Targets a nonland permanent (`harmful(PERMANENT, PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentIsLandPredicate))`); implements `RemovalEffect` (DESTROY). Fizzles if the target leaves. Used by Maelstrom Pulse |
| `ExileTargetCreatureAndSameNameFromHandIfGodEffect` | `()` | exile target creature; if it was a God (`CardSubtype.GOD` in its last-known subtypes), its controller reveals their hand and every card in it with the same name as that creature is exiled too. `RemovalEffect` (EXILE). Used by Hour of Glory |
| `ExileTargetPermanentEffect` | `()` or `(CreateTokenEffect tokenForController)` | exile target permanent (also handles multi-target via targetIds). When `tokenForController` is non-null, creates that token for each exiled permanent's controller (e.g. Crib Swap: exile target creature, its controller creates a 1/1 Shapeshifter with changeling) |
| `ExilePermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate)` | exile target permanent controlled by the damaged player (combat damage trigger); use inside MayEffect with ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER |
| `ExileUpToNAttackingCreaturesEffect` | `(int maxCount)` | "exile up to N target attacking creatures" as a resolution-time multi-select over every attacking creature on the battlefield (controller may choose zero). Non-targeting, so it rides on non-targeting resolution paths such as a cycling trigger (Resounding Silence). Completed via `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ExileAttackingCreatures`; resumes remaining effects (e.g. the cycling draw) after the choice |
| `ExileUpToOneCardFromGraveyardEffect` | `()` | "you may exile target card from a graveyard" as a resolution-time, cross-graveyard "up to one" select over every card in every graveyard (controller may choose zero = the optional "you may"). Non-targeting, so it rides on any resolution path — an `ON_DEATH` trigger and a folded cycling ability (`[this, DrawCardEffect]`). Completed via `graveyardTargetOperation.resolutionTimeExileResume` in `GraveyardChoiceHandlerService.handleMultipleCardsChosen`; exiles the chosen card and resumes remaining effects (e.g. the cycling draw). Graveyard-card analogue of `ExileUpToNAttackingCreaturesEffect`. Grixis Sojourners |
| `ReturnUpToNTargetPermanentsToHandEffect` | `(int maxCount)` | "return up to N target permanents to their owners' hands" as a resolution-time multi-select over every permanent on the battlefield (controller may choose zero). Non-targeting, so it rides on non-targeting resolution paths such as a cycling trigger (Resounding Wave). Completed via `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ReturnTargetPermanentsToHand`; resumes remaining effects (e.g. the cycling draw) after the choice. For a normal targeted bounce use `ReturnToHandEffect.target()` instead |
| `DestroyPermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, int minimumDamage)` | mandatory combat damage trigger: destroy target permanent (filtered by `predicate`, e.g. `PermanentIsLandPredicate`) controlled by the damaged player; only fires when the source dealt `minimumDamage`+ damage. Use bare (no MayEffect) on ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER. Deus of Calamity ("deals 6 or more damage → destroy target land that player controls"). Destroy variant of `ExilePermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` |
| `SacrificePermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, int minimumDamage)` | mandatory combat damage trigger: the source's controller chooses a target permanent (filtered by `predicate`, e.g. `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate`) the damaged player controls, and that player **sacrifices** it (ignores indestructible/regeneration; fires ally-sacrificed triggers). Only fires when the source dealt `minimumDamage`+ damage. Use bare on ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER. Ashling, the Extinguisher (`minimumDamage`=0). Sacrifice variant of `DestroyPermanentDamagedPlayerControlsEffect` |
| `ExileCardsFromGraveyardEffect` | `(int maxTargets, int lifeGain)` | exile up to N target cards from graveyards, gain lifeGain per card. Works in the `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` slot (Rooftop Percher — all-graveyards multi-select via `GraveyardTargetingService.handleGraveyardExileETBTargeting`), as a `"Discard this card"` hand ability (Faerie Macabre), and in the `SPELL` slot (Scarab Feast — cast-time multi-select via `GraveyardTargetingService.handleUpToNSingleGraveyardSpellTargeting`, wired in `SpellCastingService`). The SPELL path adds the **single-graveyard** restriction ("from a single graveyard"): `graveyardTargetOperation.singleGraveyard` is set so `GraveyardChoiceHandlerService.handleMultipleCardsChosen` rejects a selection spanning more than one graveyard (and `MultiGraveyardChoiceAiStrategy` confines the AI's picks to one). Resolved by `ExileCardsFromGraveyardEffectHandler` (reads `targetCardIds`) |
| `ExileCreaturesFromGraveyardAndCreateTokensEffect` | `()` or `(boolean targetPlayerGraveyard, boolean copyExiledCards, Integer powerOverride, Integer toughnessOverride, CardColor colorOverride, CardSubtype addedSubtype)` | exile creature cards from graveyards and create a token per card exiled this way. `()` = exile the individually-targeted `targetCardIds` (X-scaled multi-graveyard choice at cast time via `SpellCastingService`'s `needsGraveyardCreatureTargeting` / `handleGraveyardSpellTargeting`) and create plain 2/2 black Zombie tokens — Midnight Ritual's "exile X target creature cards from a single graveyard". `targetPlayerGraveyard=true` instead targets a player (`benign(PLAYER)`) and exiles ALL creature cards from that player's graveyard — Necromancer's Covenant; pair with a `target(PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(ANY))` on the card. Copy form (`copyExiledCards=true`) = each token is a copy of the exiled card with an Eternalize-style transform: `colorOverride` replaces the copy's color, `addedSubtype` is added in addition to its other types, `powerOverride`/`toughnessOverride` set base P/T. Hour of Eternity = `(false, true, 4, 4, CardColor.BLACK, CardSubtype.ZOMBIE)` → "a copy of that card, except it's a 4/4 black Zombie". Copy build delegates to `GraveyardReturnSupport.createTokenCopyFromCard(...)` |
| `ExileTopCardsRepeatOnDuplicateEffect` | `(int count)` | exile top N cards, repeat if duplicate names found |
| `ExileUntilNonlandToHandRepeatIfHighMVEffect` | `(int manaValueThreshold, int damagePerCard)` | exile cards from top of library until nonland found, put nonland into hand, repeat if MV >= threshold, deal damagePerCard damage per card put into hand. Provider: `DamageResolutionService` |
| `ExileSelfAtEndOfCombatAndReturnTransformedEffect` | `()` | schedule this permanent for exile at end of combat, then return it to the battlefield transformed (as its back face) under its controller's control (Conqueror's Galleon-style). Use on ON_ATTACK effect slot. Resolution adds the source permanent ID to a `ExileAndReturnTransformedAtEndOfCombat` delayed action; processing occurs in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatExileAndReturnTransformed()` |
| `ExileTargetPermanentAndImprintEffect` | `()` | exile target permanent permanently and imprint the exiled card onto the source permanent; the card does NOT return when the source leaves (Exclusion Ritual-style) |
| `ExileTargetPermanentAndTrackWithSourceEffect` | `()` | exile target permanent and track the exiled card in `permanentExiledCards` with the source permanent's ID. Unlike imprint, used for effects that reference "cards exiled with [source]" (Karn Liberated -3). Resolved by `ExileResolutionService` |
| `ReturnAllCardsExiledWithSourceEffect` | `()` | returns every card exiled with the source permanent (tracked via `exiledCards` by source permanent ID) to the battlefield under its owner's control. Designed for the `ON_DEATH` slot — `DeathTriggerCollectorService` carries the dying permanent's ID onto the stack entry's `sourcePermanentId` so resolution can look up the cards. Pairs with `ExileTargetPermanentAndTrackWithSourceEffect` activated abilities. Used by Helvault. Resolved by `ExileResolutionService` |
| `TargetPlayerExilesFromHandEffect` | `(int amount)` or `(int amount, boolean controllerMayPlay)` | target player exiles N cards from their hand (their choice), tracked in `permanentExiledCards` with source permanent. player-targeting spec. Uses `EXILE_FROM_HAND_CHOICE` awaiting input. When `controllerMayPlay=true`, the source's controller gains permission to play each exiled card for as long as it remains exiled (does not expire end of turn, persists even if the source leaves) via `exilePlayPermissions`. Resolved by `PlayerInteractionResolutionService`. Used by Karn Liberated +4 (no play permission) and Fiend of the Shadows combat damage trigger (with play permission). Works in `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` slot where targetId = damaged player |
| `TargetPlayerExilesCardFromGraveyardEffect` | `(int lifeGainIfCreature)` | target player exiles a card from their graveyard (their choice). If the exiled card is a creature and `lifeGainIfCreature > 0`, the ability's controller gains that much life. player-targeting spec. Auto-exiles when graveyard has exactly 1 card. Resolved by `GraveyardReturnResolutionService`. Used by Graveyard Shovel |
| `ExileForEachLifeLostEffect` | `()` | triggered: for each 1 life lost, exile a permanent you control or a card from your hand or graveyard. Slot: `ON_CONTROLLER_LOSES_LIFE`. Count from trigger context. Auto-selects: graveyard first, then hand, then battlefield permanents |
| `EachOpponentLosesLifeEqualToLifeLostThisTurn` | `()` | each opponent loses life equal to the life *that opponent* has lost so far this turn (read per-opponent from `GameData.lifeLostThisTurn`, which accumulates all life loss — damage included — via the shared `checkLifeLossTriggers` hook, cleared at turn cleanup). Slot: `END_STEP_TRIGGERED`. Used by Wound Reflection. Do **not** model as `LoseLifeEffect(EACH_OPPONENT, …)`: that evaluates the amount once and applies it to every opponent, which is wrong per-opponent |
| `FlickerEffect` | static factories: `exileTargetReturnAtEndStep()` / `exileTargetReturnAtEndStep(boolean returnTapped)` / `exileSelfReturnAtEndStep()` / `exilePlayersPermanentsReturnAtStep(PermanentPredicate filter, TurnStep returnStep)` / `flickerTarget()` / `flickerTargetWithCounters(int counters)` / `flickerTargetWithBonus(CardSubtype bonusSubtype, CardEffect bonusEffect)` | exile permanent(s) and return them under their **owner's** control as new objects (CR 610.3 — counters/attached Auras+Equipment lost, tokens cease to exist). `FlickerScope` = TARGET (single targeted, permanent-targeting spec), SELF (source, Argent Sphinx), TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS (every filtered permanent the target player controls, Sudden Disappearance, player-targeting spec). `ReturnTiming` = AT_STEP (delayed return at beginning of next `returnStep`, survives source leaving; `returnTapped` = Mystifying Maze) or IMMEDIATE (Cloudshift-style; `plusOnePlusOneCountersOnReturn` = Daydream, `bonusSubtype`+`bonusEffect` applies e.g. `DrawCardEffect(1)` if the exiled permanent had that subtype — Siren's Ruse) |
| `ExileTargetPermanentUntilSourceLeavesEffect` | `()` or `(boolean imprint)` | exile target permanent until source leaves the battlefield, then return it under owner's control (O-ring style). Tracked via `GameData.exileReturnOnPermanentLeave` map. Often wrapped in `MayEffect` for "you may" triggers. When `imprint=true`, also imprints the exiled card onto the source permanent (used by Ixalan's Binding for "can't cast same name" static) |
| `ImprintDyingCreatureEffect` | `(UUID dyingCardId)` or `()` | exile a dying nontoken creature and imprint it on the source permanent; previously imprinted card is returned to its owner's graveyard. No-arg constructor (dyingCardId is null) used in card definition; dyingCardId populated at trigger time |
| `ExileFromHandToImprintEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, String description)` | exiles a card matching the predicate from the controller's hand and imprints it on the source permanent. Description is used in the player prompt. Prototype Portal: `CardTypePredicate(ARTIFACT)`, Semblance Anvil: `CardNotPredicate(CardTypePredicate(LAND))` |
| `ChooseCardNameAndExileFromZonesEffect` | `(List<CardType> excludedTypes)` or `(List<CardType> excludedTypes, CardType requiredType)` | Two-step interaction: (1) choose a card name, (2) present all matching cards from target player's hand, graveyard, and library for "any number" selection — player chooses 0 to N to exile. Library is always shuffled. Targets player (benign PLAYER spec — pair with a card-level `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)` for "target opponent"). The offered names are narrowed by `excludedTypes` (drop names of cards with any of those types — Memoricide/Cranial Extraction = nonland) and, when `requiredType` is non-null, kept only if the card has that type (Dispossess = artifact card name). Uses `MULTI_ZONE_EXILE_CHOICE` awaiting input. Used by Memoricide, Cranial Extraction, Dispossess |
| `ChooseNameRevealHandDamagePerCopyAndExileEffect` | `(List<CardType> excludedTypes, int damagePerCard)` | Choose a card name (excluding given types); target player reveals their hand; the source deals `damagePerCard` damage to that player per copy revealed **from hand** this way; then **all** copies in their hand, graveyard, and library are exiled (mandatory — no "any number" choice, unlike `ChooseCardNameAndExileFromZonesEffect`) and they shuffle. Harmful player-targeting spec. Choice resolved in `ChoiceHandlerService.handleRevealHandDamageAndExileByNameChoice` (`ChoiceContext.RevealHandDamageAndExileByNameChoice`). | `ExileTargetPlayerAttackingCreaturesAndSearchBasicLandsToBattlefieldTappedEffect` | `()` | exile all attacking creatures target player controls, then that player may search their library for that many basic land cards and put them onto the battlefield tapped, then shuffle. | `TargetPlayerSearchesLibraryForBasicLandToBattlefieldTappedEffect` | `()` | target player searches their library for a basic land card, puts it onto the battlefield tapped, then shuffles. Targets player (player-targeting spec); searches the target's own library via `LibrarySearchSupport.performLibrarySearch`. Mandatory search, may fail to find. Used by Fertilid |
| `SacrificeAnyNumberOfLandsAndSearchThatManyLandsToBattlefieldTappedEffect` | `()` | controller sacrifices any number of the lands they control (chosen via a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.SacrificeLandsSearchLandsToBattlefieldTapped` multi-permanent choice, 0 to all), then searches their library for up to that many land cards and puts them onto the battlefield tapped, then shuffles. Search count equals lands sacrificed; multi-pick via `remainingCount`, may fail to find. No lands → resolves with no prompt. Used by Scapeshift |
| `ChooseFivePermanentsSearchSameNameToBattlefieldTappedEffect` | `()` | controller chooses up to five different permanents they control (chosen via a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ChooseFivePermanentsSearchSameNameToBattlefieldTapped` multi-permanent choice, capped at `min(5, permanents)`), then for each chosen permanent may search their library for a card with the same name and put it onto the battlefield tapped, then shuffles. No permanents → resolves with no prompt. Used by Clarion Ultimatum |
| `SacrificeAnyNumberOfPermanentsThenDrawPerSacrificedEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | controller sacrifices any number of the permanents they control matching `filter` (chosen via a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.SacrificePermanentsDrawPerSacrificed` multi-permanent choice, 0 to all), then draws a card for each one actually sacrificed. No eligible permanents → resolves with no prompt. Used by Reprocess with a `PermanentAnyOfPredicate` of artifact/creature/land |
| `ExileNonBasicLandGraveyardAndSameNameFromLibraryEffect` | `()` | exile all non-basic-land cards from target player's graveyard, then search their library for all cards with the same name as any exiled card and exile them too. Shuffles library. Fully automatic (no player choice). Targets player. Used by Haunting Echoes |
| `ExileTargetCardFromGraveyardAndImprintOnSourceEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | exile target card matching predicate from a graveyard and track in `permanentExiledCards` for the source permanent (imprint).
