| `ExileTargetCardFromGraveyardAndCreateTokenCopyEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, boolean ownGraveyardOnly, List<CardSubtype> additionalSubtypes, boolean grantHaste, boolean exileAtEndStep)` | exile target card matching predicate from a graveyard, then create a token that's a copy of that card. `ownGraveyardOnly=true` restricts targeting to the controller's graveyard. `additionalSubtypes` are granted to the token in addition to its other types. When `exileAtEndStep=true`, the token is exiled at the beginning of the next end step. Used by Séance (`CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)`, own graveyard, Spirit, no haste, exile at end step) via `EACH_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` + `MayEffect` |
| `ExileTargetCardFromGraveyardMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, boolean ownGraveyardOnly)` | exile a targeted graveyard card matching the filter, then grant its controller permission to play (cast) it until the end of their next turn (via `exilePlayPermissions` + `exilePlayPermissionsExpireAtTurnEnd`, expire turn = `turnNumber + 2`). Targets graveyard (per-instance spec: any graveyard unless `ownGraveyardOnly`). On an ETB, `BattlefieldEntryService` routes to `GraveyardTargetingService.handleGraveyardMayPlayETBTargeting` (single graveyard target via `MultiGraveyardChoice`). Validated by `GraveyardTargetValidators`. Used by Practiced Scrollsmith (`CardAllOfPredicate(not creature, not land)`, own graveyard) |
| `ExileTargetInstantOrSorceryFromOpponentGraveyardMayCastEffect` | `()` | exile a targeted instant or sorcery card from an opponent's graveyard, then grant its controller permission to cast it **this turn** spending mana of any type, exiling it instead of putting it into a graveyard. Uses `exilePlayPermissions` + `exilePlayPermissionsExpireEndOfTurn` (this-turn), `exilePlayAnyManaType` (checked by `CastingPermissionService.hasAnyManaTypePermission`), and `exileInsteadOfGraveyard` (checked by `GraveyardService.addCardToGraveyard`); all cleared in `TurnCleanupService`. Targets graveyard (spec `ANY_GRAVEYARD_CARD`), opponent-only + instant/sorcery enforced by `GraveyardTargetValidators`. Used by Nita, Forum Conciliator's `{2}, Sacrifice another creature` sorcery-speed ability |
| `PlayTargetCardFromGraveyardWithoutPayingManaCostEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | "You may play target [filter] card from your graveyard without paying its mana cost." Targets a card matching `filter` in the controller's **own** graveyard (spec `GRAVEYARD_CARD`; own-graveyard-only, enforced by its kept `@ValidatesTarget` validator). On resolution the handler re-validates own-graveyard + filter and queues a `PendingMayAbility`; accepting plays it for free — a land is put onto the battlefield (counts a land play), any other card is cast without paying (permanent → empty-effects spell, instant/sorcery → SPELL effects with `GraveyardCastSpellTarget` targeting). Routed by `MayAbilityHandlerService` → `MayCastHandlerService.handlePlayFromGraveyardChoice`; valid targets via `ValidTargetService.matchesGraveyardEffectTypeFilter`; validated by `GraveyardTargetValidators`. Used by Horde of Notions (`CardAnyOf(CardSubtype ELEMENTAL, CardKeyword CHANGELING)` — Elemental cards, incl. changelings) |
| `ExileGraveyardCardWithConditionalBonusEffect` | `(int creatureLifeGain, int noncreaturePowerBoost, int noncreatureToughnessBoost)` | exile target card from any graveyard; if creature card, controller gains life; if noncreature card, source permanent gets +P/+T until end of turn. Targets graveyard (spec `ANY_GRAVEYARD_CARD`). Resolved by `GraveyardReturnResolutionService`. Used by Deathgorge Scavenger |
| `ExileTargetGraveyardCardsAndSeparateIntoPilesEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, int maxTargets)` | exile up to maxTargets target cards matching filter from any graveyard, then opponent separates into two piles, controller chooses one pile to put onto battlefield under their control, rest returns to owners' graveyards. Two-step async flow: opponent assigns piles via multi-graveyard choice, then controller picks pile via may-ability choice. Multi-target all-graveyards selection at cast time via `BattlefieldEntryService.handleUpToNAllGraveyardsSpellTargeting()`. Resolved by `GraveyardReturnResolutionService`. Used by Boneyard Parley |
| `BrilliantUltimatumEffect` | `(int count)` | exile the top `count` cards of the controller's library, then an opponent separates them into two piles and the controller chooses one to play lands and cast spells from (spells cast without paying mana cost); everything not played stays exiled. Reuses the card-pile flow (`PendingPileSeparation` with `playFromExile=true`): the opponent assigns piles via a multi-graveyard choice, the controller picks a pile via may-ability, then a `BrilliantUltimatumPlayChoice` interaction offers the pile's cards — lands are put onto the battlefield (one-land-per-turn enforced), spells go through the shared exile free-cast queue (`ImprovisationCapstoneCastSupport`). Dispatch branches on `disposition == CardPileDisposition.PLAY_FROM_EXILE` in `GraveyardChoiceHandlerService` (step 1) and `MayAbilityHandlerService` (step 2). `BrilliantUltimatumEffectHandler` + `BrilliantUltimatumSupport`. Used by Brilliant Ultimatum |
| `HazoretsUndyingFuryEffect` | `(int exileCount, int maxCastableManaValue)` | Shuffle the controller's library (`LibraryShuffleHelper`), exile the top `exileCount` cards, then let the controller cast any number of the exiled spells whose mana value is ≤ `maxCastableManaValue` without paying, via the shared `ImprovisationCapstoneCastChoice` interaction (`ImprovisationCapstoneCastSupport`). Lands and pricier spells stay exiled. Non-targeting. `HazoretsUndyingFuryEffectHandler`. Used by Hazoret's Undying Fury `(4, 5)` — the card lists `SkipNextUntapEffect(CONTROLLED, land)` **before** this effect so the land lock resolves synchronously before the cast interaction pauses resolution |
| `RevealTopCardsAndSeparateEffect` | `(int count)` | Fact-or-Fiction: reveal the top `count` cards of the controller's library; an opponent separates them into two piles; the controller chooses one pile → their hand, the other → their graveyard. Non-targeting (used from enters triggers). Reuses the card-pile flow (`PendingPileSeparation` with `CardPileDisposition.HAND`): opponent assigns piles via a multi-graveyard choice (step 1), controller picks a pile via may-ability (step 2). Cards come off the top of the library and are held in the pile state (owner = controller); dispatch shares `GraveyardReturnSupport.completeCardPileSeparationStep1/2` with Boneyard Parley, branching on `disposition` in step 2 (HAND → hand/graveyard, BATTLEFIELD → battlefield/graveyard). `RevealTopCardsAndSeparateEffectHandler`. Used by Unesh, Criosphinx Sovereign |
| `ExileTargetGraveyardCardAndSameNameFromZonesEffect` | `()` | target a card in any graveyard (not a basic land), then search its owner's graveyard, hand, and library for any number of cards with the same name and exile them. Owner shuffles. Targets graveyard (spec `ANY_GRAVEYARD_CARD`). Uses `MULTI_ZONE_EXILE_CHOICE` awaiting input. Validated by `GraveyardTargetValidators`, resolved by `PlayerInteractionResolutionService`. Used by Surgical Extraction |
| `EachPlayerExilesTopCardsToSourceEffect` | `(int count)` | each player exiles top N cards of their library, tracked as "exiled with" the source permanent via `GameData.permanentExiledCards`. Used by Knowledge Pool ETB |
| `ExileTopCardsToSourceEffect` | `(int count)` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD: the **controller only** exiles top N cards of their own library face down, tracked "exiled with" the source permanent via `GameData.permanentExiledCards`. Controller-only variant of `EachPlayerExilesTopCardsToSourceEffect`. Pair with `AllowCastFromCardsExiledWithSourceEffect(false)` to let the controller play/cast them. Used by Colfenor's Plans ETB |
| `ExileTopCardsOfOpponentLibraryToSourceEffect` | `(int count)` | target-opponent variant: the controller's opponent exiles top N cards of their library face down, tracked "exiled with" the source permanent. Two-player: resolves against the single opponent (no target choice). Used by Grimoire Thief's "becomes tapped" trigger (wrap in `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect(new PermanentIsSourceCardPredicate(), …)` on `ON_ALLY_PERMANENT_BECOMES_TAPPED`) |
| `ExileTopCardsOfTargetOpponentCreateTokenPerChosenColorEffect` | `(DynamicAmount count, CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | player-targeting spec. On resolution the controller chooses a colour (`ChoiceContext.ExileTopCardsChosenColorTokensChoice`, resolved in `ChoiceHandlerService`); the target opponent exiles the top `count` cards of their library, then the controller creates one `tokenTemplate` token per exiled card whose printed colours contain the chosen colour (lands excluded, mirroring Persecute). `count` is a `DynamicAmount` so an `{X}...` activation cost flows through (`new XValue()`); the template's own `amount` is ignored. Used by Oona, Queen of the Fae |
| `CreateTokenPerPermanentOfChosenColorEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | On resolution the controller chooses a colour (`ChoiceContext.CreateTokensPerPermanentOfChosenColorChoice`, resolved in `ChoiceHandlerService`), then creates one `tokenTemplate` token for each permanent of that colour on the battlefield (any controller). A permanent is "of the chosen colour" per its effective colours (`GameQueryService.getEffectiveColors`), lands excluded (mirrors Oona). No target. Wrap in `MayPayManaEffect("{2}{G}", …)` for the "you may pay" gate. Used by Rith, the Awakener |
| `ExileTriggeringCreatureAndTrackWithSourceEffect` | `(UUID dyingCardId)` / `()` | ON_ALLY_CREATURE_DIES resolution: exile the dying creature card from its owner's graveyard tracked "exiled with" the source permanent (`GameData.exiledCards` by source id). Card definition uses the no-arg ctor; `DeathTriggerCollectorService.handleAllyCreatureMay` binds the concrete `dyingCardId` at trigger time. Wrap in `MayEffect` (and a toughness/other `TriggeringPermanentConditionalEffect`) for the "you may exile it" clause. Used by Colfenor's Urn |
| `SacrificeSelfAndReturnCardsExiledWithSourceEffect` | `(int minCount)` | END_STEP_TRIGGERED: intervening-if — if `>= minCount` cards have been exiled with the source permanent, sacrifice it and return every card exiled with it to the battlefield under its owner's control. Condition re-checked at trigger (StepTriggerService) and resolution. Used by Colfenor's Urn (`3`) |
| `SearchLibraryForCardsToExileWithSourceEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD: the controller searches their library for **any number** of cards matching `filter`, exiling each one tracked "with" the source permanent (`GameData.exiledCards` by source id), then shuffles. "Any number" = a repeated single-card pick the controller may stop at any time; driven by `LibraryChoiceHandlerService` via the `LibrarySearchDestination.EXILE_WITH_SOURCE` destination (carries `sourcePermanentId` + re-filters each pick). Pair with `PutCardExiledWithSourceIntoHandEffect`. Used by Endless Horizons (`CardSubtypePredicate(PLAINS)`) |
| `PutCardExiledWithSourceIntoHandEffect` | `()` | puts one card the controller owns exiled "with" the source permanent into their hand; with several the controller chooses which via a `LIBRARY_REVEAL_CHOICE` routed by `PendingReturnExiledWithSourceCard` (only the chosen card leaves exile). Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may". Companion to `SearchLibraryForCardsToExileWithSourceEffect`. Used by Endless Horizons's UPKEEP_TRIGGERED |
| `DealDamageToPlayersEffect` (ENCHANTED_PLAYER) | `(int, DamageRecipient.ENCHANTED_PLAYER)`, `enchantedAttachedCount(PermanentPredicate)` | deals damage to the enchanted player (the player a curse is attached to; targetId baked to that player by StepTriggerService). Fixed ctor or `enchantedAttachedCount(predicate)` for damage equal to matching permanents attached to that player. Used by Curse of the Pierced Heart (fixed 1) and Curse of Thirst (`enchantedAttachedCount(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CURSE))`), both ENCHANTED_PLAYER_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED |
| `ExileTopCardMayCastNonlandThisTurnEffect` | `()` | exile top card of controller's library; if it's a nonland card, grant temporary cast permission (expires end of turn). Uses `exilePlayPermissions` and `exilePlayPermissionsExpireEndOfTurn` in GameData. Resolved by `ExileResolutionService`. Place in UPKEEP_TRIGGERED slot. Used by Vance's Blasting Cannons |
| `ExileTargetPermanentMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect` | `()` | exile the target permanent (permanent-targeting spec; restrict via the card's target filter, e.g. nonland), then grant its owner permission to play it until the end of the owner's next turn (via `ExileSupport.grantPlayUntilOwnersNextTurn` — owner-relative expiry). A token exiled this way ceases to exist (no permission granted). Fizzles if the target left the battlefield. Used by Suspend Aggression (paired with `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect(1)` for "and the top card of your library") |
| `ReturnTargetCardFromExileToHandEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, boolean ownedOnly)` | return target exiled card matching filter to hand. When `ownedOnly=true`, restricts targeting to the controller's own exile zone (MTG "you own"). Targets exile (spec `EXILE_CARD`). Fizzles if target removed before resolution. Validated by `ExileTargetValidators`, resolved by `ExileReturnResolutionService`. Used by Runic Repetition |
| `ExileTopCardMayPlayUntilNextUpkeepEffect` | `()` | exile the top card of the controller's library; grant `exilePlayPermissions` for it (any type, lands included) and queue a `RevokeExilePlayPermissionAtNextUpkeep` delayed action. At the controller's next upkeep (`StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers`, `activePlayerId == controllerId`) the permission is removed; an unplayed card stays in exile (never moved to a graveyard, unlike Grinning Totem's `ExileToOwnerGraveyardAtNextUpkeep`). One turn shorter than `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect`. Used by Elkin Bottle (`{3}, {T}` activated ability) |
| `ExileTargetPermanentMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect` | `()` | exile the target permanent (`canTargetPermanent()=true`; restrict via the card's target filter, e.g. nonland), then grant its owner permission to play it until the end of the owner's next turn (via `ExileSupport.grantPlayUntilOwnersNextTurn` — owner-relative expiry). A token exiled this way ceases to exist (no permission granted). Fizzles if the target left the battlefield. Used by Suspend Aggression (paired with `ExileTopCardsMayPlayUntilNextTurnEffect(1)` for "and the top card of your library") |
| `ReturnTargetCardFromExileToHandEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, boolean ownedOnly)` | return target exiled card matching filter to hand. When `ownedOnly=true`, restricts targeting to the controller's own exile zone (MTG "you own"). Targets exile (`canTargetExile()=true`). Fizzles if target removed before resolution. Validated by `ExileTargetValidators`, resolved by `ExileReturnResolutionService`. Used by Runic Repetition |
| `KnowledgePoolCastTriggerEffect` | `()` | Marker effect for `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL`. When a spell is cast from hand, creates a `KnowledgePoolExileAndCastEffect` triggered ability. Only fires for spells cast from hand (prevents infinite loops) |
| `KnowledgePoolExileAndCastEffect` | `(UUID originalSpellCardId, UUID knowledgePoolPermanentId, UUID castingPlayerId)` | Resolution effect for Knowledge Pool's cast trigger. Exiles the original spell from the stack to the KP pool, then presents the casting player with a choice of nonland "other" cards from the pool to cast without paying mana cost. `castingPlayerId` tracks "that player" (the caster) since the trigger is controlled by the KP controller per CR 603.3a. Uses `KNOWLEDGE_POOL_CAST_CHOICE` awaiting input |
| `SunbirdsInvocationTriggerEffect` | `()` | Marker effect for `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL`. When controller casts a spell from hand, creates a `SunbirdsInvocationRevealAndCastEffect(manaValue)` triggered ability. Only fires for spells cast from hand (prevents infinite loops with free casts) |
| `SunbirdsInvocationRevealAndCastEffect` | `(int manaValue)` | Reveal top X cards where X = manaValue. Controller may cast a non-land spell with MV ≤ X from among revealed without paying its mana cost. Remaining cards go to bottom in random order (no player reorder). Uses `LIBRARY_SEARCH` with `CAST_WITHOUT_PAYING` destination. Resolved by `LibraryRevealResolutionService`, choice handled by `LibraryChoiceHandlerService` |
| `MirrorOfFateEffect` | `()` | choose up to seven face-up exiled cards you own, exile all cards from your library, then put the chosen cards on top of your library. Uses `MIRROR_OF_FATE_CHOICE` awaiting input. Resolved by `ExileResolutionService` |
| `DoomsdayEffect` | `()` | controller loses half their life (rounded up), then their library and graveyard are held out as one combined pool; a `PendingInteraction.DoomsdayChoice` keeps up to five of those cards on top of the library (ordered via `LibraryReorder` when >1), exiling the rest. Resolved by `DoomsdayEffectHandler`; answer applied by `DoomsdayChoiceInteractionHandler`. Used by Doomsday |
| `PermanentAuctionEffect` | `()` | exile all nontoken permanents into a shared pool; starting with the controller and going in turn order (wrapping), each player picks one exiled card and puts it onto the battlefield tapped under their control until the pool empties. Uses the `PermanentAuctionChoice` awaiting-input record (a `CHOOSE_MULTIPLE_CARDS` prompt with `maxCount == 1` per pick). Resolved by `PermanentAuctionService`. Used by Thieves' Auction |
| `IllicitAuctionEffect` | `()` | targeted SPELL (permanent-targeting spec, pair with a creature target filter): a life-bid auction for control of the target creature. The controller opens the bidding at 0 as the high bidder; then in turn order each player may top the high bid via an `IllicitAuctionBidChoice` awaiting-input record (reuses the numeric `X_VALUE_CHOICE` wire message — a value `> highBid` tops it, `<= highBid` passes). The auction ends when the bid comes back around to the high bidder with no raise; the high bidder loses life equal to the high bid (a **life loss**, so it can exceed their life total per ruling) and gains control of the creature indefinitely (`GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` machinery). Resolved by `IllicitAuctionEffectHandler`, re-run each bid via `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction`; progress on `GameData.illicitAuction`. Used by Illicit Auction |
| `OmenMachineDrawStepEffect` | `()` | Triggered at each player's draw step (via `EACH_DRAW_TRIGGERED`). Exiles top card of active player's library. If land, puts it onto the battlefield. If non-land, casts it without paying mana cost if able (mandatory). Targeted spells prompt for target via `ExileCastSpellTarget`. If no valid targets, card stays in exile. Resolved by `ExileResolutionService` |
| `RevealRandomHandCardAndPlayEffect` | `()` | Reveals a random card from the target player's hand. If land, puts it onto the battlefield. If non-land, casts it without paying mana cost if able (mandatory). Targeted spells prompt for target via `HandCastSpellTarget`. If no valid targets, card stays in hand. Resolved by `PlayerInteractionResolutionService` |

## Tokens

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `CreateTokenEffect` | `(String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, Set<Keyword> keywords, Set<CardType> additionalTypes)` or `(int amount, ...)` or multi-color: `(int amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, Set<CardColor> colors, List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` or `(String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, Set<CardColor> colors, List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` or multi-color with innate + until-end-of-turn keywords: `(int amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, Set<CardColor> colors, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, Set<Keyword> keywords, Set<Keyword> grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn)` or multi-color with +1/+1 counters on creation: `(String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, Set<CardColor> colors, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, int initialPlusOnePlusOneCounters)` or tapped-and-attacking: `(int amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, boolean tappedAndAttacking)` or tapped-attacking-with-keywords-exile: `(int amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, Set<Keyword> keywords, boolean tappedAndAttacking, boolean exileAtEndOfCombat)` or enters-tapped: `(int amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, Set<Keyword> keywords, Set<CardType> additionalTypes, boolean tapped)` or with-token-effects: `(int amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, Set<Keyword> keywords, Set<CardType> additionalTypes, Map<EffectSlot, CardEffect> tokenEffects)` or factory: `CreateTokenEffect.ofArtifactToken(int amount, String tokenName, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, List<ActivatedAbility> abilities)` or static factories for common tokens: `CreateTokenEffect.whiteSpirit(int amount)` (1/1 white Spirit with flying), `CreateTokenEffect.blackZombie(int amount)` (2/2 black Zombie), `CreateTokenEffect.whiteSoldier(int amount)` (1/1 white Soldier), `CreateTokenEffect.ofTreasureToken(int amount)` (Treasure artifact) or canonical (all params): `(CardType primaryType, DynamicAmount amount, String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, Set<CardColor> colors, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, Set<Keyword> keywords, Set<CardType> additionalTypes, boolean tappedAndAttacking, boolean tapped, Map<EffectSlot, CardEffect> tokenEffects, List<ActivatedAbility> tokenAbilities, boolean exileAtEndOfCombat, boolean exileAtEndStep, boolean legendary, int initialPlusOnePlusOneCounters, Set<Keyword> grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn)` (also with `int amount` = `Fixed` sugar) | create N tokens. The count is a `DynamicAmount` evaluated at resolution (source-relative amounts read the live source permanent, falling back to `sourcePermanentSnapshot` when it left the battlefield as a cost); every "create a token for each …" wording is this effect + an amount — never a new effect class. Power/toughness are also `DynamicAmount`s (every int ctor is `Fixed` sugar): "create an X/X token where X is …" = the `(String tokenName, DynamicAmount power, DynamicAmount toughness, CardColor, List<CardSubtype>, Set<Keyword>, Set<CardType>)` ctor, e.g. Phyrexian Rebirth's `EventValue()`/`EventValue()` colorless Horror as a `DestroyAllPermanentsEffect` rider. The single-color convenience constructor also accepts a `DynamicAmount` in the amount position. Examples: "for each charge counter on ~" = `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)` (Shrine of Loyal Legions), "create X tokens" = `XValue()` (White Sun's Zenith), "for each Aura and Equipment attached to ~" = `AttachmentsOnSource(true, true)` (Valduk) / Equipment only = `(false, true)` (Kemba, Kha Regent), "for each poison counter your opponents have" = `OpponentPoisonCounters()` (Phyrexian Swarmlord), "for each creature you control" = `PermanentCount(IsCreature, CONTROLLER)` (Chancellor of the Forge), "for each creature card in your graveyard" = `CardsInGraveyard(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CONTROLLER)` (Spider Spawning; Kessig Cagebreakers adds `tappedAndAttacking=true` via the canonical ctor), "for each Forest you control" = `PermanentCount(HasSubtype(FOREST), CONTROLLER)` (Howl of the Night Pack), "for each creature put into your graveyard from the battlefield this turn" = `CreatureDeathsThisTurn(CONTROLLER)` (Fresh Meat), "half the number of Zombies you control, rounded down" = `Divided(PermanentCount(AllOf(IsCreature, HasSubtype(ZOMBIE)), CONTROLLER), 2)` (Endless Ranks of the Dead). `primaryType` determines the token's card type (CREATURE for creature tokens, ARTIFACT for artifact tokens like Treasure/Clue/Food); all convenience constructors default to CREATURE. `tokenAbilities` adds activated abilities to the token (e.g. Treasure's tap-sacrifice-for-mana). For non-creature tokens, power/toughness are ignored and `handleCreatureEnteredBattlefield` is not called. `ofArtifactToken` factory creates colorless artifact tokens with abilities. `color` is primary display color. `colors` (Set&lt;CardColor&gt;, nullable) is full color identity for multi-color tokens. Multi-color constructors default keywords/additionalTypes to empty sets. When `initialPlusOnePlusOneCounters` &gt; 0, each created token enters with that many +1/+1 counters (e.g. Additive Evolution's 0/0 Fractal with three counters). When `tappedAndAttacking=true`, tokens enter the battlefield tapped and attacking (CR 508.8) — used for "whenever ~ attacks, create tokens tapped and attacking" abilities (e.g. Hero of Bladehold). When `tapped=true`, tokens enter the battlefield tapped but not attacking — used for cards like Army of the Damned. When `exileAtEndOfCombat=true`, tokens are exiled at end of combat step — used for temporary attack tokens (e.g. Geist of Saint Traft). When `tokenEffects` is non-empty, each entry's effect is registered on the token card at the given slot, giving the token its own triggered abilities (e.g. Mitotic Slime's cascading death triggers). When `legendary=true`, the token has the LEGENDARY supertype (subject to legend rule) — used for named legendary tokens (e.g. Verix Bladewing creating Karox Bladewing). `grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn` (defaults to empty in every convenience constructor) is added to each created token's `Permanent.grantedKeywords` after it enters, i.e. keywords the token gains until end of turn — distinct from innate `keywords`. Used for "create a ... token. It gains haste until end of turn" (e.g. Artistic Process's Elemental gains haste) |
| `CreateTokenForTargetPlayerEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenEffect)` | create tokens under the targeted player's control (not the controller's). Wraps a `CreateTokenEffect` that defines the token characteristics. Targets player (player-targeting spec). Used by Dowsing Dagger (target opponent creates Plant tokens on ETB) |
| `CreateTokenWithDyingSourceCountersEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | `ON_DEATH` only: "when this dies, if it had one or more +1/+1 counters, create the template token, then put this creature's counters on that token." The death collector checks the intervening-if (≥1 +1/+1 counter on the dying permanent) and resolves into a copy of `tokenTemplate` with `initialPlusOnePlusOneCounters` set to the dying creature's count. Used by Ambitious Augmenter (0/0 Fractal) |
| `CreateTokensForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenTemplate)` | `ON_DEATH` only: "when this dies, create one `tokenTemplate` token for each counter on it." The death collector snapshots the dying permanent's total counter count (every concrete counter type; intervening-if ≥1) and resolves into a copy of `tokenTemplate` whose amount is that count. Used by Kinsbaile Borderguard (1/1 white Kithkin Soldier per counter) |
| `MoveDyingSourceCountersToTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | `ON_DEATH` only: "when this dies, if it had counters on it, put those counters on up to one target creature." The death collector snapshots every counter type on the dying permanent (intervening-if: ≥1 counter) and queues a targeted death trigger; resolution places each snapshotted counter on the chosen creature. Targets any creature. Used by Scolding Administrator |
| `ExileDyingCreatureCardAndCreateTokenEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect token)` (card def) / `(UUID dyingCardId, CreateTokenEffect token)` (bound) | `ON_DAMAGED_CREATURE_DIES` effect, wrap in `MayEffect`: "you may exile that card. If you do, create `token`." Implements `DyingCreatureCardAwareEffect`; `GraveyardService.triggerDamagedCreatureDiesAbilities` binds the dying creature's card id onto the wrapped effect (the may flow drops `StackEntry.triggeringCardId`). On resolution, exiles the dying card from its owner's graveyard only if still present — a token or a card removed from the graveyard in response can't be exiled, and then no token is created. On an Equipment (Unscythe, Killer of Kings) the slot fires for the **currently-equipped** creature's damage: the same method scans Equipment attached to the damaging creature, so only the creature Unscythe is attached to *now* is checked, even if it wasn't equipped when the damage was dealt (any damage, not just combat). Pair with `CreateTokenEffect.blackZombie(1)` |
| `DrawCardForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` | `ON_DEATH` only: "when this dies, draw a card for each `counterType` counter on it." The death collector snapshots the dying permanent's count of that counter type (intervening-if ≥1) and resolves into a plain `DrawCardEffect` for that many cards. Used by Dusk Urchins (-1/-1 counters) |
| `PutCounterOnTargetForEachDyingSourceCounterEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int count, boolean optional)` — cards use `(CounterType)` or `(CounterType, boolean optional)` | `ON_DEATH` only: "when this dies, put a `counterType` counter on target creature for each `counterType` counter on it." The death collector snapshots the dying permanent's count into `count` and queues a targeted (any creature) death trigger; resolution places `count` counters of that type on the chosen creature. `optional=true` = "you may": the collector wraps the snapshotted effect in a `MayEffect` (target still chosen as the trigger stacks per CR 603.3d, may decline at resolution). Always triggers (no intervening-if). Used by Grief Tyrant (mandatory) and Soulstinger (optional). **Death-trigger targeting note:** `TriggeredAbilityQueueService.processNextDeathTriggerTarget` only applies the card-level `target(...)` filter when THIS trigger's effect is bound to that target group (via `getEffectTargetIndex`); a cast-time filter belonging to a different ability (e.g. Soulstinger's ETB "creature you control") does not narrow the death trigger |
| `MoveCounterFromTargetCreatureToTargetCreatureEffect` | `(boolean moveAll)`; `()` = `(false)` | effect reading the flat multi-target positions (0 = source, 1 = destination): move counters from the first target creature onto the second. `moveAll=false` moves one counter of the first kind present; `moveAll=true` moves every counter of every kind. No-op if the source has no counters or either target left the battlefield. For an activated ability, wire with the multi-target `ActivatedAbility` constructor + two creature `TargetFilter`s (min/max 2), `.withRequiresUntap()` for `{Q}` (Leech Bonder, `()`). For a spell, use two `target(creatureFilter)` groups with the effect on the first (Fate Transfer, `(true)`) |
| `CreateXTokenWithXCountersEffect` | `(String tokenName, int power, int toughness, CardColor color, Set<CardColor> colors, List<CardSubtype> subtypes, CounterType counterType)` | create a single creature token and put X counters of the given type on it, where X comes from the spell or activated ability's X value. Used by Berta, Wise Extrapolator (0/0 Fractal with `PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE`) |
| `CreateTokenCopyOfImprintedCardEffect` | `(boolean grantHaste, boolean exileAtEndStep)` | create a token that is a copy of the card imprinted on the source permanent. When `grantHaste=true`, the token gains haste. When `exileAtEndStep=true`, the token is exiled at the beginning of the next end step. No-arg constructor `()` defaults to `(true, true)` for Mimic Vat. Use `(false, false)` for permanent tokens like Prototype Portal |
| `CreateTokenCopyOfExiledCostCardEffect` | `()` | create a token that is a copy of the card exiled as part of an `ExileCardFromGraveyardCost` with `imprintOnSource=true`. The exiled card is tracked via the source permanent's imprinted card reference, set during cost payment. Used by Back from the Brink |
| `CreateTokenCopyOfSourceEffect` | `(boolean removeLegendary, int amount)` or `(boolean removeLegendary, int amount, CardColor colorOverride, CardSubtype addedSubtype, boolean removeManaCost)` or `(..., Integer powerOverride, Integer toughnessOverride)` | create token(s) that are copies of the source permanent. `removeLegendary` removes LEGENDARY supertype from copies, `amount` is the number of copies. No-arg constructor `()` defaults to `(false, 1, null, null, false, null, null)`. For planeswalker sources, tokens enter with loyalty counters. If source left the battlefield (incl. graveyard-activated abilities, where there is no source permanent), copies are based on the card stored on the stack entry (CR 608.2b). The color/subtype/mana-cost/P-T components apply the **Embalm / Eternalize** transformation to the copy — `colorOverride` recolors it (Embalm white, Eternalize black), `addedSubtype` adds a creature type (e.g. Zombie), `removeManaCost` gives it no mana cost, and `powerOverride`/`toughnessOverride` set a fixed base P/T (Eternalize's 4/4; leave `null` for Embalm, which keeps the source's P/T) — all inert for a plain copy. Used by Jace, Cunning Castaway's -5, Angel of Sanctions' Embalm, and Adorned Pouncer's Eternalize (`BLACK, ZOMBIE, true, 4, 4`) |
| `CreateTokenCopyOfTargetPermanentEffect` | `()` or `(boolean grantHaste, boolean exileAtEndStep)` or `(boolean grantHaste, boolean exileAtEndStep, boolean sacrificeAtEndStep)` or `(List<CardSubtype> additionalSubtypes, Set<CardType> additionalTypes, Integer powerOverride, Integer toughnessOverride, Map<CounterType, Integer> initialCounters)` | create a token that is a copy of the permanent referenced by `targetId` on the stack entry. Used for triggered abilities where the permanent to copy is determined at trigger time (e.g. Mirrorworks, Minion Reflector) or targeted spells (e.g. Cackling Counterpart, Applied Geometry, Heat Shimmer). Copies all copiable characteristics per CR 707.2. Optional overrides: additional subtypes/types ("in addition to its other types"), P/T overrides (skips copied CDAs per CR 707.9d), counters placed after ETB triggers are queued, `grantHaste` (token gains haste), `exileAtEndStep` (token exiled at beginning of next end step via `DelayedPermanentAction(EXILE_TOKEN_AT_END_STEP)` — Heat Shimmer), and `sacrificeAtEndStep` (token sacrificed at beginning of next end step via `DelayedPermanentAction(SACRIFICE_AT_END_STEP)`, so its dies-triggers fire — Minion Reflector) |
| `CreateTokenCopyOfEachControlledCreatureTokenEffect` | `()` | "For each creature token you control, create a token that's a copy of that creature" (populate-all). Snapshots the controller's creature tokens before creating any copies so the new copies aren't themselves copied; copies all copiable characteristics per CR 707.2 and respects the token multiplier (Doubling Season). No target. Used by Rhys the Redeemed's second ability |
| `CreateTokenCopyOfEquippedCreatureEffect` | `(boolean removeLegendary, boolean grantHaste)` | create a token that is a copy of the creature the source equipment is attached to. When `removeLegendary=true`, the token loses the LEGENDARY supertype. When `grantHaste=true`, the token gains haste. Place in `BEGINNING_OF_COMBAT_TRIGGERED` slot. Used by Helm of the Host |
| `CreateTokenCopyAndLinkToSourceEffect` | `()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD, targets a nontoken creature (`entry.getTargetId()`): builds a token copy of it (via `CreateTokenCopyOfTargetPermanentEffectHandler.buildTokenCopyCard`), then forges a two-way `chosenPermanentId` bond between the source permanent (`entry.getSourcePermanentId()`) and the token, attaching an `ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` `RemoveLinkedPermanentEffect(SACRIFICE)` to the token before it is frozen. Dance of Many |
| `RemoveLinkedPermanentEffect` | `(Mode mode)` / `(Mode mode, UUID linkedPermanentId)` | ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD: removes the permanent linked to the source via `chosenPermanentId`, `EXILE` or `SACRIFICE`. Card-authored form uses the single-arg ctor; the dedicated trigger collector in `DeathTriggerCollectorService` reads the leaving permanent's `chosenPermanentId`, bakes it into a fresh effect with the linked id set (NOT the stack entry's `targetId`, which resolution would validate against the source card's spell target filter and fizzle), and drops the trigger when the bond is absent. The handler clears the partner's back-reference before removal so the reciprocal leaves-trigger no-ops (no exile↔sacrifice ping-pong). Dance of Many |
| `CreateLifeTotalAvatarTokenEffect` | `(String tokenName, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` | create a creature token with P/T = controller's life total (CDA). Token gets `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect(new ControllerLifeTotal(), new ControllerLifeTotal())` as a static effect so P/T updates dynamically. Used by Ajani Goldmane |
| `CreateTokenFromHalfLifeTotalAndDealDamageEffect` | `(String tokenName, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` | create an X/X creature token where X = half the controller's life total (rounded up), then the token deals X damage to the controller. Used by Chainer's Torment chapter III |
| `LivingWeaponEffect` | `()` | living weapon ETB: create 0/0 black Phyrexian Germ token and attach this equipment to it (resolved by PermanentControlResolutionService) |
| `PutSlimeCounterAndCreateOozeTokenEffect` | `()` | composite: puts a slime counter on the source permanent, then creates a 0/0 green Ooze creature token with a CDA linking its P/T to the number of slime counters on the source. The token gets a `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect` with a `CountersOnLinkedPermanent(CounterType.SLIME, sourceId)` amount as a static effect (0/0 → dies to SBA if the source leaves). Place in `ON_ALLY_NONTOKEN_CREATURE_DIES` slot. Used by Gutter Grime |

## Life

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `GainLifeEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount[, GainLifeRecipient recipient])` or `(int amount)` sugar for `Fixed` | gain life; the amount is any `DynamicAmount` evaluated at resolution. `recipient` defaults to `CONTROLLER`; `TARGET_CONTROLLER` routes the life to the effect's target permanent's controller — "its controller gains life equal to its toughness" = `GainLifeEffect(new TargetToughness(), GainLifeRecipient.TARGET_CONTROLLER)` (Condemn; no legal target → nobody gains, matching fizzle). Examples: `new GainLifeEffect(3)`; per creature you control = `PermanentCount(IsCreature, CONTROLLER)`; per card in your hand = `CardsInHand(CONTROLLER)`; per card in your graveyard = `CardsInGraveyard(null, CONTROLLER)` (× N via `Scaled`); X paid / toughness snapshotted as xValue (`SacrificeCreatureCost(trackToughness)`) = `XValue()`; twice X = `Scaled(XValue(), 2)`; charge counters on sacrificed source = `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)`; greatest power among your creatures = `GreatestPowerAmongControlled()`; War Report's creatures-plus-artifacts = `Sum(...)` |
| `PayXManaGainXLifeEffect` | `()` | on resolution, pays all available mana from the controller's pool as X and gains X life. Used for "you may pay {X}. If you do, you gain X life" triggered abilities where payment happens during resolution (e.g. Vigil for the Lost) |
| `PayXManaCreateXTokensEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect token)` | on resolution, controller chooses X (up to available mana), pays it, and creates X copies of `token`. Used for "you may pay {X}. If you do, create X [tokens]" triggered abilities where payment happens during resolution (e.g. Rise of the Hobgoblins). X=0 = decline. `token`'s own amount is ignored (overridden with X). Do NOT use `MayPayManaEffect("{X}", …)` — it can't pay/plumb `{X}` at resolution |
| `PayXManaDealXDamageToAnyTargetEffect` | `(String manaCost)` | "you may pay `manaCost` (contains an {X}). If you do, it deals X damage to any target." The any-target is chosen when the ability goes on the stack (`targetSpec()` = harmful ANY_TARGET, so the Attack pipeline collects it); on resolution the controller chooses X (capped by `ManaCost.calculateMaxX`, which reserves the colored part of `manaCost`), pays `manaCost`, then deals X damage to that target. X=0 = decline. Flameblast Dragon (`"{X}{R}"`, ON_ATTACK). Implements `DamageDealingEffect` (`damageAmount()` = `XValue`). Do NOT use `MayPayManaEffect("{X}…", …)` — it can't pay/plumb `{X}` at resolution |
| `GainLifeEqualToToughnessEffect` | `()` | gain life equal to own/triggering creature's toughness (self, e.g. dies/enters trigger). NOT collapsed onto `GainLifeEffect(EventValue())`: each event site (own ETB, ally enters, damaged-creature dies) already materialises it to `GainLifeEffect(Fixed(<triggering card>.getToughness()))` at collection time — no stack `eventValue` to plumb, so folding it in would touch `EtbEffectContext` + three collectors for zero behaviour change. A `MayEffect(GainLifeEqualToToughnessEffect())` on `ON_ALLY_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` is likewise materialised to `MayEffect(GainLifeEffect(toughness))` in `EnterTriggerCollectorService.handleEnterMay` (e.g. Orchard Warden — "you may gain life equal to that creature's toughness") |
| `GainLifeEqualToTargetCreaturePowerEffect` | `()` | controller gains life equal to a single **target creature's** effective power (0 if no legal target). Declares `TargetSpec.benign(CREATURE)`, so unlike `GainLifeEffect(new TargetPower())` (whose target is established by a co-resolving targeted effect, e.g. Chastise's destroy) it can be the sole targeted effect of a triggered ability. `LifeGainEffect`. Wall of Reverence: `MayEffect(GainLifeEqualToTargetCreaturePowerEffect())` on `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` + `target(PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(creature you control))`; the target is chosen at resolution (queueMayAbility / `handleResolutionTimeTargetSelection`) |
| `GainLifeEqualToDamageDealtEffect` | `()` | gain life equal to damage dealt (lifelink-style, static). NOT collapsed onto `EventValue`: it is a `STATIC`-slot marker on an Aura (Spirit Link) scanned inline during combat-damage processing — there is no stack entry, so the `eventValue` channel (which lives on `StackEntry`) does not apply |
| `GainLifeEqualToControlledCreatureCombatDamageEffect` | `()` | "Whenever a creature you control deals combat damage, you gain that much life" — team-wide combat lifelink for an enchantment. `STATIC`-slot marker scanned inline in `CombatDamageService` over the per-creature `combatDamageDealt` map, so it fires on combat damage to any target (creatures/planeswalkers/players), once per matching enchantment the dealer's controller controls. Used by Noble Purpose. Contrast `AllyCombatDamageTriggerEffect` (players only, wraps a generic effect on the stack) |
| `TargetPlayerGainsLifeEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` / `(int amount)` | target player gains N life; `XValue` for "target player gains X life" (Stream of Life) |
| `EachTargetPlayerGainsLifeEffect` | `(int amount)` | each targeted player gains N life (multi-target, reads from `targetIds`). Pair with `setMinTargets(0)` and `setMaxTargets(99)` for "any number of target players". Used by Hunters' Feast |
| `DoubleTargetPlayerLifeEffect` | `()` | double target player's life total |
| `SetTargetPlayerLifeToHalfStartingEffect` | `()` | set target player's life total to half their starting life total, rounded down (e.g. Torgaar). Computes `GameData.STARTING_LIFE_TOTAL / 2` at resolution time. Uses `applySetLifeTotal` which respects can't-change-life, fires gain/loss triggers |
| `SetTargetPlayerLifeToSpecificValueEffect` | `(int targetLifeTotal)` | set target player's life total to an exact value (e.g. Vraska, Relic Seeker's −10 sets life to 1). Uses `applySetLifeTotal` which respects can't-change-life, fires gain/loss triggers |
| `SetEachPlayerLifeToHighestAmongPlayersEffect` | `()` | each player's life total becomes the highest life total among all players (e.g. Arbiter of Knollridge). Uses `applySetLifeTotal` per player, which respects can't-change-life / can't-gain-life and fires gain/loss triggers |
| `SetEachPlayerLifeToCreatureCountEffect` | `()` | each player's life total becomes the number of creatures they control (e.g. Biorhythm). Counts creatures per player via `GameQueryService.isCreature`; uses `applySetLifeTotal` per player, which respects can't-change-life / can't-gain-life and fires gain/loss triggers |
| `SetControllerLifeToAmountEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | non-targeting: set the effect's controller's life total to a computed amount ("your life total becomes N/that number"). `new Fixed(5)` for Form of the Dragon's end-step trigger; `new CardsInLibrary(CountScope.CONTROLLER)` for Invincible Hymn. Reads `entry.getControllerId()`, clamps negatives to 0. Uses `applySetLifeTotal` which respects can't-change-life, fires gain/loss triggers |
| `RebirthAnteEffect` | `()` | non-targeting ante spell: "Each player may ante the top card of their library. If a player does, that player's life total becomes 20." `normalfx/RebirthAnteEffectHandler` seeds one accept/decline `PendingMayAbility` per player in APNAP order (active player first; a player with an empty library has no top card and is skipped). `mayfx/RebirthAnteHandler` handles each accept: the top library card is anted (removed from the game, modelled as a move to exile — the ante-zone approximation shared with `TempestEfreetAnteExchangeEffect`) and the player's life is set to 20 via `applySetLifeTotal`. Rebirth |
| `ExchangeTargetPlayersLifeTotalsEffect` | `()` | two target players exchange life totals (multi-target player ability, reads targets from `targetIds`, `targetSpec().playerTargetCount()` = 2). CR 118.7: if either player's life can't change, the exchange doesn't occur. Works with both activated abilities (Soul Conduit) and upkeep triggers wrapped in MayEffect (Axis of Mortality) |
| `PsychicTransferEffect` | `()` | single-target-player spell (player-targeting spec): if the difference between the controller's life total and the target player's life total is 5 or less, the controller and target player exchange life totals (Psychic Transfer). Reads `entry.getControllerId()` + `entry.getTargetId()`. Same CR 118.7 / 119.7e can't-change / can't-gain handling as `ExchangeTargetPlayersLifeTotalsEffect` |
| `ExchangeLifeTotalWithCreatureStatEffect` | `(boolean usePower)` | exchange controller's life total with source creature's power (`usePower=true`, e.g. Evra) or toughness (`usePower=false`, e.g. Tree of Redemption) per CR 701.10e. Uses `sourcePermanentId` to find the creature. Player's life becomes creature's effective stat; creature's base stat is permanently set to former life total (layer 7b). Handles can't-change-life, can't-gain-life checks |
| `LoseLifeEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount, LoseLifeRecipient recipient, boolean controllerGainsLifeLost)`; sugar: `(int, recipient, boolean)`, `(DynamicAmount, recipient)`, `(int, recipient)`, `(int)` = `(Fixed, CONTROLLER, false)` | The whole life-loss family. `LoseLifeRecipient` routes who loses life (`CONTROLLER` / `TARGET_PLAYER` / `EACH_PLAYER` / `EACH_OPPONENT`, iterated over `orderedPlayerIds`); `controllerGainsLifeLost` drains the total life lost back to the controller (Blood Tithe / Chancellor of the Dross = `(3, EACH_OPPONENT, true)`; Exsanguinate = `(new XValue(), EACH_OPPONENT, true)`). Amount evaluated once at resolution — `EventValue()` for "equal to the life you gained" (Sanguine Bond, `(new EventValue(), TARGET_PLAYER)`, snapshotted by `MiscTriggerCollectorService`), `PermanentCount(HasSubtype(VAMPIRE), CONTROLLER)` for "1 life for each Vampire you control" (Bishop). the spec targets a player iff `recipient == TARGET_PLAYER`. Life loss is NOT damage (CR 118.2): CONTROLLER / EACH_* go through `LifeSupport.applyLifeLoss` (fires "loses life" triggers); TARGET_PLAYER is applied inline without firing those triggers (behaviour preserved verbatim) |
| `TargetPlayerLosesLifeEqualToPowerEffect` | `()` | ON_DEATH marker: target player loses life equal to dying creature's last-known power. `DeathTriggerCollectorService` bakes the power (`Permanent.getEffectivePower()`, clamped ≥0) into a `LoseLifeEffect(Fixed(power), TARGET_PLAYER)` at trigger time. NOT collapsed onto an amount: the value must use the dying permanent's own last-known P/T (`SourcePower` recomputes from the live battlefield, which differs after the creature is gone), and the targeted death path routes through a `DeathTriggerTarget` interaction that carries no event-value channel |
| `DealDamageOnSpellLifeGainEffect` | `(int damage, CardColor triggeringColor)` | ON_CONTROLLER_GAINS_LIFE marker: deals N damage to target creature or player when a spell of the specified color causes controller to gain life. Only triggers from instant/sorcery spell sources. MiscTriggerCollectorService queues a DealDamageToAnyTargetEffect via LifeGainTriggerAnyTarget. Used by Firesong and Sunspeaker |
| `CradleOfVitalityLifeGainEffect` | `(String manaCost)` | ON_CONTROLLER_GAINS_LIFE marker: "you may pay {manaCost}. If you do, put a +1/+1 counter on target creature for each 1 life you gained." MiscTriggerCollectorService queues the creature-only variant of `LifeGainTriggerAnyTarget` (`creaturesOnly=true`, no player targets) carrying `MayPayManaEffect(manaCost, PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, Fixed(lifeGained)))`. Counter count locked in at trigger time; "you may pay" resolved via the may-ability flow. Skipped when no creature is a legal target. Cradle of Vitality |
| _compose, no dedicated effect_ | `LoseLifeEffect(N, LoseLifeRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` + `GainLifeEffect(M)` | "target player loses N life and you gain M life" (fixed drain). Two effects on one slot; targeting auto-derives from the loss (benign PLAYER), controller gains the fixed M on resolution. Omit the `GainLifeEffect` for a pure "target player loses N life". The `TARGET_PLAYER` loss is applied inline and does NOT fire "loses life" triggers (pre-existing quirk). Used by Syphon Life, Soul Feast, Bleak Coven Vampires, Necrogen Censer (loss-only) |
| `DrainLifePerControlledPermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, int multiplier)` | target player loses X life, controller gains X life, where X = multiplier × matching permanents controlled (e.g. Tezzeret -4: twice artifacts) |
| `EnchantedCreatureControllerLosesLifeEffect` | `(int amount, UUID affectedPlayerId)` | enchanted creature's controller loses N life (trigger). Fixed-amount upkeep form is Numbing Dose. On the `ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD` slot the death collector re-bakes `amount` from the dying creature's last-known toughness (≥0) and `affectedPlayerId` from its controller — pass `(0)` in the card def (Banewasp Affliction) |
| `EnchantedControllerMayPayToPreventDamageEffect` | `(int amount)` | `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` (Power Leak): the enchanted permanent's controller (stack `targetId`, baked by `StepTriggerService`) may pay any amount of mana to prevent that much of `amount` damage dealt to them. Handler prompts that player for X via `XValueChoice` (capped at `amount`, since prevention beyond the damage is pointless), pays generic mana from their pool, then deals `amount − X` through `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` (so other prevention/replacement still applies). No payable mana ⇒ full `amount`, no prompt. `DamageDealingEffect` (players only) |
| `EachPlayerLosesFractionOfLifeRoundedUpEffect` | `(int divisor)` | each player loses 1/divisor of their life total, rounded up (e.g. divisor=3 for Dire Fleet Ravager) |
| `EachPlayerDiscardsFractionOfHandRoundedUpEffect` | `(int divisor)` | each player discards `ceil(handSize / divisor)` cards of their own choice, count recomputed per player against their own hand (APNAP, active player first). Rides the shared per-player discard queue via a variable-amount `DiscardFollowUp`, so different players discard different counts. divisor=3 for Pox |
| `EachPlayerSacrificesFractionRoundedUpEffect` | `(int divisor, PermanentPredicate filter)` | each player sacrifices `ceil(matching / divisor)` of the permanents they control matching `filter`, of their own choice, count recomputed per player. Uses the APNAP simultaneous forced-sacrifice flow (CR 101.4). divisor=3 with `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` / `PermanentIsLandPredicate` for Pox |
| `EachPlayerSacrificesDownToFewestEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | each player keeps a number of their `filter`-matching permanents equal to the fewest any player controls and sacrifices the rest, of their own choice. Same APNAP simultaneous forced-sacrifice flow (CR 101.4); when the minimum is 0 everyone sacrifices all matching permanents with no prompt. `PermanentIsLandPredicate` + `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` for Balance |
| `EachPlayerDiscardsDownToFewestEffect` | `()` | each player discards down to the smallest hand size across all players, of their own choice (APNAP; rides the variable-amount discard queue). Balance's discard step |
| `EachPlayerLosesLifePerCreatureControlledEffect` | `(int lifePerCreature, boolean attackingOnly)` | each player loses N life per creature they control; when `attackingOnly` is true only attacking creatures count (Batwing Brume), else all creatures (Stronghold Discipline) |
| `TapCreaturesGainLifePerCreatureEffect` | `(int lifePerCreature)` | tap any number of untapped creatures you control (multi-permanent choice), then controller gains lifePerCreature life for each creature tapped this way. No untapped creatures → does nothing. Handled via `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.TapCreaturesGainLife`. Used by Harmony of Nature (4) |
| `LoseLifeUnlessDiscardEffect` | `(int lifeLoss)` | target player loses N life unless they discard a card. Punisher choice made by the affected player. Place in `ON_OPPONENT_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Resolved via `PlayerInteractionResolutionService` → may ability prompt → discard choice or life loss |
| `DamageControllerUnlessDiscardThenTapSourceEffect` | `(int damage)` | UPKEEP_TRIGGERED drawback: the source deals N **damage** (normal damage path — prevention/redirection apply) to its controller unless they discard a card, then taps the source **iff** the damage actually landed (controller's life dropped) — "if it deals damage to you this way, tap it". Mishra's War Machine (3). Empty hand auto-applies the penalty. Distinct from `LoseLifeUnlessDiscardEffect` (life loss, no tap) and from `ForcedCostOrElseEffect` (whose `ForcedCostOrElseEffectHandler` doesn't support a discard cost — it would silently fall through to the penalty). Setup handler `DamageControllerUnlessDiscardThenTapSourceEffectHandler`; accept/decline in `MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService.handleDamageControllerUnlessDiscardThenTapChoice` |
| `LoseLifeUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int lifeLoss, int payAmount, CardPredicate spellFilter)` | target player loses N life unless they pay {M}. Optional `spellFilter` restricts which spells trigger it (null = any). Place in `ON_OPPONENT_CASTS_SPELL` slot. If player can't pay, auto-applies life loss. Otherwise prompts via may ability. Convenience ctor: `(int lifeLoss, int payAmount)` sets filter to null |
| `RegisterLoseLifeAtNextDrawStepUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int lifeLoss, int payAmount)` | `ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` (Nafs Asp, `(1, 1)`): registers a `LoseLifeAtNextDrawStepUnlessPays` delayed action against the damaged player (baked in as `targetId` via `CombatDamageTriggerContextEffect.DAMAGED_PLAYER`). Drained at that player's next draw step in `StepTriggerService.handleDrawStepTriggers` as a `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(PayManaCost("{payAmount}"), [LoseLifeEffect(lifeLoss)], true)` "you may pay {payAmount}; if you don't, lose lifeLoss life" prompt controlled by that player. Life loss, not damage — won't re-trigger. | `DiscardHandUnlessPaysLifeEffect` | `(int lifeCost)` | target player discards their entire hand unless they pay `lifeCost` life. Punisher choice made by the target player (player-targeting spec; pair with `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter`). A target that can't pay (life < cost, or life can't change) discards immediately; otherwise prompts via may ability. Used by Tyrannize (7 life). | `StealDyingOpponentPermanentUnlessPaysLifeEffect` | `(int lifeCost)` | triggered punisher (`ControlStealingEffect`, PERMANENT): a permanent of any type an opponent controls was put into a graveyard from the battlefield — that opponent may pay `lifeCost` life, else the ability's controller puts that card onto the battlefield under their control (tracked as a stolen permanent, so it returns to its owner on death). Used by Prince of Thralls (3 life) |
| `TapTargetCreatureUnlessControllerPaysLifeEffect` | `(int lifeCost)` | targeted activated-ability punisher: tap the target creature unless its controller pays `lifeCost` life. The decision belongs to the **target creature's controller** (baked onto the pending may-ability's `controllerId`; the target permanent id rides in `targetCardId`) — a payable controller is prompted via the may-ability system, one who can't pay (too little life / life can't change) has the creature tapped immediately. `benign(TargetCategory.CREATURE)`; pair the ability with a `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` target filter. Reuses the normal tap path (`TapPermanentsEffect(TARGET)`, fires "becomes tapped" triggers). | `TormentOfHailfireEffect` | `(int lifeLoss)` | SPELL — "Repeat X times. Each opponent loses `lifeLoss` life unless that player sacrifices a nonland permanent of their choice or discards a card." X = `entry.getXValue()`. Per opponent per iteration (APNAP), a three-way `ColorChoice` list-pick (`ChoiceContext.TormentPenaltyChoice`) pruned to what the player can do (life always offered); "lose life" applies inline, "sacrifice" runs a `PermanentChoiceContext.TormentSacrifice` nonland-permanent pick, "discard" runs a 1-card discard. One-opponent-at-a-time loop over `GameData.torment` (`TormentState`), re-running the effect after each sub-choice via `rerunCurrentEffectAfterInteraction` (same shape as `EachPlayerMayDiscardUpToThenTakeDamageEffectHandler`/Illicit Auction). Handler `TormentOfHailfireEffectHandler`; penalty pick in `ChoiceHandlerService.handleTormentPenaltyChoice`, sacrifice completion in `PermanentChoiceBattlefieldHandlerService.handleTormentSacrifice`. Torment of Hailfire (`3`) |
| `DamageUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int damage, int payAmount, CardPredicate spellFilter)` | source permanent deals N damage to the triggering player unless they pay {M} — the **damage** counterpart of `LoseLifeUnlessPaysEffect` (routed through the normal damage system, so prevention/redirection/protection/infect apply). `DamageDealingEffect`. Optional `spellFilter` (null = any). Place in `ON_OPPONENT_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Can't-pay auto-applies the damage (reusing the `DealDamageToPlayersEffect(TARGET_PLAYER)` path); otherwise prompts via may ability. | `DiscardHandUnlessPaysLifeEffect` | `(int lifeCost)` | target player discards their entire hand unless they pay `lifeCost` life. A target that can't pay (life < cost, or life can't change) discards immediately; otherwise prompts via may ability. Used by Tyrannize (7 life). Handler: `DiscardHandUnlessPaysLifeEffectHandler`; choice in `MayPenaltyChoiceHandlerService` |
| `SpellCastLifeDrainEffect` | `(int lifeLoss, int lifeGain, CardPredicate spellFilter)` | drain-on-cast: whenever an opponent casts a matching spell, that player loses `lifeLoss` life and the source's controller gains `lifeGain` life. Place in `ON_OPPONENT_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Optional `spellFilter` (null = any). Thin trigger descriptor — the collector stamps the casting opponent on `targetId` and builds the decomposed drain (`LoseLifeEffect(lifeLoss, TARGET_PLAYER)` + `GainLifeEffect(lifeGain)`, gain step omitted when `lifeGain` is 0). Yawgmoth's Edict (1, 1, white) |

## Poison counters

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `GivePoisonCountersEffect` | `(int amount, PoisonRecipient recipient)`, `(int amount, PoisonRecipient recipient, CardPredicate spellFilter)` or `(int amount, PoisonRecipient recipient, CardPredicate spellFilter, UUID affectedPlayerId)` | give N poison counters, routed by `PoisonRecipient` {CONTROLLER (self-poison, e.g. Phyrexian Vatmother upkeep), TARGET_PLAYER (targets a player; with `spellFilter` doubles as an `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` trigger descriptor firing when the controller casts a matching spell, resolving into a `spellFilter == null` copy — Hand of the Praetors), EACH_PLAYER (every player incl. controller, e.g. Ichor Rats ETB), ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER (`ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED` slot; `affectedPlayerId` is null in the card def and baked in at trigger time by `MiscTriggerCollectorService.handleEnchantedPermanentTapPoison` — Relic Putrescence)}. All placement routes through the central `LifeSupport.applyPoisonCounters` path (respects `PlayerCantGetPoisonCountersEffect` suppression) |
| `GiveControllerPoisonCountersOnTargetDeathThisTurnEffect` | `(int amount)` | delayed trigger: registers the target creature so that when it dies this turn, its controller gets N poison counters. Reads target from stack entry's `targetId`. Tracking in `GameData.creatureGivingControllerPoisonOnDeathThisTurn`, cleared at end of turn |
| `ReturnTargetCardOnDeathThisTurnEffect` | `()` / `(boolean enterTapped)` | SPELL delayed trigger: registers the target creature so that when it dies this turn, that card returns to the battlefield (tapped when `enterTapped`) under its owner's control. Reads target from stack entry's `targetId`; tracking in `GameData.creaturesReturnedToBattlefieldOnDeathThisTurn` (card ID → tapped flag, cleared at end of turn). The death pipeline pushes a `ReturnTriggeringCardFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect(enterTapped)` triggered ability. No-arg = untapped (Graceful Reprieve); `true` = tapped (Supernatural Stamina) |
| `ReturnTriggeringCardFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | triggered-ability effect: returns the stack entry's card from its owner's graveyard to the battlefield under its owner's control (fizzles if no longer in a graveyard). Pushed by the death pipeline for `ReturnTargetCardOnDeathThisTurnEffect`. Not added directly to a card |
| `CreateTokenOnTargetDeathThisTurnEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect token)` | SPELL delayed trigger: registers the target creature so that when it dies this turn, the effect's controller creates `token`'s token(s). Reads target from stack entry's `targetId`; tracking in `GameData.creatureCreatingTokenOnDeathThisTurn` (map of `DelayedTokenOnDeath`, cleared at end of turn). The death pipeline pushes a triggered ability resolving the wrapped `CreateTokenEffect` under the recorded controller. Pair with `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect`. Used by Skeletonize |

## Win / lose game

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `TargetPlayerLosesGameEffect` | `(UUID playerId)` | target player loses the game |
| `ControllerLosesGameEffect` | `()` | the controller of the resolving ability loses the game (non-targeting; resolves against the stack entry's controller, so usable by state-triggered / dynamic-controller abilities like Immortal Coil's empty-graveyard loss). Respects can't-lose (Platinum Angel). Handled by `ControllerLosesGameEffectHandler` |
| `LoseGameIfNotCastFromHandEffect` | `()` | lose the game if not cast from hand (ETB check) |
| `WinGameEffect` | `()` | controller wins the game (use inside conditional wrappers like `ConditionalEffect(new ControlsPermanentCount(minCount, filter), wrapped)`) |
| `WinGameIfCreaturesInGraveyardEffect` | `(int threshold)` | win if N+ creature cards in graveyard |
| `WinGameOnEmptyLibraryDrawEffect` | `()` | static: if controller would draw from empty library, they win the game instead (Laboratory Maniac). Checked in `DrawService.performDrawCard()` |
| `ApproachOfTheSecondSunEffect` | `()` | Approach of the Second Sun (SPELL slot, no target). On resolution: if the spell was cast from hand (`sourceZone == HAND`) and the controller has cast 2+ spells with this card's name this game (`GameData.getSpellsCastThisGameByNameCount`), delegates to `WinGameEffectHandler` (so the can't-lose guard applies). Otherwise gains 7 life and sets `StackEntry.putIntoLibraryPositionAfterResolving = 6`, so `StackResolutionService.handleSpellDisposition` tucks it seventh from the top of its owner's library instead of the graveyard |
| `CantHaveCountersEffect` | `()` | this permanent can't have counters put on it (static) |
| `CountersCantBePlacedEffect` | `()` | Solemnity: "Players can't get counters. Counters can't be put on artifacts, creatures, enchantments, or lands." STATIC global lock queried at both counter chokepoints — `GameQueryService.cantHaveCounters()` (permanent clause, restricted to artifact/creature/enchantment/land so planeswalkers still get loyalty) and `canPlayerGetPoisonCounters()` (player clause). Also replaces "enters with N counters" via `BattlefieldEntryService` |
| `CantHaveMinusOneMinusOneCountersEffect` | `()` | this creature can't have -1/-1 counters put on it (granted via GrantEffectEffect). Checked by `GameQueryService.cantHaveMinusOneMinusOneCounters()` |
| `ReduceMinusOneMinusOneCountersEffect` | `()` | Vizier of Remedies: "If one or more -1/-1 counters would be put on a creature you control, that many -1/-1 counters minus one are put on it instead." STATIC replacement marker on the source itself (NOT granted, unlike `CantHaveMinusOneMinusOneCountersEffect`). Every -1/-1 placement site routes its count through `GameQueryService.reduceMinusOneMinusOneCounters(gameData, controller/permanent, count)`, which counts the affected creature's controller's markers and subtracts one per marker (floored at zero; a count ≤ 0 is unchanged). Covers targeted/source/each-controlled/each-matching/self-transform placements, wither & infect damage (combat and noncombat), end-of-combat scheduled counters, put-counter activation costs (Devoted Druid), proliferate, "enters with -1/-1 counters", persist return, and prevent-and-add-counters (Phyrexian Hydra). Multiple copies stack |
| `PlayerCantGetPoisonCountersEffect` | `()` | controller can't get poison counters (static on source permanent). Checked at all poison counter application points |
| `RemoveKeywordEffect` | `(Keyword keyword, GrantScope scope)` or `(Keyword keyword, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` | static: creatures in scope lose the specified keyword. Added to `removedKeywords` in static bonus computation. Also works as one-shot in activated abilities and triggered abilities with SELF/TARGET scope: adds keyword to `Permanent.removedKeywords` (cleared at end of turn). the spec targets a permanent for TARGET scope, so it routes through the trigger-target pipelines (e.g. `MayEffect(RemoveKeywordEffect(FLYING, TARGET))` on `ON_ATTACK` — Kinscaer Harpoonist) |
| `LosesAllAbilitiesEffect` | `(GrantScope scope)` or `(GrantScope scope, EffectDuration duration)` | Creatures in scope lose all abilities (keywords, activated, triggered, static). With `EffectDuration.CONTINUOUS` (default): static effect for auras/equipment, resolved by `LosesAllAbilitiesEffectHandler` in `staticfx`. With `EffectDuration.UNTIL_END_OF_TURN`: one-shot effect resolved by `KeywordGrantResolutionService` — creates a floating `L6_ABILITIES` continuous effect whose CR 613.7 timestamp drives ordering (a keyword grant with a LATER timestamp than the lose-all sticks), and dual-writes `Permanent.losesAllAbilitiesUntilEndOfTurn` (cleared by `resetModifiers()`) for direct intrinsic readers. Scope: `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, `TARGET`, etc. |
| `CantLoseGameEffect` | `()` | you can't lose and opponents can't win (static). Read by `GameQueryService.canPlayerLoseGame` both as a battlefield STATIC effect (Platinum Angel) and off emblems, including when wrapped in a `ConditionalEffect` (Gideon of the Trials' emblem — only while its controller controls a Gideon) |
| `ControllerLosesGameOnLeavesEffect` | `()` | "When this permanent leaves the battlefield, you lose the game." Fires on any departure (destroy, exile, bounce, sacrifice, tuck). Slot: `ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` |
| `CantLoseGameFromLifeEffect` | `()` | you don't lose the game for having 0 or less life, but can still lose from poison or other effects (static) |
| `ReplaceControllerLossWithGameResetEffect` | `()` | Lich's Mirror: if you would lose the game, instead shuffle your hand, graveyard, and all permanents you own into your library, draw 7, and your life total becomes 20 (static replacement). One-shot — the source shuffles itself away; poison counters are NOT reset. Consulted at every rules-loss source via `GameOutcomeService.replaceLossWithGameReset`, executed by `LichsMirrorResetService`. No stack handler (queried like `CantLoseGameEffect`). |
| `DamageDealtAsInfectBelowZeroLifeEffect` | `()` | as long as you have 0 or less life, all damage dealt to you is dealt as though its source had infect (static) |
| `DamageCantReduceLifeBelowOneEffect` | `()` | Worship: while you control a creature, damage that would reduce your life total below 1 reduces it to 1 instead. Damage-only (not life loss/payment/poison); full damage is still dealt (lifelink/triggers see it), only the life-total reduction is capped. The "control a creature" condition is enforced by `GameQueryService.damageCantReduceLifeBelowOne` (static) |
| `LifeTotalCantChangeEffect` | `()` | controller's life total can't change (static) |
| `PlayersCantGainLifeEffect` | `()` | no player can gain life (static, global — checked on any battlefield) |
| `TargetPlayerCantGainLifeRestOfGameEffect` | `()` | non-targeting ability effect: the stack entry's target player (e.g. the damaged player of an `ON_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` trigger) can't gain life for the rest of the game. Persists via `GameData.playersWhoCantGainLifeRestOfGame`; enforced by `GameQueryService.canPlayerGainLife`. Used by Stigma Lasher |
| `DoubleLifeGainEffect` | `()` | static replacement: the controller's life gain is doubled (Boon Reflection). `GameQueryService.lifeGainMultiplier` counts the player's controlled doublers and `LifeSupport.applyGainLife`/`applySetLifeTotal` multiply the amount by 2^count (multiple copies stack multiplicatively) |
| `PlayersCantCastSpellsFromZonesEffect` | `(Set<Zone> zones)` | no player can cast spells from any zone in `zones` (static, global — prevents flashback, graveyard cast, library-top cast, etc.; does not prevent playing lands). Only `GRAVEYARD` and `LIBRARY` are enforced. Checked via `GameQueryService.canPlayersCastSpellsFromZone(gameData, zone)`. Ashes of the Abhorrent passes `Set.of(GRAVEYARD)`; Grafdigger's Cage passes `Set.of(GRAVEYARD, LIBRARY)` |
| `CardsCantEnterBattlefieldFromZonesEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, Set<Zone> zones)` | cards matching `filter` (null = all cards) can't enter the battlefield from any zone in `zones` (static, global — blocks reanimation/undying via the guarded graveyard-return helpers, the graveyard-choice BATTLEFIELD path, and `placeCardsOnBattlefieldSimultaneously` library searches; the blocked card stays in its zone). Only `GRAVEYARD` and `LIBRARY` are enforced; other zones silently do nothing. Checked via `GameQueryService.isCardBlockedFromEnteringFromZone(gameData, card, zone)`. Does not affect tokens or entry from hand/exile. Grafdigger's Cage passes `CardTypePredicate(CREATURE)` and `Set.of(GRAVEYARD, LIBRARY)` |
| `PlayersCantActivateAbilitiesOfGraveyardCardsEffect` | `()` | no player can activate abilities of cards in graveyards (static, global — checked in AbilityActivationService) |
| `ActivateCreatureAbilitiesAsThoughHasteEffect` | `()` | the controller may activate abilities (including tap abilities) of creatures they control as though those creatures had haste — lifts the summoning-sickness restriction on ability activation only (does NOT grant haste, so the creatures still can't attack). Static, per-controller — checked in `AbilityActivationService` via `GameQueryService.canActivateCreatureAbilitiesAsThoughHaste(gameData, playerId)`. Used by Thousand-Year Elixir |
| `SpendWhiteManaAsRedEffect` | `()` | the controller may spend white mana as though it were red mana (Sunglasses of Urza). Permission only — white mana keeps its color but may also pay red pips. Surfaced as a per-player flag on `ManaPool` (`isWhiteSpendableAsRed`) that `ManaCost.canPay`/`pay` honor (a guarded branch that leaves the ordinary path untouched); set from `GameQueryService.canSpendWhiteManaAsRed(gameData, playerId)` in `SpellCastingService`/`AbilityActivationService` payment and `GameBroadcastService` playability |
| `DamageCantBePreventedEffect` | `()` | damage can't be prevented by any means (static, global — bypasses shields, protection damage, color prevention) |
| `AllDamageDealtWithWitherEffect` | `()` | all damage is dealt as though its source had wither (static, global — every source deals creature damage as -1/-1 counters; player damage stays normal life loss). Checked in `GameQueryService.dealsCounterDamageToCreatures`/`sourceDealsCounterDamageToCreatures`. Used by Everlasting Torment |
| `NoncombatDamageToOpponentCreaturesAsMinusCountersEffect` | `()` | STATIC replacement: if a source the controller controls would deal **noncombat** damage to a creature an opponent controls, put that many -1/-1 counters on it instead (combat damage unaffected). Like wither the damage is still "dealt" (damage triggers/deathtouch/lifelink see it). Checked in `GameQueryService.noncombatDamageToOpponentCreatureAsCounters`, applied on the noncombat path in `DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage` (combat path is separate, so no combat check needed). Used by Soul-Scar Mage |
| `DamageCantBePreventedThisTurnEffect` | `()` | one-shot: for the rest of the turn, damage can't be prevented. Sets `GameData.damageCantBePreventedThisTurn` (consulted by `GameQueryService.isDamagePreventable`, cleared at turn cleanup). Used by Impractical Joke |
| `AllowExtraLoyaltyActivationEffect` | `()` | you may activate loyalty abilities of planeswalkers you control twice each turn rather than only once (static). Checked in `AbilityActivationService.validateAndPayLoyaltyCost()` via `GameQueryService.hasExtraLoyaltyActivation()`. Used by Oath of Teferi |

## Creature pump / boost

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `SetBasePowerToughnessEffect` | `(int power, int toughness, GrantScope scope)`; `(int power, int toughness)` → `GrantScope.TARGET` | set base P/T (modifiers still apply on top, CR 613 layer 7b). `scope == TARGET`: one-shot, sets target creature's base P/T **until end of turn** (Diminish, Quandrix Charm). `scope == SELF`: one-shot on the source, **until end of turn**, for a non-targeting self ability (Marsh Flitter). Any other scope (`ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, …): continuous STATIC (Deep Freeze, Darksteel Mutation). Every setter is a CR 613 sublayer-7b entry ordered by timestamp — one-shot resolutions create a floating 7b effect (per-target for the mass setter, locking the affected set per CR 611.2c) and dual-write the legacy `Permanent` UEOT override fields for last-known-information/direct readers; the latest-timestamp setter wins and beats any 7a CDA in layer order. |
| `SetAllUnblockedCreaturesBasePowerToughnessEffect` | `(int power, int toughness)` | set base P/T of **every unblocked creature (any player's)** until end of turn (CR 613 layer 7b, modifiers apply on top). "Unblocked" = attacking + no creature blocking it, evaluated and locked in at resolution (CR 611.2c); creatures that become unblocked later aren't affected. Same floating-7b + legacy-field dual-write mechanics as the mass own-creatures setter. Inkfathom Witch |
| `GrantBaseStatsToCounterBearersEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int power, int toughness, Set<Keyword> keywords)` | resolves (one-shot) into a **game-wide continuous rule**: every creature with a `counterType` counter has base P/T `power`/`toughness` (CR 613 layer 7b) and the given `keywords` (layer 6), for as long as it holds such a counter. The handler adds two **source-independent** `FloatingContinuousEffect`s (a `SetBasePowerToughnessEffect` and a `GrantKeywordEffect`) with `sourcePermanentId == null`, `EffectDuration.PERMANENT`, and `scope == PermanentHasCountersPredicate(counterType)`: the layered pass re-evaluates the scope every pass, so the rule persists after the creating card leaves the battlefield (official ruling) and lapses the instant the counter is removed. Idempotent — a second copy of the source establishes nothing new. Install once in `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`; pair with an upkeep `MayEffect(PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect(counterType))` + `target(creature)`. Aven Mimeomancer (feather counter → base 3/1 + flying). **Not a targeted effect** (`targetSpec()` NONE); the counter comes from a separate targeted trigger. Requires the `counterType` to be handled in `PermanentHasCountersPredicate` (both the `PredicateEvaluationService` and `StaticEffectSupport` switches) and in `PermanentCounterSupport.placeCounterOnPermanent`. |
| `SwitchPowerToughnessEffect` | `()` | switch target creature's power and toughness until end of turn. Each resolution adds one floating `L7D_SWITCH_PT` effect (no `Permanent` field — two switches cancel via parity); the layered queries (`GameQueryService.getEffectivePower/getEffectiveToughness`) compute full pre-switch P/T through 7c and swap the finished values (CR 613.4d), so asymmetric boosts follow the pre-switch component. `Permanent.getEffectivePower()` is intrinsic and pre-switch |
| `BoostTargetCreatureEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost[, PermanentPredicate filter])` — convenience `(int, int)` / `(int, int, PermanentPredicate)` ctors wrap in `Fixed` | target creature gets +X/+Y until end of turn. Optional `filter` narrows the `targetSpec()` predicate ("target creature an opponent controls gets -2/-0" — Ominous Sphinx's cycle/discard trigger, `AllOf(IsCreature, Not(ControlledBySourceController))`); `null` = plain "target creature". **All "target creature gets +N/+M …" wordings, including "for each …", "+X/+X" (X paid), and "where X is …", use this one effect with `DynamicAmount` parameters** — the amount evaluates against the SOURCE (effect controller), so counting contexts refer to the controller, not the pumped target. Examples: `(new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER), same)` "+X/+X where X = creatures you control" (Elder of Laurels); `(new XValue(), new Fixed(0))` "+X/+0" (Kessig Wolf Run), `(new XValue(), new XValue())` "+X/+X" (Untamed Might); `(new Sum(new Fixed(1), new CardsInGraveyard(new CardNamedPredicate("Ancestral Anger"), CountScope.CONTROLLER)), new Fixed(0))` "+X/+0 where X is 1 plus the number of cards named Ancestral Anger in your graveyard" (Ancestral Anger; count at resolution — the spell is not yet in the graveyard) |
| `BoostSelfEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost)` — convenience `(int, int)` ctor wraps in `Fixed` | this creature gets +X/+Y. One-shot (until end of turn) in triggered/activated slots, continuous when placed in `STATIC` (selfOnly static handler). **All "gets +N/+M for each …" wordings use this one effect with `DynamicAmount` parameters** — see the Dynamic amounts section.
