Examples: `(new PermanentCount(new PermanentIsArtifactPredicate(), CountScope.CONTROLLER), new Fixed(0))` "+1/+0 for each artifact you control" (Hellkite Igniter, Karn token, Deadeye Plunderers); `PermanentCount(..., CONTROLLER, true)` "+1/+0 for each *other* Rat you control" (Rat Colony); `PermanentCount(..., OPPONENTS)` "for each creature your opponents control" (Scourge of Geier Reach); `PermanentCount(new PermanentIsEnchantmentPredicate(), ANY_PLAYER)` "for each enchantment on the battlefield" (Yavimaya Enchantress); `PermanentCount(AllOf(IsAttacking, HasSubtype(PIRATE)), CONTROLLER, true)` "for each other attacking Pirate" (Dire Fleet Captain, ON_ATTACK); `CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(LAND), CONTROLLER)` "for each land card in your graveyard" (Multani); `Scaled(new AttachmentsOnSource(true, true), 2)` "+2/+2 for each Aura and Equipment attached" (Champion of the Flame; equipment-only: `AttachmentsOnSource(false, true)`, Goblin Gaveleer); `CreaturesBlockingSource()` "for each creature blocking it" (Elvish Berserker, ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED); `OpponentPoisonCounters()` (Mycosynth Fiend); `ImprintedCreaturePower()`/`ImprintedCreatureToughness()` (Phyrexian Ingester); `XValue()` "+X/+0 where X is the mana spent to cast that spell" inside `SpellCastTriggerEffect` — the trigger collector snapshots `xValue` for any amount that references X (Aberrant Manawurm) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new SpellManaSpentAtLeast(minMana), wrapped)` | see construction shape | wraps a resolved effect inside `SpellCastTriggerEffect`; resolves only if at least `minMana` was spent to cast the triggering spell. Trigger collector snapshots mana spent into stack entry `xValue`. Used by Colorstorm Stallion (5+ mana → `CreateTokenCopyOfSourceEffect`) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new SpellXAtLeast(minX), wrapped)` | `SPELL` slot (or ability) | resolves `wrapped` only if the resolving spell/ability's chosen `X` (read off the stack entry's `xValue`) is at least `minX`. Martial Coup ("If X is 5 or more, destroy all other creatures"). Distinct from `SpellManaSpentAtLeast`, which reads mana spent, not X |
| `ConditionalEffect(new ColorSpentToCast(ManaColor.X), wrapped)` | `SPELL` slot | resolves `wrapped` only if at least one mana of color `X` was spent to cast this spell (generic paid with that color counts). Payment snapshots the set of colors spent into `GameData.spellCastColorsSpent`; condition read back at resolution via `sourceCard` id. Use one wrapper per gated clause of a hybrid spell (e.g. Repel Intruders: `{W}`→create tokens, `{U}`→`CounterSpellEffect`; "do both if {W}{U} was spent" falls out for free). A targeted clause pairs with `target(filter, 0, 1)` since `registerEffectTargetIndex` unwraps the conditional |
| `IncrementTriggerEffect` | `()` | Increment keyword (SOS). **Keyword-driven — do NOT add to a card.** Any creature with the Scryfall-loaded `Keyword.INCREMENT` automatically triggers via `TriggerCollectionService.collectIncrementTriggers`: whenever its controller casts a spell, if the mana spent is greater than the source's current power **or** toughness, put a +1/+1 counter on it. The collector snapshots mana spent into the stack entry `xValue` and does the intervening-if check at trigger time; this effect is the resolution entry whose handler re-checks against current P/T (CR 603.4). Self-targeting. Used by Ambitious Augmenter |
| `DoubleSelfPowerToughnessEffect` | `()` | double this creature's power and toughness until end of turn. Per CR 701.9a/b, adds current effective P/T as modifier |
| `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost)` or `(…, PermanentPredicate filter)` — convenience `(int, int)` / `(int, int, PermanentPredicate)` ctors wrap in `Fixed` | all your creatures get +X/+Y until end of turn (one-shot). Optional predicate filter. **The amount is evaluated ONCE at resolution (before any boost lands) and applied uniformly** — so power-derived amounts don't inflate as earlier boosts raise the max. Examples: `(new GreatestPowerAmongControlled(), new GreatestPowerAmongControlled())` "+X/+X where X = greatest power among creatures you control" (Overwhelming Stampede); `(new CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CONTROLLER), same)` "+X/+X where X = creature cards in your graveyard" (Garruk, the Veil-Cursed) |
| `BoostAllCreaturesEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost)` or `(…, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(…, PermanentPredicate filter, EachPermanentScope scope)` — convenience `(int, int)` / `(int, int, PermanentPredicate)` / `(int, int, EachPermanentScope)` ctors wrap in `Fixed` | creatures get +X/+Y until end of turn (one-shot). Optional predicate filter. `EachPermanentScope` selects whose battlefield: `ALL_PLAYERS` (default) iterates every player's battlefield (unlike `BoostAllOwnCreaturesEffect`); `TARGET_PLAYER` affects only the targeted player's creatures ("creatures target player controls get +X/+Y", player-targeting spec, e.g. Shields of Velis Vel — pair with `GrantKeywordEffect(CHANGELING, GrantScope.TARGET_PLAYERS_CREATURES)`). Amount evaluated once at resolution. Examples: `(new Scaled(new XValue(), -1), new Scaled(new XValue(), -1))` "all creatures get -X/-X where X was paid" (Ichor Explosion); `(new XValue(), new Scaled(new XValue(), -1))` "+X/-X" (Flowstone Slide) |
| `StaticBoostEffect` | `(int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost, Set<Keyword> grantedKeywords, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` | unified static boost: +X/+Y and keywords with predicate-based filtering. Scope: `OWN_CREATURES`, `OPPONENT_CREATURES`, `ALL_CREATURES`, `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, `ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES`. With `GrantScope.ENCHANTED_CREATURE` it works as an aura boost (enchanted creature gets +X/+Y), with `GrantScope.EQUIPPED_CREATURE` it works as an equipment boost (equipped creature gets +X/+Y), and with `GrantScope.ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES` it affects creatures controlled by the enchanted player (for Curses). Filter: optional `PermanentPredicate` (color, subtype, not, etc). Convenience constructors: `(p, t, scope)`, `(p, t, scope, filter)`, `(p, t, keywords, scope)` |
| `BoostCreaturesOfChosenColorEffect` | `(int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost)` | static: creatures you control of the source permanent's chosen color get +X/+Y. The chosen color is stored on the permanent at runtime via `Permanent.getChosenColor()`. Used by Caged Sun |
| `AllNonlandPermanentsAreChosenColorEffect` | `()` | static layer-5 color setter (CR 105.3): every nonland permanent (any controller, including the source itself) becomes the source's chosen color, replacing its other colors. Chosen color read from `Permanent.getChosenColor()` — pair with `ChooseColorOnEnterEffect`. Two handlers (normal + `selfOnly`) so the source enchantment is colored too. Used by Shifting Sky |
| `AllPermanentsGainChosenColorEffect` | `()` | static layer-5 additive color grant (CR 105.3): every permanent (any controller, including lands and the source itself) *gains* the source's chosen color in addition to its other colors (does not replace). Chosen color read from `Permanent.getChosenColor()` — pair with `ChooseColorOnEnterEffect`. Two handlers (normal + `selfOnly`) so the source is colored too. Battlefield permanents only — spells on the stack and cards in other zones are not recolored. Used by Painter's Servant |
| `BoostCreaturesOfChosenSubtypeEffect` | `(int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost[, CounterType scalingCounter[, boolean allControllers]])` | static: creatures of the source permanent's chosen subtype get +X/+Y. The chosen subtype is stored on the permanent at runtime via `Permanent.getChosenSubtype()`. When `scalingCounter` is non-null the boost is multiplied by the count of that counter type on the source ("+1/+1 for each charge counter" — Door of Destinies with `CounterType.CHARGE`); `null`/2-arg = flat boost (Vanquisher's Banner). `allControllers=false` (default) boosts only creatures you control; `allControllers=true` boosts every creature of the chosen type regardless of controller, including the source itself if it is a creature of that type (Brass Herald = `(1, 1, null, true)`) |
| `AttachedBoostEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost, GrantScope scope)` | static: the attached creature (Aura/Equipment) gets +X/+Y where the amounts are `DynamicAmount`s. Scope: `ENCHANTED_CREATURE` or `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`. The attached-scope sibling of `BoostSelfEffect` — collapsed the whole `BoostCreaturePer*` family. Amounts evaluate against the Aura/Equipment's controller (CR 109.5), so `CountScope.CONTROLLER` = "you"/"you control". Examples: `+X/+X` per creature card in all graveyards `(CardsInGraveyard(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), ANY_PLAYER), same, EQUIPPED_CREATURE)` (Bonehoard); per creature card in your graveyard uses `CONTROLLER` (Wreath of Geists); `+X/+0` instants+sorceries in your graveyard uses `(CardsInGraveyard(anyOf(INSTANT,SORCERY), CONTROLLER), Fixed(0), …)` (Runechanter's Pike); `+1/+1` per land you control `(PermanentCount(PermanentIsLandPredicate, CONTROLLER), same, …)` (Blackblade Reforged); per basic-land subtype you control `(PermanentCount(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(FOREST), CONTROLLER), same, …)` (Blanchwood Armor, Lashwrithe, Armored Ascension); `-1/-1` per Swamp uses `Scaled(…, -1)` (Quag Sickness); `+1/+1` per matching-name land `(LandsMatchingImprintedName(), same, …)` (Strata Scythe) |
| `BoostByOtherCreaturesWithSameNameEffect` | `(int powerPerCreature, int toughnessPerCreature)` | +X/+Y per other creature with same name (static) |
| `BoostBySharedCreatureTypeEffect` | `()` | +1/+1 for each other creature sharing a creature type (static) |
| `BoostOwnCreaturesByManaSymbolEffect` | `(ManaColor manaColor, int powerPerSymbol, int toughnessPerSymbol)` | chroma anthem: each creature you control gets +powerPerSymbol/+toughnessPerSymbol for each mana symbol of `manaColor` in its own mana cost (static). Hybrid ({G/W}) and Phyrexian ({W/P}) symbols of that color each count once (via `ManaCost.countColorSymbols`). Used by Light from Within `(ManaColor.WHITE, 1, 1)` |
| `BoostOtherMulticoloredCreaturesByColorCountEffect` | `(int powerPerColor, int toughnessPerColor)` | anthem: each *other* multicolored creature you control gets +powerPerColor/+toughnessPerColor for each of its colors (static). Monocolored/colorless creatures and the source permanent itself get nothing; the color count is layer-5-aware (respects color-changing effects). Used by Knight of New Alara `(1, 1)` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new AnyPlayerControlsPermanent(filter), wrapped)` | see construction shape | conditional wrapper: "as long as any player controls a permanent matching [filter]". Wraps StaticBoostEffect, GrantKeywordEffect, ProtectionFromColorsEffect, or GrantEffectEffect (selfOnly handler). Use `PermanentColorInPredicate(Set.of(...))` for color cases. Used by Knight of Malice and Knight of Grace |
| `BoostSelfWhenBlockingKeywordEffect` | `(Keyword requiredKeyword, int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost)` | +X/+Y when blocking a creature with the required keyword (e.g. flying). Place in `ON_BLOCK` slot. CombatService converts to BoostSelfEffect at trigger time |
| `BoostSelfWhenCombatOpponentMatchesEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate opponentFilter, int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost)` | "Whenever this creature blocks or becomes blocked by one or more [filter] creatures, it gets +X/+Y until end of turn." Place in `ON_BLOCK` and/or `ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED` (plain, non-PER_BLOCKER). Non-targeting — the trigger always goes on the stack; `BoostSelfWhenCombatOpponentMatchesEffectHandler` gathers this creature's combat opponents (creatures it is blocking + creatures blocking it, read from the still-intact blocking relationships during the declare-blockers step) and applies the boost only if at least one matches `opponentFilter`. Fires once regardless of how many match. Dwarven Soldier (`PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(ORC)`, +0/+2) |
| `TapSubtypeBoostSelfAndDamageDefenderEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | when this creature attacks, you may tap any number of untapped creatures of subtype you control → gets +X/+0 until end of turn and deals X damage to defending player. Place in `ON_ATTACK` slot. Prompts multi-permanent choice for eligible untapped creatures |
| `BoostSelfEffect` + `RemoveKeywordEffect(kw, SELF)` | _compose, no dedicated effect_ | "gets +X/+Y and loses a keyword until end of turn": flat pair on a plain effect list, or `SequenceEffect.of(new BoostSelfEffect(x, y), new RemoveKeywordEffect(kw, GrantScope.SELF))` under a single-child wrapper. Sentry Oak = `ClashEffect(SequenceEffect.of(...))` (clash win reward) |

## P/T setting / counters

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `SetPowerToughnessToAmountEffect` | `(DynamicAmount power, DynamicAmount toughness)` | CDA (`isPowerToughnessDefining()=true`): sets P/T on a 0/0 base to the given amounts, via the selfOnly `SetPowerToughnessToAmountSelfEffectHandler`. Pass the same amount instance for both fields for "P/T are each equal to …". Replaced the entire `PowerToughnessEqualTo*` family and `BoostSelfBySlimeCountersOnLinkedPermanentEffect`. Examples: `PermanentCount(new PermanentIsLandPredicate(), CONTROLLER)` (lands you control — Molimo), `PermanentCount(new PermanentIsCreaturePredicate(), CONTROLLER)` (creatures you control — Scion of the Wild), `PermanentCount(new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(CardSubtype.SWAMP), CONTROLLER)` (Swamps you control — Nightmare), `CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CardType.CREATURE), ANY_PLAYER)` (creature cards in all graveyards — Mortivore), `CardsInGraveyard(new CardTypePredicate(CardType.CREATURE), CONTROLLER)` (your graveyard only — Boneyard Wurm), `CardsInHand(CONTROLLER)` (your hand size — Psychosis Crawler), `ControllerLifeTotal()` (Ajani's Avatar token), `CountersOnLinkedPermanent(CounterType.SLIME, sourceId)` (Gutter Grime's Ooze tokens) |
| `PutCountersOnSourceEffect` | `(int powerModifier, int toughnessModifier, int amount)` | put N counters on this creature (e.g. `(1,1,1)` for +1/+1, `(-1,-1,2)` for two -1/-1) |
| `EachPlayerLosesLifeAndPutCountersOnSourceEqualToLifeLostEffect` | `(int lifeLossPerPlayer)` | Blood Tyrant (UPKEEP_TRIGGERED): each player loses `lifeLossPerPlayer` life, then the source gets one +1/+1 counter for each 1 life actually lost this way. Per-player loss is measured before/after so a player whose life can't change adds no counters (CR "this way"). Life loss is not damage (CR 118.2) and fires "loses life" triggers |
| `AllyCombatDamageTriggerEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate dealerPredicate, CardEffect effect, boolean bindSourceToDealer)` / sugar `(dealerPredicate, effect)` = `bindSourceToDealer=false` | ON_ALLY_CREATURE_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER slot: when a creature you control matching `dealerPredicate` (null = any) deals combat damage to a player, put `effect` on the stack for its controller. `bindSourceToDealer=false` binds the stack entry's source to the permanent carrying the trigger; `true` binds it to the damage dealer so source-referencing effects apply to the dealer. The damaged player is bound as the stack entry's target, so target-player effects like `DiscardEffect(N, DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)` resolve against them (Oona's Blackguard: `(PermanentHasCountersPredicate(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE), DiscardEffect(1, TARGET_PLAYER))` — "that player discards a card"). Wrap `effect` in a `MayEffect` for "you may" wordings. Used by Boggart Mob (Goblin predicate → may create a 1/1 black Goblin Rogue token) and Rakish Heir (`(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(VAMPIRE), PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1,1,1), true)` — counter goes on the dealing Vampire). Also works in the `GRAVEYARD_ON_ALLY_CREATURE_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` slot (fires from the controller's graveyard, source = the graveyard card) — Auntie's Snitch: Goblin-or-Rogue dealer predicate → `MayEffect(ReturnSourceCardFromGraveyardToOwnerHandEffect(), ...)` |
| `PutCountersOnSourceEqualToEnteringPowerEffect` | `(int powerModifier, int toughnessModifier, boolean optional)` | ON_ANY_OTHER_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD slot: put N counters on this creature where N = the entering creature's power (read at trigger time, mirrors `GainLifeEqualToToughnessEffect`). `optional=true` queues it as a "you may". Resolved via `PutCountersOnSourceEffect`. Used by Hamletback Goliath (`(1, 1, true)`) |
| `PutCountersOnSourceEqualToDyingPowerEffect` | `(int powerModifier, int toughnessModifier, boolean optional)` | ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES slot: put N counters on this creature where N = the dying creature's last-known effective power (snapshotted into `TriggerContext.CreatureDeath.dyingCreaturePower` from `dyingPermanent.getEffectivePower()`, so +1/+1 counters and boosts count). `optional=true` queues it as a "you may". Resolved via `PutCountersOnSourceEffect`. Death sibling of `PutCountersOnSourceEqualToEnteringPowerEffect`. Used by Kresh the Bloodbraided (`(1, 1, true)`) |
| `PutCounterOnEachControlledPermanentEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, DynamicAmount amount, PermanentPredicate predicate)` / int sugar `(CounterType, int count, PermanentPredicate)` | put `amount` counters of the specified type on each permanent **you control** matching the predicate. Use `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate` for "each creature you control", `PermanentAllOfPredicate` to combine filters (e.g. artifact + creature). For counter placement on permanents **outside** the controller's battlefield (each attacking creature, each other creature, each creature target player controls, each creature) use `PutCounterOnEachMatchingPermanentEffect` |
| `RemoveCounterFromEachControlledPermanentEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int amount, PermanentPredicate predicate)` | mirror of `PutCounterOnEachControlledPermanentEffect`: remove up to `amount` counters of the type from each permanent **you control** matching the predicate, clamped at zero (a permanent with none is unaffected). Heartmender ("remove a -1/-1 counter from each creature you control", UPKEEP_TRIGGERED) |
| `RemoveAndPutCounterOnAttackEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` or `()` (=`MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE`) | **ON_ATTACK only, two-target.** Remove one counter of the type from `targetIds[0]` (a creature you control; no-op if none) and put one of the same type on `targetIds[1]` (up to one creature the defending player controls). The put half goes through `PermanentCounterSupport.placeCounterOnPermanent` (fires the "-1/-1 counter put on a creature" triggers, respects `cantHaveCounters`/`cantHaveMinusOneMinusOneCounters`); the remove half is a plain `setCounterCount` decrement. Independent halves (CR-accurate). Implements marker interface `AttackCounterMoveEffect` so `CombatAttackService` routes it to the two-step `AttackCounterMoveFirstTarget`/`AttackCounterMoveSecondTarget` target flow — the ordinary Attack pipeline collects only one target. Decimator Beetle |
| `RemoveCounterFromTargetPermanentEffect` | `()` or `(CounterType counterType, PermanentPredicate targetPredicate)` | no-arg: remove one counter of any kind from the target permanent — scans `CounterType` (skipping the `ANY`/`SILVER` wildcards) and removes one of the first present kind; no-op if the target has no counters. Targets any permanent. Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may". Medicine Runner. Two-arg: remove one counter of exactly `counterType` (no-op if the target has none of it) and narrow legal targets to `targetPredicate` — Defiant Greatmaw ("remove a -1/-1 counter from another target creature you control": `MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE` + `AllOf(IsCreature, ControlledBySourceController, Not(IsSourceCard))`, in the `ON_SELF_MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE_COUNTERS_PUT` slot) |
| `PutPlusOnePlusOneCounterOnSourceOnColorSpellCastEffect` | `(Set<CardColor> triggerColors, int amount, boolean onlyOwnSpells)` | put +1/+1 counters when spell of matching color is cast. Use `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL` with `onlyOwnSpells=true` for "whenever you cast" cards; use `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL` with `onlyOwnSpells=false` for "whenever a player casts" cards; use `ON_OPPONENT_CASTS_SPELL` with `onlyOwnSpells=false` for "whenever an opponent casts" cards (wrap in MayEffect for "you may" triggers like Mold Adder) |
| `PutCounterOnEachMatchingPermanentEffect` | `(CounterType, DynamicAmount amount, PermanentPredicate predicate, EachPermanentScope scope)` / int sugar `(CounterType, int count, PermanentPredicate, EachPermanentScope)` | put `amount` counters on each permanent matching the predicate across the battlefields chosen by `scope` (`ALL_PLAYERS` / `TARGET_PLAYER`). Replaced the whole cross-battlefield each-creature family: "each attacking creature" = `(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, AllOf(IsCreature, IsAttacking), ALL_PLAYERS)` (Choking Fumes), "each other creature" = `(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, AllOf(IsCreature, Not(IsSourceCard)), ALL_PLAYERS)` (Carnifex Demon), "each creature target player controls" = `(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, IsCreature, TARGET_PLAYER)` (Contagion Engine — makes the spec player-targeting), "each creature, X counters" = `(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, XValue(), IsCreature, ALL_PLAYERS)` (Black Sun's Zenith), "each creature your opponents control" = `(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 1, AllOf(IsCreature, Not(ControlledBySourceController)), ALL_PLAYERS)` (Archfiend of Ifnir — the handler stamps `sourceControllerId` on the `FilterContext`, so controller-relative predicates resolve). Also valid in the `ON_CONTROLLER_DISCARDS` slot (Archfiend of Ifnir; enqueued by `DiscardTriggerCollectorService.handlePutCountersOnDiscard`). +1/+1 self-triggers fire after all placements |
| `PutCounterOnEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` or `(CounterType counterType, int count)` | put N counters of the specified type on the enchanted creature (default 1 counter). Re-derives the enchanted creature from the source Aura's `attachedTo` at resolution. Use with UPKEEP_TRIGGERED for auras like Primal Cocoon (PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE) or Glistening Oil (MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE), or with ON_ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_TAPPED for Spirit Shackle (MINUS_ZERO_MINUS_TWO — "whenever enchanted creature becomes tapped") |
| `PutPlusOnePlusOneCounterOnEachCreatureTargetPlayerControlsEffect` | `()` | put a +1/+1 counter on each creature the target player controls. Bind it to the spell's player target group via `target(playerFilter).addEffect(...)` (Practiced Offense), or drop it in `ON_SELF_LEAVES_BATTLEFIELD` with no card-level target filter for a leaves-the-battlefield trigger whose player target is chosen when the source leaves (Meadowboon) |
| `EnterWithCountersEffect` | `(CounterType type, DynamicAmount count)` | as-enters replacement effect (CR 614.1c): "enters the battlefield with [count] [type] counters". The count is a `DynamicAmount` — every "enters with … counters" wording is this one effect + an amount, never a new effect class. Examples: "with three charge counters" = `(CHARGE, Fixed(3))` (Trigons, Tumble Magnet), "with three wish counters" = `(WISH, Fixed(3))` (Djinn of Wishes), "with X charge counters" = `(CHARGE, XValue())` (Chimeric Mass), "with X +1/+1 counters" = `(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, XValue())` (Protean Hydra, Mikaeus the Lunarch), "for each creature that died this turn" = `(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, CreatureDeathsThisTurn(ANY_PLAYER))` (Bloodcrazed Paladin), "for each other Zombie you control and each Zombie card in your graveyard" = `(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, Sum(PermanentCount(HasSubtype(ZOMBIE), CONTROLLER), CardsInGraveyard(CardSubtypePredicate(ZOMBIE), CONTROLLER)))` (Unbreathing Horde — the entering permanent isn't on the battlefield yet, so "other" is automatic). Conditional variants wrap it in `ConditionalEffect`: "if kicked, enters with N +1/+1 counters" = `ConditionalEffect(new Kicked(), new EnterWithCountersEffect(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, new Fixed(N)))` (Academy Drake, Grunn; pair with `KickerEffect` on STATIC), "Raid — enters with N counters" = `ConditionalEffect(new Raid(), …)` (Rigging Runner). Applied in `BattlefieldEntryService.putPermanentOntoBattlefield()` before the permanent is added to the battlefield (CR 614.12), so it works on every entry path; `XValue`/`Kicked` read the resolving spell's stack-entry context (0/false when the permanent wasn't cast). Blocked by `CantHaveCountersEffect` |
| `DevourEffect` | `(int multiplier)` | Devour N (CR 702.82) as-enters replacement: "As this creature enters, you may sacrifice any number of creatures. It enters with N times that many +1/+1 counters on it." A `ReplacementEffect` in `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD` (excluded from the triggered pipeline). Handled in `BattlefieldEntryService.handleCreatureEnteredBattlefield` — before ETB triggers it prompts the controller with a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.DevourSacrifice` multi-permanent choice over their *other* creatures (0 to all); the sacrificed count × `multiplier` is added as +1/+1 counters and the devoured creatures are recorded on the permanent via `Permanent.recordDevouredCreature`. Read the count back with the `CreaturesDevoured` amount ("… for each creature it devoured"), or a per-subtype count with `DevouredCreaturesOfSubtype(CardSubtype)` (Voracious Dragon's "twice the number of Goblins it devoured"; a devoured Changeling counts as any type). Tar Fiend = `new DevourEffect(2)` + `DiscardEffect(new CreaturesDevoured(), DiscardRecipient.TARGET_PLAYER)`. No other creatures ⇒ no prompt, devours 0 |
| `KickerEffect` | `(String cost)` or `(PermanentPredicate sacrificePredicate, String sacrificeDescription)` or `(String cost, PermanentPredicate sacrificePredicate, String sacrificeDescription)` | STATIC effect declaring that a spell has kicker. Cost can be mana only (e.g. "{4}"), sacrifice only (e.g. sacrifice an artifact or Goblin), or both. SpellCastingService reads this to pay the optional additional cost. Combine with kicker-conditional effects on ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD or SPELL slot |
| `ConditionalEffect(new CastFromZone(sourceZone), wrapped)` | see construction shape | conditional wrapper that resolves its inner effect only when the spell or permanent was cast from the required source zone. Pass `Zone.HAND` for "When this enters, if you cast it from your hand, [effect]" patterns, e.g. Wakening Sun's Avatar uses `ConditionalEffect(new CastFromZone(Zone.HAND), new DestroyAllPermanentsEffect(...))`. Can also be placed on SPELL effects, e.g. Increasing Devotion uses `ConditionalEffect(new CastFromZone(Zone.GRAVEYARD), CreateTokenEffect(...))` for the additional graveyard-cast tokens, and Increasing Vengeance uses `ConditionalEffect(new CastFromZone(Zone.GRAVEYARD), new CopySpellEffect())` for the extra graveyard-cast copy |
| `ConditionalEffect(new CastNotFromHand(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | conditional wrapper that resolves its inner effect only when the spell was cast from anywhere other than the controller's hand (`StackEntry.getSourceZone() != Zone.HAND`). Use for "Then if this spell was cast from anywhere other than your hand, [effect]" patterns. E.g. Antiquities on the Loose |
| `ConditionalEffect(new Kicked(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | conditional wrapper that resolves its inner effect only when the spell was kicked (MTG Rule 702.32c). Place on SPELL slot alongside other spell effects. Use when kicked *adds* an extra effect. E.g. Blink of an Eye uses `ConditionalEffect(new Kicked(), new DrawCardEffect())` |
| `ConditionalEffect(new NotKicked(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | conditional wrapper that resolves its inner effect only when the permanent was NOT kicked. Intervening-if checked at trigger time (StepTriggerService) and resolution time (EffectResolutionService). Place on END_STEP_TRIGGERED slot. Use for "if wasn't kicked, sacrifice it" patterns. E.g. Skizzik uses `ConditionalEffect(new NotKicked(), new SacrificeSelfEffect())` |
| `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new Kicked(), baseEffect, upgradedEffect)` | see construction shape | replacement wrapper that picks between base and kicked effects. At resolution, if kicked resolves `kickedEffect`; otherwise resolves `baseEffect`. Use when kicked mode *replaces* the base mode ("instead" in oracle text). E.g. Fight with Fire uses `ConditionalReplacementEffect(new Kicked(), new DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(5), DealDividedDamageEffect.chosenAmongAnyTargets(10))` |
| `GraveyardEnterWithAdditionalCountersEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype, int count)` | graveyard static ability (replacement effect): while this card is in your graveyard, creatures with the specified subtype you control enter with N additional +1/+1 counters. Uses CR 614.12 lookahead via `GameQueryService.permanentWouldHaveSubtype()` to account for static subtype-granting effects (e.g. Xenograft). Simultaneously entering permanents are excluded per CR 614.12. Checked in BattlefieldEntryService.putPermanentOntoBattlefield(). Used by Dearly Departed |
| `ControlledCreaturesEnterWithAdditionalCountersEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype, int count)` | battlefield static ability (replacement effect): while the source is on the battlefield, each other creature with the specified subtype its controller controls enters with N additional +1/+1 counters. Battlefield twin of `GraveyardEnterWithAdditionalCountersEffect` (add via `EffectSlot.STATIC`). "Other" is implicit — the entering permanent isn't on the battlefield yet, and a source entering simultaneously doesn't apply its effect (CR 614.12). Same CR 614.12 subtype lookahead. Checked in BattlefieldEntryService.putPermanentOntoBattlefield(). Used by Sage of Fables (WIZARD) |
| `PutCountersOnSelfEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` or `(CounterType counterType, int count)` or `(CounterType counterType, DynamicAmount amount)` | put N counters of the specified type on this permanent (self-target). Single-arg form defaults to 1 counter; `DynamicAmount` ctor resolves the count at resolution time (`new XValue()` for "{X}: Put X tower counters", Helix Pinnacle). Delegates to `placeCounterOnPermanent`. Use for any self-counter ability: charge counters (`CounterType.CHARGE`), +1/+1 (`CounterType.PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE`), study (`CounterType.STUDY`), tower (`CounterType.TOWER`), etc. Binds `SOURCE_SELF` in `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` triggers, so "whenever this creature deals combat damage to a player, put a charge counter on it" works directly (Lightning Reaver) — the +1/+1-only `PutCountersOnSourceEffect` is the sibling for power/toughness counters. Used by Trigons, Shrines, Grimoire of the Dead, Withengar Unbound, Helix Pinnacle |
| `PutCounterOnSelfThenTransformIfThresholdEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int threshold)` or `(CounterType counterType, int threshold, boolean optional)` or `(CounterType counterType, int threshold, boolean optional, List<CardEffect> onTransformEffects)` | put a counter of the specified type on this permanent, then if the count reaches the threshold, remove all counters of that type and transform. When `optional` is true, the player is prompted ("you may") before removing counters and transforming. When `onTransformEffects` is non-empty, those effects are appended to the resolving stack entry after the transform completes (e.g. create tokens). Used by Ludevic's Test Subject (HATCHLING, 5), Primal Amulet (CHARGE, 4, true), Treasure Map (LANDMARK, 3, false, [CreateTokenEffect.ofTreasureToken(3)]) |
| `RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect` + `TransformSelfEffect` | _compose, no dedicated effect_ | "remove all counters of a type, then transform this": `SequenceEffect.of(new RemoveAllCountersFromSelfEffect(type), new TransformSelfEffect())`. Accepted half of optional counter-threshold transform abilities — Primal Amulet wraps it in the `MayEffect` queued by `PutCounterOnSelfThenTransformIfThresholdEffect` |
| `PutCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect` | `(CounterType)` / `(CounterType, int count)` / `(CounterType, DynamicAmount amount)` / `(CounterType, int count, PermanentPredicate predicate)` / `(CounterType, int count, boolean regenerateIfSurvives)` / `withTargetRestriction(CounterType, int count, PermanentPredicate targetPredicate)` | put `amount` counter(s) of the specified type on a permanent. **The one targeted counter-placement effect** — absorbed `PutPlusOnePlusOneCounterOnTargetCreatureEffect` (`(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, n)`), `PutMinusOneMinusOneCounterOnTargetCreatureEffect` (`(MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, n)`, `(…, 1, true)` for Gore Vassal's regenerate) and `PutXPlusOnePlusOneCountersOnTargetPermanentEffect` (`(PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE, new XValue())` — Waker of the Wilds). Default mode targets a permanent (permanent-targeting spec); `amount` is a `DynamicAmount`; the handler resolves multi-group-spell / multi-target-list / single targets. `withTargetRestriction` keeps targeting on but restricts legal targets via `targetPredicate()` (saga chapters — Triumph of Gerrard's greatest-power). `withResolutionCondition(CounterType, int count, PermanentPredicate)` gates placement at resolution WITHOUT restricting target legality ("if it's legendary" — Ancient Animus). In a multi-group spell, bind it to its target group via `target(...).addEffect(...)` (Savage Stomp, River Heralds' Boon). A non-null **`predicate`** instead makes it a resolution-time own-permanent choice (non-targeting spec; Settle the Score `(LOYALTY, 2, PermanentIsPlaneswalkerPredicate)`). LORE counters on Sagas trigger chapter abilities (MTG Rule 714.3b); +1/+1 fires ON_SELF triggers; -1/-1 respects prevention |
| `DistributeCountersAmongTargetsEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int total)` | distribute `total` counters **evenly** across this effect's chosen target group (`floor(total / targetCount)` on each) — the forced CR 601.2d split for "distribute two counters among one or two target creatures" (1 target → 2, 2 targets → 1 each). Counter-type generic: harmful `CREATURE` target spec for `MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE` (Splendid Agony), benign for `PLUS_ONE_PLUS_ONE` (Common Bond). Bind to a `target(creatureFilter, 1, 2)` group; the handler reads `StackEntry.targetsForEffect(this)` and routes each placement through `PermanentCounterSupport.placeCounterOnPermanent` (so -1/-1 prevention/reduction and +1/+1 triggers apply). NOT for a genuine three-plus choose-your-division distribute |
| `PutPhylacteryCounterOnTargetPermanentEffect` | `()` | put a phylactery counter on an artifact you control as an "as enters" replacement effect. Does NOT target (shroud/hexproof don't prevent it). Counter is placed directly when creature enters, not via stack. Artifact choice is validated at resolution: must be an artifact controlled by the caster. If no valid artifact is chosen, ability does nothing. Used by Phylactery Lich |
| `StateTriggerEffect` | `(StateTriggerPredicate, List<CardEffect>, String)` | state-triggered ability (MTG rule 603.8). When predicate condition is met after SBAs, pushes effects onto the stack as a triggered ability. Won't retrigger while the ability is on the stack. Place in `STATE_TRIGGERED` slot. Used by Phylactery Lich |
| `RemoveChargeCountersFromTargetPermanentEffect` | `(int maxCount)` | remove up to N charge counters from target permanent (targets permanent, use with PermanentPredicateTargetFilter to restrict targets) |
| `DoubleCountersOnTargetPermanentEffect` | `()` | double the number of each kind of counter on target permanent (for every counter kind present, adds that many more of the same kind). permanent-targeting spec; use with `PermanentPredicateTargetFilter(new PermanentTruePredicate(), ...)` for "target permanent". Used by Gilder Bairn (`{2}{G/U}, {Q}` activated ability, `.withRequiresUntap()`) |
| `RemoveCountersFromTargetAndBoostSelfEffect` | `()` | remove up to X counters of any type from target permanent (X from xValue), then boost source +1/+0 per counter removed until end of turn. Removes in order: +1/+1, charge, phylactery, loyalty, -1/-1, awakening. Used by Hex Parasite |
| `RemoveCounterFromTargetAndGainLifeEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int lifeGain)` | remove one counter of the given type from target permanent; controller gains `lifeGain` life only if a counter was actually removed ("If you do"). Targets permanent, restrict with PermanentPredicateTargetFilter. Used by Woeleecher (MINUS_ONE_MINUS_ONE, 2) |
| `RemoveCounterFromSourceAndGainLifeEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int lifeGain)` | SOURCE (non-targeting) analogue of the above: remove one counter from this permanent; controller gains `lifeGain` life only if a counter was actually removed ("If you do"). Resolves against the stack entry's `sourcePermanentId`. Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may". Used by Living Artifact (VITALITY, 1, UPKEEP_TRIGGERED) |
| `ProliferateEffect` | `()` | proliferate: choose any number of permanents with counters, add one of each counter type already there |
| `AdjustEachCounterKindOnTargetEffect` | `()` | Quarry Hauler: "for each kind of counter on target permanent, put another counter of that kind on it or remove one from it." Targets any permanent (benign `PERMANENT` spec). At resolution snapshots every distinct counter kind present on the target and prompts the controller ADD/REMOVE once per kind through the generic list-choice (`ChoiceContext.AdjustCounterKindChoice`, handled by `ChoiceHandlerService.handleAdjustCounterKindChoice`); each kind is an independent decision. No-op if the target has no counters. ADD routes through `PermanentCounterSupport.placeCounterOnPermanent` (preserves +1/+1 self-triggers, -1/-1 prevention/watchers, saga chapters); REMOVE decrements; SBAs run once all kinds are resolved |
| `PutAwakeningCountersOnTargetLandsEffect` | `()` | combat damage trigger: choose any number of lands you control, put an awakening counter on each. Lands with awakening counters are 8/8 green Elemental creatures (permanent). Place in `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER` slot. Handled inline in CombatService via multi-permanent choice |
| `ChooseOpponentPermanentsAndPutCountersEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int maxCount, PermanentPredicate filter)` | ETB: choose up to N permanents opponents control matching filter, put a counter of the specified type on each. Auto-selects all if ≤maxCount eligible; prompts multi-permanent choice if more. Place in `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`. Resolved by `PermanentCounterResolutionService`. Used by Haphazard Bombardment (AIM, 4, nonenchantment) |
| `DestroyRandomOpponentPermanentWithCounterEffect` | `(CounterType counterType, int minRequired)` | end step trigger with intervening-if: if at least minRequired opponent permanents have the specified counter, destroy one at random. Place in `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED`. Intervening-if checked in `StepTriggerService`; resolved by `DestructionResolutionService`. Used by Haphazard Bombardment (AIM, 2) |

## Keywords / abilities

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `GrantKeywordEffect` | `(Keyword keyword, GrantScope scope)` or `(Keyword keyword, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(Set<Keyword> keywords, GrantScope scope)` or `(Set<Keyword> keywords, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` or with explicit duration: `(Keyword keyword, GrantScope scope, GrantDuration duration)` / `(Set<Keyword> keywords, GrantScope scope, GrantDuration duration)` / static factory `GrantKeywordEffect.toTargetIf(Keyword keyword, PermanentPredicate grantCondition)` / canonical `(Set<Keyword> keywords, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter, GrantDuration duration, PermanentPredicate grantCondition)` | grant one or more keywords. Scope: `SELF`, `TARGET`, `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, `OWN_TAPPED_CREATURES`, `OWN_CREATURES`, `ALL_CREATURES`, `TARGET_PLAYERS_CREATURES` (one-shot, all creatures the targeted player controls — player-targeting spec, e.g. Shields of Velis Vel), `ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES`, `TOKENS_CREATED_THIS_RESOLUTION` (one-shot, the tokens created by an earlier effect on the **same** stack entry — read from `StackEntry.createdPermanentIds`, which the token-creation handlers populate; e.g. Gilt-Leaf Ambush's `ClashEffect` onWin grants deathtouch to the two Elf Warriors it just created). `filter` selects the eligible permanents for multi-permanent scopes and (for `TARGET`) feeds the spec predicate — a targeting restriction. `grantCondition` (OPTIONAL, distinct from `filter`) is checked against the selected permanent at resolution: if it doesn't match, only the keyword grant is skipped, the target stays legal — use `toTargetIf(...)` for "target creature does X; if it's a [type], it also gains [keyword]" (Vampire's Zeal with `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(VAMPIRE)`, Blessing of Belzenlok with `PermanentHasSupertypePredicate(LEGENDARY)`). Use `Set<Keyword>` overload for multiple keywords at once. `GrantDuration` governs the **one-shot** (normalfx) grant's expiry — `END_OF_TURN` (default, → `Permanent.grantedKeywords`) or `UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN` (→ `Permanent.untilNextTurnKeywords`). In `EffectSlot.STATIC` the grant is continuous (anthem), duration and `grantCondition` are ignored |
| `GrantKeywordToChosenCreatureUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(Keyword keyword, UUID chosenCreatureId)` | grant keyword to the creature chosen when the source permanent entered the battlefield (via `Permanent.chosenPermanentId`). `chosenCreatureId` is null in card definition and baked in during snapshotting from `permanent.getChosenPermanentId()`. If chosen creature left the battlefield, does nothing. Used by Dauntless Bodyguard |
| `BoostEquippedCreatureAndGrantKeywordUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost, Keyword keyword)` | the source Equipment's attached creature gets +powerBoost/+toughnessBoost and gains the keyword until end of turn (via `setPowerModifier`/`setToughnessModifier` + `getGrantedKeywords`, cleared by `resetModifiers`). Fizzles if the Equipment is unattached or its creature is gone. Place on the Equipment in a trigger slot (e.g. `ON_CONTROLLER_DRAWS`) to model equipment-granted triggered abilities. Used by Diviner's Wand ("Whenever you draw a card, this creature gets +1/+1 and gains flying until end of turn") |
| `BoostEquippedCreatureUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost)` | the source Equipment's attached creature gets +powerBoost/+toughnessBoost until end of turn, with amounts evaluated relative to that creature at resolution (via `setPowerModifier`/`setToughnessModifier`, cleared by `resetModifiers`). Fizzles if the Equipment is unattached or its creature is gone. Dynamic sibling of `BoostEquippedCreatureAndGrantKeywordUntilEndOfTurnEffect` (no keyword). Place on the Equipment in a trigger slot (e.g. `ON_ATTACK`/`ON_BLOCK`) to model equipment-granted triggered abilities. Used by Veteran's Armaments ("Whenever this creature attacks or blocks, it gets +1/+1 until end of turn for each attacking creature" via `PermanentCount(PermanentIsAttackingPredicate, ANY_PLAYER)`) |
| `UntapEquippedCreatureEffect` | `()` | untaps the source Equipment's attached creature (via `Permanent.untap()`). Fizzles if the Equipment is unattached or its creature is gone. Place on the Equipment in a trigger slot (e.g. `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES`) to model equipment-granted untap triggered abilities. Used by Thornbite Staff ("Whenever a creature dies, untap this creature") |
| `GrantFlashToCardTypeEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | controller may cast spells matching the given predicate as though they had flash. When `filter` is `null`, grants flash to all spell types. Checked in `GameBroadcastService.hasFlashGrantForCard()`. Used by Shimmer Myr (CardTypePredicate(ARTIFACT)), Leyline of Anticipation (null = all types), Raff Capashen (CardIsHistoricPredicate) |
| `GrantConspireToSpellsEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter)` | STATIC: each spell the controller casts matching `filter` has conspire (CR 702.78) even without the innate `CONSPIRE` keyword. Checked by `SpellCastingService.hasConspireGrantForCard()` alongside the keyword gate in the conspire-cost path. Used by Wort, the Raidmother (red or green instant or sorcery spells) |
| `ConditionalEffect(new Equipped(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as equipped" condition. Analogous to `ConditionalEffect(new Metalcraft(), wrapped)`. For static effects: wraps `GrantKeywordEffect`, `StaticBoostEffect`, or `ProtectionFromColorsEffect`, applied only while at least one Equipment is attached (selfOnly handler). Used by Sunspear Shikari |
| `ConditionalEffect(new Enchanted(), wrapped)` | see construction shape | Wraps any effect with "as long as this creature is enchanted" condition. Analogous to `ConditionalEffect(new Equipped(), wrapped)` but checks for an attached Aura (subtype AURA) instead of Equipment. For static effects: wraps `StaticBoostEffect` / `GrantKeywordEffect` etc. (selfOnly handler). Used by Thran Golem (+2/+2, flying, first strike, trample while enchanted) |
| `GrantChosenKeywordToTargetEffect` | `(List<Keyword> options)` | on resolution, prompts controller to choose one keyword from `options`, then grants it to target permanent until end of turn. Uses COLOR_CHOICE wire protocol with `KeywordGrantChoice` context. In a multi-target spell, bind it to its target group via `target(...).addEffect(...)`. Used by Golem Artisan, Practiced Offense |
| `GrantChosenKeywordToSelfEffect` | `(List<Keyword> options)` | non-targeted SELF variant of the above: prompts controller to choose one keyword from `options`, then grants it to the source permanent (this creature) until end of turn. Resolves against `entry.getSourcePermanentId()`. Used by Urza's Avenger's `{0}` ability (paired with `BoostSelfEffect(-1, -1)`) |
| `GrantActivatedAbilityEffect` | `(ActivatedAbility ability, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(ActivatedAbility ability, GrantScope scope)` or `(ActivatedAbility ability, GrantScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter, EffectDuration duration)` | grant activated ability to permanents matching scope + filter. Duration defaults to `CONTINUOUS` (static). When `UNTIL_END_OF_TURN`: stored in `Permanent.temporaryActivatedAbilities`, cleared at end of turn. When `UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN`: stored in `Permanent.untilNextTurnActivatedAbilities`, survives end-of-turn cleanup, cleared at start of controller's next turn. For non-CONTINUOUS durations, only creatures on the battlefield at resolution time receive the ability. Supported scopes: `OWN_PERMANENTS`, `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT`, `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, `OWN_TAPPED_CREATURES`, `OWN_CREATURES`, `ALL_CREATURES`, and other creature scopes. Use `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT` for auras that enchant non-creature permanents (e.g. land auras granting mana abilities) |
| `GainActivatedAbilitiesOfCreatureCardsInAllGraveyardsEffect` | `()` | this creature has all activated abilities of all creature cards in all graveyards (static, selfOnly). Used by Necrotic Ooze |
| `GainKeywordsOfCreatureCardsInAllGraveyardsEffect` | `()` | this creature gains each of a fixed watched keyword set (flying, fear, first strike, double strike, deathtouch, haste, landwalk variants, lifelink, reach, shroud, trample, vigilance) for as long as a creature card with that keyword is in any graveyard (static, selfOnly). Protection is not granted (inherent protection is not a modelled card characteristic). Used by Cairn Wanderer |
| `GainActivatedAbilitiesOfExiledCardsEffect` | `()` | this permanent has all activated abilities of all cards exiled with it via `permanentExiledCards` (static, selfOnly). Used by Myr Welder |
| `GainActivatedAbilitiesOfTopLibraryCardEffect` | `()` | while the top card of the controller's library is an artifact or creature card, this creature has all of that card's activated abilities (static, selfOnly). Pair with `PlayWithTopCardRevealedEffect`. Used by Skill Borrower |
| `GrantAdditionalBlockEffect` | `(int additionalBlocks)` or `(int additionalBlocks, PermanentPredicate controlledFilter)` | can block N additional creatures. Default: self-only on a creature source, the equipped/enchanted creature on an Equipment/Aura, global otherwise. With `controlledFilter`: grants to every permanent the source's controller controls matching the predicate (Cenn's Tactician = each creature you control with a +1/+1 counter) |
| `GrantAdditionalBlockPerEquipmentEffect` | `()` | can block an additional creature for each Equipment attached (static, self-only). Used by Kemba's Legion |
| `GrantAdditionalBlockToTargetUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(int additionalBlocks)` | one-shot, until-end-of-turn "target creature can block N additional creatures this turn". Targeted (benign CREATURE spec); adds to the target `Permanent.additionalBlocksUntilEndOfTurn` counter (read by `CombatBlockService.getMaxBlocksForCreature`, cleared by `resetModifiers()`). The temporary sibling of the static `GrantAdditionalBlockEffect`. Act of Heroism (pair with `UntapPermanentsEffect(TARGET)` + `BoostTargetCreatureEffect`) |
| `RegenerateEffect` | `()` or `(boolean targetsPermanent)` | regenerate self (default) or target creature when `targetsPermanent=true` |
| `RegenerateAllOwnCreaturesEffect` | `()` or `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | regenerate all creatures you control matching filter (or all if null). Used by Full Moon's Rise |
| `RegeneratesIfWouldBeDestroyedEffect` | `()` | STATIC self-replacement: "if this creature would be destroyed, regenerate it". Always-on intrinsic regeneration — regenerates every time it would be destroyed (no shield consumed), still blocked by `cantRegenerateThisTurn`. Checked in `GraveyardService.tryRegenerate` before the shield path. Used by Mossbridge Troll |
| `PreventTargetCreatureRegenerationThisTurnEffect` | `()` | "Target creature can't be regenerated this turn." Sets `cantRegenerateThisTurn` on the target; `GraveyardService.tryRegenerate` returns false for it for the rest of the turn (beats regeneration shields and intrinsic regen alike). Flag cleared during turn cleanup. `targetSpec()` narrows to a CREATURE, harmful (protection from the source honoured). Used by Hurr Jackal |
| `GrantCardTypeEffect` | `(CardType cardType, GrantScope scope)` | grant a card type to permanents matching scope (e.g. "is an artifact in addition to its other types"). Flows through static bonus system and updates `isArtifact(GameData, Permanent)` / `isEnchantment(GameData, Permanent)` / metalcraft / targeting. Scope: `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, `ALL_PERMANENTS`, etc. Used by Silverskin Armor (ARTIFACT/EQUIPPED_CREATURE) and Enchanted Evening (ENCHANTMENT/ALL_PERMANENTS, "all permanents are enchantments") |
| `GrantColorEffect` | `(CardColor color, GrantScope scope)` or `(CardColor color, GrantScope scope, boolean overriding)` | grant a color to permanents matching scope. When `overriding=true`, replaces all existing colors (e.g. "is a black Zombie"). Scope: `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, etc. Used by Nim Deathmantle |
| `GrantSubtypeEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype, GrantScope scope)` or `(CardSubtype subtype, GrantScope scope, boolean overriding)` | grant a creature subtype to permanents matching scope. When `overriding=true`, replaces all existing creature subtypes (non-creature subtypes like Equipment/Aura are preserved). Scope: `EQUIPPED_CREATURE`, `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`, etc. `OWN_LANDS`/`ALL_LANDS` grant a (basic) land subtype additively to the lands you control / all lands (layer-4 pass, rule 305.6) — e.g. Prismatic Omen grants all five basic land types via five `OWN_LANDS` grants. Used by Nim Deathmantle |
| `GrantSubtypeToTargetCreatureEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | one-shot effect that permanently grants a subtype to the targeted creature ("becomes a [subtype] in addition to its other types"). Added to `grantedSubtypes`, survives turn resets. Used by Olivia Voldaren |
| `LoseAllCreatureTypesEffect` | `()` / `(GrantScope scope)` | one-shot: creatures lose all creature types until end of turn. `GrantScope.TARGET` (default, permanent-targeting spec) strips the single targeted creature (Amoeboid Changeling); `GrantScope.TARGET_PLAYERS_CREATURES` (player-targeting spec) strips every creature the targeted player controls (Ego Erasure). Sets `Permanent.losesAllCreatureTypesUntilEndOfTurn`, which makes every creature subtype (base/transient/granted) read as absent and nullifies the Changeling keyword's type grant; cleared by `resetModifiers()`. Inverse "gains all creature types" is `GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.CHANGELING, scope)`. |
| `EnchantedPermanentBecomesTypeEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | static effect for auras that set the enchanted permanent's subtype ("enchanted [permanent] is a [type]"). When the subtype is a basic land type (SWAMP, ISLAND, FOREST, MOUNTAIN, PLAINS), per MTG rule 305.7 replaces all existing basic land subtypes and overrides the land's mana production. Handled by static bonus system (`landSubtypeOverriding` flag) and `AbilityActivationService.tapPermanent`. Used by Evil Presence |
| `EnchantedPermanentBecomesChosenTypeEffect` | `()` | static effect for auras that set the enchanted permanent's subtype to the chosen basic land type stored on the source permanent's `chosenSubtype` field ("enchanted land is the chosen type"). Works like `EnchantedPermanentBecomesTypeEffect` but reads the subtype dynamically. Pair with `ChooseBasicLandTypeOnEnterEffect` in `ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD`. Used by Convincing Mirage |
| `EnchantedPermanentBecomesCreatureEffect` | `(int power, int toughness, CardColor color, List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` / `(..., boolean powerToughnessEqualsManaValue)` | STATIC effect for auras that continuously animate the enchanted permanent into a creature that keeps its existing types ("Enchanted land is a 5/6 green Treefolk creature that's still a land"). The creature card type + subtypes are added in the CR 613 layer-4 pass; the colour (overriding) and base P/T are contributed by the static handler (`animatedCreature` + `basePTOverride`). `GameQueryService.isCreature` recognizes it via `hasAuraBecomeCreatureEffect` (scans attached auras), so the enchanted land is a creature for combat/targeting/summoning-sickness and reverts automatically when the aura leaves. Used by Living Terrain. Pass `powerToughnessEqualsManaValue=true` (fixed power/toughness ignored, pass 0/0) for the Animate Artifact variant: base P/T each equal the enchanted permanent's mana value, and the animation only applies while it isn't already a creature (enchanting an artifact creature does nothing) |
| `NonbasicLandsBecomeTypeEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | global STATIC effect: every nonbasic land (any controller, not attached) becomes the given basic land type, losing its other land types/abilities and producing that type's mana per rule 305.7 (`landSubtypeOverriding`). Basic lands unaffected. Applied by the CR 613 layer-4 pass (`LayerSystemService`), which resolves competing land-type setters by timestamp and drives `GameQueryService.getOverriddenLandManaColor`. Used by Blood Moon |
| `LandsOfSubtypeBecomeTypeEffect` | `(CardSubtype fromSubtype, CardSubtype toSubtype)` | global STATIC effect: every land (any controller, basic or nonbasic) carrying `fromSubtype` becomes the `toSubtype` basic land type, losing its other land types/abilities and producing that type's mana per rule 305.7 (`landSubtypeOverriding`). Lands lacking `fromSubtype` unaffected. Subtype-keyed sibling of `NonbasicLandsBecomeTypeEffect` (which is nonbasic-only, unconditional); same layer-4 pass (`LayerSystemService`). Used by Conversion (MOUNTAIN → PLAINS) |
| `OwnLandsBecomeChosenTypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | no-target effect: prompts the controller to choose a basic land type (`OwnLandsBecomeBasicTypeChoice`), then each land they control **becomes** that type until end of turn — type-replacing per rule 305.7 (`Permanent.transientLandTypeOverride`, cleared by `resetModifiers()`). Applied once at resolution to the lands controlled at that moment via the shared `GrantBasicLandTypeToTargetEffectHandler.applyBasicLandType(..., replacing=true)`. Used by Elsewhere Flask |
| `GrantColorUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(CardColor color)` / `(CardColor color, boolean additive)` | target permanent becomes the specified color until end of turn. Default (`additive=false`) replaces all previous colors (CR 105.3); pass `additive=true` for "in addition to its other colors" (Indigo Faerie — adds the color, leaving the rest and not flipping `colorOverridden`). Creates a floating `L5_COLOR` setting effect (its CR 613.7 timestamp orders it against other color effects in the layered pass) and dual-writes the legacy `Permanent.transientColors`/`colorOverridden` fields (cleared on `resetModifiers()`) for direct intrinsic readers. Layered color queries (`GameQueryService.getEffectiveColors`/`hasColor`) answer for static effects, targeting, and costs |
| `SetChosenColorUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | target permanent becomes a color the controller chooses until end of turn — the "color of your choice" version of `GrantColorUntilEndOfTurnEffect`. permanent-targeting spec; targets any permanent. On resolution it pauses for a color choice (`ChoiceContext.ColorSetChoice`, handled in `ChoiceHandlerService`), which then applies a floating `L5_COLOR` setter wrapping a `GrantColorUntilEndOfTurnEffect(chosenColor)` (so it reuses the exact same layer machinery and wears off at cleanup). Used by Distorting Lens |
| `SetTargetColorEffect` | `(CardColor color)` | "target spell or permanent becomes [color]" **indefinitely** (the no-duration "lace" instants — Purelace → white). Like Glamerdye it targets a spell OR a permanent: the permanent case is its `benign(PERMANENT)` spec, the spell case is exposed through `EffectResolution.targetsSpellOnStack` (so the generic "spell or permanent" cast path handles it — no `target()` call needed on the card). Permanent target → replaces colors (CR 105.3) via a floating `L5_COLOR` setter with `EffectDuration.PERMANENT` (no wear-off), dual-writing `transientColors`/`colorOverridden`. Spell target → records the color in `GameData.spellColorOverrides` (keyed by spell card id); `BattlefieldEntryService.carrySpellColorOverride` re-seeds it + floats the permanent setter when the spell resolves into a permanent (CR 613.7), no-op for instants/sorceries |
| `GrantProtectionFromCardTypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(CardType cardType)` | target creature gains protection from the specified card type until end of turn. Adds to `Permanent.protectionFromCardTypes`. Cleared on `resetModifiers()`. Protection prevents blocking by, damage from, and targeting by sources of that card type. Checked via `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromSourceCardTypes()` in combat, damage, and targeting services |
| `GrantProtectionFromNonSubtypeCreaturesUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(CardSubtype excludedSubtype)` | all creatures you control gain protection from creatures that do NOT have the specified subtype until end of turn. Mass grant (no target). Adds to `Permanent.protectionFromNonSubtypeCreaturesUntilEndOfTurn`. Cleared on `resetModifiers()`. Changeling creatures (all subtypes) are NOT affected. Checked via `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromNonSubtypeCreatures()` integrated into `hasProtectionFromSource()`. Used by Spare from Evil (HUMAN) |
| `GrantProtectionChoiceUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(boolean includeArtifacts, boolean targetControllerChooses)`, `(boolean includeArtifacts)`, or `()` | on resolution, prompts a player to choose a color (and optionally "artifacts" when `includeArtifacts=true`), then grants the target permanent protection from that choice until end of turn. Color protection stored in `Permanent.protectionFromColorsUntilEndOfTurn`, artifact protection in `Permanent.protectionFromCardTypes`. Both cleared on `resetModifiers()`. Triggers `ChoiceContext.ProtectionColorChoice` interaction. When `targetControllerChooses=true` the target permanent's controller chooses instead of the ability's controller (Pale Wayfarer's "the color of its controller's choice"). Used by Apostle's Blessing (`includeArtifacts=true`). The no-arg / single-arg constructors default `targetControllerChooses=false` for cards like Gods Willing |
| `GrantProtectionChoiceToControllerAndPermanentsUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | on resolution, prompts the controller to choose a color (colors only), then grants that controller **and each permanent they control** protection from the chosen color until end of turn (single color for all). Per-permanent protection stored in `Permanent.protectionFromColorsUntilEndOfTurn`; player protection stored in `GameData.playerProtectionFromColorsUntilEndOfTurn` (cleared by `TurnCleanupService`). A player with protection from a color can't be targeted by spells/abilities of that color (`TargetLegalityService`) and can't be dealt damage by sources of that color (`DamageResolutionService.dealDamageToPlayer`, `CombatDamageService`); query via `GameQueryService.playerHasProtectionFromColor`. Triggers `ChoiceContext.MassProtectionColorChoice` interaction. Used by the fateful hour mode of Faith's Shield (combine with `ConditionalEffect(new ControllerLifeAtMost(threshold), wrapped)`) |
| `GrantDamageToOpponentCreatureBounceUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | until end of turn, creatures you control gain "Whenever this creature deals damage to an opponent, you may return target creature that player controls to its owner's hand." Sets `hasDamageToOpponentCreatureBounce` flag on controlled creatures; CombatService creates `ReturnPermanentsOnCombatDamageToPlayerEffect(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate)` trigger with xValue=1. Cleared on `resetModifiers()`. Used by Arm with Aether |
| `GrantEffectToTargetUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(EffectSlot slot, CardEffect grantedEffect)` | until end of turn, the target creature(s) gain a triggered ability for the specified slot. Stores the effect via `Permanent.addTemporaryTriggeredEffect(slot, effect)`. Trigger collection checks `Permanent.getTemporaryTriggeredEffects(slot)` alongside the card's native effects. Cleared on `resetModifiers()`. **Multi-target:** the handler fans over `entry.getTargetIds()` (falling back to `targetId`), so pair it with `target(filter, 0, 99)` for "any number of target creatures". Used by Verdant Rebirth (single-target ON_DEATH bounce) and Rabid Attack (with `BoostTargetCreatureEffect(1, 0)` on the same target list: "+1/+0 and gain 'when this dies, draw a card'"). **ON_ATTACK granted triggers** are collected off the attacker in `CombatAttackService` (native + `getTemporaryTriggeredEffects(ON_ATTACK)`); a granted `MustBlockSourceEffect(null)` has its source snapshotted to the attacker there. Used by Tower Above ("gains 'When this creature attacks, target creature blocks it this turn if able'"). **ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER granted triggers** are likewise collected off the damage-dealing creature in `CombatDamageService` (native + `getTemporaryTriggeredEffects(ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER)`); the controller draws via a plain `DrawCardEffect(1)`. Used by Open into Wonder ("gains 'Whenever this creature deals combat damage to a player, draw a card'", bound to a `targetX` group) |
| `ReturnSourceCardFromGraveyardToOwnerHandEffect` | `()` | when resolved as a death trigger, returns the dying creature's card from its owner's graveyard to its owner's hand. Uses the stack entry's card ID (the trigger source) to identify which card to return. Unlike ReturnEnchantedCreatureToOwnerHandOnDeathEffect (for auras), this returns the source card itself. Used by Verdant Rebirth |
| `GrantFlashbackToGraveyardCardsEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | grants flashback to cards of the specified types in the controller's graveyard until end of turn. The flashback cost equals the card's mana cost. Tracks granted card IDs in `GameData.cardsGrantedFlashbackUntilEndOfTurn`. Cards that already have native flashback are skipped. Cleared at end of turn by `TurnCleanupService`. Used by Past in Flames |
| `GrantFlashbackToTargetGraveyardCardEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | targets a single card of a matching type in the controller's graveyard and grants it flashback until end of turn. The flashback cost equals the card's mana cost. Own-graveyard-only (kept `@ValidatesTarget` validator enforces the controller's graveyard). Uses multi-graveyard targeting at ETB trigger time (`BattlefieldEntryService.handleGrantFlashbackETBTargeting`) or spell targeting (`targetId` in graveyard). Resolved by `KeywordGrantResolutionService`. Fizzles if target leaves graveyard. Tracks via `GameData.cardsGrantedFlashbackUntilEndOfTurn`. Used by Snapcaster Mage, Flashback (SOS) |
| `GrantTargetCreatureCardGraveyardCastAndCopyActivatedAbilitiesEffect` | `()` | targets a creature card in any graveyard and grants permission to cast that specific card this turn. Tracks card ID -> source permanent ID + casting player ID in `GameData.graveyardCreatureCastPermissionsUntilEndOfTurn`; cleared at cleanup. `SpellCastingService` consumes the permission when the allowed player casts the card from any graveyard by card ID, puts the permanent spell on the stack, then queues a delayed trigger above it. Used by Havengul Lich |
| `GrantSourceActivatedAbilitiesUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(List<ActivatedAbility> abilities, String copiedFromCardName)` | delayed triggered ability effect that grants the stack entry's source permanent the provided activated abilities until end of turn via `Permanent.temporaryActivatedAbilities`. Fizzles if the source permanent is gone. Used by Havengul Lich after the selected graveyard creature card is cast |

## Combat restrictions / evasion

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `CantBeBlockedEffect` | `()` | can't be blocked (static) |
| `CantAttackOrBlockAloneEffect` | `()` | this creature can't attack or block alone (CR 508.1b/509.1b, static) |
| `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessGreaterPowerAlsoDoesEffect` | `()` | Okk: can't attack unless another declared attacker has strictly greater power; can't block unless another declared blocker has strictly greater power (static). Combat-set-dependent, so not a `Condition` — validated in `CombatAttackService.validateGreaterPowerAlsoAttacks` / `CombatBlockService.validateGreaterPowerAlsoBlocks` against the current combat's declared set, at declaration time only |
| `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessCountAlsoDoesEffect` | `(int otherCount)` | Orcish Conscripts (`2`): can't attack unless at least N other creatures are declared as attackers; can't block unless at least N other creatures are declared as blockers (static). Combat-set-dependent, so not a `Condition` — validated in `CombatAttackService.validateCountAlsoAttacks` / `CombatBlockService.validateCountAlsoBlocks` against the current combat's declared set, at declaration time only |
| `CreaturesWithPowerGreaterThanAmountCantAttackEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | global static: any creature (either player's) whose effective power is strictly greater than `amount` can't attack (Ensnaring Bridge `new CardsInHand(CountScope.CONTROLLER)`). `amount` is evaluated from the source's controller via `AmountContext.forStaticEffect`; checked in `CombatAttackService.isCantAttackDueToGlobalRestriction` |
| `CantAttackNextTurnCombatOpponentEffect` | `()` | combat trigger (Wall of Dust): the combat opponent (the creature this permanent blocks) can't attack during its controller's next turn. Placed on `ON_BLOCK`; a `CombatOpponentReferencingEffect`, so `CombatBlockService` auto-targets the blocked attacker (non-targeting). The handler sets `Permanent.cantAttackNextTurn`, which `TurnProgressionService` promotes to `cantAttackThisTurn` at that creature's controller's next turn start (scoped to that player's turn) and self-clears after the one turn; barred in `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack` |
| `OtherCreaturesCantAttackThisTurnEffect` | `()` | SPELL one-shot rider (Intimidation Bolt "Other creatures can't attack this turn"). Appends the accompanying spell's creature target (`entry.getTargetId()`) to the turn-scoped `GameData.otherCreaturesCantAttackExemptCreatureIds`; `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack` lets a creature attack only if its ID equals EVERY exemption — so only the targeted survivor may attack, a dead target locks everyone, and creatures entering later are barred too. Untargeted itself (reads the damage effect's target), so `targetSpec()` stays `NONE`; pair with `DealDamageToTargetCreatureEffect(N)`. Cleared at each turn transition |
| `CantBlockEffect` | `()` | this creature can't block (static) |
| `CantBlockUnlessEffect` | `(Condition condition, String requirementDescription)` | static: this creature can't block unless `condition` is met (Marauding Boneslasher: `new ControlsOtherPermanentCount(1, new PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(ZOMBIE))`, "you control another Zombie"). The block-only counterpart of `CantAttackUnlessEffect` and the block half of `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessEffect`. `BlockingRestrictionEffect` facet `cantBlockUnless()`; evaluated in `GameQueryService.canBlock` (via `isCantBlockUnlessConditionUnmet`) relative to the source's controller. Does NOT restrict attacking |
| `TargetPlayerChoosesCreatureRestCantBlockEffect` | `()` | SPELL, player-targeting spec: the targeted player chooses one creature they control to keep able to block; every OTHER creature they control can't block this turn (sets `Permanent.cantBlockThisTurn`). Presents a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ChooseCreatureRestCantBlock` to the target player (count 1); 0-1 creatures ⇒ no choice, resolves harmlessly. Pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)`. Used by Goblin War Cry |
| `CantBlockCreaturesWithPowerGreaterOrEqualToOwnToughnessEffect` | `()` | static self-referential restriction (Ironclaw Curse): this creature can't block an attacker whose effective power ≥ its own effective toughness. `BlockingRestrictionEffect` facet `cantBlockCreaturesWithPowerAtLeastOwnToughness()`; comparison resolved in `GameQueryService.findBlockDenial`, recognized on the blocker's own STATIC effects or via an attached aura |
| `CantBlockCreaturesWithPowerAtLeastEffect` | `(int minAttackerPower)` | static hard fixed-threshold restriction (Ironclaw Orcs, `(2)`): this creature can't block an attacker whose effective power ≥ `minAttackerPower`. No cost, not self-referential. `BlockingRestrictionEffect` facet `cantBlockCreaturesWithPowerAtLeast()`; resolved in `GameQueryService.findBlockDenial` against the attacker's effective power |
| `TargetPlayerChoosesCreatureRestCantBlockEffect` | `()` | SPELL, `canTargetPlayer`: the targeted player chooses one creature they control to keep able to block; every OTHER creature they control can't block this turn (sets `Permanent.cantBlockThisTurn`). Presents a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.ChooseCreatureRestCantBlock` to the target player (count 1); 0-1 creatures ⇒ no choice, resolves harmlessly. Pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter(OPPONENT)`. Used by Goblin War Cry |
| `CantBlockSourceEffect` | `(UUID sourcePermanentId)` | target creature can't block source permanent |
| `MatchingCreaturesCantBlockMatchingCreaturesEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate blockerPredicate, PermanentPredicate attackerPredicate, String description)` | global static: while the source is on the battlefield, any creature matching `blockerPredicate` can't block any creature matching `attackerPredicate`, board-wide (Boldwyr Intimidator "Cowards can't block Warriors"). Evaluated in `GameQueryService.getBlockRestriction` |
| `MatchingCreaturesCantAttackOrBlockEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate affectedPredicate, String description)` | global static: while the source is on the battlefield, any creature matching `affectedPredicate` can't attack OR block, board-wide. `affectedPredicate` is evaluated relative to the source's controller (`sourceControllerId`/`sourceCardId` supplied), so `PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate` etc. resolve "you"/"your opponents". Kulrath Knight "Creatures your opponents control with counters on them can't attack or block" = `PermanentAllOfPredicate(PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate()), PermanentHasCountersPredicate(ANY))`; Light of Day "Black creatures can't attack or block" = `PermanentColorInPredicate(BLACK)`. Attack side in `CombatAttackService.isCantAttackDueToGlobalRestriction`; block side in `GameQueryService.canBlock`/`buildBlockerFacts` |
| `TargetCreatureBecomesSubtypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | target creature **becomes** the creature type until end of turn, **replacing** all its other creature types (Boldwyr Intimidator). Sets `Permanent.transientCreatureTypeOverride`, read by the layered pass; contrast additive/permanent `GrantSubtypeToTargetCreatureEffect` |
| `SourceBecomesSubtypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | self analog (no target): the **source** permanent becomes the creature type until end of turn, **replacing** all its other creature types (Paragon of the Amesha). Sets `Permanent.transientCreatureTypeOverride` on the source; pair with `BoostSelfEffect` + `GrantKeywordEffect(GrantScope.SELF)` for a full self-transform ability |
| `CanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate blockerPredicate, String allowedBlockersDescription)` | can only be blocked by matching creatures (static; also stored transiently on a `Permanent` for until-end-of-turn grants) |
| `CantBeBlockedByCreaturesMatchingPredicateEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate blockerPredicate)` | negative evasion: this creature can't be blocked by blockers matching the predicate (static, validated in `GameQueryService.getBlockingIllegalityReason`). Taoist Mystic = `PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(HORSEMANSHIP)` |
| `GrantCanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterToOwnCreaturesEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate creatureFilter, PermanentPredicate blockerPredicate, String allowedBlockersDescription)` | SPELL one-shot: each of the controller's creatures matching `creatureFilter` (null = all) can be blocked only by blockers matching `blockerPredicate` until end of turn (Dread Charge). Affected creatures snapshotted at resolution (CR 611); the `CanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterEffect` restriction is added to each `Permanent.blockRestrictionsUntilEndOfTurn` and consumed by `GameQueryService.getBlockRestriction`, cleared by `resetModifiers` |
| `CanBeBlockedByAtMostNCreaturesEffect` | `(int maxBlockers)` | can be blocked by at most N creatures (static) |
| `EachControlledCreatureCanBeBlockedByAtMostNCreaturesEffect` | `(int maxBlockers)` | team-wide version: each creature the controller controls can be blocked by at most N creatures (static, validated in CombatBlockService by scanning the active player's battlefield). Yuan Shao, the Indecisive uses maxBlockers=1 |
| `CantBeBlockedByFewerThanNCreaturesEffect` | `(int minBlockers)` | generalized menace: can't be blocked except by N or more creatures — if blocked, must be blocked by at least N (static, validated in CombatBlockService alongside menace). Menace is the minBlockers=2 case; Guile uses 3 |
| `CanBlockAnyNumberOfCreaturesEffect` | `()` | this creature can block any number of creatures (static) |
| `CanBlockOnlyIfAttackerMatchesPredicateEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate attackerPredicate, String allowedAttackersDescription)` | this creature can only block attackers matching predicate (static) |
| `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessEquippedEffect` | `()` | this creature can't attack or block unless it's equipped (static) |
| `CantAttackUnlessEffect` | `(Condition condition, String requirementDescription)` | can't attack unless the condition is met (static, evaluated at attack-declaration legality via ConditionEvaluationService). Map the "unless" clause to a Condition: `ControlsPermanentCount(1, filter)` = controller controls a matching permanent (Desperate Castaways); `DefendingPlayerControlsPermanent(filter)` = defending player controls a matching permanent (Sea Monster, Serpent of the Endless Sea); `AnyPlayerControlsPermanentCount(N, filter)` = N+ matching permanents across all battlefields (Harbor Serpent, N=5); `DefendingPlayerPoisoned()` = defending player poisoned (Chained Throatseeker); `OpponentDealtDamageThisTurn()` = an opponent was dealt damage this turn (Bloodcrazed Goblin). requirementDescription is the user-facing "unless" clause. |
| `CantAttackOrBlockUnlessEffect` | `(Condition condition, String requirementDescription)` | can't attack **or** block unless the condition is met (static). Block-side counterpart of `CantAttackUnlessEffect`: attack legality evaluated in `CombatAttackService`, block legality in `GameQueryService.canBlock`, both via `ConditionEvaluationService`. Map the "unless" clause to a Condition — e.g. `ControlsAnotherPermanent(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(GIANT))` = controller controls another Giant (Blind-Spot Giant). |
| `CreaturesCantAttackUnlessPredicateEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate exemptionPredicate)` | global static: ALL creatures can't attack unless they match the exemption predicate (e.g. flying or islandwalk). NOT folded into CantAttackUnlessEffect — it is a per-attacker exemption applied from any permanent, not a source-creature condition. |
| `CreaturesCantAttackControllerUnlessPredicateEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate exemptionPredicate[, boolean protectsPlaneswalkers])` | defender-scoped static: creatures not matching the exemption predicate can't attack THIS permanent's controller (they may still attack other players). "Creatures without flying can't attack you" = exemption `PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(Keyword.FLYING)` (Form of the Dragon). Pass `protectsPlaneswalkers=true` to also bar attacks on the controller's planeswalkers ("can't attack you or planeswalkers you control", Sandwurm Convergence → exemption `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentHasKeywordPredicate(Keyword.FLYING))`); single-arg overload defaults to player-only. Contrast `CreaturesCantAttackUnlessPredicateEffect`, which is global (no attacking at all). Enforced per attacked player in `CombatAttackService`. |
| `ControlledCreaturesCantAttackUnlessPredicateEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate exemptionPredicate)` | controller-scoped static: creatures the source's controller controls that do NOT match the exemption can't attack (own team only; the source itself is exempt if it matches). "Non-Eye creatures you control can't attack" = exemption `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(EYE)` (Evil Eye of Orms-by-Gore). Contrast `CreaturesCantAttackUnlessPredicateEffect` (global). Checked in `CombatAttackService.isCantAttackDueToGlobalRestriction`. |
| `CantBeBlockedIfDefenderControlsMatchingPermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate defenderPermanentPredicate)` | can't be blocked as long as defender controls matching permanent (static) |
| `CantBeBlockedIfControllerCastHistoricSpellThisTurnEffect` | `()` | can't be blocked as long as controller cast a historic spell (artifact, legendary, or Saga) this turn (static) |
| `CantBeBlockedIfAttackingAloneEffect` | `()` | can't be blocked as long as it's attacking alone — the only declared attacker (static, validated in CombatBlockService/GameQueryService; e.g. Dream Prowler) |
| `CanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect` | `()` | this creature can attack as though it didn't have defender. In a STATIC slot it is read directly by the layered pass (typically wrapped in ConditionalEffect(new Metalcraft(), wrapped)); as an activated-ability effect it resolves into an until-end-of-turn floating grant on the source (creature keeps defender), also honored by `canAttackDespiteDefender`. Used by Spire Serpent (static) and Wall of Wonder (activated, alongside `BoostSelfEffect(4, -4)`) |
| `MatchingCreaturesCanAttackAsThoughNoDefenderEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate matcher)` | global static on a permanent (any controller): every creature matching `matcher` can attack as though it didn't have defender. Checked in `GameQueryService.canAttackDespiteDefender` by scanning all battlefields. Used by Rolling Stones (`PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(WALL)`) |
| `MustAttackEffect` | `()` | this creature must attack each turn if able (static) |
