| `MatchingCreaturesMustAttackEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate matcher)` | global static on a permanent (any controller): every creature matching `matcher` must attack each combat if able, regardless of who controls it. Global analogue of self-only `MustAttackEffect`; read in `CombatAttackService.getMustAttackRequirementCount` by scanning all battlefields. Respects CR 508.1d (no attack tax payment required). Used by Goblin Assault (`PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(GOBLIN)`) |
| `MustAttackThisTurnEffect` | `(boolean forceAttackController)` | target creature must attack this turn if able (one-shot, sets transient flag, cleared at end of turn). If forceAttackController=true, also sets mustAttackTargetId to ability controller (e.g. Alluring Siren "attacks you"). If false, creature may attack any legal target (e.g. Incite "attacks this turn if able"). |
| `MatchingCreaturesMustAttackThisTurnEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate matcher)` | one-shot, non-targeted: every creature matching `matcher` (any controller) must attack this turn if able. Sets the transient `mustAttackThisTurn` flag on each match (cleared at end of turn), so the requirement only bites when a matching creature's controller is the active player during combat. Predicate evaluated with the effect's source controller as `sourceControllerId`. One-shot analogue of the static `MatchingCreaturesMustAttackEffect`. Used by Suicidal Charge with `PermanentNotPredicate(PermanentControlledBySourceControllerPredicate())` ("creatures your opponents control attack this turn if able"). |
| `TargetPlayersCreaturesMustAttackThisTurnEffect` | `()` | one-shot, **player-targeted**: every creature the target player (`entry.getTargetId()`) controls must attack this turn if able (may attack any legal target — no forced defender). Sets the transient `mustAttackThisTurn` flag on each of that player's creatures at resolution (cleared at end of turn), read in `CombatAttackService.getMustAttackRequirementCount`. Player-targeted analogue of `MatchingCreaturesMustAttackThisTurnEffect` for "creatures **target** opponent controls attack this turn if able" (which the non-targeted, `sourceControllerId`-relative matcher can't express). `benign(PLAYER)` spec. Used by Imaginary Threats (paired with `SkipNextUntapEffect(TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS, PermanentIsCreaturePredicate)` on the same player target). |
| `MustAttackControllerNextTurnEffect` | `()` | targets a player: during that player's next turn, every creature they control attacks the effect's controller if able (Taunt). Handler stores affectedPlayer→controller in `GameData.tauntedNextTurn`; `TurnProgressionService.advanceTurn` promotes it to `tauntedThisTurn` when that player's turn begins; `CombatAttackService` reads `tauntedThisTurn` live at declare-attackers to add a must-attack requirement per creature and force each declared attacker onto the taunter. Respects CR 508.1d (no attack tax payment required). |
| `OpponentsMustAttackControllerEffect` | `()` | each opponent must attack the controller (or a planeswalker the controller controls) with at least one creature each combat if able (static). Unlike MustAttackEffect, does NOT force every creature to attack — only requires at least one attacker. Respects CR 508.1d (no attack tax payment required). Used by Trove of Temptation |
| `SirensCallEffect` | `()` | SPELL, non-targeted (Siren's Call). Resolution sets the transient `mustAttackThisTurn` flag on every creature the active player controls (combat's "if able" gate applies) and queues a `DestroyNonAttackersAtEndStep(activePlayerId)` delayed action. At the next end step, `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers` destroys every non-Wall creature that player controls with `!attackedThisTurn && !summoningSick` (`summoningSick` == "didn't control continuously since the beginning of the turn"). Regeneration/indestructible apply (regular destruction). Pair with `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(OPPONENTS_TURN_BEFORE_ATTACKERS)`. |
| `MustBeBlockedByAllCreaturesEffect` | `()` | all creatures able to block this must do so (static, Lure-style) |
| `MustBeBlockedByAllCreaturesThisTurnEffect` | `()` | all creatures able to block the target creature this turn do so (one-shot, sets transient flag, cleared at end of turn). Unlike MustBeBlockedByAllCreaturesEffect which is static, this is for spells like Alluring Scent |
| `MustBeBlockedIfAbleEffect` | `()` | at least one creature must block this if able (static, Gaea's Protector-style) |
| `MustBeBlockedIfAbleThisTurnEffect` | `()` | target creature must be blocked this turn if able (one-shot, sets transient flag, cleared at end of turn). Unlike MustBeBlockedIfAbleEffect which is static, this is for spells like Emergent Growth |
| `MustBlockSourceEffect` | `(UUID sourcePermanentId)` | target creature must block source permanent this turn if able. Pass `null` and the source is snapshotted at resolution: from the permanent for activated abilities / combat triggers, or (in a targeted `MayEffect` ETB — Giant Ambush Beetle) from the ETB stack entry's `sourcePermanentId` |
| `MustBlockTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` = groups (0, 1) / `(int blockerTargetGroup, int blockedTargetGroup)` | two-target spell: the creature chosen for the blocker group must block the creature chosen for the blocked group this turn if able (Hunt Down). Group indices address the card's `target()` declarations, like `FightTargetsEffect` |
| `MustBlockThisTurnIfAbleEffect` | `()` | single-target: the target creature must be declared as a blocker this turn if it can block any attacker — the general "blocks this turn if able" requirement with no particular attacker (sets `Permanent.mustBlockThisTurnIfAble`, cleared at end of turn by `resetModifiers`). Unlike `MustBlockSourceEffect` (Provoke, block one specific attacker), no source snapshot. Enforced in `CombatBlockService.validateMustBlockIfAbleRequirements` (satisfied vacuously when the creature can't legally block any declared attacker). Used by Nacatl Hunt-Pride |
| `AssignCombatDamageAsThoughUnblockedEffect` | `()` | assign combat damage as though unblocked (static) |
| `AssignCombatDamageToDefendingCreatureWhenUnblockedEffect` | `()` | static (e.g. Cunning Giant): "If this creature is unblocked, you may have it assign its combat damage to a creature defending player controls." When the source attacks unblocked and the defending player controls a creature, the attacking player is prompted (combat-damage-assignment interaction) to send all of the source's combat damage either to the defending player or to a single defending creature — no splitting (CR 510.1c). |
| `AssignCombatDamageWithToughnessEffect` | `()` or `(GrantScope scope)` | assign combat damage using toughness instead of power (static). No-arg defaults to `EQUIPPED_CREATURE` (toughness > power only, equipment/aura pattern). Use `ALL_OWN_CREATURES` for controller-wide effect that always uses toughness (e.g. Belligerent Brontodon), or `ALL_CREATURES` for a global effect covering every creature regardless of controller (e.g. Doran, the Siege Tower). |
| `MakeCreatureUnblockableEffect` | `()` or `(boolean selfTargeting)` | target creature is unblockable this turn. No-arg (false) targets another permanent; `true` makes the source creature unblockable (self-targeting, e.g. Trespassing Souleater). **Multi-target:** the handler fans over `entry.getTargetIds()` (falling back to `targetId`/`sourcePermanentId`), so it can bind to a `targetX` creature group for "X target creatures can't be blocked this turn" (Open into Wonder) |
| `MakeAllCreaturesUnblockableEffect` | `()` | all creatures on all battlefields can't be blocked this turn |
| `MakeCreatureBlockableOnlyByFilterThisTurnEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate blockerPredicate, String allowedBlockersDescription)` | targeted one-shot: the target creature can be blocked only by blockers matching the predicate until end of turn — the single-target counterpart of `GrantCanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterToOwnCreaturesEffect`. Adds a `CanBeBlockedOnlyByFilterEffect` to the target's `blockRestrictionsUntilEndOfTurn` (consumed by `GameQueryService.getBlockRestriction`, cleared by `resetModifiers`). Joven's Tools = `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(WALL)`, "Walls" |
| `CantBlockThisTurnEffect` | `(TapUntapScope scope[, PermanentPredicate filter])` | creature(s) can't block this turn (one-shot). Scope axis (reuses `TapUntapScope`): `TARGET` (target creature, with multi-target-group handling — Seismic Shift/Panic Attack up to N), `TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS` (creatures controlled by target player, or the targeted planeswalker's controller — rides the shared target, e.g. Concussive Bolt), `ALL_CREATURES` (every battlefield's creatures matching `filter` — Hero of Oxid Ridge `PermanentPowerAtMostPredicate(1)`, Ruthless Invasion `Not(IsArtifact)`). Replaces the former `TargetCreatureCantBlockThisTurnEffect`, `TargetPlayerCreaturesCantBlockThisTurnEffect` and the predicate-filtered mass `CantBlockThisTurnEffect(PermanentPredicate)`. Distinct from the static `CantBlockEffect` and `CantBlockSourceEffect`. |
| `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackOrBlockEffect` | `()` | enchanted creature can't attack or block (static, Pacifism-style) |
| `EnchantedPermanentConditionalEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, CardEffect ifMatch, CardEffect ifNotMatch)` | conditional wrapper for aura static effects: if the enchanted permanent matches the predicate, `ifMatch` is active; otherwise `ifNotMatch` is active. Only applies while the source aura is attached to the target permanent. Composes existing effects (e.g. `StaticBoostEffect` + `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackOrBlockEffect`). Static handler delegates to the active inner effect's handler and evaluates predicates with `matchesStaticFilter(...)`; combat system unwraps automatically via `hasAuraWithEffect`. Use `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(...)` for subtype cases. |
| `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackEffect` | `()` | enchanted creature can't attack but can still block (static, Forced Worship-style) |
| `EnchantedCreatureCanAttackAsThoughHasteEffect` | `()` | enchanted creature can attack as though it had haste (attack-only summoning-sickness bypass, static, Instill Energy-style; read in `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack` via `hasAuraWithEffect`). Does NOT lift summoning sickness for `{T}` ability activation — that's why it isn't `GrantKeywordEffect(HASTE, ENCHANTED)` |
| `EnchantedCreatureCanOnlyAttackAloneEffect` | `()` | enchanted creature can be declared as an attacker only if it is the sole attacker (static, Errantry-style; validated at declaration time in CombatAttackService — the mirror of `CantAttackOrBlockAloneEffect`) |
| `EnchantedCreatureCantActivateAbilitiesEffect` | `()` | enchanted creature's activated abilities can't be activated (static, Arrest-style) |
| `EnchantedCreatureCantActivateTapAbilitiesEffect` | `()` | enchanted creature's activated abilities with `{T}` in their costs can't be activated — non-tap abilities stay usable (static, Serra Bestiary). Enforced in `AbilityActivationService` on the mana-tap and `isRequiresTap()` paths |
| `EnchantedPlayerCantActivateNonManaNonLoyaltyAbilitiesEffect` | `()` | static on a Curse Aura enchanting a player: that player can activate only mana abilities (CR 605.1a) and loyalty abilities — every other activated ability (battlefield/graveyard/hand) is blocked (Overwhelming Splendor). Detected via `GameQueryService.playerCantActivateNonManaOrLoyaltyAbilities`; enforced at each activation entry point in `AbilityActivationService`. Pair with `LosesAllAbilitiesEffect(ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES)` + `SetBasePowerToughnessEffect(1, 1, ENCHANTED_PLAYER_CREATURES)` for the full card |
| `LockTargetPermanentEffect` | `(boolean locksAttacking, boolean locksBlocking, boolean locksActivatedAbilities, EffectDuration duration)` | resolved (non-static) targeted lock: stamps a `FloatingContinuousEffect` carrying the `PermanentLockEffect` facts onto the target creature. Attack side read in `CombatAttackService.canCreatureAttack`, block side in `GameQueryService.findBlockDenial`, activation side in `AbilityActivationService.validateNotBlockedByStaticAbilityLock` (mana abilities included; triggered abilities unaffected). Duration drives expiry (`UNTIL_END_OF_TURN` = cleanup, `UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN` = ability controller's next turn start). Edifice of Authority: `(true,false,false,UNTIL_END_OF_TURN)` = "can't attack this turn"; `(true,true,true,UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN)` = Detain. Targeted `harmful(CREATURE)`. |

## Tap / untap

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `TapPermanentsEffect` | `(TapUntapScope scope[, PermanentPredicate filter])` | taps permanent(s) as an effect (fires "becomes tapped" triggers). Scope axis (see `TapUntapScope`): `TARGET` (tap target, with mixed multi-target-group handling), `SELF` (tap the source, works even if already tapped), `ENCHANTED` (tap the aura's attached creature), `TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS` (targets a player, taps their permanents matching `filter`), `ALL_CREATURES` (every battlefield's creatures matching `filter` — e.g. `Not(HasKeyword(FLYING))` for Deluge, `PermanentIsAttackingPredicate` for Clinging Mists). Replaces the former Tap{Target,Self,EnchantedCreature,PermanentsOfTargetPlayer,AllAttackingCreatures,Creatures} records |
| `UntapPermanentsEffect` | `(TapUntapScope scope[, PermanentPredicate filter])` | untaps permanent(s) as an effect (no triggers). Scope axis: `TARGET` (untap target; `filter` acts as targeting restriction via the spec predicate, e.g. `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate` for Voltaic Servant), `ALL_TARGETS` (multi-target, iterates `getTargetIds()`), `SELF`, `CONTROLLED` (untap all permanents you control matching `filter`, e.g. `PermanentIsLandPredicate`), `OTHER_CONTROLLED_CREATURES` (untap each other creature you control matching `filter`; excludes source by permanent id), `ATTACKED_CREATURES` (untap creatures that attacked this turn). Replaces the former Untap{Target,AllTarget,Self,AllControlled,EachOtherCreatureYouControl,AttackedCreatures} records |
| `TapOrUntapTargetPermanentEffect` | `()` | tap or untap target permanent (controller's choice) |
| `RemoveTargetFromCombatEffect` | `()` | removes target permanent from combat (clears attacking/blocking state); combine with `UntapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)` for Maze of Ith / Spires of Orazca style effects |
| `DoesntUntapEffect` | build via static factories (raw ctor is `(TapUntapScope scope, UntapLockCondition condition)`, validated so scope↔condition pairings are legal): `DoesntUntapEffect.self()`, `.enchanted()`, `.targetWhileSourceOnBattlefield()`, `.targetWhileSourceTapped()` | permanent doesn't untap during its controller's untap step. Reuses the `TapUntapScope` enum. Factories: `self()` = `SELF`+`ALWAYS` (this permanent never untaps — a continuous static effect in `EffectSlot.STATIC`; Colossus of Sardia, Traxos, Grimgrin, Elaborate Firecannon), `enchanted()` = `ENCHANTED`+`ALWAYS` (the attached aura/equipment's host never untaps — STATIC on the aura, read via aura lookup; Claustrophobia, Dehydration, Numbing Dose, Heavy Arbalest), `targetWhileSourceOnBattlefield()` = `TARGET`+`WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD` (target doesn't untap while the source stays on the battlefield — resolved on the stack, uses `untapPreventedWhileSourceOnBattlefieldIds`; Dungeon Geists, Time of Ice), `targetWhileSourceTapped()` = `TARGET`+`WHILE_SOURCE_TAPPED` (target doesn't untap while the source stays tapped — uses `untapPreventedByPermanentIds`; Rust Tick). The `TARGET` variants declare no targeting flags — they piggyback on a companion `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)` (or a saga-chapter/ability target filter) on the same slot |
| `MayNotUntapDuringUntapStepEffect` | `()` | controller may choose not to untap this permanent during untap step (static); prompts player via may-ability system |
| `PayManaPerTappedCreatureToUntapEffect` | `(int manaPerCreature, PermanentPredicate creatureFilter)` | `EACH_UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` (Magnetic Mountain): "that player may choose any number of tapped [matching] creatures they control and pay {manaPerCreature} for each creature chosen this way. If the player does, untap those." Acting player = the stack entry's `targetId` (the active player). The handler gathers that player's tapped permanents matching `creatureFilter`, caps the count by what they can afford (`pool.getTotal() / manaPerCreature`), and begins a `MultiPermanentChoice` (`MultiPermanentChoiceContext.PayManaPerCreatureUntap`). When answered, `MultiPermanentChoiceHandlerService` pays `manaPerCreature`×chosen generic from that player's pool and untaps the chosen creatures (via `TapUntapSupport.untapPermanent`, firing becomes-untapped triggers); empty selection = untap none. Pair with STATIC `MatchingPermanentsDoesntUntapEffect(sameFilter)` for the untap lock |
| `StaticOrbEffect` | `(maxUntap, filter, requiresUntappedSource)` | global "can't untap more than N [matching] permanents during untap steps" lock (Static Orb `()`=cap 2/all/while-untapped; Stoic Angel and Smoke `(1, PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, false)`=cap 1/creatures/always; Winter Orb `(1, PermanentIsLandPredicate, true)`=cap 1/lands/while-untapped). `TurnProgressionService.advanceTurn` pauses the untap step when `UntapStepService.bindingUntapRestriction` finds an active carrier whose filtered candidate pool exceeds `maxUntap`, and begins a `MultiPermanentChoice` (`MultiPermanentChoiceContext.StaticOrbUntap`, maxCount `maxUntap`) over the matching candidates; the answer resumes via `resumeStaticOrbUntap` → `untapChosenPermanents`, so only the chosen matching permanents untap while permanents the filter excludes untap normally. No card-side targeting |
| `SkipNextUntapEffect` | `(TapUntapScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(TapUntapScope scope)` | one-shot "doesn't untap during its controller's next untap step"; increments `skipUntapCount` (decremented each untap step) on the scoped permanent(s). Scopes: `TARGET` (the entry's target — piggybacks on companion targeting effect e.g. `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)`, permanent-targeting spec; Frost Titan / Watertrap Weaver / Wall of Frost / Deluge Virtuoso), `SELF` (the source permanent itself — no targeting; use on a self-referential trigger like `ON_ATTACK`; Lead Golem), `TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS` (permanents matching `filter` that the target player controls, player-targeting spec; Sleep = `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate`), `ALL_CREATURES` (every creature matching `filter` across all battlefields; Clinging Mists = `PermanentIsAttackingPredicate`, pair with `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.ALL_CREATURES, new PermanentIsAttackingPredicate())`). Reuses the `TapUntapScope` enum |
| `SkipNextUntapEffect` | `(TapUntapScope scope, PermanentPredicate filter)` or `(TapUntapScope scope)` | one-shot "doesn't untap during its controller's next untap step"; increments `skipUntapCount` (decremented each untap step) on the scoped permanent(s). Scopes: `TARGET` (the entry's target — piggybacks on companion targeting effect e.g. `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.TARGET)`, `canTargetPermanent()`; Frost Titan / Watertrap Weaver / Wall of Frost / Deluge Virtuoso), `SELF` (the source permanent itself — no targeting; use on a self-referential trigger like `ON_ATTACK`; Lead Golem), `TARGET_PLAYERS_PERMANENTS` (permanents matching `filter` that the target player controls, `canTargetPlayer()`; Sleep = `PermanentIsCreaturePredicate`), `ALL_CREATURES` (every creature matching `filter` across all battlefields; Clinging Mists = `PermanentIsAttackingPredicate`, pair with `TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.ALL_CREATURES, new PermanentIsAttackingPredicate())`). Reuses the `TapUntapScope` enum |
| `SkipNextCombatPhaseEffect` | `()` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER trigger: the player dealt combat damage skips their next combat phase. Non-targeting — `CombatDamageService` bakes the damaged player in as the stack entry's `targetId`; the handler increments per-player `GameData.skipNextCombatPhaseCount`. `TurnProgressionService.advanceStep` reads it when that player leaves precombat main and jumps straight to postcombat main, decrementing the counter. Blinding Angel |
| `IfWonClashEffect` | `(CardEffect wrapped)` | clash-only marker for the "If you won, ..." clause on `EffectSlot.ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES`. Not a stack effect — `TriggerCollectionService.fireClashTriggers` includes the wrapped effect in the trigger's resolved effect list only when the controller won the clash (winner fixed at trigger time). Targeting delegates to `wrapped`. Clash itself is a 2-player action performed by `performClash` (both reveal top card, strictly-higher mana value wins). `ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES` triggers are inert until a card *initiates* a clash (see `ClashEffect`). See Entangling Trap: `TapPermanentsEffect(TARGET)` + `IfWonClashEffect(SkipNextUntapEffect(TARGET))` |
| `IfLostClashEffect` | `(CardEffect wrapped)` | mirror of `IfWonClashEffect` on `EffectSlot.ON_CONTROLLER_CLASHES`: `fireClashTriggers` includes the wrapped effect only when the controller did **not** win (loss or tie). Pair a won-variant (`IfWonClashEffect`) with a lost-variant when the clash trigger does the same base thing either way but only a detail differs by outcome, so exactly one branch fires. See Rebellion of the Flamekin: two `MayPayManaEffect("{1}", CreateTokenEffect(3/1 Elemental Shaman …))` entries that differ only in `grantedKeywordsUntilEndOfTurn = HASTE` on the won branch. Non-targeting, so the trigger goes straight onto the stack |
| `ClashEffect` | `(List<CardEffect> beforeClash, CardEffect onWin, boolean repeatWhileWinning)`; convenience `(CardEffect onWin)` = `(List.of(), onWin, false)` | the clash-*source* stack effect. Each iteration the handler dispatches the `beforeClash` effects (via their own handlers, against the same entry), calls `TriggerCollectionService.performClash` for the controller, on a win dispatches `onWin` against the same stack entry (so it acts on the source permanent), and with `repeatWhileWinning` repeats the whole sequence until the first lost clash (deck-out counts as a loss). "Clash with an opponent. If you win, [X]" = `ClashEffect(X)` (`onWin` may be null for a bare clash); "[body], then clash with an opponent. If you win, repeat this process" = `ClashEffect(body, null, true)`. Mirrors `FlipCoinWinEffect`. See Oaken Brawler: `ClashEffect(new PutCountersOnSourceEffect(1, 1, 1))`; Hoarder's Greed: `ClashEffect(List.of(new LoseLifeEffect(2), new DrawCardEffect(2)), null, true)`. Delegates its `targetSpec()` to `onWin`/`beforeClash`, so a targeted win reward works on a targeting slot — Springjack Knight: `ON_ATTACK` `ClashEffect(new GrantKeywordEffect(Keyword.DOUBLE_STRIKE, GrantScope.TARGET))` (target chosen when the trigger goes on the stack) |
| `UntapAllPermanentsYouControlDuringEachOtherPlayersStepEffect` | `(TurnStep step)` or `(TurnStep step, PermanentPredicate filter)` | untap permanents you control during each other player's step. `filter=null` (1-arg form) untaps all; provide a predicate (e.g. `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate`) to untap only matching permanents |
| `UntapUpToControlledPermanentsEffect` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter)` | untap up to N tapped permanents the controller controls matching filter; if filter is null, any tapped permanent qualifies |
| `UntapChosenPermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate)` | "untap target [permanent]" for a triggered ability on a slot with **no targeting pipeline** (e.g. `ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER`). The effect is pushed non-targeting; at resolution `UntapChosenPermanentEffectHandler` collects every permanent matching `predicate` across all battlefields and begins a `MultiPermanentChoiceContext.UntapChosenPermanent` (maxCount 1) — the controller's chosen permanent is untapped when answered. Use instead of `UntapPermanentsEffect(TARGET)` when the trigger slot can't carry a cast-time target. Initiate's Companion: `PermanentAnyOfPredicate(creature, land)` |
| `RegisterDelayedUntapPermanentsEffect` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter)` | registers a delayed trigger that fires at the beginning of the next end step, putting an `UntapUpToControlledPermanentsEffect(count, filter)` on the stack. Used by Teferi, Hero of Dominaria +1 with `PermanentIsLandPredicate` |
| `RegisterDelayedCreateTokenEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect tokenEffect)` | registers a delayed trigger that fires at the beginning of the next end step, putting the wrapped `tokenEffect` on the stack so the token(s) are created under the resolving controller's control. Stored in `GameData.delayedActions` (`DelayedCreateToken`), drained in `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers`. Used by Rukh Egg's ON_DEATH trigger |
| `RegisterDrawCardsAtNextUpkeepEffect` | `(int count)` | `CardDrawingEffect`; registers a `DrawCardsAtNextUpkeep` delayed action so the resolving controller draws `count` cards at the beginning of the next turn's upkeep. Drained in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers` regardless of active player. No-arg `()` = 1. Used by Blessed Wine |
| `RegisterDamageAtNextUpkeepUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int damage, String manaCost)` | SPELL registrar (Quenchable Fire). Reads the spell's already-chosen target (player or planeswalker) from `entry.targetId` — declares no target of its own (`TargetSpec.NONE`), so pair it with a `DealDamageToTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerEffect` in the same slot — and queues a `DamageAtNextUpkeepUnlessPays(spellControllerId, targetId, damage, manaCost, sourceCard)` delayed action. Drained in `StepTriggerService.handleUpkeepTriggers` only at the **spell controller's** upkeep: resolves the paying party (targeted player, else targeted planeswalker's controller; fizzles if gone) and pushes a `DamageTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerUnlessPaysEffect` trigger controlled by that payer with the target on `entry.targetId` |
| `DamageTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int damage, String manaCost)` | `DamageDealingEffect` (player-only). The pushed half of Quenchable Fire's delayed trigger — never cast directly. On resolution its handler prompts the payer (`entry.controllerId`) with a "you may pay `manaCost`" may-ability, stashing the damage recipient on `PendingMayAbility.targetCardId`; declining or being unable to pay deals `damage` to that player/planeswalker via `DealDamageToTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerEffectHandler` (mayfx `DamageTargetPlayerOrPlaneswalkerUnlessPaysHandler`) |
| `RegisterDelayedCombatDamageLootEffect` | `(int drawAmount, int discardAmount)` | registers a delayed triggered ability for the rest of the turn: whenever one or more creatures you control deal combat damage to a player, draw N then discard N. Fires once per combat damage step. Stored in `GameData.delayedActions` (`DelayedCombatDamageLoot`), checked in `CombatDamageService`. Used by Jace, Cunning Castaway's +1 |
| `RegisterDelayedReturnCardFromGraveyardToHandEffect` | `(UUID cardId)` | registers a delayed trigger that fires at the beginning of the next end step, returning the card from its owner's graveyard to their hand (if still there). Used by Tiana, Ship's Caretaker with `ON_ALLY_AURA_OR_EQUIPMENT_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_FROM_BATTLEFIELD` slot |
| `RegisterDelayedReturnDamagedCreatureUnderControlEffect` | `()` | `ON_DAMAGED_CREATURE_DIES` effect (Seraph). Reads the dying creature's card id from `StackEntry.triggeringCardId` (baked in by `GraveyardService.triggerDamagedCreatureDiesAbilities`) and queues `DelayedGraveyardToBattlefieldUnderControl(cardId, controllerId, seraphPermanentId)`. Drained in `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers`: the card returns from its owner's graveyard onto the battlefield under the controller with a PERMANENT `GainControlOfTargetEffect` floating control effect + `stolenCreatures` ownership record (so a stolen opponent's creature stays controlled yet dies to its owner's graveyard). The returned permanent is linked to the Seraph in `GameData.seraphReturnedCreatures`; `StateBasedActionService.sacrificeCreaturesOnSeraphControlLoss` sacrifices linked creatures when their controller loses control of the still-on-battlefield Seraph (a Seraph that leaves drops the linkage — no sacrifice) |
| `RegisterCombatDamageReflectionEffect` | `()` | registers a delayed triggered ability for the rest of the turn: whenever an attacking creature deals combat damage to the resolving controller, it deals that much damage back to its controller (the attacking player), with the attacking creature as the damage source. Fires once per attacking creature per combat damage step. Stored in `GameData.delayedActions` (`DelayedCombatDamageReflection`), checked in `CombatDamageService.processCombatDamageReflectionTriggers`, cleared at turn cleanup. Used by Harsh Justice (paired with `DECLARE_ATTACKERS_IF_ATTACKED` cast restriction) |
| `ReturnTriggeringLandFromGraveyardToBattlefieldEffect` | `(UUID landCardId)` | immediately returns the identified land from the graveyard to the battlefield under the ability controller's (= graveyard owner's) control; fizzles if it is no longer in a graveyard. Register the template with `null`; the `ON_ALLY_LAND_PUT_INTO_GRAVEYARD_BY_OPPONENT` collector stamps the concrete land card id. Used by Sacred Ground |
| `RegisterDelayedManaEqualToTargetSpellManaValueEffect` | `(ManaColor color)` | Scattering Stroke's clash-win reward. Wrap in `ClashEffect` on a "counter target spell" card **before** the `CounterSpellEffect` so the targeted spell is still on the stack; reads `entry.getTargetId()`'s mana value (`getManaValue()+getXValue()`) and queues an `AddManaAtNextMainPhase` delayed action. Drained in `StepTriggerService.handlePrecombatMainTriggers` for the active player, which pushes a `MayEffect(AwardManaEffect(color, amount))` ("you may add that much mana") onto the stack at the beginning of their next main phase |
| `UnattachEquipmentFromTargetPermanentsEffect` | `()` | unattach all equipment from target permanents (multi-target) |

## Control / steal

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `TargetPlayerGainsControlOfSourceCreatureEffect` | `()` | target opponent gains control of this creature (ETB) |
| `PlayerWithMostLifeGainsControlOfSourceCreatureEffect` | `()` | the player with strictly the most life gains permanent control of this creature; no-op on a tie for most life (intervening-if). Ghazbán Ogre (`UPKEEP_TRIGGERED`) |
| `GainControlOfTargetEffect` | `(ControlDuration duration[, CardSubtype grantedSubtype][, boolean tapWhenControlLost])` | gain control of target permanent for the given duration. `ControlDuration{PERMANENT, END_OF_TURN, WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD}`. PERMANENT optionally grants a subtype (Captivating Vampire "It becomes a Vampire") and supports multi-target (iterates `getTargetIds()` for "up to N target" abilities); END_OF_TURN (Threaten, Metallic Mastery — card's target filter handles type restriction) wears off in end-of-turn cleanup; WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD (Olivia Voldaren) ends when the source leaves the battlefield or its creator stops controlling it. Every resolution creates a floating `L2_CONTROL` continuous effect (CR 613.2/613.7) via `CreatureControlService.applyControlEffect`; the controller of a permanent is DERIVED from the newest active control effect (`GameData.deriveControllerOf`), so an expiring steal falls back to the next most recent still-active effect, not blindly to the owner. Haste/untap riders (Act of Treason) are composed as separate effects on the card. `tapWhenControlLost=true` (Magus of the Unseen "When you lose control of the artifact, tap it") records the target in `GameData.permanentsToTapWhenControlLost` at resolution; `TurnCleanupService.applyCleanupResets` taps those permanents as the END_OF_TURN control effect expires and clears the set |
| `AttachTargetToSourcePermanentEffect` | `()` | attach the targeted permanent to the source permanent (e.g. steal Equipment and equip it — combine with `GainControlOfTargetEffect(END_OF_TURN)`) |
| `GainControlOfAllLandsTargetPlayerControlsEffect` | `()` | gain permanent control of every land the target player controls at resolution (player-targeting spec, Gilt-Leaf Archdruid). Applies one per-land `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating `L2_CONTROL` effect via `CreatureControlService.applyControlEffect` — reuses the standard control machinery, adds no new layer classification |
| `GainControlOfAllPermanentsMatchingEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate)` | non-targeted mass steal: at resolution gain permanent control of every permanent (any controller) matching the predicate that you don't already control (Karrthus, Tyrant of Jund — `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(DRAGON)`). Collects matches first (control-gain moves permanents between battlefield lists), then applies one per-permanent `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating `L2_CONTROL` effect via `CreatureControlService.applyControlEffect` — same machinery as `GainControlOfAllLandsTargetPlayerControlsEffect`, selected by predicate instead of target player, adds no new layer classification |
| `JuxtaposeEffect` | `()` | Juxtapose: `SPELL`, self-declares a single player target (player-targeting spec, read from `entry.getTargetId()`). The controller and target player exchange control of the creature they each control with the greatest mana value, then exchange artifacts the same way. Driven by `JuxtaposeSupport`: one type at a time (creatures first, then artifacts on the updated board, so an artifact creature can move in both steps); each type resolves the controller's participant then the target's; a tie for greatest MV prompts that permanent's controller via `PermanentChoiceContext.JuxtaposeTieBreak`; if either player controls no permanent of the current type that exchange is skipped. Swaps controllers permanently via two `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating effects (same swap mechanic as `ExchangeControlOfTargetPermanentsEffect`) |
| `GainControlOfAllLandsTargetPlayerControlsEffect` | `()` | gain permanent control of every land the target player controls at resolution (`canTargetPlayer`, Gilt-Leaf Archdruid). Applies one per-land `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating `L2_CONTROL` effect via `CreatureControlService.applyControlEffect` — reuses the standard control machinery, adds no new layer classification |
| `GainControlOfCombatOpponentAtEndOfCombatEffect` | `()` | The Wretched's "At end of combat, gain control of all creatures blocking this creature for as long as you control this creature". Implements `ControlStealingEffect` (`controlDuration()` = `WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD`). Placed on `ON_BECOMES_BLOCKED` with `TriggerMode.PER_BLOCKER` (blockers only — not creatures this permanent blocks). Resolution (handler) carries the blocker as `entry.getTargetId()` and the source as `entry.getSourcePermanentId()`, and queues a `GainControlOfPermanentAtEndOfCombat` delayed action. Drained in `CombatService.processEndOfCombatControlGains()`, which re-checks the source still exists and is still controlled by the gaining player, then applies a `WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD` `GainControlOfTargetEffect` floating `L2_CONTROL` effect keyed to the source via `CreatureControlService.applyControlEffect` |
| `JuxtaposeEffect` | `()` | Juxtapose: `SPELL`, self-declares a single player target (`canTargetPlayer()`, read from `entry.getTargetId()`). The controller and target player exchange control of the creature they each control with the greatest mana value, then exchange artifacts the same way. Driven by `JuxtaposeSupport`: one type at a time (creatures first, then artifacts on the updated board, so an artifact creature can move in both steps); each type resolves the controller's participant then the target's; a tie for greatest MV prompts that permanent's controller via `PermanentChoiceContext.JuxtaposeTieBreak`; if either player controls no permanent of the current type that exchange is skipped. Swaps controllers permanently via two `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating effects (same swap mechanic as `ExchangeControlOfTargetPermanentsEffect`) |
| `ExchangeControlOfTargetPermanentsEffect` | `()` | Puca's Mischief: exchange control of the two `targetIds` — `[0]` a nonland permanent you control, `[1]` a nonland permanent an opponent controls with mana value ≤ target [0]. `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED`, wrapped in `MayEffect` (resolution-time "may", like Axis of Mortality). The two interdependent targets are chosen at trigger time by a bespoke two-step permanent choice (`StepTriggerService.processNextPucasMischiefTarget` → `PermanentChoiceContext.PucasMischiefOwnTarget`/`PucasMischiefOpponentTarget`, patterned on Capricious Efreet). At resolution re-checks legality (both still on the battlefield, control roles unchanged, MV restriction still holds; CR 701.10) and, if legal, swaps controllers permanently via two `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating `L2_CONTROL` effects |
| `ExchangeControlOfSharedTypeTargetsAndDestroyAurasEffect` | `()` | Gauntlets of Chaos: exchange control of the two `targetIds` — `[0]` an artifact/creature/land you control, `[1]` a permanent an opponent controls sharing one of those types. Multi-target activated ability (`{5}` + `SacrificeSelfCost`). The interdependent "shares one of those types" restriction is enforced at announcement via `ActivatedAbility.withMultiTargetConstraint(MultiTargetConstraint.SHARE_ARTIFACT_CREATURE_OR_LAND_TYPE)` (checked in `TargetLegalityService.validateMultiTargetConstraint` using `GameQueryService.sharesArtifactCreatureOrLandType`); per-position filter [1] is just "artifact/creature/land an opponent controls". At resolution re-checks legality (control roles unchanged, still share a type; CR 701.10), swaps controllers permanently via two `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` floating `L2_CONTROL` effects, then destroys every Aura attached to either permanent (snapshotted before the swap; `DestructionSupport.tryDestroyAndLog`) |
| `GainControlOfEnchantedTargetEffect` | `()` | gain control of enchanted permanent (static, Control Magic-style) |
| `GainControlOfLandDefendingPlayerControlsAndAssignNoCombatDamageEffect` | `()` | Orcish Squatters. `ControlStealingEffect` (WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD). Wrap in `MayEffect` on `ON_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED` (`targetId`=defender, `sourcePermanentId`=attacker). Handler presents a max-1 choice among the defender's lands; completion in `MultiPermanentChoiceHandlerService.handleGainControlOfLandAndAssignNoCombatDamage` takes control via a wrapped `GainControlOfTargetEffect(WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD)` and, only when a land is taken, adds the attacker to `creaturesPreventedFromDealingCombatDamage` |
| `GainControlOfTargetAuraEffect` | `()` | gain control of target aura |
| `GainControlIfSubtypesDealtCombatDamageEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype, int threshold)` | end-step trigger: gain control of target nonland permanent controlled by a player dealt combat damage by `threshold`+ creatures of `subtype` this turn. Intervening-if + targeting handled by StepTriggerService; resolves via `GainControlOfTargetEffect(PERMANENT)` |
| `ControlEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | control enchanted creature (static) |
| `ClashForControlOfEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | Captivating Glance. Non-targeting `CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` effect on an Aura: clashes with an opponent for the aura's controller, then gives control of the enchanted creature to the clash winner — the controller on a win, otherwise the clash opponent (a tie counts as "otherwise"). Uses `entry.getSourcePermanentId()` → aura's `attachedTo` to find the creature; delegates to `performClash` + `CreatureControlService.applyControlEffect` (PERMANENT floating control effect) |
| `SacrificeEnchantedPermanentAndReattachSourceAuraEffect` | `()` | Nettlevine Blight. `ENCHANTED_PERMANENT_CONTROLLER_END_STEP_TRIGGERED` Aura effect (fires on the enchanted permanent's controller's end step; slot handled in `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers`, keyed on `findPermanentController(aura.attachedTo) == activePlayer`). Resolution: that player sacrifices the enchanted permanent, then moves the Aura (via `Permanent.setAttachedTo`, keeping its controller) onto another creature/land they control. Uses `entry.getSourcePermanentId()` for the Aura. Auto-attaches with 0/1 destination; prompts (`PermanentChoiceContext.ReattachSourceAuraAfterSacrifice`, completed in `PermanentChoiceBattlefieldHandlerService`) with 2+, deferring the sacrifice so the Aura isn't orphaned mid-choice. No destination → Aura left unattached, removed by `removeOrphanedAuras` SBA |
| `GrantSupertypeToEnchantedPermanentEffect` | `(CardSupertype supertype)` | enchanted permanent gains the specified supertype (static). E.g. In Bolas's Clutches — "Enchanted permanent is legendary." Integrates with legend rule |
| `EnchantedCreatureDealsDamageToItsOwnerEffect` | `(int damage)` | enchanted creature deals N damage to its owner (the original owner, not current controller). Use on `UPKEEP_TRIGGERED` slot for auras that steal + ping owner |
| `EnchantedCreatureDealsDamageEqualToDealtDamageToControllerEffect` | `()` | deals xValue damage to the enchanted creature's controller. Use on `ON_ENCHANTED_CREATURE_DEALT_DAMAGE` (Spiteful Shadows — damage the creature *was dealt*) or `ON_ENCHANTED_CREATURE_DEALS_DAMAGE_TO_YOU` (Backfire — damage the creature *dealt to* the Aura's controller) |

## Prevention / protection / redirection

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `PreventDamageEffect` | static factories: `nextToAny(int)` (Samite Healer), `nextToController(int)` (Esper Battlemage), `nextToSelf(int)` (Ethereal Champion), `nextToTarget(int)` / `nextToTarget(DynamicAmount)` (Healing Salve; `new XValue()` for Alabaster Potion), `allCombat()` (Fog, Holy Day), `allToCreatures()` (Blinding Fog), `allToTargetCreatures()` (Wellgabber Apothecary, Redeem multi-target), `allCombatToTargetCreatures()` (Foxfire), `allByTargetCreatures()` (Soul Parry, Inquisitor's Snare), `allCombatByTargetCreatures()` (Resistance Fighter; Foxfire pairs to-and-by), `allToSelf()` (Gideon of the Trials 0 — no target, shields the source and stops planeswalker loyalty loss), `allByTargetPermanentUntilNextTurn()` (Gideon of the Trials +1 — benign PERMANENT target; stored in `permanentsPreventedFromDealingDamageUntilNextTurn` and expires at the controller's next turn, read via `GameData.isPreventedFromDealingDamage`), `allToControllerAndCreatures()` (Safe Passage, Endure), `allToControllerFromAttackers()` (Deep Wood, Heavy Fog — pair with `setSpellCastTimingRestriction(DECLARE_ATTACKERS_IF_ATTACKED)`), `fromColors(Set<CardColor>)` (Luminesce), `allCombatExcept(PermanentPredicate)` (Moonmist `PermanentHasAnySubtypePredicate(Set.of(WEREWOLF, WOLF))`) | **collapsed one-shot shield family.** Every "prevent the next N damage to <victim>" and "prevent all [combat] damage to/by <victim> this turn" wording is this record with a `PreventionScope` — never a new effect class. One `PreventDamageEffectHandler` writes the scope's shield-state slot (global/player/creature amount shields, until-end-of-turn flags, color set, combat-exempt predicate); consumption stays in `DamagePreventionService` and shields clear at turn cleanup. `NEXT_TO_TARGET` targets any target (benign ANY_TARGET spec); the two target-creature scopes target creatures (benign CREATURE spec, multi-target via the effect's target group); everything else takes no target. Chosen-source shields (CoP cycle, Sanctum Guardian, Healing Grace), `PreventDividedDamageEffect`, `PreventNextColorDamageToControllerEffect`, and the static always-on markers with riders remain separate records |
| `PreventDividedDamageEffect` | `(int amount)` | "prevent the next N damage this turn to any number of targets, divided as you choose" (Remedy). No `target()` call — per-target shield amounts ride on the cast-time `damageAssignments` map (must sum to N; N caps target count). Each target (creature and/or player) gets a "next X damage" shield. Reuses the divided-damage cast flow (`EffectResolution.needsDamageDistribution`); resolved by `PreventDividedDamageEffectHandler`. Shields cleared at turn cleanup |
| `PreventAllCombatDamageToAndByEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | prevent all combat damage to and dealt by enchanted creature (non-combat damage still applies) |
| `AssignNoCombatDamageAndDefendingPlayerDiscardsEffect` | `()` | the trigger's source (attacking) creature is added to `creaturesPreventedFromDealingCombatDamage` (assigns no combat damage this turn, cleared at turn cleanup) and the defending player (`targetId`) discards a card at random. Reads `sourcePermanentId`=attacker and `targetId`=defender off the stack entry — designed for `ON_ENCHANTED_CREATURE_ATTACKS_UNBLOCKED` (which bakes both). Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may". Used by Cloak of Confusion |
| `PreventCombatDamageToAttackingCreaturesYouControlEffect` | `()` | static: prevent all combat damage that would be dealt to attacking creatures the source's controller controls (e.g. Dolmen Gate). Noncombat damage unaffected. Hooked in `DamagePreventionService.applyCreaturePreventionShield` (checks `permanent.isAttacking()` + `isCombatDamage`) |
| `PreventAllDamageEffect` | `()` | prevent all damage (e.g. Fog-style) |
| `PreventAllDamageToAndByEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | prevent all damage to and dealt by enchanted creature |
| `PreventAllNoncombatDamageToAttachedCreatureEffect` | `()` | prevent all noncombat damage to attached (equipped/enchanted) creature (e.g. Magebane Armor) |
| `PreventColorDamageToEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | STATIC marker on an Aura: prevent all damage (combat + noncombat) to enchanted creature from sources whose colours include the Aura's chosen colour (Prismatic Ward). Pair with `ChooseColorOnEnterEffect`; chosen colour read from the Aura permanent's `getChosenColor()`. Damage-only (unlike protection). Queried in `GameQueryService.isColorDamageToEnchantedCreaturePrevented` from `DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage` + `CombatDamageService.applyCombatCreatureDamage` |
| `PreventXDamageFromEachSourceToAttachedCreatureEffect` | `(int amount)` | prevent N damage from each source to attached (equipped/enchanted) creature (e.g. Shield of the Realm) |
| `PreventNextColorDamageToControllerEffect` | `(CardColor chosenColor)` | prevent next damage of chosen color to controller |
| `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceEffect` | `(ChosenSourcePreventionScope scope, boolean gainLife, boolean controllerOnly, PermanentPredicate sourceFilter, String sourceLabel)`; use the static factories `nextDamageToYou()` / `nextDamageToYouAndGainLife()` / `nextDamageToYou(filter, label)` / `nextDamageToAnyTarget()` / `allDamageToYou()` / `allDamage(filter, label)` | "a source of your choice would deal damage" prevention; the source is chosen on resolution (optionally restricted by `sourceFilter`, with `sourceLabel` filling the choice prompt). Scopes: `NEXT_DAMAGE_TO_CONTROLLER` = one-shot shield on the controller, `gainLife` adds Reverse Damage's "gain that much life" (Pentagram of the Ages plain; Circle of Protection cycle passes a filter â€” colored variants `PermanentColorInPredicate`, CoP: Artifacts `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate`; shield in `gameData.playerSourceNextDamageShields`, consumed by `DamagePreventionService.applyPlayerNextSourceDamageShield`; subsequent events like double strike's second hit still land). `NEXT_DAMAGE_TO_ANY_TARGET` = one-shot shield covering any recipient â€” player, planeswalker, or creature (Sanctum Guardian; source ID in `gameData.sourceNextDamageToAnyTargetShields`, consumed by `DamagePreventionService.applyChosenSourceNextDamageToAnyTargetShield`). `ALL_DAMAGE_THIS_TURN` = whole-turn shield: `controllerOnly` protects just the controller (Auriok Replica; `gameData.playerSourceDamagePreventionIds`) vs everything (Burrenton Forge-Tender with a red filter; `gameData.permanentsPreventedFromDealingDamage`). All cleared at turn cleanup |
| `PreventDamageToTargetFromChosenSourceEffect` | `(int amount)` | prevent next N damage from a chosen source to a specific target this turn. Target chosen on cast, source chosen on resolution (prompts permanent choice). Spec `ANY_TARGET` (e.g. Healing Grace) |
| `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceAndRedirectToAnyTargetEffect` | `(int amount)` | prevent next N damage from a chosen source to controller/controller's permanents this turn; redirects to any target (player or creature). Source chosen on resolution, target chosen on cast. Spec `ANY_TARGET` (e.g. Harm's Way) |
| `PreventXDamageToControllerAndRedirectToTargetPlayerEffect` | `()` | prevent next X damage to controller this turn; if prevented, source creature deals that much to target player (e.g. Vengeful Archon). Uses X-cost ability. player-targeting spec |
| `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceEffect` | `(ChosenSourcePreventionScope scope, boolean gainLife, boolean controllerOnly, PermanentPredicate sourceFilter, String sourceLabel)`; use the static factories `nextDamageToYou()` / `nextDamageToYouAndGainLife()` / `nextDamageToYou(filter, label)` / `nextDamageToAnyTarget()` / `allDamageToYou()` / `allDamage(filter, label)` | "a source of your choice would deal damage" prevention; the source is chosen on resolution (optionally restricted by `sourceFilter`, with `sourceLabel` filling the choice prompt). Scopes: `NEXT_DAMAGE_TO_CONTROLLER` = one-shot shield on the controller, `gainLife` adds Reverse Damage's "gain that much life" (Pentagram of the Ages plain; Circle of Protection cycle passes a filter â€” colored variants `PermanentColorInPredicate`, CoP: Artifacts `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate`; shield in `gameData.playerSourceNextDamageShields`, consumed by `DamagePreventionService.applyPlayerNextSourceDamageShield`; subsequent events like double strike's second hit still land). `NEXT_DAMAGE_TO_ANY_TARGET` = one-shot shield covering any recipient â€” player, planeswalker, or creature (Sanctum Guardian; source ID in `gameData.sourceNextDamageToAnyTargetShields`, consumed by `DamagePreventionService.applyChosenSourceNextDamageToAnyTargetShield`). `ALL_DAMAGE_THIS_TURN` = whole-turn shield: `controllerOnly` protects just the controller (Auriok Replica; `gameData.playerSourceDamagePreventionIds`) vs everything (Burrenton Forge-Tender with a red filter; `gameData.permanentsPreventedFromDealingDamage`). All cleared at turn cleanup |
| `PreventDamageToTargetFromChosenSourceEffect` | `(int amount)` | prevent next N damage from a chosen source to a specific target this turn. Target chosen on cast, source chosen on resolution (prompts permanent choice). `canTargetPlayer()=true`, `canTargetPermanent()=true` (e.g. Healing Grace) |
| `PreventDamageFromChosenSourceAndRedirectToAnyTargetEffect` | `(int amount)` | prevent next N damage from a chosen source to controller/controller's permanents this turn; redirects to any target (player or creature). Source chosen on resolution, target chosen on cast. `canTargetPlayer()=true`, `canTargetPermanent()=true` (e.g. Harm's Way) |
| `EyeForAnEyeEffect` | `()` | one-shot reflection (NOT prevention): the next time the chosen source would deal damage to the controller this turn, that damage still hits the controller AND an equal reflected damage event is dealt back at the source's controller by Eye for an Eye. Source chosen on resolution among all battlefield permanents; stored in `gameData.eyeForAnEyeShields`, applied by `DamagePreventionService.applyEyeForAnEyeReflection` (hooked in `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` + `CombatDamageService.accumulatePlayerDamage`), reflected damage queued in `gameData.pendingEyeForAnEyeReflections` and processed by `processEyeForAnEyeReflections` in both services. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `PreventXDamageToControllerAndRedirectToTargetPlayerEffect` | `()` | prevent next X damage to controller this turn; if prevented, source creature deals that much to target player (e.g. Vengeful Archon). Uses X-cost ability. `canTargetPlayer()=true` |
| `PreventDamageFromOpponentSourcesEffect` | `(int amount)` | prevent N damage from each opponent-controlled source that would deal damage to this permanent's controller (static, e.g. Guardian Seraph). Applied per damage event in both combat and non-combat paths |
| `PreventNoncombatDamageToControllerAndGainLifeEffect` | `()` | static: prevent all noncombat damage that would be dealt to this permanent's controller; they gain life equal to the damage prevented this way (e.g. Purity). Applied in `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` (the noncombat player-damage path) via `DamagePreventionService.applyControllerNoncombatDamagePrevention`; combat damage is unaffected |
| `PreventFixedDamagePerSourceToControllerEffect` | `(int amount)` | static: "If a source would deal damage to you, prevent N of that damage" (e.g. Urza's Armor). Prevents up to `amount` from each source that would deal damage to this permanent's controller, combat and noncombat; multiple copies sum. Applied in `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` (noncombat) and `CombatDamageService.accumulatePlayerDamage` (combat, per attacker) via `DamagePreventionService.applyControllerFixedPerSourceDamagePrevention` |
| `PreventFixedDamageToPlaneswalkersYouControlEffect` | `(int amount)` | static: "If a source would deal damage to a planeswalker you control, prevent N of that damage" (Djeru, With Eyes Open). Planeswalker analogue of Urza's Armor: prevents up to `amount` per source from each damage event to a planeswalker the source's controller controls, combat and noncombat; multiple copies sum. Implements the `PlaneswalkerDamagePreventionEffect` marker interface (query-time FACT, ratchet-exempt). Applied in the planeswalker branches of `DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage` / `resolveAnyTargetDamage` (noncombat) and `CombatDamageService.accumulatePlayerDamage` (combat, per attacker) via `DamagePreventionService.applyPlaneswalkerFixedPerSourceDamagePrevention` |
| `PreventSpellDamageToOpponentAndCreateTokensEffect` | `(CreateTokenEffect token)` | static: if a spell this permanent's controller controls would deal damage to an opponent, prevent that damage and create one `token` per 1 damage prevented (e.g. Hostility). Applied in `DamageSupport.dealDamageToPlayer` via `DamagePreventionService.findSpellDamageToOpponentPrevention`; only spell damage (not abilities/combat) to an opponent qualifies. The `token` blueprint's own amount is ignored — count equals damage prevented |
| `PreventDamageAndAddMinusCountersEffect` | `()` | prevent all damage to this creature and put a -1/-1 counter for each 1 damage prevented (static, e.g. Phyrexian Hydra) |
| `PreventDamageToOtherCreaturesAndAddPlusCountersEffect` | `()` | static: if damage would be dealt to another creature this permanent's controller controls (not the source itself), prevent it and put a +1/+1 counter on that creature for each 1 damage prevented (e.g. Vigor). Applied in `DamagePreventionService.applyCreaturePreventionShield` for both combat and noncombat damage; covers damage from any source |
| `PreventDamageToSelfFromCreaturesEffect` | `()` | static: prevent all damage that would be dealt to this creature by creatures (e.g. Uncle Istvan). Combat + noncombat, but only when the damage source is a creature — noncreature sources (spells, artifacts) still deal damage. Combat prevented in `DamagePreventionService.applyCreaturePreventionShield` (combat source is always a creature); noncombat via `GameQueryService.isCreatureSourceDamageToSelfPrevented` hooked in `DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage` |
| `PreventDamageAndRemovePlusOnePlusOneCountersEffect` | `()` or `(boolean removeOneOnly)` | prevent all damage to this creature and remove +1/+1 counters (static). Default `removeOneOnly=false`: removes counters equal to damage (Protean Hydra). With `removeOneOnly=true`: removes exactly one counter per damage event regardless of damage amount (Unbreathing Horde). Can only remove counters up to the number currently on the creature |
| `DelayedPlusOnePlusOneCounterRegrowthEffect` | `()` | whenever a +1/+1 counter is removed from this creature, put two +1/+1 counters on it at the beginning of the next end step (static, e.g. Protean Hydra). Works with PreventDamageAndRemovePlusOnePlusOneCountersEffect. Registers delayed triggers in GameData.delayedActions (DelayedPlusOneCounters) |
| `ProtectionFromCardTypesEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | protection from specified card types (static, permanent). Unlike `GrantProtectionFromCardTypeUntilEndOfTurnEffect`, this is NOT cleared by `resetModifiers()` — it lives on the card's STATIC effects. Checked by `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromSourceCardTypes()` in both overloads (permanent source and card source) |
| `ProtectionFromColorsEffect` | `(Set<CardColor> colors)` | protection from specified colors (static) |
| `ProtectionFromSubtypesEffect` | `(Set<CardSubtype> subtypes)` | protection from specified creature subtypes (static). Prevents blocking, damage, targeting, and enchanting/equipping by sources with any of the listed subtypes. Also checks transient/granted subtypes and Changeling. Checked by `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromSourceSubtypes()`. Used by Baneslayer Angel (DEMON, DRAGON) |
| `ProtectionFromManaValueEffect` | `(int minManaValue)` | protection from all sources whose mana value is ≥ `minManaValue` (static). Prevents blocking, damage, targeting, and enchanting/equipping by such sources. Checked by `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromSourceManaValue()` in both `hasProtectionFromSource` overloads. Used by Mistmeadow Skulk (3) |
| `ProtectionFromEverythingEffect` | `()` | protection from everything (static, permanent): protection from every source regardless of colour, card type, subtype or mana value. Surfaced via `ProtectionGrantingEffect.protectsFromEverything()`; because every source has a card type it is consulted in `GameQueryService.hasProtectionFromSourceCardTypes()` (both overloads), the shared gate for damage, combat, targeting and enchant/equip. Used by Progenitus |
| `ProtectionFromChosenColorEffect` | `()` | protection from chosen color (static, requires ChooseColorOnEnterEffect) |
| `TargetingRestrictionEffect` | `(TargetingSourceKind kind, boolean opponentOnly, Set<CardColor> colors, TargetColorMode mode)` | static "can't be the target of X" marker scanned at targeting time (collapsed family). Prefer the static factories: `opponentAbilities()` = opponents' abilities can't target, spells still work (Shanna, Sisay's Legacy); `hexproof()` = opponents' spells AND abilities can't target, use with `GrantEffectEffect` (Asceticism); `fromNonColorSources(CardColor)` = can't be targeted by spells/abilities from sources that aren't the allowed color, applies to everyone (Gaea's Revenge); `spells()` = can't be the target of any spell (any color/controller), abilities still work, use with `GrantEffectEffect(..., ALL_CREATURES)` (Dense Foliage); `fromSpellColors(Set<CardColor>)` = can't be the target of spells of those colors, spells only (Karplusan Strider); `hexproofFromColors(Set<CardColor>)` = hexproof from those colors, opponents' colored spells/abilities can't target, CR 702.11 (Knight of Grace BLACK / Knight of Malice WHITE — Scryfall adds a bare "Hexproof" keyword, call `removeKeyword(Keyword.HEXPROOF)`) |
| `GrantEffectEffect` | `(CardEffect effect, GrantScope scope)` | grant a CardEffect to permanents matching scope (e.g. OWN_CREATURES) |
| `RedirectPlayerDamageToEnchantedCreatureEffect` | `()` | redirect damage dealt to player to enchanted creature |
| `RedirectPlayerDamageToSelfEffect` | `()` | STATIC (self): all damage dealt to controller is dealt to this permanent instead (Empyrial Archangel). Queried in `PermanentRemovalService.redirectPlayerDamageToEnchantedCreature` alongside the aura variant |
| `RedirectYourDamageToEnchantedCreatureThisTurnEffect` | `()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD one-shot (Saving Grace): "all damage that would be dealt this turn to you and permanents you control is dealt to enchanted creature instead." Handler installs a turn-scoped `TurnDamageRedirectToCreatureShield(auraController, currentlyEnchantedCreatureId)` in `gameData.turnDamageRedirectToCreatureShields` (destination locked in at resolution — persists even if the aura leaves). Applied via `DamagePreventionService.applyTurnDamageRedirectToCreature` at all four damage entry points (noncombat player/creature in `DamageSupport`, combat player/creature in `CombatDamageService`), keyed on the damaged player or the damaged permanent's controller. Any source, unlimited, reuses `pendingSourceRedirectDamage`/`processSourceRedirectDamage`. Redirect is skipped while the destination is no longer a creature on the battlefield (ruling) and for damage dealt to that destination creature itself. Cleared at turn cleanup. Not a prevention effect — applies even when damage can't be prevented |
| `RedirectUnblockedCombatDamageToSelfEffect` | `()` | redirect unblocked combat damage to this creature |
| `RedirectTargetCreatureDamageFromChosenSourceToSelfEffect` | `()` | activated-ability redirect: all damage a chosen source would deal to the target creature this turn is dealt to the source permanent instead (Oracle's Attendants). permanent-targeting spec — the ability targets the protected creature; the source is chosen on resolution (prompts a battlefield permanent choice). Stores an unlimited `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected creature + chosen source + `UNLIMITED` amount + redirect target) in `gameData.creatureDamageRedirectShields`, checked via `DamagePreventionService.applyCreatureRedirectShields` in both the combat (`CombatDamageService.applyCombatCreatureDamage`) and noncombat (`DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage`) creature-damage paths. Unlike Harm's Way, protects one specific creature (not a player's permanents) with no amount limit; reuses `pendingSourceRedirectDamage`/`processSourceRedirectDamage` to deal the redirected damage. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `RedirectTargetCreatureNextDamageFromChosenSourceToControllerEffect` | `()` | activated-ability redirect: the next single damage event a chosen source would deal to the target creature this turn is dealt to the ability's controller (you) instead (Jade Monolith). permanent-targeting spec — the ability targets the protected creature; the source is chosen on resolution (prompts a battlefield permanent choice). Stores a next-event `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected creature + chosen source + `NEXT_EVENT` amount + `redirectTargetId` = controller player) which `applyCreatureRedirectShields` redirects in full then consumes, over both combat and noncombat creature-damage paths. Like Oracle's Attendants' `RedirectTargetCreatureDamageFromChosenSourceToSelfEffect` but redirects to the controller (a player) and only for the next single event. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `RedirectNextDamageToTargetCreatureEffect` | `(int amount)` | activated-ability redirect: the next `amount` damage that would be dealt to this ability's source creature this turn (from ANY source) is dealt to the target creature instead (Zealous Inquisitor). permanent-targeting spec — the ability targets the redirect destination creature; the protected creature is `entry.getSourcePermanentId()`. Stores an amount-limited `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected = source creature, `damageSourceId=null` for any source, `remainingAmount=amount`, redirect target) which `applyCreatureRedirectShields` consumes/reduces over the same combat + noncombat creature-damage paths. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `RedirectTargetCreatureDamageFromChosenSourceToSelfEffect` | `()` | activated-ability redirect: all damage a chosen source would deal to the target creature this turn is dealt to the source permanent instead (Oracle's Attendants). `canTargetPermanent()=true` — the ability targets the protected creature; the source is chosen on resolution (prompts a battlefield permanent choice). Stores an unlimited `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected creature + chosen source + `UNLIMITED` amount + redirect target) in `gameData.creatureDamageRedirectShields`, checked via `DamagePreventionService.applyCreatureRedirectShields` in both the combat (`CombatDamageService.applyCombatCreatureDamage`) and noncombat (`DamageSupport.dealCreatureDamage`) creature-damage paths. Unlike Harm's Way, protects one specific creature (not a player's permanents) with no amount limit; reuses `pendingSourceRedirectDamage`/`processSourceRedirectDamage` to deal the redirected damage. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `RedirectTargetCreatureNextDamageFromChosenSourceToControllerEffect` | `()` | activated-ability redirect: the next single damage event a chosen source would deal to the target creature this turn is dealt to the ability's controller (you) instead (Jade Monolith). `canTargetPermanent()=true` — the ability targets the protected creature; the source is chosen on resolution (prompts a battlefield permanent choice). Stores a next-event `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected creature + chosen source + `NEXT_EVENT` amount + `redirectTargetId` = controller player) which `applyCreatureRedirectShields` redirects in full then consumes, over both combat and noncombat creature-damage paths. Like Oracle's Attendants' `RedirectTargetCreatureDamageFromChosenSourceToSelfEffect` but redirects to the controller (a player) and only for the next single event. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `RedirectNextDamageToTargetCreatureEffect` | `(int amount)` | activated-ability redirect: the next `amount` damage that would be dealt to this ability's source creature this turn (from ANY source) is dealt to the target creature instead (Zealous Inquisitor). `canTargetPermanent()=true` — the ability targets the redirect destination creature; the protected creature is `entry.getSourcePermanentId()`. Stores an amount-limited `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected = source creature, `damageSourceId=null` for any source, `remainingAmount=amount`, redirect target) which `applyCreatureRedirectShields` consumes/reduces over the same combat + noncombat creature-damage paths. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `RedirectNextDamageToSelfToOwnerEffect` | `(int amount)` | activated-ability redirect (no target): the next `amount` damage that would be dealt to this ability's source creature this turn (from ANY source) is dealt to its owner (the source's controller, a player) instead (Personal Incarnation). Stores an amount-limited `CreatureDamageRedirectShield` (protected = source creature, `damageSourceId=null`, `remainingAmount=amount`, `redirectTargetId` = controller player) which `applyCreatureRedirectShields` consumes over combat + noncombat creature-damage paths; the player branch of `processSourceRedirectDamage` deals it to life. Like Zealous Inquisitor's `RedirectNextDamageToTargetCreatureEffect` but no target and destined for the owner. Cleared at turn cleanup |
| `GrantControllerHexproofEffect` | `()` | controller has hexproof (can't be targeted by opponents) (static) |
| `GrantControllerShroudEffect` | `()` | controller has shroud (can't be targeted) (static) |
| `CantBeEnchantedByOtherAurasEffect` | `()` | static marker: the permanent can't be enchanted by other Auras (Anti-Magic Aura). No handler — read at Aura-spell targeting time by `GameQueryService.cantBeEnchantedByOtherAuras`, enforced in `TargetLegalityService.checkSpellProtection` guarded by `card.isAura()`. Only ever used wrapped in `GrantEffectEffect` (e.g. scoped to `ENCHANTED_CREATURE`) |
| `GrantControllerSpellsCantBeCounteredByColorsEffect` | `(Set<CardColor> colors)` | controller's spells can't be countered by spells of specified colors this turn (one-shot, cleared at end of turn) |
| `GrantControllerCreaturesCantBeTargetedByColorsEffect` | `(Set<CardColor> colors)` | controller's creatures can't be targeted by spells of specified colors this turn (one-shot, cleared at end of turn) |

## Mana

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `AwardManaEffect` | `(ManaColor color, DynamicAmount amount)`, `(ManaColor color, int amount)`, or `(ManaColor color)` (defaults amount to 1) | add mana of the specified color; the quantity is a `DynamicAmount` (see "Dynamic amounts"). Flat: `(color)`/`(color, N)`. "for each X you control": `PermanentCount(filter, CountScope.CONTROLLER)`. "for each charge counter on it": `CountersOnSource(CounterType.CHARGE)` (Shrine of Boundless Growth). "equal to its power": `SourcePower()` (Marwyn, the Nurturer; Molten-Core Maestro). Implements `ManaProducingEffect`. Resolves inline for mana abilities (from the source permanent) and on the stack via `AwardManaEffectHandler` for triggered/loyalty mana (needs the stack entry's `sourcePermanentId`); dynamic amounts produce no mana when they evaluate to ≤ 0 and track creature mana when the source is a creature |
| `AwardManaToChosenPlayerEffect` | `(ManaColor color, int amount)` | "Choose a player. That player adds N mana of `color`." A mana ability (CR 605.1a) whose recipient may be any player — choosing a player is NOT targeting, so it resolves inline: `doResolveManaAbility` begins a `PermanentChoice` (validPlayerIds = all players) and `PermanentChoiceBattlefieldHandlerService.handleManaAbilityAddToChosenPlayer` routes the mana into the chosen player's pool (tracking creature mana when the source is a creature; Mana Reflection multiplier applied). Used by Valleymaker (`GREEN, 3`) |
| `AwardAnyColorManaEffect` | `(int amount)` or `()` (defaults amount to 1) | add N mana of any one color (player chooses) |
| `AwardManaOfColorsEffect` | `(List<ManaColor> colors)` | add one mana of a single color the player chooses from the fixed `colors` list. A single-element list adds that color directly (no prompt); otherwise begins a `PendingInteraction.ColorChoice` with the listed colors (reuses `ChoiceContext.ManaColorChoice`, tracks creature mana when the source is a creature). Implements `ManaProducingEffect`, resolves inline as a mana ability. Used by Manaforge Cinder (`List.of(BLACK, RED)` = "Add {B} or {R}"). Prefer this over splitting into one activated ability per color when the printed ability has a shared per-turn activation cap (`maxActivationsPerTurn`), since separate abilities track their caps independently |
| `AwardAnyColorManaWithInstantSorceryCopyEffect` | `(int amount)` or `()` (defaults amount to 1) | add N mana of any color and register a delayed one-shot trigger that copies the next instant or sorcery the controller casts. Cleared when mana pools drain. Used by Primal Wellspring |
| `AddManaOnEnchantedLandTapEffect` | `(ManaProducingEffect mana)` | when enchanted land is tapped, add the mana described by `mana` (e.g. `AwardManaEffect`, `AwardAnyColorManaEffect`). Wild Growth, Fertile Ground |
| `AddExtraManaOfChosenColorOnLandTapEffect` | `()` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_TAPS_LAND trigger: when a land you control taps for mana of the source permanent's chosen color, add one additional mana of that color. Checks ON_TAP effects of the tapped land. Used by Caged Sun |
| `AddOneOfEachManaTypeProducedByLandEffect` | `(boolean controllerOnly)` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_TAPS_LAND trigger: when a land taps for mana, the tapping player adds one additional mana of any type that land produced (exactly 1 mana, picks first type if multiple). `controllerOnly=true` fires only for the source controller's land taps (Vorinclex, Voice of Hunger); `controllerOnly=false` is symmetric — every player's land taps add the extra mana (Mana Flare) |
| `AddManaWhenLandOfSubtypeTappedForManaEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype, ManaColor color)` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_TAPS_LAND trigger: whenever ANY land with `subtype` taps for mana (symmetric — every player's matching lands), its controller adds one additional mana of `color`. Used by Vernal Bloom (FOREST → GREEN) |
| `AddProducedManaWhenLandOfSubtypeTappedEffect` | `(List<CardSubtype> subtypes)` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_TAPS_LAND trigger: whenever ANY player taps a land whose subtypes include at least one of `subtypes` for mana (symmetric), that player adds one additional mana of a type the land produced (first ON_TAP `AwardManaEffect` color when multiple). Triggers once per land tap even with several matching subtypes. Used by Keeper of Progenitus (MOUNTAIN/FOREST/PLAINS). Combines the subtype gate of `AddManaWhenLandOfSubtypeTappedForManaEffect` with the produced-type payout of `AddOneOfEachManaTypeProducedByLandEffect` |
| `MatchingPermanentsDoesntUntapEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | Global static in `EffectSlot.STATIC`: during each player's untap step, `UntapStepService` scans every battlefield for a source carrying this effect and skips untapping any of the active player's permanents that match `filter` — regardless of who controls the source, and including the source itself. Unlike `DoesntUntapEffect` (which locks one specific permanent) this locks an open-ended predicate-selected set. Marble Titan = `PermanentPowerAtLeastPredicate(3)` |
| `OpponentTappedLandDoesntUntapEffect` | `()` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_TAPS_LAND trigger: when an opponent taps a land for mana, increments skipUntapCount on the tapped land so it doesn't untap during its controller's next untap step. Multiple taps stack. Used by Vorinclex, Voice of Hunger |
| `ReturnTappedLandToHandEffect` | `()` | ON_ANY_PLAYER_TAPS_LAND trigger: whenever ANY land is tapped for mana (symmetric — every player's lands), returns that land to its owner's hand. The mana was already added before the trigger runs, so it stays in the pool. Used by Storm Cauldron |
| `DoubleManaPoolEffect` | `()` | double your mana pool |
| `ManaReflectionEffect` | `()` | STATIC replacement: if the controller taps a permanent for mana, it produces twice as much of that mana instead (Mana Reflection). Applied in `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService`'s mana-ability resolution via `GameQueryService.manaProductionMultiplier` — multiplies both fixed `AwardManaEffect` output and the amount of any-color color-choice producers. Controller-scoped; multiple stack multiplicatively (2^count). Distinct from `DoubleManaPoolEffect`, which doubles the entire pool once |
| `AddManaPerAttackingCreatureEffect` | `(ManaColor color1, ManaColor color2)` | triggered: counts controller's attacking creatures, player chooses color1 or color2, adds that many mana of the chosen color. Also sets per-player mana drain prevention until end of turn. Use with `ON_ALLY_CREATURES_ATTACK` slot. The attacker count is snapshotted into the trigger's `xValue` at trigger time (NOT counted at resolution) — per the Grand Warlord Radha ruling, creatures that leave combat before it resolves still count and creatures that enter attacking later don't, so this stays a dedicated effect rather than a resolution-time `PermanentCount`. Used by Grand Warlord Radha |
| `AwardManaOfColorsAmongControlledEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate)` | add one mana of any color among permanents matching the predicate you control. If only one color is available, auto-adds it. If multiple colors, player chooses. If no colors, produces nothing. Used by Mox Amber with a predicate matching legendary creatures or planeswalkers |
| `AwardOneManaOfEachColorAmongControlledEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate)` | "For each color among permanents you control matching `predicate`, add one mana of that color." Unlike `AwardManaOfColorsAmongControlledEffect` (single color, player-chosen), this adds one mana of **every** color found simultaneously — no choice. Respects the mana-production multiplier and marks creature mana. Bloom Tender (Vivid) uses it with `PermanentTruePredicate`. Implements `ManaProducingEffect` |
| `AwardManaOfColorsLandsCouldProduceEffect` | `(ManaColorLandScope scope, PermanentPredicate landPredicate)` | add one mana of any color that a land in `scope` (CONTROLLER or OPPONENTS) matching `landPredicate` could produce (scans those lands' ON_TAP and activated mana abilities: `AwardManaEffect` colored + `AwardAnyColorManaEffect` = all 5; colorless excluded). If only one color is available, auto-adds it; if multiple, player chooses; if none, produces nothing. Implements `ManaProducingEffect`. `(OPPONENTS, PermanentIsLandPredicate)` = Fellwar Stone; `(CONTROLLER, AllOf(land, BASIC supertype))` = Star Compass |
| `MayTapLandsYouDontControlForSpellsUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | SPELL slot. Marks the controller in `GameData.mayTapLandsForSpellsUntilEndOfTurn` (cleared by `TurnCleanupService`). While marked, the player may call `GameService.tapForeignLandForMana(gameData, player, permanentId)` to tap an untapped land they don't control; the produced mana is routed into `ManaPool`'s spell-only bucket (`addSpellOnlyMana` — a tag on a subset of the regular pool, so spell casting draws from it automatically). Ability activation withdraws spell-only mana for the duration of payment (`ManaPool.withdrawSpellOnlyMana`/`restoreSpellOnlyMana`), so it can be spent only to cast spells. Used by Piracy |
| `MayPayLifeForColorlessManaUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | SPELL slot. Marks the controller in `GameData.mayPayLifeForColorlessManaUntilEndOfTurn` (cleared by `TurnCleanupService`). While marked, the player may call `GameService.payLifeForColorlessMana(gameData, player)` any time they could activate a mana ability to pay 1 life (requires life ≥ 1) and add one **unrestricted** colorless mana to their pool (`ManaPool.add(COLORLESS, 1)` — spendable on anything, unlike Piracy's spell-only mana). Repeatable. Used by Channel |
| `AwardAnyColorChosenSubtypeCreatureManaEffect` | `()` | add one mana of any color (player chooses) that can only be spent to cast a creature spell of the source permanent's chosen creature type. Stored in `ManaPool.subtypeCreatureMana` keyed by `CardSubtype`. Requires `ChooseSubtypeOnEnterEffect` on the source permanent. `ManaCost.canPay/pay` accept `Set<CardSubtype> subtypeCreatureContext` to include this mana. Used by Pillar of Origins, Unclaimed Territory |
| `AwardAnyColorCreatureSpellManaEffect` | `()` | add one mana of any color (player chooses) spendable only to cast a creature spell of **any** type. Stored per-color in `ManaPool.creatureSpellOnlyMana`; `ManaCost.canPay/pay` take a `creatureSpellOnlyContext` boolean (10-arg overload) that `SpellCastingService`/`GameBroadcastService` set to `card.hasType(CREATURE)`. Cannot pay ability costs (not passed by `AbilityActivationService`) or non-creature spells. Distinct from `AwardAnyColorChosenSubtypeCreatureManaEffect`, which restricts to one chosen creature subtype. Resolved inline in `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService.doResolveManaAbility` (begins a `ManaColorChoice.creatureSpellOnly`). Used by Ancient Ziggurat |
| `AwardRestrictedManaEffect` | `(ManaColor color, int amount, ManaRestriction restriction)` | add N mana of the given color spendable only under `restriction`. Implements `ManaProducingEffect` so it works as a mana ability. `restriction.applyTo(pool, color, amount)` routes into the matching `ManaPool` bucket; the spend side (`ManaCost.canPay/pay` context flags) keys on the bucket, not the effect. `ManaRestriction` cases: `SpellTypes(Set<CardType>)` — instant/sorcery-only → `instantSorceryOnlyColorless`/`instantSorceryOnlyColored`, red creature+artifact-only (Geosurge) → `restrictedRed`, else plain mana; `ArtifactSpells()` → `artifactOnlyColorless` (Grand Architect); `SubtypeSpells(CardSubtype)` → `myrOnlyColorless` (Myr Reservoir); `KickedCosts()` → `kickedOnlyGreen` (Elfhame Druid); `XCosts()` → `xCostOnlyColorless` (Rosheen Meanderer). `XCosts()` mana is usable only when the cost being paid contains an {X} symbol (`ManaCost.hasX()`), for any generic portion of that cost — the spend logic gates on `hasX()` directly (no context flag), so it works for both X spells and X activated abilities |
