| `AwardAnyColorSubtypeSpellOrAbilityManaEffect` | `(int amount, CardSubtype subtype)` | add N mana in any combination of colors (player chooses one color per mana, looped like the flashback any-combination flow) spendable only to cast spells of `subtype` **or** activate abilities of permanents of that subtype. Routed into `ManaPool.subtypeSpellOrAbilityMana` (per-subtype/per-color). `ManaCost.canPay/pay` accept a `Set<CardSubtype> subtypeSpellOrAbilityContext` (9-arg overload): spell casting passes the spell's subtypes (`SpellCastingService.ManaRestrictionFlags`); ability activation passes the source permanent's effective subtypes (`AbilityActivationService.payManaCost`). Distinct from `AwardAnyColorChosenSubtypeCreatureManaEffect` (spell-only, cannot pay abilities). Used by Smokebraider = `(2, ELEMENTAL)` |
| `AwardFlashbackOnlyAnyColorManaEffect` | `(int amount)` | add N mana of any color (player chooses) that can only be spent to cast spells with flashback from a graveyard. Stored per-color in `ManaPool.flashbackOnlyMana`; `ManaCost.canPayFlashback/payFlashback` include this mana. Used by Altar of the Lost. NOT folded into `AwardRestrictedManaEffect` — its any-color choice needs `PendingInteraction.ColorChoice` plumbing (resolved in `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService`), not a direct `applyTo(pool)` |
| `PreventManaDrainEffect` | `()` | players don't lose unspent mana as steps/phases end (static) |
| `TargetPlayerLosesAllUnspentManaEffect` | `()` | targeted player empties their mana pool, losing all unspent mana of every kind (regular, restricted, and persistent). Reads `entry.getTargetId()` as a player; pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter`. Used by Mana Short |
| `DrainTargetPlayersLandManaEffect` | `()` | targeted player activates a mana ability of each untapped land they control (mana added to their own pool), then loses all unspent mana; the spell's controller adds an equal amount. Reads `entry.getTargetId()` as a player; pair with a `PlayerPredicateTargetFilter`. Fixed single-color lands are exact; multi-ability lands use their first tap-for-mana ability and any-color producers contribute colorless. Used by Drain Power |

## Copy / clone

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `CopyPermanentOnEnterEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter, String typeLabel)` or `(PermanentPredicate filter, String typeLabel, Integer powerOverride, Integer toughnessOverride)` or `(PermanentPredicate filter, String typeLabel, Integer powerOverride, Integer toughnessOverride, Set<CardType> additionalTypesOverride)` or `(PermanentPredicate filter, String typeLabel, Integer powerOverride, Integer toughnessOverride, Set<CardType> additionalTypesOverride, List<ActivatedAbility> additionalActivatedAbilities)` | enter as copy of permanent matching filter (Clone-style). Optional P/T overrides for "copy except it's X/Y" (e.g. Quicksilver Gargantuan). Optional `additionalTypesOverride` for "copy except it's also an [type]" (e.g. Phyrexian Metamorph is always an artifact). Optional `additionalActivatedAbilities` for "copy except it has [ability]" (e.g. Evil Twin's destroy same-name ability) |
| `CopySpellEffect` | `()`, `(StackEntryPredicate spellFilter)`, or `(StackEntryPredicate spellFilter, boolean tokenWithHaste, boolean sacrificeAtEndStep)` | copy target spell. No-arg form for SPELL slot (filter on Card's SpellTarget). Filter form for ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD slot — carries the filter to restrict which spells can be targeted (e.g. Naru Meha uses `StackEntryAllOfPredicate(StackEntryTypeInPredicate(INSTANT, SORCERY), StackEntryControlledByPredicate())`). For "copy twice if cast from a graveyard" (Increasing Vengeance), add a base `CopySpellEffect()` plus `ConditionalEffect(new CastFromZone(Zone.GRAVEYARD), new CopySpellEffect())` rather than a count parameter. `tokenWithHaste=true` (for copying a **creature** spell): the copy becomes a token, gains `HASTE`, and the retarget prompt is suppressed; with `sacrificeAtEndStep=true` the resulting permanent is registered in `GameData.delayedActions` (a `DelayedPermanentAction(SACRIFICE_AT_END_STEP)`) and sacrificed by `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers` (Choreographed Sparks). All copy handlers skip spells whose card has `cantBeCopied=true` |
| `CopySpellForEachOtherPlayerEffect` | `(StackEntryPredicate spellFilter)` mandatory / `(boolean optional, StackEntryPredicate spellFilter)` | trigger descriptor for `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL`: whenever a player casts a spell matching `spellFilter`, each other player copies that spell and may choose new targets. `spellFilter` (a `StackEntryPredicate`, evaluated against the cast spell's stack entry) fully expresses the trigger condition — both cards pass `StackEntryTypeInPredicate(INSTANT_SPELL, SORCERY_SPELL)`. `optional=true` makes each other player *may* copy (offered as a PendingMayAbility that, on accept, creates one copy for that player via `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect`). Hive Mind = `new CopySpellForEachOtherPlayerEffect(typeFilter)`; Curse of Echoes = `new CopySpellForEachOtherPlayerEffect(true, StackEntryAllOfPredicate(typeFilter, StackEntryControlledByEnchantedPlayerPredicate))` so it only fires when the enchanted player is the caster. Resolution snapshot populated at trigger time |
| `CopySpellForEachOtherSubtypePermanentEffect` | `(CardSubtype subtype)` | trigger descriptor: whenever a player casts an instant or sorcery spell that targets only a single permanent with the given subtype, copy the spell for each other permanent with that subtype the spell could target. Each copy targets a different one of those permanents. Place in `ON_ANY_PLAYER_CASTS_SPELL` slot. Resolution snapshot populated at trigger time by `checkSpellCastTriggers`. Used by Precursor Golem |
| `GrantInstantSorceryCopyUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | when resolved, grants the controller the ability to copy every instant or sorcery spell they cast for the rest of the turn. Each copy may have new targets chosen. Adds controller to `GameData.playersWithSpellCopyUntilEndOfTurn` (cleared at end of turn). Used by The Mirari Conjecture chapter III |
| `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect` | `(StackEntry spellSnapshot, UUID castingPlayerId)` | resolution-time effect that creates a single copy of a spell for its controller. The copy's controller may choose new targets. Populated at trigger time by `TriggerCollectionService` when a player in `playersWithSpellCopyUntilEndOfTurn` casts an instant or sorcery |
| `CopyControllerCastSpellOnSpellCastEffect` | `(CardPredicate spellFilter, TapMultiplePermanentsCost tapCost)` or `(CardPredicate spellFilter, String manaCost)` | trigger descriptor for `ON_CONTROLLER_CASTS_SPELL`: whenever the controller casts a spell matching `spellFilter`, they may pay a cost to copy that spell (may choose new targets). Snapshots the cast spell at trigger time and places `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect` on the stack, wrapped in `MayPayTapPermanentsEffect` (tapCost variant, Aziza, Mage Tower Captain) or `MayPayManaEffect` (manaCost variant, Cloven Casting — "you may pay {1}"). Set at most one cost. **Pass `tapCost = null` and wrap the effect in `MayEffect`** for a free "you may copy that spell" (no cost) — the collector then queues a `PendingMayAbility` carrying `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect`. Used by Swarm Intelligence |
| `CopyControllerActivatedAbilityTriggerEffect` | `(String manaCost)` | trigger descriptor for `ON_CONTROLLER_ACTIVATES_NONMANA_ABILITY`: "whenever you activate an ability, if it isn't a mana ability, you may pay `manaCost`. If you do, copy that ability (may choose new targets)." Collected in `TriggerCollectionService.checkControllerActivatesNonManaAbilityTriggers` (called from `ActivatedAbilityExecutionService` after the non-mana ability is on the stack), which snapshots the ability and places `MayPayManaEffect` wrapping `CopyControllerActivatedAbilityEffect` on the stack. Used by Rings of Brighthearth |
| `CopyControllerActivatedAbilityEffect` | `(StackEntry abilitySnapshot, ActivatedAbility ability, UUID activatingPlayerId)` | resolution-time effect that copies the snapshotted activated ability onto the stack (CR 707.10) for its controller. For a single-target ability, queues a `CopyActivatedAbilityRetargetEffect` may-ability so the controller may choose a new target for the copy. Used by Rings of Brighthearth |
| `CopyActivatedAbilityRetargetEffect` | `(ActivatedAbility ability, UUID sourcePermanentId)` | marker on the "choose a new target for the copy" `PendingMayAbility`; handled by `MayCopyHandlerService.handleCopyActivatedAbilityRetargetChoice`, which recomputes legal targets via `ValidTargetService.computeValidTargetsForAbility` and reuses the `SpellRetarget` flow. Used by Rings of Brighthearth |
| `CopyThisSpellIfConditionEffect` | `(Condition condition)` | trigger descriptor for the `ON_SELF_CAST` slot (a spell's own "when you cast this spell" ability): "copy it if `condition`. You may choose new targets for the copy." Scanned against the just-cast spell card in `TriggerCollectionService.checkSpellCastTriggers`, which snapshots the spell and queues a triggered ability wrapping `CopyControllerCastSpellEffect` in a `ConditionalEffect` on `condition` (so the copy happens only when the condition holds at resolution). Used by the SOS Infusion copy cycle, e.g. Lumaret's Favor (`new GainedLifeThisTurn()`) |
| `StormEffect` | `()` | trigger descriptor for the `ON_SELF_CAST` slot implementing the Storm keyword (CR 702.40): "When you cast this spell, copy it for each spell cast before it this turn. You may choose new targets for the copies." Scanned in `TriggerCollectionService.checkSpellCastTriggers`, which snapshots the spell and queues a triggered ability wrapping `StormCopyEffect(snapshot, caster, copies)` where `copies = gameData.getTotalSpellsCastThisTurnCount() - 1` (subtracts this spell, already recorded). Used by Dragonstorm |
| `StormCopyEffect` | `(StackEntry spellSnapshot, UUID castingPlayerId, int copies)` | resolution-time effect that creates `copies` copies of a spell for its controller, each of which may choose new targets. Honors CR 706.2 (`isCantBeCopied`). Populated by `StormEffect` at trigger time |
| `CascadeEffect` | `()` | trigger descriptor for the `ON_SELF_CAST` slot implementing the Cascade keyword (CR 702.85): "When you cast this spell, exile cards from the top of your library until you exile a nonland card that costs less. You may cast it without paying its mana cost. Put the exiled cards on the bottom in a random order." Falls through the generic self-cast branch in `TriggerCollectionService.checkSpellCastTriggers` and is queued as a plain triggered ability; `CascadeEffectHandler` digs until a nonland card with `getManaValue() < entry.getCard().getManaValue()`, then begins a `CAST_WITHOUT_PAYING` `LibrarySearch` (single-card castable list, `sourceCards` = all exiled, `reorderRemainingToBottom`) to cast that card for free and bottom the rest randomly — reusing Sunbird's Invocation's cast/bottom/AI path. No hit → all exiled cards go to the bottom. Used by Ardent Plea. Also placed in the `GRANT_CASCADE_TO_FIRST_SPELL` marker slot to model a permanent that grants cascade to the first spell each turn (Maelstrom Nexus): `checkSpellCastTriggers` detects the slot by presence, and when the caster's spell count for the turn is 1 it queues this `CascadeEffect` keyed to the just-cast spell (threshold = that spell's mana value) |
| `BecomeCopyOfTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | source permanent becomes a copy of target creature, retaining the triggered ability that granted this effect. Used by Cryptoplasm. Place in UPKEEP_TRIGGERED wrapped in MayEffect. permanent-targeting spec |
| `BecomeCopyOfDyingCreatureEffect` | `(UUID dyingCardId)` or `()` | source permanent becomes a copy of a creature that just died, copying its last-known information from the graveyard and re-granting the source's own `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` ability ("except it has this ability"). No-arg constructor in the card definition; dyingCardId baked in at trigger time. Place in `ON_ANY_CREATURE_DIES` wrapped in `MayPayManaEffect`. Used by Cemetery Puca |
| `BecomeCopyOfTargetCreatureUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | source permanent becomes a copy of target creature until end of turn (CR 707.2 copiable values via `PermanentCopierService.applyCloneCopy`). Registers a floating `L1_COPY` effect; at the cleanup step its expiry drives the card revert via `Permanent.revertEndOfTurnCopy()` (NOT `resetModifiers()` — pre-copy pumps/counters persist per CR 611.2c). Used by Tilonalli's Skinshifter. Place in ON_ATTACK with target filter. permanent-targeting spec |
| `EachOtherCreatureBecomesCopyOfTargetCreatureUntilEndOfTurnEffect` | `()` | every creature on the battlefield except the target becomes a copy of the target creature until end of turn (Mirrorweave). Snapshots the battlefield, then for each other creature applies `PermanentCopierService.applyCloneCopy` and registers a per-permanent `BecomeCopyOfTargetCreatureUntilEndOfTurnEffect` floating effect so each reverts at cleanup. Single target; place in SPELL with a nonlegendary-creature filter. permanent-targeting spec |
| `MakeTargetCopyOfTargetCreatureUntilNextTurnEffect` | `()` | **two targets** — `targetIds[0]` (a Shapeshifter) becomes a copy of `targetIds[1]` (a creature) until the ability controller's next turn. Registers a floating `L1_COPY` effect (`UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN`); its turn-start expiry drives the revert via `Permanent.revertUntilNextTurnCopy()` (survives end-of-turn cleanup; the copied permanent may be on any battlefield). Used by Shapesharer. Wire with the multi-target `ActivatedAbility` ctor (`multiTargetFilters`, min/max 2). permanent-targeting spec |
| `ChangeTargetOfTargetSpellWithSingleTargetEffect` | `()` | change target of target spell with single target |
| `ChangeTargetOfTargetSpellToSourceEffect` | `()` | change a target of target spell or ability to source permanent (e.g. Spellskite). Automatically redirects without player choice. If source is not a legal target or spell has no targets, does nothing. Use with StackEntryHasTargetPredicate to allow targeting spells and abilities on the stack. |
| `ChooseNewTargetsForTargetSpellEffect` | `()` | you may choose new targets for target spell (e.g. Redirect). Targets any spell on the stack. On resolution, if target spell has targets, offers a may-ability prompt to choose new targets. No target filter needed — works on any spell. |

## Turn / phase

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `ControllerExtraTurnEffect` | `(int count)` / `(int count, boolean skipUntapStep)` | controller takes N extra turns (no targeting); `skipUntapStep=true` skips each granted turn's untap step (permanents stay tapped, summoning sickness still clears) — Savor the Moment |
| `RegisterLoseGameAtEndStepEffect` | `()` | schedules a `LoseGameAtEndStep` delayed action (tagged with the resolving turn number) — "at the beginning of your next end step, you lose the game" (Last Chance, Glorious End). Drained in `StepTriggerService.handleEndStepTriggers` only once the turn has advanced **and** the scheduling player is the active player, so it skips both the scheduling turn's own end step and every opponent's end step, firing at the controller's own next end step (Last Chance's extra turn; Glorious End's next turn after the ended one). Pushes `TargetPlayerLosesGameEffect` onto the stack, so it respects can't-lose (Platinum Angel). SPELL, non-targeting |
| `ExtraTurnEffect` | `(int count)` | target player takes N extra turns |
| `AdditionalCombatMainPhaseEffect` | `(int count)` | get N additional combat + main phases (Relentless Assault). Increments `additionalCombatMainPhasePairs`; consumed at POSTCOMBAT_MAIN |
| `AdditionalCombatPhaseEffect` | `(int count)` | get N additional combat phases with NO additional main phase (Finest Hour). Increments `additionalCombatPhasesOnly`; consumed when leaving END_OF_COMBAT so the extra combat follows directly with no main phase between |
| `EndTurnEffect` | `()` | end the turn |
| `ControlTargetPlayerNextTurnEffect` | `()` | control target player during their next turn (Mindslaver) |
| `PermanentsEnterTappedThisTurnEffect` | `()` | all permanents enter tapped this turn (Due Respect) |

## Animate / transform

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `AnimatePermanentsEffect` | `(DynamicAmount power, DynamicAmount toughness, List<CardSubtype> grantedSubtypes, Set<Keyword> grantedKeywords, CardColor animatedColor, Set<CardType> grantedCardTypes, GrantScope scope, EffectDuration duration, PermanentPredicate filter)` — canonical; plus int-P/T sugar ctors: `(int,int,subtypes,keywords,color)` (manland SELF/UEOT), `(…,color,cardTypes)` (Inkmoth), `(int,int,subtypes,keywords)` (self, no colour — Glint Hawk/Rusted Relic/Warden), `(int,int,subtypes,keywords,color,cardTypes,scope,duration)` (Sylvan Awakening OWN_LANDS, Awakener Druid TARGET/WHILE_SOURCE, Tezzeret/Waker TARGET/PERMANENT); `AnimatePermanentsEffect.crew()` = printed-P/T self+CREATURE (Vehicles). One or more permanents become creatures with the given P/T. **Scope** (`GrantScope`): `SELF` (source, UEOT — manlands/Crew/Chimeric/Warden; `targetSpec().selfTargeting()=true`), `TARGET` (permanent-targeting spec; PERMANENT=Tezzeret/Waker, WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD=Awakener Druid with `sourceLinkedAnimations` tracking + source-left fizzle), `OWN_LANDS` (all lands you control — Sylvan Awakening, supports UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN), `OWN_PERMANENTS`+`filter` (mass, +CREATURE type, Equipment unattach — The Antiquities War III). **Duration** (`EffectDuration`): UNTIL_END_OF_TURN (`animatedUntilEndOfTurn`), UNTIL_END_OF_COMBAT (`animatedUntilEndOfCombat`, SELF scope — Jade Statue; reverts when combat ends via `Permanent.clearCombatState()`), UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN (`animatedUntilNextTurn`, own-lands), PERMANENT/WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD (`permanentlyAnimated`). P/T `DynamicAmount`: `Fixed`, `XValue()` (Chimeric Staff), `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)` (Chimeric Mass); a **null** P/T means "use the source's printed value" (Crew). `animatedColor` null for OWN_LANDS; for WHILE_SOURCE it's added to `grantedColors`. |
| `AnimateNoncreatureArtifactsEffect` | `()` | animate all noncreature artifacts into creatures (March of the Machines-style) |
| `AnimatePermanentsEffect` | `(DynamicAmount power, DynamicAmount toughness, List<CardSubtype> grantedSubtypes, Set<Keyword> grantedKeywords, CardColor animatedColor, Set<CardType> grantedCardTypes, GrantScope scope, EffectDuration duration, PermanentPredicate filter)` — canonical; plus int-P/T sugar ctors: `(int,int,subtypes,keywords,color)` (manland SELF/UEOT), `(…,color,cardTypes)` (Inkmoth), `(int,int,subtypes,keywords)` (self, no colour — Glint Hawk/Rusted Relic/Warden), `(int,int,subtypes,keywords,color,cardTypes,scope,duration)` (Sylvan Awakening OWN_LANDS, Awakener Druid TARGET/WHILE_SOURCE, Tezzeret/Waker TARGET/PERMANENT); `AnimatePermanentsEffect.crew()` = printed-P/T self+CREATURE (Vehicles). One or more permanents become creatures with the given P/T. **Scope** (`GrantScope`): `SELF` (source, UEOT — manlands/Crew/Chimeric/Warden; `isSelfTargeting()=true`), `TARGET` (`canTargetPermanent()=true`; PERMANENT=Tezzeret/Waker, WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD=Awakener Druid with `sourceLinkedAnimations` tracking + source-left fizzle), `OWN_LANDS` (all lands you control — Sylvan Awakening, supports UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN), `OWN_PERMANENTS`+`filter` (mass, +CREATURE type, Equipment unattach — The Antiquities War III). **Duration** (`EffectDuration`): UNTIL_END_OF_TURN (`animatedUntilEndOfTurn`), UNTIL_END_OF_COMBAT (`animatedUntilEndOfCombat`, SELF scope — Jade Statue; reverts when combat ends via `Permanent.clearCombatState()`), UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN (`animatedUntilNextTurn`, own-lands), PERMANENT/WHILE_SOURCE_ON_BATTLEFIELD (`permanentlyAnimated`). P/T `DynamicAmount`: `Fixed`, `XValue()` (Chimeric Staff), `CountersOnSource(CHARGE)` (Chimeric Mass); a **null** P/T means "use the source's printed value" (Crew). `animatedColor` null for OWN_LANDS; for WHILE_SOURCE it's added to `grantedColors`. |
| `AnimateNoncreatureArtifactsEffect` | `([boolean losesAllAbilities])` | animate all noncreature artifacts into creatures with P/T = mana value (March of the Machines-style). `losesAllAbilities=true` also strips their abilities in layer 6 (Titania's Song); classifies into L4+L7B, plus L6 when the flag is set. |
| `AllArtifactsUpkeepSacrificeUnlessPayEffect` | `(String manaCost)` | STATIC global marker (Energy Flux): grants every artifact "At the beginning of your upkeep, sacrifice this artifact unless you pay {N}." Read by `StepTriggerService.handleGrantedArtifactSacrificeTriggers` (has no `LayerClassifier` entry, so the board ignores it): during each upkeep, for every artifact the active player controls it pushes a `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(PayManaCost(manaCost), [SacrificeSelfEffect()], true)` trigger sourced at that artifact (so the pay prompt and the sacrifice both act on the individual artifact). Global — fires regardless of who controls the enchantment. |
| `AddCounterThenPayCountersOrTapAndDamageEffect` | `(CounterType counterType)` | single UPKEEP_TRIGGERED effect (Primordial Ooze): "put a `counterType` counter on this, then you may pay {X} (X = that counter type's count on it); if you don't, tap this and it deals X damage to you." Handler places the counter via `PermanentCounterSupport`, reads X, then builds a `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(PayManaCost("{X}"), [TapPermanentsEffect(SELF), DealDamageToPlayersEffect(X, CONTROLLER)], true)` and delegates to `ForcedCostOrElseEffectHandler`. Modelled as one effect (not counter+punish separately) because both halves are one ability and X depends on the counter added first. |
| `AllLandsAreCreaturesEffect` | `(int power, int toughness[, CardSubtype requiredSubtype])` | STATIC global: lands on the battlefield (all players) become fixed-P/T creatures that are still lands. No `requiredSubtype` = every land (Nature's Revolt = 2/2); a land subtype animates only lands carrying it (Living Lands = Forest → 1/1; Kormus Bell = Swamp → 1/1). The loader colors basic lands by their identity, so an animated Swamp already reads as black (a Kormus Bell "black creature") and a Forest as green — no separate color grant is needed. Layer-4 pass adds the CREATURE type; `AllLandsAreCreaturesEffectHandler` fills the base P/T + creature-ness; `GameQueryService.matchesAnimateLand`/`isCreature` and `StaticEffectSupport.isEffectivelyCreature` recognise animated lands (so anthems/lords see them). Manlands keep their own self-animation P/T. |
| `TransformSelfEffect` | `()` | Transforms the source permanent to its back face (or back to front if already transformed). Used by double-faced cards with Transform |
| `TransformAllEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | Transforms all permanents on the battlefield matching the given predicate. Each matching permanent flips to its back face (or back to front if already transformed). Used by Moonmist with `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(HUMAN)` |
| `TapPermanentsEffect(SELF)` + `TransformSelfEffect` | _compose, no dedicated effect_ | "tap this, then transform it": `SequenceEffect.of(new TapPermanentsEffect(TapUntapScope.SELF), new TransformSelfEffect())`, typically under `ConditionalEffect(new DidntAttack(), ...)` for back-face end-step triggers (e.g. Homicidal Brute) |
| `PreventTransformEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | STATIC restriction: permanents controlled by the source's controller that match `filter` (evaluated against their current face) can't transform. Consulted by `GameQueryService.isTransformPrevented` in all transform resolution paths (`TransformSelfEffect`, `TransformAllEffect`). Used by Immerwolf with a non-Human Werewolf filter (`PermanentAllOfPredicate(WEREWOLF, NOT HUMAN)`) for "Non-Human Werewolves you control can't transform" |
| `DrawDiscardTransformIfCreatureDiscardedEffect` | `()` | Draw 1, discard 1; if creature discarded, untap + transform source. Loot with conditional transform (e.g. Civilized Scholar) |
| `DrawDiscardBoostSelfByDiscardedManaValueEffect` | `()` | Draw 1, discard 1; source then gets +X/+0 until end of turn where X = discarded card's mana value. The boost is applied via a pending hook (`pendingBoostSourceByDiscardedManaValue`) once the player picks the discard, so it works with the interactive discard choice (e.g. Spellbound Dragon on `ON_ATTACK`). Non-targeting |
| `AddCardTypeToTargetPermanentEffect` | `(CardType cardType)` or `(CardType cardType, boolean persistent)` | target permanent becomes the given card type in addition to its other types. When persistent=false (default, 1-arg constructor), stored in `grantedCardTypes` and cleared at end of turn (e.g. Liquimetal Coating). When persistent=true, stored in `persistentGrantedCardTypes` and survives turn resets (e.g. Phyrexian Scriptures chapter I making a creature an artifact permanently) |
| `GrantBasicLandTypeToTargetEffect` | `(EffectDuration duration)`, `(EffectDuration duration, CardSubtype fixedSubtype)`, or `(EffectDuration duration, CardSubtype fixedSubtype, boolean replacing)` | changes a target land's basic land type. When `replacing == false` (default): adds the type "in addition to its other types" + grants that type's mana ability; UNTIL_END_OF_TURN uses transient subtypes + temporary abilities, CONTINUOUS uses granted subtypes + permanent abilities. When `replacing == true`: the land **becomes** the chosen type (UNTIL_END_OF_TURN only), losing its other land types/mana ability per rule 305.7 — stored in `Permanent.transientLandTypeOverride`, applied by the layered pass as the last layer-4 land-type override (legacy precedence: after all static setters) and read by `getOverriddenLandManaColor` (tap produces the new color), cleared by `resetModifiers()`. With `fixedSubtype == null`, prompts controller to choose (AddBasicLandTypeChoice, carrying the `replacing` flag); with a fixed subtype, applies directly. permanent-targeting spec. Used by Navigator's Compass (prompt, add, UNTIL_END_OF_TURN), Aquitect's Will (fixed ISLAND, add, CONTINUOUS), Tideshaper Mystic (prompt, replacing, UNTIL_END_OF_TURN) |
| `GrantBasicLandTypeToTargetEffect` | `(EffectDuration duration)`, `(EffectDuration duration, CardSubtype fixedSubtype)`, or `(EffectDuration duration, CardSubtype fixedSubtype, boolean replacing)` | changes a target land's basic land type. When `replacing == false` (default): adds the type "in addition to its other types" + grants that type's mana ability; UNTIL_END_OF_TURN uses transient subtypes + temporary abilities, CONTINUOUS uses granted subtypes + permanent abilities. When `replacing == true`: the land **becomes** the chosen type, losing its other land types/mana ability per rule 305.7 — applied by the layered pass as the last layer-4 land-type override (legacy precedence: after all static setters) and read by `getOverriddenLandManaColor` (tap produces the new color). UNTIL_END_OF_TURN stores it in `Permanent.transientLandTypeOverride` (cleared by `resetModifiers()`); UNTIL_CONTROLLERS_NEXT_UNTAP_STEP stores it in `Permanent.untilNextTurnLandTypeOverride` (survives end-of-turn cleanup, cleared at the land controller's next turn by `clearUntilNextTurnEffects()`). Both read via `Permanent.getEffectiveLandTypeOverride()`. With `fixedSubtype == null`, prompts controller to choose (AddBasicLandTypeChoice, carrying the `replacing` flag); with a fixed subtype, applies directly. canTargetPermanent=true. Used by Navigator's Compass (prompt, add, UNTIL_END_OF_TURN), Aquitect's Will (fixed ISLAND, add, CONTINUOUS), Tideshaper Mystic (prompt, replacing, UNTIL_END_OF_TURN), Orcish Farmer (fixed SWAMP, replacing, UNTIL_CONTROLLERS_NEXT_UNTAP_STEP) |
| `GrantEquipByManaValueEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate filter)` | grants matching permanents an equip ability with cost {X} and boosts equipped creatures +X/+0, where X = permanent's mana value (static) |

## Enchantment-specific

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `PutAuraFromHandOntoSelfEffect` | `()` | put an aura from hand onto this creature (ETB) |
| `PutAuraFromHandOntoSelfWithinXManaValueOrExileEffect` | `()` | Evershrike: "You may put an Aura card with mana value X or less from your hand onto the battlefield attached to this creature. If you don't, exile this creature." The mana-value cap is the ability's paid X (`entry.getXValue()`); only Aura cards with `getManaValue() <= X` are offered. Declining, or having no eligible Aura, exiles the source (via the `exileSourceIfDeclinedId` field on `PendingInteraction.TargetedHandCardChoice`). Pair after a self-return-to-battlefield `ReturnCardFromGraveyardEffect` in a graveyard activated ability |
| `GainControlOfTargetAuraEffect` | `()` | gain control of target aura |
| `ChangeColorTextEffect` | `(boolean colorWordsAllowed, boolean landTypesAllowed, boolean canTargetSpell)` | change color words (when `colorWordsAllowed`) and/or basic land type words (when `landTypesAllowed`) in target permanent's text (Mind Bend = `(true, true, false)` / Sleight of Mind-style; Magical Hack = `(false, true, true)`, land types only). When `canTargetSpell` the target may instead be a spell on the stack (Glamerdye = `(true, false, true)`, color words only): the change is recorded in `gameData.spellTextReplacements` keyed by the spell's card id and carried onto the permanent it resolves into by `BattlefieldEntryService` (CR 613.7); on an instant/sorcery it is an inert no-op. Resolution writes a `TextReplacement` into `Permanent.textReplacements` — a CR 613 layer-3 text change: `TextChangeTransformer` rewrites the words of every effect instance the permanent contributes before layers 4–7 apply them, and its own printed protection/basic land types are seeded rewritten. Persists indefinitely (survives `resetModifiers()`), NOT copiable (CR 707.2). A "spell or permanent" single target is routed by zone inference in `SpellCastingService` (hand + retrace paths) via `TargetLegalityService.isSpellOnStack`. See `agent-docs/LAYER_SYSTEM.md` step 9 for the covered effect types |

## Equipment

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `EquipEffect` | `()` | equip to target creature. Prefer using `EquipActivatedAbility(manaCost)` which wraps this effect with sorcery-speed timing and "creature you control" filter |
| `StaticBoostEffect` | `(int powerBoost, int toughnessBoost, GrantScope.EQUIPPED_CREATURE)` | equipped creature gets +X/+Y (static). See Boost Effects section for full constructor signatures |
| `AttachedBoostEffect` | `(DynamicAmount powerBoost, DynamicAmount toughnessBoost, GrantScope.EQUIPPED_CREATURE)` | equipped creature gets +X/+Y where the amounts are `DynamicAmount`s (static). Collapsed the `BoostCreaturePer*` family; amounts evaluate against the Equipment's controller (see Boost Effects section). Bonehoard/Runechanter's Pike (`CardsInGraveyard`), Blackblade Reforged (`PermanentCount(PermanentIsLandPredicate, CONTROLLER)`), Lashwrithe (`PermanentCount(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(SWAMP), CONTROLLER)`), Strata Scythe (`LandsMatchingImprintedName()`) |
| `SacrificeOnUnattachEffect` | `()` | whenever this equipment becomes unattached, sacrifice the previously-equipped creature (static marker) |
| `AttachSourceEquipmentToTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | attach source equipment to target creature. Reads targetId as creature; finds equipment via sourcePermanentId (ETB path) or by card ID fallback (death trigger path). Used by equipment with "When this Equipment enters, attach it to target creature you control" (ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD) or "Whenever equipped creature dies, attach this Equipment to target creature you control" (ON_EQUIPPED_CREATURE_DIES). |
| `AttachSourceEquipmentToEnteringCreatureEffect` | `()` | `ON_ANY_OTHER_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` trigger-materialising marker: "you may attach this Equipment to it" (the creature that entered — non-targeting). The enter collector resolves the entering permanent and queues `MayEffect(AttachSourceEquipmentToTargetCreatureEffect)` with targetId = entering creature, sourcePermanentId = this Equipment; the equipment may attach to a creature under any player's control. Gate the subtype via `TriggeringCardConditionalEffect(new CardSubtypePredicate(subtype), …)`. Used by Cloak and Dagger (Rogue). |
| `AttachSourceAuraToTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | move the source Aura (already on the battlefield) onto target creature. Reads targetId as creature, sourcePermanentId as the Aura; reattaches and gives a new timestamp (CR 613.7e). Queued by the enter collector for Prison Term. |
| `AttachAllAurasToAnotherPermanentEffect` | `()` | targeted ETB (targets any permanent): move **all** Auras enchanting the targeted permanent onto another permanent controlled by the same player that every one of those Auras can legally enchant. On resolution collects the Auras, computes valid recipients (same controller, passes every Aura's enchant filter), and prompts the controller via `PermanentChoiceContext.AttachAllAurasToAnotherPermanent`; each Aura gets a new timestamp (CR 613.7e) and control is recomputed. No Auras, or no legal recipient → nothing moves. Used by Glamer Spinners. |
| `AttachSourceAuraToEnteringCreatureEffect` | `()` | `ON_OPPONENT_CREATURE_ENTERS_BATTLEFIELD` trigger-materialising marker: "you may attach this Aura to that creature" (the creature an opponent controls that just entered — non-targeting). The enter collector resolves the entering permanent and queues `MayEffect(AttachSourceAuraToTargetCreatureEffect)` with targetId = entering creature, sourcePermanentId = this Aura, so the Aura's controller chooses whether to move it. Used by Prison Term. |
| `AttachTargetEquipmentToTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | attach target Equipment to target creature (multi-target; reads targetIds[0] as equipment, [1] as creature) |
| `AttachTargetAuraToTargetCreatureEffect` | `()` | move a target Aura (already on the battlefield) onto target creature (multi-target; reads targetIds[0] as the Aura, [1] as the creature; expires floating effects for the old host and gives a new timestamp per CR 613.7e). Aura variant of `AttachTargetEquipmentToTargetCreatureEffect`. Pair the aura target with `PermanentIsAuraAttachedToCreaturePredicate`. Used by Crown of the Ages ("{4}, {T}: Attach target Aura attached to a creature to another creature") |
| `SacrificeSourceEquipmentCost` | `()` | cost effect that sacrifices the equipment granting this ability (not the equipped creature). Used for equipment-granted abilities like Blazing Torch's "{T}, Sacrifice Blazing Torch: ..." where the creature activates the ability but the equipment is sacrificed. The source equipment is identified via `ActivatedAbility.grantSourcePermanentId`, which is set automatically by the static bonus system |

## Static restrictions / taxes

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `CantCastSpellsWithSameNameAsExiledCardEffect` | `()` or `(boolean opponentsOnly)` | prevents casting spells with the same name as the card imprinted on the source permanent. When `opponentsOnly=false` (default), restricts all players (Exclusion Ritual); when `opponentsOnly=true`, only opponents of the source's controller are restricted (Ixalan's Binding) |
| `SpellsWithChosenNameCantBeCastEffect` | `()` or `(boolean opponentsOnly)` | spells with the chosen name on the source permanent can't be cast (static). Default (`opponentsOnly=false`) restricts every player, incl. the controller (Nevermore); `true` restricts only the controller's opponents (Gideon's Intervention). Enforced in `CastingPermissionService.getForbiddenCardNames` |
| `PlayerHasProtectionFromChosenNameEffect` | `()` | the source permanent's controller has protection from the chosen card name on the source permanent (static, Runed Halo). The player can't be targeted, dealt damage (combat or noncombat), or enchanted by anything with that name. Pair with `ChooseCardNameOnEnterEffect()`. Scanned by `GameQueryService.playerHasProtectionFromChosenName` from targeting/damage services |
| `PreventDamageFromChosenNameEffect` | `()` | static: prevent all damage (combat or noncombat) that would be dealt to the source's controller and the permanents they control by sources whose name equals the chosen name (Gideon's Intervention). Damage only — unlike `PlayerHasProtectionFromChosenNameEffect` it does not stop targeting/enchanting, and it also covers the controller's permanents. Pair with `ChooseCardNameOnEnterEffect()`. Scanned by `GameQueryService.isDamageFromChosenNamePreventedForController` from `DamageSupport` (player + creature/planeswalker noncombat) and `CombatDamageService` (player, creature, and planeswalker combat) |
| `CantCastSpellTypeEffect` | `(Set<CardType> restrictedTypes)` / `(Set<CardType> restrictedTypes, boolean appliesToAllPlayers)` | can't cast spells of the specified types (static). Default (`appliesToAllPlayers=false`) restricts only the source's controller (Steel Golem: "You can't cast creature spells"); pass `true` for a symmetric restriction affecting every player (Aether Storm: "Creature spells can't be cast"). Enforced in `CastingPermissionService.getRestrictedSpellTypes` |
| `NoncreatureSpellsCantBeCastEffect` | `(int minManaValue, boolean restrictXSpells)` | global/symmetric: no player (incl. controller) can cast a noncreature spell with mana value >= `minManaValue`, or (if `restrictXSpells`) a noncreature spell with `{X}` in its cost. Gaddock Teeg uses `(4, true)`. Enforced via `CastingPermissionService.isNoncreatureSpellCastRestricted` at the hand/exile/library-top playable sites |
| `CantSearchLibrariesEffect` | `(boolean payableToIgnore)` | players can't search libraries (static). `payableToIgnore=true` (no-arg default, Leonin Arbiter): any player may pay {2} to ignore until end of turn. `payableToIgnore=false` (Mindlock Orb): absolute, no pay-to-ignore |
| `OpponentSearchesTopCardsInsteadEffect` | `(int count)` | static: when an opponent of this permanent's controller would search ANY library, they search only the top `count` cards of that library instead (Aven Mindcensor, `count=4`). Passive rules-modifier (like `CantSearchLibrariesEffect`) — no `NormalEffectHandlerBean`; read at search-initiation time in `LibrarySearchSupport.sendLibrarySearchToPlayer`, which narrows the candidate list to the top-N of the searched library (owner = `params.targetPlayerId()` else searcher) and, if that becomes empty, ends the search with nothing found + shuffle. A player's own copy never limits their own searches |
| `PlayersCannotDrawCardsEffect` | `()` | players can't draw cards (static, Omen Machine, Maralen of the Mornsong) |
| `TargetPlayerLosesLifeAndSearchesLibraryToHandEffect` | `(int lifeLoss)` | EACH_DRAW_TRIGGERED: the draw-step player (`entry.getTargetId()`) loses `lifeLoss` life, then performs a mandatory unrestricted search of their own library for a card to hand, then shuffles. Both parts act on the draw-step player (not the controller). Used by Maralen of the Mornsong paired with a static `PlayersCannotDrawCardsEffect` |
| `LimitSpellsPerTurnEffect` | `(int maxSpells)` | each player can cast at most N spells per turn (static) |
| `LimitSpellsForEnchantedPlayerEffect` | `(int maxSpells)` | enchanted player can cast at most N spells per turn (static, Curse Aura on a player, e.g. Curse of Exhaustion) |
| `LimitSpellsForControllerEffect` | `(int maxSpells)` | the source's **controller** can cast at most N spells per turn (static). Controller-only variant of `LimitSpellsPerTurnEffect`; enforced in `CastingPermissionService.getMaxSpellsPerTurn`. Used by Colfenor's Plans ("You can't cast more than one spell each turn") |
| `SkipDrawStepEffect` | `()` | static marker: the controller skips their draw step (no turn-based draw, no draw-step triggers). Enforced in `StepTriggerService.handleDrawStep`. Used by Colfenor's Plans |
| `IslandSanctuaryEffect` | `()` | marker placed in the `MAY_SKIP_DRAW_STEP_DRAW` slot (never resolved). Its presence makes `StepTriggerService.handleDrawStep` offer the controller a may-ability to skip the draw-step draw; accepting stamps an `UNTIL_YOUR_NEXT_TURN` player-scoped `CreaturesCantAttackControllerUnlessPredicateEffect(PermanentAnyOfPredicate(flying, islandwalk))` floating effect. Used by Island Sanctuary. The attack shield is checked in `CombatAttackService.isCantAttackDefenderDueToRestriction`, which scans both defender static abilities and player-scoped floating effects |
| `IncreaseOpponentCastCostEffect` | `(Set<CardType> affectedTypes, int amount)` | opponent's spells of types cost N more (static) |
| `IncreaseSpellCostEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate, int amount)` | matching spells cost N more for all players (static, symmetric; e.g. Thalia with CardNotPredicate(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE))) |
| `IncreaseOwnCastCostEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate, int amount)` | matching spells cost N more, but only when cast by the source permanent's controller (static, self-scoped — unlike the symmetric `IncreaseSpellCostEffect`). E.g. Derelor with `CardColorPredicate(BLACK)`, 1 ("Black spells you cast cost {B} more"; the {B} tax is modeled as +1 generic). Handled by `IncreaseOwnCastCostEffectHandler` |
| `IncreaseSpellCostExceptOnControllersTurnEffect` | `(int amount)` | every spell costs N more for all players, except while it is the spell's controller's own turn (static, symmetric; e.g. Defense Grid, {3}). Handled by `IncreaseSpellCostExceptOnControllersTurnEffectHandler` (battlefield source; waives the tax when `castingPlayerId == activePlayerId`) |
| `IncreaseOwnCastCostUnlessRevealSubtypeEffect` | `(int amount, CardSubtype subtype)` | spell-self cost modifier (STATIC slot): this spell costs `amount` more to cast unless the caster holds a card of `subtype` (other than the spell itself) to reveal from hand. Models the Lorwyn "reveal a creature-type card or pay {N}" additional cost (e.g. Goldmeadow Stalwart, Kithkin/{3}); auto-reveal is game-state-equivalent since revealing never removes the card. Handled by `IncreaseOwnCastCostUnlessRevealSubtypeEffectHandler` |
| `IncreaseOpponentCostForTargetingControlledPermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, int amount)` | opponent spells/abilities that target a permanent matching the predicate you control cost N more (static; e.g. Kopala with `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(MERFOLK)`, 2) |
| `IncreaseActivatedAbilityCostEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, int amount)` | activated abilities of permanents matching the predicate cost N more generic mana to activate, for all players (static, symmetric; e.g. Gloom with a white-enchantment predicate, 3). Implements the `ActivatedAbilityCostIncreasingEffect` capability interface; `CastingCostService.getActivatedAbilityActivationTax` sums matching taxes and `AbilityActivationService` folds the result into the activation's generic-mana cost |
| `ReduceGraveyardCardActivatedAbilityCostEffect` | `(CardPredicate filter, int amount)` | activated abilities of graveyard cards matching the predicate cost N less generic mana to activate, controller-scoped ("in your graveyard"; static; e.g. Embalmer's Tools with a creature-card predicate, 1 — also cheapens Embalm/Eternalize). Implements the `GraveyardActivatedAbilityCostReducingEffect` capability interface; `CastingCostService.getGraveyardActivatedAbilityCostReduction` sums matching reductions from the activating player's battlefield and `AbilityActivationService` subtracts the result (floored to the generic portion) from the graveyard ability's cost |
| `IncreaseEachPlayerCastCostPerSpellThisTurnEffect` | `(int amountPerSpell)` | each spell a player casts costs N more for each other spell that player has already cast this turn; affects all players (static, Damping Sphere) |
| `ReplaceLandExcessManaWithColorlessEffect` | `()` | if a land is tapped for two or more mana, it produces {C} instead of any other type and amount (static, Damping Sphere) |
| `RequirePaymentToAttackEffect` | `(int amountPerAttacker)` | must pay N mana per attacking creature — uniform tax read from the DEFENDER's battlefield, applies to every attacker (static, e.g. Windborn Muse). For a tax scoped to a single enchanted creature use `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackUnlessPaysEffect` |
| `EnchantedCreatureCantAttackUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int amount)` | Aura static: the enchanted creature can't attack unless its controller pays {amount} generic as an additional cost to declare it (Brainwash, {3}). Summed per declared attacker in `CombatAttackService.declareAttackers` via `GameQueryService.getEnchantedCreatureAttackTax`; no handler (read directly). Contrast `RequirePaymentToAttackEffect` (uniform, all attackers) |
| `CantBlockHighPowerCreaturesUnlessPaysEffect` | `(int minAttackerPower, int amount)` | static: this creature can't block a creature with effective power ≥ `minAttackerPower` unless its controller pays {amount} generic as an additional cost to declare the block (Hipparion — power 3+, {1}). Block-side counterpart of the attack tax: summed per qualifying block in `CombatBlockService.declareBlockers` (validated + charged from the defender's pool), read via the `BlockCostEffect` capability interface; no handler. The block stays legal for target-legality purposes — it's only the mana cost that gates it |
| `AlternativeCostForSpellsEffect` | `(String manaCost, CardPredicate filter)` or `(String manaCost, CardPredicate filter, CounterType manaValueCapCounter, boolean oncePerTurn)` | controller may pay the alternative mana cost rather than the mana cost for spells matching the filter (static, from battlefield permanent, e.g. Rooftop Storm with "{0}" and creature+zombie filter, Jodah with "{W}{U}{B}{R}{G}" and null filter for all spells). Optional `manaValueCapCounter` (nullable) caps the alternative cost to spells whose mana value ≤ the count of that counter on the source; `oncePerTurn` limits the source to one use per turn (As Foretold: `"{0}"`, null filter, `CounterType.TIME`, `true`). Applied by `CastingCostService` (consumed via `consumeFreeCastFromBattlefield`; once-per-turn use tracked in `GameData.freeCastPermanentUsedThisTurn`, cleared each turn). |
| `FreeCyclingWhileHandSizeEffect` | `(int minCardsInHand)` | static (from battlefield permanent, `EffectSlot.STATIC`): "you may pay {0} rather than pay cycling costs as long as you have `minCardsInHand`+ cards in hand" (New Perspectives, 7). The ability analog of `AlternativeCostForSpellsEffect` — CR 118.9 alt cost that replaces only the mana cost; the intrinsic "discard this card" cost of cycling is still paid. Read directly in `AbilityActivationService.activateHandAbility` (cycling identified by its reminder-text `"Cycling"` description prefix) via the `FreeCyclingEffect` capability interface; the hand-size check counts the card being cycled (checked before it's discarded). No handler bean. |
| `ReduceOwnCastCostEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | reduce this spell's own cast cost by the evaluated amount of generic mana (spell-self). Fixed reductions use `Fixed(N)`; "for each …" reductions use a counting amount — Ghoultree `CardsInGraveyard(CardTypePredicate(CREATURE), CONTROLLER)`, Blasphemous Act `PermanentCount(PermanentIsCreaturePredicate, ANY_PLAYER)`. **Conditional reductions ("costs {N} less to cast if …") wrap this in `ConditionalEffect(condition, ReduceOwnCastCostEffect(Fixed(N)))`** — e.g. Academy Journeymage `ControlsPermanent(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(WIZARD))`, Stoic Rebuttal `Metalcraft()`, Avatar of Might `OpponentControlsMoreCreatures(4)`, Wilt in the Heat `CardsLeftGraveyardThisTurn()`. **Do NOT add per-variant `ReduceOwnCastCostIf*`/`ReduceOwnCastCostPer*` records** — see `COST_MODIFICATION_HANDLERS.md` |
| `ReduceOwnCastCostForCardTypeEffect` | `(Set<CardType> affectedTypes, DynamicAmount amount)` | reduce controller's spells of given types by the amount (static, from battlefield permanent, e.g. Heartless Summoning) |
| `ReduceCastCostForMatchingSpellsEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate, int amount, CostModificationScope scope)` | reduce cast cost of spells matching the predicate by N generic mana; scope SELF = controller's spells, OPPONENT = opponents' spells (static, from battlefield permanent, e.g. Jhoira's Familiar with CardIsHistoricPredicate, Goblin Warchief with CardSubtypePredicate(GOBLIN), Danitha Capashen with CardAnyOfPredicate of CardSubtypePredicate(AURA/EQUIPMENT)) |
| `ReduceOwnCastCostForSharedCardTypeWithImprintEffect` | `(DynamicAmount amount)` | reduce cast cost of controller's spells by the amount if they share a card type with the imprinted card (static, Semblance Anvil) |
| `ReduceOwnCastCostIfTargetingControlledPermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, int amount)` | reduce this spell's cast cost by N if it targets a permanent matching the predicate that the caster controls (static, Savage Stomp uses `PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(DINOSAUR)`). **Kept as its own record** because the reduction gates on the being-cast spell's chosen first target, which the generic cost path does not see — resolved inline in `CastingCostService.computeTargetBasedCostReduction`, not via a costmod handler. Playability optimistically checks if controller controls a matching permanent; actual reduction is validated against the chosen first target in `SpellCastingService` |
| `ReduceOwnCastCostIfTargetingStackEntryEffect` | `(StackEntryPredicate predicate, int amount)` | reduce this spell's cast cost by N if its first target is a spell on the stack matching the predicate (static, Brush Off uses `StackEntryTypeInPredicate(INSTANT_SPELL, SORCERY_SPELL)`). Kept as its own record (target-gated, see above). Playability optimistically checks if any stack spell matches; actual reduction is validated against the chosen first target in `SpellCastingService` |
| `ReduceOwnCastCostIfTargetingPermanentEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate, int amount)` | reduce this spell's cast cost by N if its first target is a permanent matching the predicate (static, Ajani's Response uses `PermanentAllOfPredicate(creature, tapped)`). Kept as its own record (target-gated, see above). Playability optimistically checks if any battlefield permanent matches; actual reduction is validated against the chosen first target in `SpellCastingService` |
| `SacrificeCreaturesForCostReductionEffect` | `(int reductionPerCreature)` | as an additional cost, you may sacrifice any number of creatures; this spell costs N less for each creature sacrificed (static, Torgaar). Frontend sends creature IDs via `alternateCostSacrificePermanentIds`. Uses `paySacrificeCreaturesForCostReduction` in SpellCastingService |
| `NoMaximumHandSizeEffect` | `()` | you have no maximum hand size (static, requires permanent on battlefield) |
| `GrantPermanentNoMaxHandSizeEffect` | `()` | you have no maximum hand size for the rest of the game (one-shot spell effect, persists via GameData.playersWithNoMaximumHandSize) |
| `ReduceOpponentMaxHandSizeEffect` | `(int reduction)` | each opponent's maximum hand size is reduced by N (static, checked during cleanup discard). Implements `OpponentMaxHandSizeEffect` |
| `SetOpponentMaximumHandSizeEffect` | `(int maximumHandSize)` | the chosen opponent's maximum hand size is set to a specific value (Cursed Rack — four; modeled as applying to the controller's opponent(s)). Static, checked during cleanup discard. Implements `OpponentMaxHandSizeEffect`; `TurnCleanupService.getMaxHandSize` folds all such effects over the running value in timestamp order (CR 402.2), so a "set" applied last overrides earlier reductions and a "reduce" applied after a "set" subtracts from it. `NoMaximumHandSizeEffect` still wins (checked separately in `hasNoMaximumHandSize`) |
| `EntersTappedEffect` | `()` | this permanent enters the battlefield tapped (static, implements `ReplacementEffect`). Replaces `setEntersTapped(true)` |
| `SacrificePermanentsToUntapSelfEffect` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter, String description)` | resolution: all-or-nothing "sacrifice `count` matching permanents. If you do, untap this creature." Handler no-ops (source stays tapped) unless the controller controls ≥ `count` matching; auto-selects which to sacrifice, then untaps `entry.getSourcePermanentId()`. Wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may" (Leviathan, UPKEEP_TRIGGERED) |
| `CantAttackUnlessSacrificeEffect` | `(int count, PermanentPredicate filter, String description)` | STATIC additional attack cost: this creature can't attack unless its controller sacrifices `count` matching permanents (paid as attackers are declared). No dispatch handler — read directly by `AttackSacrificeCostService.paySacrificeAttackCosts` from the declare-attackers commit phase (sacrifice deferred to last so it can't shift battlefield indices). Pair with a `CantAttackUnlessEffect(ControlsPermanentCount(count, filter), …)` legality gate; Leviathan (`2, Island`) |
| `EnterPermanentsOfTypesTappedEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` or `(Set<CardType> cardTypes, boolean opponentsOnly)` | permanents of specified types enter tapped (static). When `opponentsOnly` is true, only opponents' permanents are affected (e.g. Urabrask the Hidden) |
| conditional enters-tapped (check/fast/slow lands) | `ConditionalReplacementEffect(condition, new EntersTappedEffect())` in STATIC | "enters tapped unless …" — the condition is the **negated** unless-clause (true ⇒ tapped), evaluated during entry (`BattlefieldEntryService.applyConditionalEnterTapped`) against the entering permanent's controller. Check land = `ControlsPermanentCountAtMost(0, PermanentHasAnySubtypePredicate)`; fast land ("N or fewer other lands") = `ControlsPermanentCount(N+1, PermanentIsLandPredicate)`; slow land ("N or more other lands") = `ControlsPermanentCountAtMost(N-1, PermanentIsLandPredicate)`. No dedicated per-cycle record — the old `EntersTappedUnless{ControlsPermanent,FewLands,ManyLands}Effect` were collapsed onto this |
| `CreaturesOfUnchosenParityEnterTappedEffect` | `()` | replacement (STATIC): each creature (any controller) whose mana value does NOT match the source permanent's chosen odd/even quality enters tapped. Pairs with `ChooseManaValueParityOnEnterEffect`; parity read from `Permanent.getChosenManaValueParity()` (no effect while null). Handled in `BattlefieldEntryService.applyUnchosenParityEnterTapped`. Used by Ashling's Prerogative |
| `GrantKeywordToCreaturesOfChosenParityEffect` | `(Set<Keyword> keywords)` or `(Keyword)` | static: each creature (any controller) whose mana value matches the source permanent's chosen odd/even quality gains the keyword(s). Parity read from `Permanent.getChosenManaValueParity()` (no grant while null). Used by Ashling's Prerogative (haste) |
| `ChooseManaValueParityOnEnterEffect` | `()` | ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD marker: "As this enchantment enters, choose odd or even. (Zero is even.)" Prompts an ODD/EVEN list choice and stores it via `Permanent.setChosenManaValueParity`. For enchantments, dispatched in `StackResolutionService.resolveEnchantmentSpell`. Used by Ashling's Prerogative |
| `ChooseNumberOnEnterEffect` / `ChooseNumberEffect` | `(int minNumber, int maxNumber)` | "choose a number between min and max", stored on the permanent via `Permanent.setChosenNumber`. Both implement the marker interface `NumberChoiceEffect`. `ChooseNumberOnEnterEffect` is the ON_ENTER_BATTLEFIELD "as this enters" variant (dispatched in `StackResolutionService.resolveArtifactSpell`, no registry handler); `ChooseNumberEffect` is the resolvable, on-the-stack variant (registry handler `ChooseNumberEffectHandler`) — wrap in `MayEffect` for "you may choose". Both prompt via `PlayerInputService.beginNumberChoice` (`ChoiceContext.NumberChoice`, options are the range as strings). Read back with the `ChosenNumberOnSource` amount. Used by Shapeshifter |
| `OpponentsCantAttackIfCastSpellThisTurnEffect` | `()` | each opponent who cast a spell this turn can't attack with creatures (static, Angelic Arbiter) |
| `OpponentsCantCastSpellsIfAttackedThisTurnEffect` | `()` | each opponent who attacked with a creature this turn can't cast spells (static, Angelic Arbiter) |
| `OpponentsCantCastSpellsThisTurnEffect` | `()` | opponents of the controller can't cast spells this turn (spell, Silence) |
| `WardOfBonesEffect` | `()` | static (Ward of Bones): each opponent controlling more creatures/artifacts/enchantments than the source's controller can't cast spells of that type (each type compared independently), and each opponent controlling more lands can't play lands. Casting side folded into `CastingPermissionService.getRestrictedSpellTypes`; land side via `CastingPermissionService.isLandPlayRestrictedByWardOfBones` (checked in `GameBroadcastService` land-playable computation). Controller is never restricted |
| `TargetPlayerCantPlayLandsThisTurnEffect` | `()` | the stack entry's target player can't play lands for the rest of this turn (declare the player target on the card via `target(...)`); tracked in `GameData.playersCantPlayLandsThisTurn`, cleared at end of turn. Moonhold |
| `TargetPlayerCantCastCreatureSpellsThisTurnEffect` | `()` | the stack entry's target player can't cast creature spells for the rest of this turn (declare the player target via `target(...)`); tracked in `GameData.playersCantCastCreatureSpellsThisTurn` and folded into `CastingPermissionService.getRestrictedSpellTypes`, cleared at end of turn. Moonhold |

## Choose / name

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `ChooseCardNameOnEnterEffect` | `()` or `(List<CardType> excludedTypes)` or `(List<CardType> excludedTypes, boolean lookAtOpponentHand)` | choose a card name as ETB (implements `ChooseCardNameEffect` marker). No-arg allows any name (Pithing Needle); with excludedTypes filters the name list (e.g. `List.of(LAND)` for Phyrexian Revoker); `lookAtOpponentHand=true` reveals opponent's hand before choice (Sorcerous Spyglass) |
| `ActivatedAbilitiesOfChosenNameCantBeActivatedEffect` | `()` or `(boolean blocksManaAbilities)` | activated abilities of chosen name can't be activated (static). No-arg (false) excludes mana abilities (Pithing Needle); `true` also blocks mana abilities (Phyrexian Revoker) |
| `ActivatedAbilitiesOfMatchingPermanentsCantBeActivatedEffect` | `(PermanentPredicate predicate)` | all activated abilities (including mana abilities) of permanents matching the predicate can't be activated (static). Used by Stony Silence with `PermanentIsArtifactPredicate` |
| `ChooseColorOnEnterEffect` | `()` | choose a color as ETB (implements `ChooseColorEffect` marker) |
| `ChooseSubtypeOnEnterEffect` | `()` | choose a creature type as ETB. Detected by `StackResolutionService.resolveEnchantmentSpell()` to prompt `beginSubtypeChoice`. Stores result in `Permanent.chosenSubtype` |
| `ChooseBasicLandTypeOnEnterEffect` | `()` | choose a basic land type as ETB. Detected by `StackResolutionService.resolveEnchantmentSpell()` (aura path) to prompt `beginBasicLandTypeChoice`. Stores result in `Permanent.chosenSubtype`. Used by Convincing Mirage |
| `ChooseAnotherCreatureOnEnterEffect` | `()` | "As this creature enters, choose another creature you control." Replacement effect (CR 614.1c) — not suppressed by Torpor Orb. Detected by `BattlefieldEntryService.handleCreatureEnteredBattlefield()`. Prompts permanent choice, stores result in `Permanent.chosenPermanentId`. If no other creatures exist, enters with no choice. Used by Dauntless Bodyguard |
| `GrantChosenSubtypeToOwnCreaturesEffect` | `(boolean affectsAllZones)` | static effect: each creature you control is the chosen type in addition to its other types. Reads `chosenSubtype` from source permanent. No-arg constructor defaults to `affectsAllZones=false` (battlefield only, e.g. Xenograft). When `affectsAllZones=true`, also applies to creature spells on the stack and creature cards you own in hand/graveyard/library/exile (e.g. Arcane Adaptation). Engine checks via `GameQueryService.cardHasSubtype()` and `computeGrantedSubtypesForOwnedCreatureCard()` |

## Draw replacement / library interaction

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `AbundanceDrawReplacementEffect` | `()` | replace draws with Abundance's reveal-until mechanic (static) |
| `ReturnFromGraveyardInsteadOfDrawEffect` | `()` | static marker (Forbidden Crypt): if the controller would draw a card, they return a card from their graveyard to their hand instead (forced `GraveyardChoice` HAND over the whole graveyard); if the graveyard is empty they lose the game. Detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard`. Usually paired with `ExileOwnCardsInsteadOfGraveyardEffect` |
| `DoubleDrawReplacementEffect` | `()` | static marker (Thought Reflection): if the source's controller would draw a card, they draw two cards instead. Detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard` (draws via two `performDrawCard` calls, so the replaced draws aren't themselves re-doubled) |
| `ZursWeirdingDrawReplacementEffect` | `()` | static marker (Zur's Weirding): every player's draw is replaced — the drawing player reveals the top card, then the other player may pay 2 life (`ReplaceSingleDrawEffect` + `DrawReplacementKind.ZURS_WEIRDING`, may-ability offered to the opponent) to put it into the drawer's graveyard; otherwise they draw it. Detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard`; the accept branch is handled in `MayMiscHandlerService.handleSingleDrawReplacementChoice`. Pairs with `PlayWithHandsRevealedEffect` |
| `ReplaceSingleDrawEffect` | `(UUID playerId, DrawReplacementKind kind)` | replace a single draw with a replacement effect (`ABUNDANCE`, `ZURS_WEIRDING`) |
| `SagesOfTheAnimaDrawReplacementEffect` | `()` | static marker (Sages of the Anima): if the controller would draw a card, instead reveal the top three cards, put every revealed creature card into their hand, and put the rest on the bottom of their library in any order. Implements the capability interface `RevealTopCardsCreaturesToHandDrawReplacementEffect` (`int revealCount()`); detected in `DrawService.resolveDrawCard` via that interface (so no concrete `instanceof` is added). The draw is fully replaced — revealed creatures are put into hand, not "drawn" (no draw triggers), and an empty library does not lose the game. 2+ non-creatures are bottomed via an async `LibraryReorder` |
| `BoobyTrapEffect` | `()` | static marker (Booby Trap): the source controller's opponent (the chosen player) reveals each card they draw; when they draw a card whose name equals the source permanent's `chosenName`, a triggered ability is pushed that sacrifices the trap and deals 10 damage to that player. Detected in `DrawService.performDrawCard` (`checkBoobyTraps`). Pair with `ChooseCardNameOnEnterEffect(List.of(CardType.LAND))` (stamps `chosenName`); the trigger uses `SacrificeSelfThenDealDamageToTargetPlayerEffect(10)` |
| `RevealFirstDrawDrawOnBasicLandEffect` | `()` | static marker (Rowen): the controller reveals the first card they draw each turn; when that card is a basic land, a "draw a card" triggered ability is pushed (`DrawCardEffect(1)`). Detected in `DrawService.performDrawCard` (`checkRevealFirstDrawTriggers`); gated to the turn's first draw via `cardsDrawnThisTurn == 1`, so the extra draw is never revealed itself |
| `PlayLandsFromGraveyardEffect` | `()` | you may play lands from your graveyard (static) |
| `CastPermanentSpellsFromGraveyardEffect` | `()` | you may cast one permanent spell of each type from your graveyard per turn (static, Muldrotha) |

## Put onto battlefield

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `PutCardToBattlefieldEffect` | `(CardPredicate predicate, String label)` or `(…, boolean enterTapped)` or `(…, boolean enterTapped, boolean maxManaValueBoundedByX)` or `(…, boolean enterTapped, boolean maxManaValueBoundedByX, boolean grantHaste, boolean sacrificeAtEndStep)` | you may put a card matching predicate from hand onto battlefield (wrap in MayEffect). `label` is used in prompt text. `grantHaste`=chosen card gains haste until end of turn; `sacrificeAtEndStep`=chosen card is sacrificed at the beginning of the next end step (both `true` for Incandescent Soulstoke's Sneak-Attack-for-Elementals ability). `PutCardToBattlefieldEffect.tappedAndAttacking(predicate, label)` factory = `enterTapped`+`enterAttacking` (chosen creature enters tapped and attacking; Preeminent Captain's ON_ATTACK trigger). E.g. `new PutCardToBattlefieldEffect(new CardTypePredicate(CardType.CREATURE), "creature")`, `new PutCardToBattlefieldEffect(new CardAllOfPredicate(List.of(new CardIsHistoricPredicate(), new CardIsPermanentPredicate())), "historic permanent")` |
| `PutCreatureFromHandThenSacrificeUnlessPayReducedEffect` | `(int genericReduction)` | SPELL: "you may put a creature card from your hand onto the battlefield. If you do, sacrifice it unless you pay its mana cost reduced by {genericReduction}." Reuses the declinable hand-to-battlefield card choice; after the creature enters, a resolution-time pay-or-sacrifice may ability (a `ForcedCostOrElseEffect(new PayManaCost(reducedCost), List.of(new SacrificeSelfEffect()), true)` built in `CardChoiceHandlerService`) charges the reduced cost or sacrifices the creature. Only the generic portion is reduced (floored at 0). Flash (`2`) |
| `OpponentMayPlayCreatureEffect` | `()` | opponent may put a creature card from hand onto battlefield |
| `OpponentMayReturnExiledCardOrDrawEffect` | `(int drawCount)` | opponent may let controller have an exiled card; if declined, controller draws N cards. Used as may-ability marker after library-search-to-exile |

## Card-specific / one-off

| Effect | Constructor | Intent |
|--------|-------------|--------|
| `AjaniUltimateEffect` | `()` | Ajani's ultimate: put 100 counters (planeswalker-specific) |
| `KothEmblemEffect` | `()` | Koth's emblem: Mountains you control have '{T}: This land deals 1 damage to any target.' |
| `VenserEmblemEffect` | `()` | Venser's emblem: "Whenever you cast a spell, exile target permanent." Creates emblem with ExileTargetOnControllerSpellCastEffect |
| `JayaBallardEmblemEffect` | `()` | Jaya Ballard's emblem: "You may cast instant and sorcery spells from your graveyard. If a spell cast this way would be put into your graveyard, exile it instead." Creates emblem with EmblemGrantsFlashbackEffect |
| `TeferiHeroEmblemEffect` | `()` | Teferi, Hero of Dominaria's emblem: "Whenever you draw a card, exile target permanent an opponent controls." Creates emblem with ExileTargetOpponentPermanentOnDrawEffect |
| `GideonOfTheTrialsEmblemEffect` | `()` | Gideon of the Trials' emblem: "As long as you control a Gideon planeswalker, you can't lose the game and your opponents can't win the game." Creates an emblem whose static effect is `ConditionalEffect(ControlsPermanent(PermanentHasSubtypePredicate(GIDEON)), CantLoseGameEffect())`. `GameQueryService.canPlayerLoseGame` reads bare + conditional `CantLoseGameEffect`s off emblems (evaluated with `ConditionContext.forCasting(playerId)`), so no separate win-side hook is needed |
| `ElspethKnightErrantEmblemEffect` | `()` | Elspeth, Knight-Errant's emblem: "Artifacts, creatures, enchantments, and lands you control have indestructible." Creates emblem with GrantKeywordEffect(INDESTRUCTIBLE, OWN_PERMANENTS) filtered to artifact/creature/enchantment/land |
| `ExileTargetOnControllerSpellCastEffect` | `()` | Marker effect stored in Emblem.staticEffects. Triggers when controller casts a spell, prompting target permanent choice then exiling it |
| `ExileTargetOpponentPermanentOnDrawEffect` | `()` | Marker effect stored in Emblem.staticEffects. Triggers when controller draws a card, prompting controller to choose target permanent an opponent controls to exile |
| `EmblemGrantsFlashbackEffect` | `(Set<CardType> cardTypes)` | Static effect stored in Emblem.staticEffects. Permanently grants flashback (at card's mana cost) to cards of matching types in controller's graveyard. Cast spells are exiled after resolution (flashback disposition). |
| `KarnRestartGameEffect` | `()` | Karn's ultimate: restart the game per CR 727, leaving non-Aura permanent cards exiled with Karn in exile, then put them onto battlefield under controller's control. Resets life totals, hands, libraries, graveyards, exile zones, battlefields, and all game state. Controller goes first, no mulligans |
| `KarnScionRevealTwoOpponentChoosesEffect` | `()` | Karn Scion +1: reveal top 2 cards, opponent chooses one for controller's hand, the other is exiled with a silver counter. Uses LIBRARY_REVEAL_CHOICE with pendingKarnScionControllerId |
| `KarnScionReturnSilverCounterCardEffect` | `()` | Karn Scion −1: put a card you own with a silver counter on it from exile into your hand. If multiple, presents LIBRARY_REVEAL_CHOICE to controller. Tracked via GameData.exiledCardsWithSilverCounters |
| `GenesisWaveEffect` | `()` | reveal top X cards, put any number of permanent cards with MV ≤ X onto battlefield, rest to graveyard. X read from `StackEntry.getXValue()` |
| `SphinxAmbassadorEffect` | `()` | ON_COMBAT_DAMAGE_TO_PLAYER trigger: search damaged player's library for a card, that player names a card, if you found a creature with a different name you may put it onto battlefield under your control, then shuffle |
| `SphinxAmbassadorPutOnBattlefieldEffect` | `()` | Marker effect used in PendingMayAbility for the "you may put it onto the battlefield" step of Sphinx Ambassador's trigger |

---

## Provider map (where to add normal effect handlers)

All stack-resolution ("normal") effects use one `@Component` handler class per effect in `service/effect/normalfx/`, implementing `NormalEffectHandlerBean`. Shared logic lives in domain `*Support` classes in the same package (e.g. `DamageSupport`, `LibraryRevealSupport`). New handlers need only the `@Component` annotation — `GameEngineConfig` registers them at startup.

| Category | Handler location | Shared helpers |
|----------|------------------|----------------|
| Damage | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `DamageSupport` |
| Destruction/sacrifice | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `DestructionSupport` |
| Bounce | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `BounceSupport` |
| Counter | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `CounterSupport` |
| Library reveal/search/mill/shuffle | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `LibraryRevealSupport`, `LibrarySearchSupport`, `LibraryShuffleSupport` |
| Graveyard return/exile | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `GraveyardReturnSupport` |
| Player interaction (draw/discard/choices) | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `PlayerInteractionSupport` |
| Life | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `LifeSupport` |
| Boost/pump | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | (handler-local or `GameQueryService`) |
| Tap/untap | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `TapUntapSupport` |
| Keyword grant | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | — |
| Animation/transform | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `AnimationSupport` |
| Permanent control/tokens/regeneration | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `PermanentControlSupport` |
| Permanent counters | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `PermanentCounterSupport` |
| Static continuous effects | `staticfx/*Handler` (see **STATIC_EFFECT_HANDLERS.md**) | `StaticEffectSupport` |
| Cast-cost modifiers (reductions/taxes) | `cast/costmod/*Handler` (see **COST_MODIFICATION_HANDLERS.md**) | `CostModificationSupport` |
| Prevention | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `PreventionSupport` |
| Turn effects | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `TurnSupport` |
| Copy/retarget | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `CopySupport`, `TargetRedirectionSupport` |
| Exile permanent | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `ExileSupport` |
| Return from exile / egg counters | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `ExileSupport` |
| Combat restrictions | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | — |
| Equip | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | — |
| Card-specific one-offs | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | `CardSpecificSupport` |
| Win conditions | `normalfx/*EffectHandler` | — |
| Land-tap triggers | `GameHelper` (`checkLandTapTriggers`) | — |

Orchestration (conditionals, `MayEffect`, stack dispatch) remains in `EffectResolutionService`.

## Target validator map — the `@ValidatesTarget` ESCAPE HATCH (where to add one, rarely)

Structural targeting (category + predicate) is handled entirely by the declarative `TargetSpec`
interpreter in `TargetValidationService` — you do NOT write a validator for it. A hand-written
`@ValidatesTarget` method is now an ESCAPE HATCH, used ONLY when legal targeting turns on a rule the
spec cannot express: opponent-relation, controller/owner compare ("from your graveyard"),
chosen-source inspection, or null-target tolerance (divided-damage / ETB-assignment paths). Such an
effect must STILL declare its structural `targetSpec()` (redundant with the validator's structural
checks — harmless, and the `TargetSpecRatchetTest` guard requires it). Validator classes live in
`service/validate/`, auto-registered via the annotation.

| Category | Validator class | Dependencies |
|----------|----------------|--------------|
| Damage (opponent-or-planeswalker, divided-damage null tolerance, per-recipient player guard) | `DamageTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService`, `GameQueryService` |
| Creature mods (only the equip/attach boost validators — target outside the single-target pipeline) | `CreatureModTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService` |
| Destruction (per-recipient player guard, combat-state "creature blocking this") | `DestructionTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService`, `GameQueryService` |
| Graveyard (own/opponent graveyard controller-compare, card-zone/type checks) | `GraveyardTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService`, `GameQueryService` |
| Exile (return from exile — zone + card filter) | `ExileTargetValidators` | `GameQueryService` |
| Library (no-op-PLAYER `requireTargetPlayer` guards) | `LibraryTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService` |
| Permanent control (aura attachment-state, no-op-PLAYER guard) | `PermanentControlTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService`, `GameQueryService` |
| Life (no-op-PLAYER `requireTargetPlayer` guards) | `LifeTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService` |
| Prevention (divided-prevention null tolerance) | `PreventionTargetValidators` | `TargetValidationService` |

(There is no `BounceTargetValidators` — bounce targeting is fully declarative.)

**Two method signatures supported:**
- **Pattern A:** `void method(TargetValidationContext ctx)` — effect not needed
- **Pattern B:** `void method(TargetValidationContext ctx, ConcreteEffectType effect)` — effect auto-cast

Helper methods on `TargetValidationService`: `requireTarget()`, `requireBattlefieldTarget()`, `requireCreature()`, `checkProtection()`, `requireTargetPlayer()`, `findSourcePermanentIndex()`, `findSourcePermanentController()`.

## Canonical card examples

- Burn spell: `cards/s/Shock.java`
- Multi-effect targeted spell: `cards/c/Condemn.java`
- Effect composition in activated ability: `cards/o/OrcishArtillery.java`
- Spell-copy targeting stack: `cards/t/Twincast.java`
- Aura static lock: `cards/p/Pacifism.java`
- Static "can't block" creature: `cards/s/SpinelessThug.java`
- ETB token + activated cost/effect composition: `cards/s/SiegeGangCommander.java`
- ETB control handoff + upkeep drawback: `cards/s/SleeperAgent.java`
- Opponent draw trigger damage: `cards/u/UnderworldDreams.java`
- Conditional self cast-cost reduction: `cards/a/AvatarOfMight.java`
- Evasion blocked-only-by-wall-or-flying: `cards/e/ElvenRiders.java`
- ETB card name choice + static ability lock: `cards/p/PithingNeedle.java`
- Pain land (tap for colorless or colored + damage): `cards/s/SulfurousSprings.java`
- Creature land (manland): `cards/t/TreetopVillage.java`
- Lord with subtype boost + keywords: `cards/g/GoblinKing.java`
- Equipment with boost: `cards/l/LoxodonWarhammer.java`
